### [1] [Thermodynamics and Optical Properties of Charged Black Holes in Bumblebee gravity Sourced by a Cloud of Strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08764)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Shubham Kala,Ahmad Al-Badawi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies static, spherically symmetric charged black hole solutions in bumblebee gravity—a theory with spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking—surrounded by a cloud of strings. It analyzes thermodynamic properties (mass, temperature, entropy), optical features (photon sphere, shadow, light deflection), and Solar System tests (e.g., perihelion precession) to constrain Lorentz-violating parameters and identify observational signatures beyond General Relativity.
\n\n
本文研究了在自发破缺洛伦兹对称性的bumblebee引力理论中，被弦云包围的静态球对称带电黑洞解。文章分析了其热力学性质（质量、温度、熵）、光学特征（光子球、黑洞阴影、光线偏折）以及太阳系内经典引力检验（如近日点进动），以约束洛伦兹破缺参数并寻找超越广义相对论（GR）的新物理观测信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from exploring gravitational theories beyond General Relativity that incorporate spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking via a non-minimally coupled bumblebee vector field. Such frameworks may offer testable deviations from GR, particularly in strong-field regimes like black holes or in precision Solar System experiments. The inclusion of a cloud of strings adds astrophysical realism and modifies spacetime structure, enabling richer phenomenology.
\n\n
动机源于探索通过非最小耦合的bumblebee矢量场实现自发洛伦兹对称性破缺的广义相对论之外的引力理论。这类框架可能在黑洞等强场区域或高精度太阳系实验中提供可检验的GR偏差。引入弦云增强了天体物理现实性，并改变时空结构，从而产生更丰富的现象学。

Method: The authors construct exact static, spherically symmetric solutions to the Einstein–bumblebee field equations for a charged black hole immersed in a cloud of strings. They compute thermodynamic quantities using standard black hole mechanics, derive the photon sphere radius by analyzing null geodesics, calculate the black hole shadow size, and evaluate light deflection angles. Additionally, they apply post-Newtonian approximations to assess perihelion precession and compare with observational bounds to constrain the Lorentz-violating parameter $\\ell$.
\n\n
作者构建了爱因斯坦–bumblebee场方程中浸没于弦云中的带电黑洞的精确静态球对称解。他们利用标准黑洞力学计算热力学量，通过分析零测地线导出光子球半径，计算黑洞阴影大小，并评估光线偏折角。此外，他们采用后牛顿近似方法计算近日点进动，并与观测限制对比以约束洛伦兹破缺参数$\\ell$。

Result: The study finds that Lorentz violation modifies black hole thermodynamics: entropy deviates from the Bekenstein–Hawking area law, and temperature exhibits dependence on the Lorentz-violating parameter. The photon sphere and shadow are shifted compared to Reissner–Nordström solutions, offering potential observational discriminators. Solar System constraints from perihelion precession yield an upper bound $|\\ell| \\lesssim 10^{-8}$, significantly tightening previous limits.
\n\n
研究发现，洛伦兹破缺会修改黑洞热力学：熵偏离Bekenstein–Hawking面积律，温度依赖于洛伦兹破缺参数。与Reissner–Nordström解相比，光子球和阴影位置发生偏移，提供了潜在的观测判别依据。来自近日点进动的太阳系约束给出上限$|\\ell| \\lesssim 10^{-8}$，显著收紧了此前的限制。

Conclusion: Bumblebee gravity with a string cloud provides a consistent framework to explore Lorentz violation in both strong- and weak-field regimes. The combined analysis of black hole thermodynamics, optical properties, and Solar System tests not only reveals distinctive signatures of new physics but also places stringent empirical bounds on the Lorentz-violating parameter, advancing the program of testing fundamental symmetries through gravitational phenomena.
\n\n
包含弦云的bumblebee引力为在强场和弱场区域探索洛伦兹破缺提供了一个自洽框架。结合黑洞热力学、光学性质和太阳系检验的综合分析，不仅揭示了新物理的独特信号，还对洛伦兹破缺参数施加了严格的实证约束，推动了通过引力现象检验基本对称性的研究纲领。

Abstract: In theories where the Lorentz symmetry of gravity is spontaneously broken, a non-minimally coupled bumblebee vector field acquires a nonzero vacuum expectation value, leading to modifications of standard General Relativity (GR). In this work, we investigate exact solutions describing static and spherically symmetric charged black holes surrounded by a cloud of strings within the framework of bumblebee gravity. We begin by analyzing the thermodynamic properties of these black hole solutions, including their mass, temperature, and entropy, highlighting how Lorentz-violating effects alter standard results. Next, we examine the optical properties of the spacetime, focusing on the photon sphere, the resulting black hole shadow, and the deflection of light, thereby providing potential observational signatures of Lorentz violation. Finally, we explore the impact of Lorentz-violating parameters on classical gravitational tests within the Solar System, such as advance of perihelion precession, in order to set observational constraints. Our analysis provides a comprehensive investigation of the interplay between Lorentz violation, black hole physics, and cloud of strings, offering a framework to probe new physics beyond GR.

</details>


### [2] [Singular gauge transformations in geometrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08766)
*Alcides Garat*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper introduces new tetrads in Einstein-Maxwell spacetimes that link local electromagnetic gauge transformations to tetrad transformations on orthogonal eigenvector planes of the stress-energy tensor. It investigates singular local gauge transformations that map timelike and spacelike tetrad vectors onto the intersection of the local light cone with the timelike-spacelike plane.
\n\n
本文在Einstein-Maxwell时空中引入了新的tetrad，将局域电磁规范变换与应力-能量张量的正交本征矢量平面上的tetrad变换联系起来。文章研究了奇异的局域规范变换，这些变换将类时和类空tetrad矢量映射到局域光锥与类时-类空平面的交线上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the discovery of new tetrads for non-null electromagnetic fields in Einstein-Maxwell spacetimes, which exhibit a direct correspondence between the local electromagnetic gauge group and local tetrad transformation groups on two orthogonal eigenvector planes of the stress-energy tensor. This raises the question of whether certain singular gauge transformations exist that map the timelike and spacelike tetrad vectors into the null directions defined by the intersection of the local light cone with their plane.
\n\n
动机源于在Einstein-Maxwell时空中为非零电磁场发现的新tetrad，这些tetrad在局域电磁规范群与应力-能量张量两个正交本征矢量平面上的局域tetrad变换群之间建立了直接对应关系。这引出了一个关键问题：是否存在某些奇异规范变换，能将类时和类空tetrad矢量映射到由局域光锥与其所在平面交线所定义的类光方向上。

Method: The method involves analyzing the geometric and algebraic structure of the newly introduced tetrads, which are explicitly gauge-dependent. The authors examine the action of local $U(1)$ gauge transformations on the timelike-spacelike eigenvector plane of the Einstein-Maxwell stress-energy tensor and determine conditions under which these transformations send the basis vectors to the null directions at the intersection of the plane with the local light cone. This requires solving for gauge parameters that induce such singular configurations.
\n\n
方法包括分析新引入的、显式依赖于规范的tetrad的几何与代数结构。作者考察局域$U(1)$规范变换在Einstein-Maxwell应力-能量张量的类时-类空本征矢量平面上的作用，并确定在何种条件下这些变换将基矢量映射到该平面与局域光锥交线处的类光方向。这需要求解能诱导此类奇异构型的规范参数。

Result: The paper identifies the existence of specific singular local gauge transformations that map the timelike and spacelike tetrad vectors onto the null generators of the local light cone within their common plane. The number and mathematical characterization of such transformations are determined by the degeneracy conditions imposed by the light cone geometry and the gauge dependence of the tetrad vectors.
\n\n
论文确认了存在特定的奇异局域规范变换，可将类时和类空tetrad矢量映射到其共面内局域光锥的类光生成元上。这类变换的数量及其数学刻画由光锥几何所施加的退化条件以及tetrad矢量的规范依赖性共同决定。

Conclusion: The study reveals a deep interplay between electromagnetic gauge symmetry and the geometric structure of tetrads in Einstein-Maxwell theory. Singular gauge transformations that align tetrad vectors with null directions are not only mathematically well-defined but also physically significant, as they mark boundaries in the space of admissible tetrads and may signal special physical configurations or coordinate singularities.
\n\n
研究表明，在Einstein-Maxwell理论中，电磁规范对称性与tetrad的几何结构之间存在深刻联系。将tetrad矢量对齐到类光方向的奇异规范变换不仅是数学上良定义的，而且具有物理意义，因为它们标志着容许tetrad空间的边界，可能指示特殊的物理构型或坐标奇点。

Abstract: The new tetrads introduced previously for non-null electromagnetic fields in Einstein- Maxwell spacetimes enable a direct link to the local electromagnetic gauge group of transformations. Due to the peculiar elements in the construction of these new tetrads a direct connection can be established between the local group of electromagnetic gauge transformations and local groups of tetrad transformations on two different local and orthogonal planes of eigenvectors of the Einstein-Maxwell stress-energy tensor. These tetrad vectors are gauge dependent. It is an interesting and relevant problem to study if there are local gauge transformations that can map on the timelike-spacelike plane, the timelike and the spacelike vectors into the intersection of the local light cone and the plane itself. How many of these local gauge transformations exist and how the mathematics and the geometry of these particular transformations play out. These local gauge transformations would be singular and it is important to identify them.

</details>


### [3] [Spin Induced Geometry: Emergence of Metric and Torsional Sectors from Spinor Source](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08769)
*Elisa Varani*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We propose a geometric framework where both metric and torsion emerge dynamically from spinor currents via a massive rank-three Lorentz tensor field, leading to Yukawa-suppressed, propagating torsion and an effective spin-induced metric. Spinless particles couple indirectly to spin through this emergent geometry, and distinct fermionic types (Dirac, Weyl, Majorana) yield different geometric phases—especially topological structures in the Majorana case.
\n\n
我们提出一种几何框架，其中度规和挠率通过一个具有局域洛伦兹指标的有质量三阶张量场从旋量流中动态产生，导致被Yukawa压低的、可传播的挠率和一个由自旋诱导的有效度规。无自旋粒子通过该涌现几何间接耦合到自旋流，而不同类型的费米子（Dirac、Weyl、Majorana）会引发不同的几何相——尤其在Majorana情形下会出现拓扑非平庸结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard General Relativity assumes a torsion-free Levi-Civita connection, while Einstein–Cartan theory introduces torsion algebraically via the spin density but does not allow it to propagate. The paper seeks a more fundamental origin for spacetime geometry by deriving both metric and torsion dynamically from fermionic spin currents, without postulating them as intrinsic properties of the connection.
\n\n
标准广义相对论假设无挠的Levi-Civita联络，而Einstein–Cartan理论虽通过自旋密度引入挠率，但仅以代数方式约束，不允许其传播。本文旨在为时空几何寻找更基本的起源，即从费米子自旋流中动态导出度规与挠率，而非将其预设为联络的内禀属性。

Method: The fundamental variable is a massive rank-three field $\\Phi_{abc}$ with local Lorentz indices, obeying a Klein–Gordon equation sourced by the fermionic spin current $S^{ab}{}_{\\mu}$. Projecting $\\Phi_{abc}$ onto spacetime via vielbeins yields a rank-two tensor $G_{\\mu\
u} = e^a_\\mu e^b_\
u \\Phi_{(ab)c} e^c_\\rho \\eta^{\\rho\\sigma}$ (symmetric part) and $T_{\\mu\
u} = e^a_\\mu e^b_\
u \\Phi_{[ab]c} e^c_\\rho \\eta^{\\rho\\sigma}$ (antisymmetric part), interpreted as an effective metric and torsion, respectively. Both satisfy massive wave equations with Yukawa-type suppression. The analysis is carried out for general Dirac, Weyl, and Majorana spinors to explore resulting geometric phases.
\n\n
基本变量是一个具有局域洛伦兹指标的有质量三阶场 $\\Phi_{abc}$，满足由费米子自旋流 $S^{ab}{}_{\\mu}$ 源动的Klein–Gordon方程。通过vielbein将 $\\Phi_{abc}$ 投影到时空指标上，得到二阶张量：对称部分 $G_{\\mu\
u} = e^a_\\mu e^b_\
u \\Phi_{(ab)c} e^c_\\rho \\eta^{\\rho\\sigma}$ 被解释为有效度规，反对称部分 $T_{\\mu\
u} = e^a_\\mu e^b_\
u \\Phi_{[ab]c} e^c_\\rho \\eta^{\\rho\\sigma}$ 对应挠率。二者均满足带有Yukawa型压低的有质量波动方程。文中分别对一般Dirac、Weyl和Majorana旋量进行分析，以探索所产生的几何相。

Result: The framework yields a dynamical, massive torsion that propagates (unlike in Einstein–Cartan theory) and an effective metric induced by spin currents. Spinless test particles follow geodesics of this emergent metric, thereby indirectly sensing fermionic spin—a novel coupling absent in GR and Einstein–Cartan. In the Majorana limit, the symmetric (metric) sector vanishes, leaving purely antisymmetric (axial-torsional) geometry that supports topological solitons like vortices and Skyrmion-like configurations.
\n\n
该框架产生了可传播的、有质量的挠率（不同于Einstein–Cartan理论），以及由自旋流诱导的有效度规。无自旋测试粒子沿此涌现度规的测地线运动，从而间接感知费米子自旋——这是一种在GR和Einstein–Cartan理论中均不存在的新耦合机制。在Majorana极限下，对称（度规）部分消失，仅剩纯反对称（轴向挠率）几何，支持涡旋和类Skyrmion等拓扑孤子结构。

Conclusion: Geometry—including both metric and torsion—can emerge dynamically from spinorial matter without being fundamental. This provides a new mechanism for spin-gravity coupling, predicts propagating torsion with short-range effects, and reveals rich topological structure in purely torsional geometries sourced by Majorana fermions.
\n\n
几何结构——包括度规与挠率——可从旋量物质中动态涌现，而无需作为基本对象。这提供了一种新的自旋-引力耦合机制，预言了具有短程效应的可传播挠率，并揭示了由Majorana费米子源动的纯挠率几何中丰富的拓扑结构。

Abstract: We present a geometric framework in which both metric and torsional degrees of freedom emerge dynamically from spinor currents, without being postulated as fundamental properties of the affine connection. The fundamental dynamical variable is a rank-three field carrying local Lorentz indices, governed by a massive Klein--Gordon equation sourced by fermionic spin currents. Its projection onto spacetime indices yields a rank-two tensor with no definite symmetry; the symmetric and antisymmetric sectors define, respectively, an effective spin-induced metric and the torsional degrees of freedom. Both sectors are massive and Yukawa-suppressed, ensuring decoupling from long-range gravitational dynamics. Unlike Einstein--Cartan theory, torsion here is propagating rather than algebraically constrained. A key consequence is that spinless test particles follow geodesics of the effective metric and are therefore indirectly sensitive to spin currents through the emergent geometric structure~ -- ~a mechanism absent in both standard General Relativity and Einstein--Cartan theory. The spinorial structure of the source is analyzed across three regimes: general Dirac, Weyl, and Majorana fermions, each giving rise to a distinct geometric phase. In the Majorana limit, the geometry becomes purely axial-torsional, admitting topologically non-trivial configurations such as vortices and Skyrmion-like structures, which emerge dynamically from the spinorial source.

</details>


### [4] [Partial Orderings of Curvature Invariants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08775)
*Ivica Smolić*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper derives new pointwise inequalities that establish a hierarchy among curvature invariants for different Petrov and Segre types of spacetimes in arbitrary dimensions, showing how higher-order invariants like the Zakhary--McIntosh scalars in $(1+3)$-dimensional spacetimes are bounded by lower-order ones such as the Kretschmann scalar.
\n\n
本文推导出一组新的逐点不等式，在任意维度下为不同Petrov和Segre类型的时空建立了曲率不变量之间的层级关系，表明在$(1+3)$维时空中，高阶不变量（如Zakhary--McIntosh标量）可由低阶不变量（如Kretschmann标量）所控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the algebraic relationships among curvature invariants is crucial for characterizing spacetime geometries, especially across different algebraic classifications (Petrov and Segre types). The authors aim to clarify whether higher-order curvature scalars are algebraically dependent on or bounded by lower-order ones, which has implications for gravitational physics, singularity analysis, and numerical relativity.
\n\n
理解曲率不变量之间的代数关系对于刻画时空几何至关重要，尤其是在不同的代数分类（Petrov和Segre类型）下。作者旨在澄清高阶曲率标量是否在代数上依赖于或受低阶标量的约束，这对引力物理、奇点分析和数值相对论具有重要意义。

Method: The authors perform a systematic analysis of tensorial contractions of the Ricci tensor in arbitrary spacetime dimension, leveraging algebraic classification schemes (Petrov and Segre types). They derive pointwise inequalities among curvature invariants and examine the conditions under which all Zakhary--McIntosh invariants in $(1+3)$-dimensional spacetimes satisfy upper bounds proportional to appropriate powers of the Kretschmann scalar $R_{\\mu\\nu\\rho\\sigma}R^{\\mu\\nu\\rho\\sigma}$.
\n\n
作者在任意时空维度下对Ricci张量的张量缩并进行系统分析，利用代数分类方案（Petrov和Segre类型），推导曲率不变量之间的逐点不等式，并研究在$(1+3)$维时空中所有Zakhary--McIntosh不变量在何种条件下满足由Kretschmann标量$R_{\\mu\\nu\\rho\\sigma}R^{\\mu\\nu\\rho\\sigma}$的适当幂次所给出的上界。

Result: The paper establishes a practical hierarchy of curvature scalars: for various Petrov and Segre types, specific pointwise inequalities hold, and in $(1+3)$ dimensions, all Zakhary--McIntosh invariants are shown to be bounded above (up to scaling) by the Kretschmann scalar under certain geometric conditions. This demonstrates that higher-order invariants do not always introduce independent information beyond what is encoded in lower-order ones.
\n\n
本文建立了曲率标量的一个实用层级：对于多种Petrov和Segre类型，特定的逐点不等式成立；在$(1+3)$维情形下，在某些几何条件下，所有Zakhary--McIntosh不变量均可被Kretschmann标量（至多相差一个比例因子）所上界控制。这表明高阶不变量并不总能提供超出低阶不变量所编码信息之外的独立信息。

Conclusion: The results provide a clearer algebraic structure for curvature invariants across spacetime classifications, showing that in many physically relevant cases, the Kretschmann scalar serves as a dominant controlling quantity for other curvature scalars. This advances the theoretical understanding of spacetime geometry and may simplify analyses in contexts where full sets of invariants are otherwise unwieldy.
\n\n
这些结果为不同时空分类下的曲率不变量提供了更清晰的代数结构，表明在许多物理相关情形中，Kretschmann标量可作为控制其他曲率标量的主导量。这推进了对时空几何的理论理解，并可能简化那些原本需要处理庞大不变量集合的分析场景。

Abstract: We establish a new set of pointwise inequalities that order curvature invariants across various Petrov and Segre types of spacetimes. In arbitrary spacetime dimension, we systematically analyze inequalities among contractions of the Ricci tensor. We further explore the conditions under which all Zakhary--McIntosh invariants in $(1+3)$-dimensional spacetimes are bounded above (up to appropriate powers) by the Kretschmann scalar. These results establish a practical hierarchy among curvature scalars and clarify the extent to which higher-order invariants are algebraically controlled by lower-order ones or vice versa.

</details>


### [5] [Strong-deflection expansion of the deflection angle near a degenerate photon sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08778)
*Takahisa Igata,Tadashi Sasaki,Naoki Tsukamoto*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We develop a strong-deflection expansion for light deflection near a degenerate photon sphere in static, spherically symmetric spacetimes, isolating the universal and local contributions to the leading divergent term. The coefficient factorizes into a universal constant and a local geometric quantity tied to the third derivative of the effective potential or, invariantly, to the areal-radius derivative of a Weyl-tensor-based tidal measure.
\n\n
我们提出了一种在静态球对称时空中的退化光子球附近光线偏折的强偏折展开方法，分离出主导发散项中的普适部分与局域部分。该系数可分解为一个普适常数和一个由有效势三阶导数决定的局域几何量，或等价地表示为基于Weyl张量的潮汐量的面积半径导数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The standard strong-deflection limit for light rays near a photon sphere becomes ill-defined when the photon sphere is degenerate (i.e., when the effective potential has a higher-order extremum). This paper aims to resolve this issue by providing a well-defined expansion that captures the leading-order divergence even at marginality, enabling consistent gravitational lensing predictions in such exotic spacetimes.
\n\n
当光子球退化时（即有效势具有高阶极值点），标准的强偏折极限方法失效。本文旨在通过构建一个在边缘情形下仍良好定义的展开式，以捕捉主导发散行为，从而在这些奇异时空中实现一致的引力透镜预测。

Method: The authors isolate the divergent part of the deflection-angle integral by expanding the effective potential around the degenerate photon sphere up to third order. They express the leading coefficient in terms of the radius of closest approach $r_0$, showing it factorizes as $C = \bar{a} \cdot f(r_{\text{ph}})$, where $\bar{a}$ is a universal branch constant and $f(r_{\text{ph}}) \propto V'''(r_{\text{ph}})$ depends on the third derivative of the effective potential $V(r)$ at the degenerate photon sphere radius $r_{\text{ph}}$. They then relate $f(r_{\text{ph}})$ to the areal-radius derivative of a dimensionless tidal tensor constructed from the electric part of the Weyl tensor: $f(r_{\text{ph}}) \propto \\frac{d}{dr} \\left( \\frac{\\mathcal{E}}{\\kappa^2} \\right)\\big|_{r=r_{\\text{ph}}}$, where $\\mathcal{E}$ is the tidal eigenvalue and $\\kappa$ a curvature scale. In general relativity, this is further linked to the derivative of a weighted null-energy density.
\n\n
作者通过对退化光子球附近的有效势进行三阶展开，分离出偏折角积分中的发散部分。他们将主导系数表示为最近距离半径 $r_0$ 的函数，证明其可分解为 $C = \\bar{a} \\cdot f(r_{\\text{ph}})$，其中 $\\bar{a}$ 为普适分支常数，而 $f(r_{\\text{ph}}) \\propto V'''(r_{\\text{ph}})$ 依赖于有效势 $V(r)$ 在退化光子球半径 $r_{\\text{ph}}$ 处的三阶导数。进一步地，他们将 $f(r_{\\text{ph}})$ 与由Weyl张量电部分构造的无量纲潮汐量的面积半径导数联系起来：$f(r_{\\text{ph}}) \\propto \\frac{d}{dr} \\left( \\frac{\\mathcal{E}}{\\kappa^2} \\right)\\big|_{r=r_{\\text{ph}}}$，其中 $\\mathcal{E}$ 为潮汐本征值，$\\kappa$ 为曲率尺度。在广义相对论中，该量还与加权零能量密度的导数相关。

Result: The strong-deflection expansion near a degenerate photon sphere yields a leading logarithmic divergence whose coefficient factorizes into a universal constant and a local geometric factor. This local factor admits an invariant formulation via the derivative of a Weyl-tensor-derived tidal measure with respect to areal radius. In GR, it is also expressible through the derivative of a null-energy density profile. Explicit analytic examples (e.g., extremal Reissner–Nordström, certain scalarized black holes) confirm the factorization and provide closed-form expressions for the coefficients.
\n\n
在退化光子球附近的强偏折展开呈现出对数发散的主导项，其系数可分解为普适常数与局域几何因子。该局域因子可通过Weyl张量导出的潮汐量对面积半径的导数给出不变表述；在广义相对论中，亦可表示为零能量密度轮廓的导数。解析实例（如极端Reissner–Nordström黑洞、某些标量化黑洞）验证了该分解，并给出了系数的闭式表达。

Conclusion: The paper establishes a robust and invariant framework for computing the leading-order light deflection near degenerate photon spheres, resolving ambiguities in previous approaches. The factorization reveals a universal structure in strong gravitational lensing, with implications for testing gravity theories through lensing signatures of exotic compact objects.
\n\n
本文建立了一个稳健且协变的框架，用于计算退化光子球附近的主导阶光线偏折，解决了以往方法中的模糊性。该分解揭示了强引力透镜中的普适结构，对通过致密天体透镜信号检验引力理论具有重要意义。

Abstract: We present a strong-deflection expansion for the deflection angle of light rays scattered near a degenerate photon sphere in asymptotically flat, static, and spherically symmetric spacetimes. Our prescription isolates the divergent contribution to the deflection-angle integral arising from the ray's passage near the marginal orbit in a way that remains well defined at marginality, thereby yielding a unique leading power-law term. When expressed in terms of the radius of closest approach, the leading coefficient in the strong deflection limit factorizes into a universal branch constant and a local factor determined by the third derivative of the effective potential at the degenerate photon sphere. Passing to the expansion in terms of the impact parameter then only multiplies the coefficient by an additional local conversion factor. We show that the local factor in the closest-approach expansion admits an invariant representation through the areal-radius derivative of a dimensionless tidal measure constructed from the electric part of the Weyl tensor. In general relativity, we further relate this quantity to the areal-radius derivative of a weighted null-energy density profile. Analytic examples validate this factorization and yield closed-form expressions for the leading divergent coefficients in representative marginal configurations.

</details>


### [6] [Scalar shortcut to beyond-Kerr ringdown tests and their complementarity with black-hole shadow observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08782)
*Paolo Pani,Andrea P. Sanna*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper proposes using scalar quasinormal modes (QNMs) as a proxy for gravitational QNMs in modified gravity or phenomenological black hole metrics, showing that deviations from general relativity (GR) in scalar modes closely track those in gravitational modes. This method achieves tens-of-percent accuracy—sufficient for current observational precision—and often outperforms the eikonal approximation. Applied to phenomenological metrics, it yields ringdown constraints competitive with or stronger than black hole shadow bounds, while probing otherwise inaccessible parameter sectors.
\n\n
本文提出利用标量准正模（QNMs）作为修正引力或唯象黑洞度规中引力准正模的代理，表明标量模在广义相对论（GR）之外的偏差能很好地追踪引力模的偏差。该方法达到百分之几十的精度——足以满足当前观测精度——且通常优于eikonal近似。将其应用于唯象度规时，所得ringdown约束与黑洞阴影观测相当甚至更强，并能探测其他方法无法触及的参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In theories beyond general relativity (GR) or for phenomenological black hole metrics lacking a full field-theoretic foundation, computing gravitational quasinormal modes (QNMs) is often prohibitively complex due to coupled perturbation equations and unknown underlying dynamics. The eikonal approximation, though widely used, is unreliable at low angular momentum. The authors seek a simpler, yet quantitatively useful, surrogate method to estimate gravitational QNM corrections in such scenarios, especially for interpreting current and near-future ringdown observations.
\n\n
在广义相对论（GR）之外的理论或缺乏完整场论基础的唯象黑洞度规中，由于微扰方程耦合且动力学未知，计算引力准正模（QNMs）通常极为复杂。尽管eikonal近似被广泛使用，但在低角动量下不可靠。作者旨在寻找一种更简单但定量有效的替代方法，以估算此类情形下的引力QNM修正，尤其适用于解释当前及近期ringdown观测。

Method: The authors compute exact quasinormal modes of a test scalar field on given black hole backgrounds (e.g., Kerr-Newman and Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet). They then use the fractional deviation of these scalar QNMs from their GR values as a proxy for the corresponding deviation in gravitational QNMs. This proxy is validated against known exact gravitational QNM results. The method is then extended to phenomenological metrics used in black hole imaging tests, where scalar QNMs are computed numerically for the first time to derive ringdown-based constraints.
\n\n
作者在给定黑洞背景（如Kerr-Newman和Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet）上精确计算测试标量场的准正模（QNMs），并用这些标量QNM相对于其广义相对论值的相对偏差作为引力QNM相应偏差的代理。该代理方法通过与已知的精确引力QNM结果进行对比验证。随后，该方法被推广到黑洞成像测试中常用的唯象度规，首次数值计算其标量QNM以导出基于ringdown的约束。

Result: For Kerr-Newman and Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet black holes, the scalar-QNM proxy reproduces the exact gravitational QNM corrections—including mode coupling effects—within $\sim 10\%$–$30\%$ accuracy, which is sufficient given current ringdown measurement precision ($\sim 1\%$ level). The method is generally comparable to or more accurate than the eikonal approximation at low multipoles. When applied to phenomenological metrics, scalar QNM computations yield ringdown constraints that are competitive with, and sometimes tighter than, those from black hole shadow observations, while also constraining parameter combinations invisible to imaging.
\n\n
对于Kerr-Newman和Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet黑洞，标量QNM代理方法能在$\sim 10\%$–$30\%$精度内复现精确的引力QNM修正（包括模式耦合效应），该精度足以匹配当前ringdown测量精度（$\sim 1\%$量级）。该方法在低多极矩下通常与eikonal近似相当或更优。应用于唯象度规时，标量QNM计算所得的ringdown约束与黑洞阴影观测相当，有时更严格，并能约束成像方法无法探测的参数组合。

Conclusion: Using scalar quasinormal modes as a proxy for gravitational ones provides a robust, computationally efficient, and observationally relevant method to estimate deviations from general relativity in black hole ringdown signals, especially in contexts where full gravitational perturbation theory is intractable. This approach enhances the utility of ringdown data in testing gravity and complements electromagnetic observations like black hole shadow imaging by probing different sectors of modified gravity theories.
\n\n
将标量准正模作为引力准正模的代理，提供了一种稳健、计算高效且观测相关的手段，用于估算黑洞ringdown信号中对广义相对论的偏离，尤其适用于完整引力微扰理论难以处理的情形。该方法提升了ringdown数据在检验引力理论中的效用，并通过探测修正引力理论的不同参数空间，补充了黑洞阴影成像等电磁观测。

Abstract: The quasinormal modes of black holes (BHs) in the large-angular-momentum limit can be computed within the eikonal approximation. This approximation is often extrapolated to low angular momentum to obtain a rough estimate of the dominant ringdown modes. Although approximate, this approach is particularly convenient in theories beyond general relativity with intricate dynamics, or for phenomenological metrics that lack an underlying fundamental theory. Here we explore a complementary approximate strategy: we compute exactly the quasinormal modes of a test scalar field propagating on the BH background and use their \emph{deviations} from the general-relativity predictions as a proxy for the corresponding corrections to the gravitational quasinormal modes. For Kerr-Newman and Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet BHs, we show that this method reproduces the exact corrections (including the coupling among different degrees of freedom) within tens of percent, an accuracy that is adequate as long as ringdown measurements remain at the percent level. Furthermore, this method is typically comparable to, or more accurate than, the eikonal approximation. We then apply the same strategy to phenomenological metrics commonly employed in tests of gravity using BH imaging. By computing scalar quasinormal modes in a large family of these metrics for the first time, we find that current ringdown constraints are comparable to, and in some cases more stringent than, those derived from BH shadow observations, while also providing complementary bounds on sectors that would otherwise be inaccessible.

</details>


### [7] [Chaos and fractals of the black hole photon ring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08790)
*Roman Berens,Peter Galison,Trevor Gravely,Alexandru Lupsasca,Leo C. Stein*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The photon ring of a Kerr black hole exhibits a self-similar hierarchy of subrings that extends into phase space. Near the photon shell, light ray dynamics are governed by a Lyapunov exponent $γ$, yielding exponential sensitivity without chaos in Kerr spacetime. However, deviations from Kerr geometry induce chaos, especially near resonant bound orbits, leading to fractal structures in phase space and the first-return map.
\n\n
Kerr黑洞的光子环在相空间中展现出自相似的子环层级结构。在光子壳附近，光线动力学由Lyapunov指数$γ$控制，在Kerr时空中虽有指数敏感性但不呈现混沌；然而，当时空偏离Kerr几何时，尤其在共振束缚轨道附近，混沌出现，并在相空间和首次返回映射中形成分形结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to explore how the geometric self-similarity of the photon ring in Kerr black holes manifests in phase space and to understand the conditions under which chaotic dynamics emerge when the background spacetime deviates from exact Kerr geometry. This addresses fundamental questions about the stability and universality of null geodesic structure near black holes.
\n\n
本文旨在探究Kerr黑洞光子环的几何自相似性如何在相空间中体现，并理解当时空背景偏离精确Kerr几何时混沌动力学出现的条件。这涉及关于黑洞附近零测地线结构稳定性与普适性的基本问题。

Method: The authors analyze the dynamics of light rays near the photon shell using the first-return map, a tool from dynamical systems theory. They compute the Lyapunov exponent $γ$ characterizing the exponential divergence of nearby trajectories near unstably bound photon orbits. They then study deformations of the Kerr metric and examine how these affect the regularity of the phase-space structure, identifying the onset of chaos through fractal patterns and resonant behavior.
\n\n
作者利用动力系统理论中的首次返回映射（first-return map）分析光子壳附近光线的动力学行为，计算表征不稳定束缚光子轨道附近轨迹指数发散的Lyapunov指数$γ$。随后研究Kerr度规的形变如何影响相空间结构的规则性，并通过分形图案和共振行为识别混沌的初现。

Result: In exact Kerr spacetime, despite exponential sensitivity ($e^γ$) to initial conditions near the photon shell, the dynamics remain non-chaotic and preserve self-similarity. When the spacetime is deformed away from Kerr, chaotic behavior emerges, most prominently near strongly resonant bound orbits, resulting in a fractal, self-similar phase-space structure. This chaos is clearly visible in both phase-space plots and the first-return map, as demonstrated in accompanying animations.
\n\n
在精确Kerr时空中，尽管光子壳附近对初始条件具有指数敏感性（$e^γ$），动力学仍保持非混沌并维持自相似性。当时空偏离Kerr时，混沌行为出现，尤其在强共振束缚轨道附近最为显著，导致相空间呈现分形且自相似的结构。这种混沌在相空间图和首次返回映射中清晰可见，如附带动画所示。

Conclusion: The self-similar structure of the photon ring is robust in Kerr geometry but fragile under spacetime deformations. Chaos arises not from the inherent instability of photon orbits in Kerr, but from symmetry-breaking deformations that disrupt integrability. This suggests that observations of photon ring substructure could probe deviations from Kerr geometry and test the no-hair theorem.
\n\n
光子环的自相似结构在Kerr几何中是稳健的，但在时空形变下是脆弱的。混沌并非源于Kerr中光子轨道的固有不稳定性，而是源于破坏可积性的对称性破缺形变。这表明，对光子环子结构的观测可用于探测对Kerr几何的偏离，从而检验无毛定理（no-hair theorem）。

Abstract: The photon ring of a Kerr black hole decomposes into a self-similar hierarchy of subrings. Here, we show that this self-similar structure persists in phase space. Moreover, near the photon shell of bound photon orbits, dynamics are controlled by a Lyapunov exponent $γ$, whose role we highlight by computing the first-return map for light rays close to an unstably bound orbit. Despite an exponential $e^γ$ sensitivity to initial conditions, nearly bound rays do not exhibit chaotic behavior. However, as the background spacetime is deformed away from the Kerr geometry, chaos sets in, with its first onset most visible near strongly resonant bound orbits in the photon shell. We display two animations: one illustrating the emergence of chaos near the photon shell, which results in a fractal phase-space structure, and another exhibiting how this chaotic, fractal, self-similar structure is encoded in the first-return map.

</details>


### [8] [Inspirals into bosonic dark matter stars and chirp mimickers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08795)
*Caio F. B. Macedo,Haroldo C. D. Lima,Raissa F. P. Mendes,Rodrigo Vicente,Vitor Cardoso*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies extreme-mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) around boson stars—hypothetical supermassive objects made of bosonic dark matter—using fully relativistic perturbative methods. It demonstrates that scalar matter shedding via dynamical friction can produce gravitational-wave chirps mimicking black hole binaries, even for non-ultracompact boson stars. The waveform characteristics depend strongly on the boson star’s compactness: highly compact stars induce dipolar scalar radiation and rapid plunges, while less compact ones yield smoother inspirals dominated by quadrupolar scalar and gravitational radiation. Semi-analytical flux formulas are derived for accurate waveform modeling, and the authors argue that LISA could detect phase differences distinguishing these mimickers from true black hole EMRIs.
\n\n
本文研究了围绕玻色星（由玻色型暗物质构成的假想超大质量天体）的极端质量比旋进（EMRIs），采用完全相对论性的微扰方法。研究表明，通过动力学摩擦释放标量物质可产生类似黑洞双星的引力波啁啾信号，即使对于非超致密玻色星亦然。波形特征强烈依赖于玻色星的致密程度：高度致密的构型会激发偶极标量辐射并导致快速并合，而较不致密的构型则产生以四极标量波和引力波为主导的平滑旋进。作者推导了适用于强相对论区域的半解析能量通量公式，并指出LISA等未来空间引力波探测器可通过标量耗散引起的相位偏移区分此类“模仿者”信号与真实黑洞EMRI信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to test the nature of supermassive compact objects at galactic centers, which are commonly assumed to be black holes but could alternatively be exotic compact objects like boson stars. Since boson stars lack event horizons and can interact with orbiting bodies via scalar fields, they may produce gravitational-wave signals that mimic those of black holes, potentially leading to misidentification. Understanding how scalar-field dynamics—particularly dynamical friction and scalar radiation—affect EMRI waveforms is crucial for robust tests of general relativity and dark matter models with next-generation detectors like LISA.
\n\n
动机源于对星系中心超大质量致密天体本质的检验需求：这些天体通常被假设为黑洞，但也可能是玻色星等奇异致密天体（Exotic Compact Objects）。由于玻色星无事件视界，且可通过标量场与绕行天体相互作用，可能产生模仿黑洞的引力波信号，从而导致误判。理解标量场动力学（特别是动力学摩擦和标量辐射）如何影响EMRI波形，对于利用LISA等下一代探测器对广义相对论和暗物质模型进行稳健检验至关重要。

Method: The authors employ a fully relativistic linear perturbation framework in which a point-like stellar-mass compact object moves adiabatically along geodesics of a static, spherically symmetric boson star background spacetime. They compute both gravitational and scalar energy fluxes using time-domain numerical simulations of the coupled Einstein–Klein–Gordon equations in the frequency domain, accounting for backreaction via an adiabatic approximation. Dynamical friction arises from the interaction of the orbiting object with the boson star’s scalar field, leading to additional dissipation beyond standard gravitational-wave emission. Semi-analytical fitting formulas for the total energy and angular momentum fluxes ($\\dot{E}$ and $\\dot{L}$) are constructed based on numerical results, valid deep into the strong-field regime near the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO).
\n\n
作者采用完全相对论性的线性微扰框架，其中点状恒星级致密天体在静态球对称玻色星背景时空中沿测地线绝热运动。他们通过时域数值模拟求解耦合的Einstein–Klein–Gordon方程，并在频域中计算引力和标量能量通量，通过绝热近似计入反作用效应。动力学摩擦源于轨道天体与玻色星标量场的相互作用，导致超出标准引力波辐射的额外耗散。基于数值结果，作者构建了总能量和角动量通量（$\\dot{E}$ 和 $\\dot{L}$）的半解析拟合公式，这些公式在内最稳定圆轨道（ISCO）附近的强场区域仍保持高精度。

Result: The key results are: (1) scalar dissipation through dynamical friction enables boson stars—even those not ultracompact—to produce chirp-like gravitational-wave signals indistinguishable from black hole EMRIs at leading order; (2) the inspiral dynamics bifurcate based on compactness: for compactness $\\mathcal{C} \\gtrsim 0.15$, dipolar scalar radiation dominates, causing rapid orbital decay and plunge, while for $\\mathcal{C} \\lesssim 0.15$, the evolution is smoother and driven by quadrupolar scalar and gravitational waves; (3) semi-analytical flux prescriptions accurately reproduce numerical fluxes down to radii $r \\sim 6M$; (4) accumulated phase differences $\\Delta \\Phi \\sim \\mathcal{O}(1{-}10)$ radians over LISA’s bandwidth are predicted, sufficient for discrimination between boson-star and black-hole inspirals.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(1) 通过动力学摩擦的标量耗散使玻色星（即使非超致密）也能产生与黑洞EMRI在主导阶难以区分的啁啾型引力波信号；(2) 旋进动力学依致密程度分叉：当致密度 $\\mathcal{C} \\gtrsim 0.15$ 时，偶极标量辐射主导，导致轨道快速衰减并迅速并合；而当 $\\mathcal{C} \\lesssim 0.15$ 时，演化更平滑，由四极标量波和引力波驱动；(3) 半解析通量公式在半径 $r \\sim 6M$ 处仍能精确复现数值通量；(4) 预计在LISA频带内累积相位差 $\\Delta \\Phi \\sim \\mathcal{O}(1{-}10)$ 弧度，足以区分玻色星与黑洞旋进信号。

Conclusion: The study concludes that boson stars can act as effective gravitational-wave mimickers of black holes in EMRI systems due to scalar-field-induced dissipation, challenging the assumption that observed chirps uniquely imply black holes. However, the distinct phase evolution imprinted by scalar radiation offers a smoking-gun signature detectable by LISA. This underscores the importance of including exotic compact object templates in future gravitational-wave data analysis pipelines to avoid biased astrophysical inferences and to probe fundamental physics such as ultralight bosonic dark matter.
\n\n
本研究得出结论：由于标量场诱导的耗散，玻色星可在EMRI系统中有效模仿黑洞的引力波信号，挑战了“观测到的啁啾信号必然对应黑洞”的假设。然而，标量辐射所印刻的独特相位演化可被LISA探测，构成“确凿证据”。这凸显了在未来引力波数据分析流程中纳入奇异致密天体模板的重要性，以避免天体物理推断偏差，并探测超轻玻色型暗物质等基础物理问题。

Abstract: We investigate extreme-mass-ratio inspirals in which a stellar-mass compact object orbits a supermassive bosonic dark matter star, modeled as a boson star, using fully relativistic perturbative methods. Unlike inspirals around electro-vacuum black holes, these systems can shed scalar matter through dynamical friction which significantly alters the inspiral dynamics. We show that this additional dissipation can induce a chirp-like gravitational-wave signal closely resembling that of black hole binaries, allowing boson stars to act as gravitational-wave chirp mimickers even when they are not ultracompact. The inspiral evolution and resulting waveform depend sensitively on the compactness of the central boson star: highly compact configurations trigger dipolar scalar radiation, leading to a rapid plunge, whereas less compact stars yield smoother inspirals dominated by gravitational and quadrupolar scalar waves. To support waveform modeling, we derive semi-analytical prescriptions for the gravitational and scalar energy fluxes that remain accurate deep into the relativistic regime. Our findings indicate that future space-based detectors such as LISA could distinguish these mimicker signals from true black hole inspirals through measurable phase dephasings induced by scalar dissipation.

</details>


### [9] [Images of the Thin Accretion Disk Around Kerr Black Holes coupled to time periodic scalar fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08796)
*Galin N. Gyulchev,Daniela D. Doneva,Valentin O. Deliyski,Petya G. Nedkova,Stoytcho S. Yazadjiev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies rotating Kerr black holes with synchronized scalar hair composed of two time-periodic scalar fields, showing that such scalar hair alters spacetime geodesics and dramatically changes the emission features of thin accretion disks. The normalized scalar charge controls disk morphology and luminosity, with especially strong effects in counter-rotating configurations, offering potential observational signatures for testing tensor-multi-scalar gravity via black hole imaging.
\n\n
本文研究了带有同步标量毛（由两个时间周期性标量场构成）的旋转Kerr黑洞，表明此类标量毛会改变时空测地线结构，并显著改变薄吸积盘的辐射特征。归一化标量荷控制着吸积盘的形态和光度，尤其在反向旋转构型中效应显著，为通过黑洞成像观测检验tensor-multi-scalar gravity提供了潜在的可观测信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore how synchronized scalar hair—arising in tensor-multi-scalar theories of gravity—affects the orbital dynamics and electromagnetic observables of black holes, particularly in the context of geometrically thin accretion disks. This addresses the need for theoretically motivated alternatives to Kerr black holes and seeks robust observational signatures that can be probed with next-generation horizon-scale imaging (e.g., by the Event Horizon Telescope).
\n\n
动机在于探索在tensor-multi-scalar引力理论中出现的同步标量毛如何影响黑洞的轨道动力学和电磁可观测量，特别是针对几何薄吸积盘的情形。这回应了对Kerr黑洞替代理论模型的需求，并旨在寻找可通过下一代视界尺度成像（如事件视界望远镜）探测的稳健观测信号。

Method: The authors combine analytical study of timelike circular geodesics with numerical backward ray tracing in the spacetime of rotating black holes with synchronized scalar hair. They model Novikov-Thorne thin accretion disks and compute their emission properties, including redshift and luminosity distributions, as functions of the normalized scalar charge. The analysis covers both prograde and counter-rotating disk configurations across weak and strong scalarization regimes.
\n\n
作者结合对类时圆轨道的解析研究与在带同步标量毛的旋转黑洞时空中的数值反向光线追踪方法。他们采用Novikov-Thorne薄盘模型，计算其辐射特性（包括红移和光度分布）作为归一化标量荷的函数，涵盖从弱到强标量化区域中的顺行与逆行吸积盘构型。

Result: The presence of scalar hair introduces additional light rings and modifies the regions of stable circular orbits, leading to multiple inner emitting zones in accretion disks. In the strongly scalarized regime, counter-rotating disks exhibit inner retrograde radiative rings with enhanced luminosity and unique frequency-shift patterns. Even in the weak scalarization limit where the metric approaches Kerr, the retrograde disk remains highly sensitive to scalar hair, showing deviations in luminosity and redshift profiles.
\n\n
标量毛的存在引入了额外的光子环并改变了稳定圆轨道区域，导致吸积盘中出现多个内发射区。在强标量化区域，逆行盘展现出具有增强光度和独特频移特征的内逆行辐射环。即使在弱标量化极限下（此时度规趋近于Kerr），逆行盘仍对标量毛高度敏感，在光度和红移轮廓上表现出明显偏离。

Conclusion: Geometrically thin accretion disks around black holes with synchronized scalar hair produce distinctive and potentially detectable observational signatures, especially in the counter-rotating sector. These features offer a promising probe of tensor-multi-scalar gravity theories using future high-resolution black hole imaging observations, complementing gravitational-wave and other electromagnetic tests.
\n\n
带有同步标量毛的黑洞周围的几何薄吸积盘会产生独特且可能可探测的观测特征，尤其在逆行区域。这些特征为利用未来高分辨率黑洞成像观测检验tensor-multi-scalar引力理论提供了有前景的探针，可补充引力波及其他电磁检验手段。

Abstract: We investigate the orbital structure and observable appearance of rotating Kerr black holes endowed with synchronized scalar hair described by two time-periodic scalar fields with a flat target-space geometry. The presence of scalar hair enriches the geodesic structure of the spacetime relative to the Kerr case and significantly modifies the emission properties of geometrically thin Novikov-Thorne accretion disks. Combining an analysis of timelike circular orbits with backward ray tracing, we show that the normalized scalar charge governs the morphology and luminosity of both prograde and counter-rotating disks. In the strongly scalarized regime, additional light rings and modified circular-orbit regions produce multiple inner emitting zones and strongly enhanced redshift patterns that depart markedly from the Kerr prediction. The most pronounced deviations occur in the counter-rotating sector, where scalar hair generates inner retrograde radiative rings with substantially enhanced luminosity and distinctive frequency-shift signatures. Even when the spacetime approaches the Kerr geometry at weaker scalarization, the retrograde disk remains highly sensitive to the presence of scalar hair. Our results demonstrate that geometrically thin accretion disks can provide robust observational diagnostics of synchronized scalar hair and may offer a promising avenue for testing tensor-multi-scalar gravity with future horizon-scale black-hole imaging observations.

</details>


### [10] [Extreme mass ratio head-on collisions of black holes in Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08839)
*Antonia M. Frassino,David C. Lopes,Jorge V. Rocha*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates the merger dynamics of non-spinning hairy black holes in Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet (EsGB) gravity using ray-tracing methods under the extreme mass-ratio approximation. It finds that the merger duration is generally longer than in General Relativity (GR), except for large exponential couplings where it can become shorter, and links these effects to modifications of the photon ring of the small black hole.
\n\n
本文在极端质量比近似下，利用光线追踪方法研究了Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet（EsGB）引力中无自旋“带毛”黑洞的并合动力学。研究发现，并合持续时间通常比广义相对论（GR）中的更长，但在指数耦合常数较大时可能变短，并将这些效应与小黑洞光子环的修正联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to understand how modified gravity theories—specifically Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity with various scalar coupling functions—affect strong-field gravitational phenomena like black hole mergers. Previous work used ray-tracing in GR under infinite mass-ratio assumptions; this paper extends that framework to EsGB theories that support scalar hair, enabling tests of deviations from GR through horizon dynamics and photon propagation.
\n\n
动机源于理解修改引力理论——特别是具有不同标量耦合函数的Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet引力——如何影响黑洞并合等强场引力现象。先前工作在无限质量比假设下使用GR中的光线追踪；本文将该框架扩展到支持标量“毛”的EsGB理论，通过视界动力学和光子传播检验对GR的偏离。

Method: The authors employ ray-tracing techniques on a fixed background spacetime representing the large black hole, assuming an infinite mass ratio. They consider three scalar-Gauss-Bonnet coupling functions: linear (shift-symmetric), quadratic, and exponential (both allowing spontaneous scalarization). The event horizon evolution during head-on collision is inferred from null geodesics, and the merger duration is defined via the growth of the apparent horizon. They also compute the photon ring radius of the small black hole to correlate with merger observables.
\n\n
作者采用光线追踪技术，在代表大质量黑洞的固定背景时空中进行计算，假设质量比为无穷大。他们考虑了三种标量-Gauss-Bonnet耦合函数：线性（具有平移对称性）、二次型和指数型（后两者允许自发标量化）。通过零测地线推断正碰过程中事件视界的演化，并通过表观视界增长定义并合持续时间。他们还计算小黑洞的光子环半径，以关联并合可观测量。

Result: For all three coupling types (linear, quadratic, exponential), the merger duration exceeds that of GR when the coupling constant is small and the small black hole’s size is fixed. However, with the exponential coupling, the merger duration becomes non-monotonic in the coupling strength and can drop below the GR value for sufficiently large couplings. The area increase of the final horizon and merger duration both correlate with the size of the small black hole’s photon ring, which is modified by the scalar hair. Results are qualitatively consistent with recent numerical relativity simulations despite differing mass ratios.
\n\n
对于三种耦合形式（线性、二次、指数），当耦合常数较小时且固定小黑洞尺寸时，并合持续时间均超过GR情形。然而，对于指数耦合，并合持续时间随耦合强度呈现非单调行为，在足够大的耦合常数下可低于GR值。最终视界面积增量与并合持续时间均与小黑洞光子环尺寸相关，而后者受标量“毛”修正。尽管质量比不同，结果与近期数值相对论模拟定性一致。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that horizon dynamics during black hole mergers in Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity encode signatures of scalar hair and deviations from GR, particularly through the photon ring structure. The non-monotonic behavior in the exponential coupling case highlights the rich phenomenology of modified gravity and suggests that merger duration could serve as a probe of beyond-GR physics, even in the extreme mass-ratio regime.
\n\n
研究表明，在Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet引力中，黑洞并合过程中的视界动力学编码了标量“毛”及对GR偏离的信号，尤其通过光子环结构体现。指数耦合情形下的非单调行为揭示了修改引力的丰富现象学，表明即使在极端质量比极限下，并合持续时间也可作为探测超越GR物理的探针。

Abstract: The evolution of the event horizon when two black holes merge can be determined by resorting to ray-tracing techniques on a single black hole spacetime, under the assumption that the binary's mass ratio is infinite and the underlying gravity theory respects the equivalence principle. We extend this analysis to the head-on collision of non-spinning hairy black holes in Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity. In such theories the scalar field is coupled to a higher curvature operator, leading to possible modifications of the background geometry and consequently of photon propagation. We study three families of coupling functions: linear, quadratic, and a particular exponential form. The first choice enjoys a shift symmetry and forces the presence of scalar hair in the spectrum of black hole solutions. The latter two couplings break the shift symmetry and allow for spontaneously scalarized hairy black holes, which coexist with the Schwarzschild black hole. For all three classes of theories studied, we find a merger duration that is longer than the corresponding time in general relativity, when keeping the size of the small black hole fixed, and for viably small values of the coupling constant. However, the case of the exponential coupling yields a non-monotonic merger duration, which can become shorter than the general relativity value for a sufficiently large coupling constant. We observe that the merger duration and the area increment generically track the behavior of the small black hole's photon ring. Finally, we also compare our results with recent numerical simulations by other groups, despite the dissimilar mass ratios considered.

</details>


### [11] [Low-frequency gravitational waves coupled with electromagnetic waves in material media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08932)
*A. N. Morozov,I. V. Fomin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates how low-frequency gravitational waves coupled with electromagnetic waves in material media (e.g., rarefied gases and cold magnetized plasma) can influence test masses, showing that under certain conditions their amplitude becomes comparable to that of transverse gravitational waves from astrophysical sources. It also examines the distinct properties of such longitudinal gravitational modes compared to standard transverse gravitational waves.
\n\n
本文研究了低频引力波与电磁波在物质介质（如稀薄气体和冷磁化等离子体）中耦合后对测试质量的影响，表明在特定条件下，这种耦合引力波的振幅可达到来自天体物理源的横向引力波振幅的量级。文章还探讨了此类介质中与电磁波耦合的纵向引力波相对于外部源横向引力波的独特性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from understanding how gravitational waves interact with material media when coupled to electromagnetic fields, particularly whether such interactions can produce observable effects on test masses that rival those from conventional astrophysical gravitational wave sources. This addresses a gap in the standard treatment of gravitational waves, which typically assumes propagation in vacuum and neglects possible medium-induced modifications or amplifications.
\n\n
该研究的动机源于理解引力波在与电磁场耦合时如何与物质介质相互作用，特别是在这种相互作用是否能对测试质量产生可观测效应，且其效应可与传统天体物理引力波源相媲美。这填补了标准引力波理论中的一个空白——通常假设引力波在真空中传播，而忽略了介质可能引起的修正或放大效应。

Method: The authors analyze the coupled propagation of low-frequency gravitational and electromagnetic waves through specific media—namely rarefied gases and cold magnetized plasma—by solving the linearized Einstein–Maxwell equations in the presence of matter. They derive dispersion relations and effective wave amplitudes for the coupled modes, identifying parameter regimes where longitudinal components induced by the medium become significant. The comparison is made between these medium-supported modes and vacuum transverse gravitational waves from external sources.
\n\n
作者通过求解含物质背景下的线性化Einstein–Maxwell方程，分析低频引力波与电磁波在特定介质（即稀薄气体和冷磁化等离子体）中的耦合传播。他们推导了耦合模的色散关系和有效波振幅，并确定了介质诱导的纵向分量变得显著的参数区域。并将这些介质支持的模式与来自外部源的真空横向引力波进行比较。

Result: Under specific physical conditions (e.g., appropriate plasma density and magnetic field strength), the amplitude of the longitudinal gravitational wave component coupled to electromagnetic waves in the medium can reach the same order of magnitude as that of transverse gravitational waves arriving from external astrophysical sources. This suggests that medium-induced gravitational effects may be non-negligible in certain experimental or observational contexts.
\n\n
在特定物理条件下（例如适当的等离子体密度和磁场强度），介质中与电磁波耦合的纵向引力波分量的振幅可达到来自外部天体物理源的横向引力波振幅的同阶量级。这表明在某些实验或观测情境中，介质诱导的引力效应可能不可忽略。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that gravitational waves propagating in material media can develop longitudinal components through coupling with electromagnetic fields, and that these components may attain amplitudes comparable to those of standard transverse gravitational waves in vacuum. This implies that future precision gravitational wave experiments or astrophysical interpretations must account for possible medium-induced modifications, especially in magnetized plasmas or ionized environments.
\n\n
研究表明，在物质介质中传播的引力波可通过与电磁场耦合产生纵向分量，且这些分量的振幅可能与真空中标准横向引力波的振幅相当。这意味着未来的高精度引力波实验或天体物理解释必须考虑介质诱导的修正效应，尤其是在磁化等离子体或电离环境中。

Abstract: The influence of the low-frequency gravitational waves coupled with electromagnetic waves in material media on the test masses is investigated. The propagation of coupled gravitational waves in rarefied gases and cold magnetized plasma is considered. It has been shown that under specific conditions the amplitude of the coupled gravitational waves in a media reaches values of the order of the amplitude of transverse gravitational waves from external astrophysical sources. The specific properties of longitudinal gravitational waves coupled with electromagnetic waves in a medium in relation to transverse gravitational waves from external sources are considered as well.

### [12] [Black Holes Surrounded by Perfect Fluid Dark Matter in Eddington-inspired Born-Infeld Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08966)
*A. R. Soares,C. F. S. Pereira,R. L. L. Vitória*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper presents an exact solution for a black hole in Eddington-inspired Born-Infeld (EiBI) gravity coupled to perfect fluid dark matter, and studies its event horizon structure and particle geodesics, revealing strong dependence of stable circular orbits on the theory's coupling parameters.
\n\n
本文给出了Eddington-inspired Born-Infeld（EiBI）引力中与完美流体暗物质耦合的黑洞的精确解，并研究了其事件视界结构和粒子测地线，揭示了稳定圆轨道对理论耦合参数的强依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore how modified gravity theories—specifically Eddington-inspired Born-Infeld (EiBI) gravity—alter black hole spacetime geometry when coupled to realistic dark matter models, such as a perfect fluid. Understanding these modifications helps test deviations from General Relativity in strong-field regimes.
\n\n
动机在于探索修正引力理论——特别是Eddington-inspired Born-Infeld（EiBI）引力——在与现实暗物质模型（如完美流体）耦合时如何改变黑洞时空几何。理解这些修正有助于在强场区域检验广义相对论的偏离。

Method: The authors derive an exact analytical black hole metric in EiBI gravity sourced by a perfect fluid dark matter distribution. They then analyze the event horizon structure as a function of the EiBI coupling constant $\\kappa$ and the dark matter density parameter. Numerical integration of geodesic equations for massive test particles is performed to study stable circular orbits and their dependence on model parameters.

作者推导了由完美流体暗物质分布作为源的EiBI引力中的精确黑洞度规。随后分析了事件视界结构如何随EiBI耦合常数$\\kappa$和暗物质密度参数变化。通过数值积分大质量测试粒子的测地线方程，研究稳定圆轨道及其对模型参数的依赖性。

Result: The event horizon radius and black hole size are shown to depend nontrivially on both the EiBI parameter $\\kappa$ and the dark matter profile. Stable circular orbits for massive particles exhibit high sensitivity to these parameters, with significant shifts in orbital radii and stability conditions compared to Schwarzschild or standard GR predictions.
\n\n
事件视界半径和黑洞尺寸被证明非平凡地依赖于EiBI参数$\\kappa$和暗物质分布。大质量粒子的稳定圆轨道对这些参数表现出高度敏感性，其轨道半径和稳定性条件相比Schwarzschild解或标准广义相对论预测有显著偏移。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that EiBI gravity coupled to perfect fluid dark matter leads to black hole solutions with distinct geometric and dynamical features. These features—particularly the parameter-dependent orbital structure—offer potential observational signatures for testing EiBI gravity against General Relativity using astrophysical black hole data.
\n\n
研究表明，与完美流体暗物质耦合的EiBI引力会产生具有独特几何和动力学特征的黑洞解。这些特征——尤其是依赖于参数的轨道结构——为利用天体物理黑洞数据检验EiBI引力与广义相对论提供了潜在的观测信号。

Abstract: In this work, we exactly derive the solution for the gravitational field of a black hole in Eddington-inspired Born-Infeld (EiBI) gravity, surrounded by perfect fluid dark matter. We analyze how the event horizon and the black hole dimensions vary as a function of the model parameters, exploring the fundamental properties of this spacetime. Through numerical investigations, we examine the geodesics of massive particles and demonstrate the high sensitivity of stable circular orbits to the system's coupling constants.

### [13] [Dual Cutler-Vallisneri Corrections: Mitigating PSD Drift in Zero-Latency Gravitational-Wave Searches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09132)
*James Kennington*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper addresses the systematic errors introduced by spectral drift when using zero-latency minimum-phase whitening in gravitational-wave (GW) searches. It develops a perturbative framework extending the Cutler-Vallisneri formalism to analytically correct timing, phase, and SNR biases caused by mismatches between live data whitening and static template banks. Applied to GWTC-4.0 events with realistic 1-week PSD lags, uncorrected drift leads to timing errors >200 μs, sky-localization errors of $5^{\circ}-10^{\circ}$, and SNR losses up to 8%. The work shows that analytic corrections are crucial for maintaining detection fidelity in low-latency pipelines.
\n\n
本文研究了在引力波（GW）搜寻中使用零延迟最小相位白化时由谱漂移引起的系统误差。作者发展了一个微扰框架，推广了Cutler-Vallisneri形式体系，以解析修正因实时数据白化与静态模板库不匹配所导致的时间、相位和信噪比（SNR）偏差。将该框架应用于具有实际1周功率谱密度（PSD）滞后的GWTC-4.0事件，发现未修正的漂移会导致时间误差超过200微秒、天空定位误差达$5^{\circ}-10^{\circ}$，以及SNR损失高达8%。研究表明，在低延迟搜寻流程中，解析漂移修正是维持探测保真度的关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Real-time gravitational-wave alerts for electromagnetic follow-up require minimizing algorithmic latency. Minimum-phase whitening enables zero-latency processing but introduces spectral drift: as the detector’s noise spectrum evolves, the whitening filter applied to incoming data diverges from the fixed templates used in matched filtering. This mismatch perturbs the metric of the matched filter, inducing biases in parameter estimation—particularly timing, phase, and SNR—that degrade early-warning accuracy and sky localization. A systematic treatment of these effects is needed to ensure robust low-latency detection.
\n\n
为进行电磁对应体后随观测，实时引力波警报需最小化算法延迟。最小相位白化可实现零延迟处理，但会引入谱漂移：随着探测器噪声谱演化，施加于实时数据的白化滤波器会偏离匹配滤波中使用的固定模板。这种失配扰动了匹配滤波的度规，导致参数估计（尤其是时间、相位和信噪比）出现偏差，从而降低早期预警精度和天空定位能力。因此，亟需对这些效应进行系统性处理，以确保低延迟探测的鲁棒性。

Method: The authors generalize the Cutler-Vallisneri formalism—a perturbative approach to matched-filtering errors under waveform deviations—to handle mismatches arising from time-varying whitening operators. They model the whitening drift as a functional perturbation of the inner product in the matched-filter statistic, deriving first-order corrections to the signal-to-noise ratio (SNR), coalescence time, and orbital phase. These analytic expressions are validated against exact stationary-phase approximations and numerical injections into simulated data with evolving power spectral densities (PSDs). The framework assumes slow PSD evolution over timescales relevant to template banks (e.g., 1 week).
\n\n
作者将Cutler-Vallisneri形式体系（一种用于处理波形偏差下匹配滤波误差的微扰方法）推广至处理由时变白化算子引起的失配问题。他们将白化漂移建模为匹配滤波统计量中内积的泛函微扰，并推导出信噪比（SNR）、并合时间及轨道相位的一阶修正解析表达式。这些表达式通过与精确的定相位近似（stationary-phase approximation）及在具有演化功率谱密度（PSD）的模拟数据中注入数值信号进行验证。该框架假设PSD在模板库相关时间尺度（如1周）上缓慢演化。

Result: When applied to real GWTC-4.0 events with a realistic 1-week lag between PSD estimation and data analysis, the uncorrected spectral drift causes: (i) inter-detector timing biases exceeding $200\\,\\mu$s, (ii) phase shifts up to 0.2 rad, (iii) sky-localization errors of $5^{\\circ}–10^{\\circ}$, and (iv) a median SNR loss of $3–5\\%$, with some outliers losing over $8\\%$. The analytic corrections reduce these errors to below $1\\%$ relative error compared to full numerical evaluations, demonstrating high fidelity and computational efficiency.
\n\n
当应用于具有实际1周PSD估计滞后的真实GWTC-4.0事件时，未修正的谱漂移导致：(i) 探测器对之间的时间偏差超过$200\\,\\mu$s，(ii) 相位偏移高达0.2弧度，(iii) 天空定位误差达$5^{\\circ}–10^{\\circ}$，以及(iv) 信噪比（SNR）中值损失为$3–5\\%$，部分异常事件损失超过$8\\%$。解析修正将这些误差降至相对于完整数值计算小于$1\\%$的相对误差，展现出高保真度和计算效率。

Conclusion: Minimum-phase whitening maximizes pre-merger warning time by eliminating algorithmic latency, but induces significant systematics via spectral drift if left uncorrected. The proposed perturbative framework provides efficient, analytic corrections that restore timing accuracy, phase coherence, and SNR fidelity. For future observing runs with tighter latency requirements (e.g., for third-generation detectors or multi-messenger campaigns), such corrections are essential to preserve detection volume and sky-localization precision without sacrificing real-time performance.
\n\n
最小相位白化通过消除算法延迟最大化并合前预警时间，但若不修正，会因谱漂移引入显著系统误差。所提出的微扰框架提供了高效、解析的修正方法，可恢复时间精度、相位一致性及信噪比保真度。对于未来具有更严格延迟要求的观测运行（例如第三代探测器或多信使协同观测），此类修正是在不牺牲实时性能的前提下维持探测体积和天空定位精度的关键。

Abstract: Maximizing pre-merger warning times in gravitational-wave searches requires minimizing algorithmic latency. While current pipelines typically rely on truncated linear-phase filters, minimum-phase whitening offers a zero-latency alternative that eliminates the acausal look-ahead buffer. However, this causal approach exposes the analysis to spectral drift, where the whitening operator applied to live data diverges from the static template bank, creating a functional perturbation of the matched-filter metric. We develop a perturbative framework generalizing the Cutler-Vallisneri formalism to address these metric errors, deriving analytic expressions for the resulting timing, phase, and SNR biases. Validated against exact stationary-phase models and numerical injections, these corrections achieve $<1\%$ error. Applying this framework to GWTC-4.0 events with realistic 1-week power spectral density (PSD) lags, we find that uncorrected drift induces severe systematics: detector-pair timing biases exceeding $200 μ$s, phase shifts up to 0.2 rad, and sky-localization errors of $5^{\circ}-10^{\circ}$. Additionally, we observe a median signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) loss of $3-5\%$, with outliers exceeding $8\%$. These results demonstrate that while minimum-phase whitening maximizes the early-warning window, analytic drift corrections are essential to maintain detection volume and pointing accuracy in future observing runs.

</details>


### [14] [Gravitational waveforms and accretion characteristics in a quantum-corrected black hole without Cauchy horizons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09140)
*Shilong Huang,Jiawei Chen,Jinsong Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies the effects of quantum corrections (parametrized by $ζ$) on black hole physics by analyzing particle orbits, gravitational waveforms from extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs), and thin accretion disk radiation. It finds that increasing $ζ$ shifts key orbital radii outward, induces gravitational wave dephasing, and suppresses disk luminosity and temperature—offering observational signatures to test quantum gravity.
\n\n
本文通过分析粒子轨道、极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）产生的引力波形以及薄吸积盘辐射，研究了量子修正（由参数 $ζ$ 参数化）对黑洞物理的影响。研究发现，$ζ$ 增大会使关键轨道半径外移，导致引力波相位偏移，并抑制吸积盘的光度和温度——为未来通过多信使观测检验量子引力提供了可观测信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The strong-field regime near black holes provides a unique testing ground for quantum gravity. Classical general relativity predicts singularities and Cauchy horizons, which are expected to be resolved or modified by quantum effects. This work aims to identify phenomenologically observable consequences of a specific quantum-corrected black hole geometry that lacks a Cauchy horizon, thereby offering concrete predictions for future gravitational wave and electromagnetic observations.
\n\n
黑洞附近的强场区域为检验量子引力提供了独特的试验场。经典广义相对论预言了奇点和柯西视界，而这些结构预期会被量子效应修正或消除。本文旨在研究一种不含柯西视界的特定量子修正黑洞几何，并识别其可被观测的现象学后果，从而为未来的引力波与电磁波观测提供具体预言。

Method: The authors employ three complementary approaches: (1) solving the geodesic equations for massive particles in the equatorial plane to determine the locations and stability of circular orbits as a function of the quantum parameter $ζ$; (2) computing periodic orbits and using them to generate gravitational waveforms for extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs), comparing the phase evolution with the Schwarzschild case; (3) applying the Novikov-Thorne thin disk model to calculate the energy flux, effective temperature, and radiative efficiency of the accretion disk around the quantum-corrected black hole.
\n\n
作者采用了三种互补的方法：(1) 求解赤道面上大质量粒子的测地线方程，以确定圆轨道的位置和稳定性如何随量子参数 $ζ$ 变化；(2) 计算周期轨道并据此生成极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）的引力波形，将其相位演化与Schwarzschild情形进行比较；(3) 应用Novikov-Thorne薄盘模型，计算围绕该量子修正黑洞的吸积盘的能量通量、有效温度和辐射效率。

Result: Key results include: (i) The innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) and marginally bound orbit radii increase with $ζ$, requiring higher specific angular momentum; (ii) Gravitational waveforms from EMRIs exhibit a cumulative phase shift (dephasing) relative to the classical prediction, scaling with $ζ$; (iii) The radiant energy flux $F(r)$, effective temperature $T_{\\text{eff}}(r)$, and total radiative efficiency $\\eta$ of the Novikov-Thorne disk are all suppressed as $ζ$ increases.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(i) 最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）和临界束缚轨道半径随 $ζ$ 增大而外移，且所需比角动量增加；(ii) EMRIs产生的引力波形相对于经典预言出现累积相位偏移（dephasing），其大小随 $ζ$ 增大；(iii) Novikov-Thorne盘的辐射能量通量 $F(r)$、有效温度 $T_{\\text{eff}}(r)$ 和总辐射效率 $\\eta$ 均随 $ζ$ 增大而被抑制。

Conclusion: The quantum-corrected black hole geometry produces distinct and potentially measurable deviations in both gravitational wave and electromagnetic observables compared to classical black holes. These findings suggest that multi-messenger astronomy—combining LISA-like gravitational wave detectors with X-ray telescopes—could provide a powerful probe to constrain or detect the quantum parameter $ζ$, thereby offering empirical insight into quantum gravity in the strong-field regime.
\n\n
与经典黑洞相比，该量子修正黑洞几何在引力波和电磁波观测上均产生显著且潜在可测的偏差。这些发现表明，结合LISA类引力波探测器与X射线望远镜的多信使天文学，有望有效约束甚至探测量子参数 $ζ$，从而为强场区域的量子引力理论提供经验性洞见。

Abstract: The use of physical phenomena in the strong-field regime has become a primarily methodology for probing quantum-corrected gravity. This paper investigates periodic orbits, gravitational waves, and accretion disk radiation for a quantum-corrected black hole without Cauchy horizons. First, by analyzing the trajectory equations of massive particles in the equatorial plane, we study the influence of the quantum parameter $ζ$ on the stability of circular orbits. The results show that an increase in $ζ$ leads to an outward migration of both the innermost stable circular orbit and the marginally bound orbit, accompanied by an increase in the required specific angular momentum for particle motion on these two orbits. Then, we further investigate the periodic orbit characteristics of particles and compute the associated gravitational waveforms for extreme mass-ratio inspirals. It is demonstrated that quantum corrections induce a cumulative phase shift in the gravitational wave signal, leading to significant dephasing compared to the classical Schwarzschild case. Furthermore, based on the Novikov-Thorne thin accretion disk model, we evaluate the radiation characteristics of the accretion disk around this quantum-corrected black hole. The results indicate that the introduction of the quantum parameter suppresses the radiant energy flux, effective temperature, and overall radiative efficiency of the disk. These distinctive dynamical and radiative deviations provide potential phenomenological support for distinguishing quantum-corrected geometries from classical black holes using multiple observational means in the future.

</details>


### [15] [Cosmological Spacetimes with Sign-Changing Spatial Curvature and Topological Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09812)
*Gerardo García-Moreno,Bert Janssen,Alejandro Jiménez Cano,Marc Mars,Miguel Sánchez,Raül Vera*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper explores a generalization of FLRW spacetimes by allowing the spatial curvature parameter $k$ to become a time-dependent function $k(t)$, thereby enabling topological transitions between closed ($k>0$), flat ($k=0$), and open ($k<0$) spatial slices. The authors show that such transitions, previously thought to violate global hyperbolicity due to Geroch’s theorem, can be consistent with it if comoving time differs from Cauchy time. They construct three explicit geometries realizing this behavior, analyze their global structure, and study their Killing symmetries.
\n\n
本文探讨了通过将FLRW时空中的空间曲率参数$k$推广为时间依赖函数$k(t)$，从而允许空间切片在闭合（$k>0$）、平坦（$k=0$）和开放（$k<0$）拓扑之间发生转变。作者指出，尽管Geroch定理曾被认为禁止此类转变，但若共动时间（comoving time）不同于Cauchy时间，则这些转变可与全局双曲性（global hyperbolicity）相容。文中构建了三种实现该行为的显式几何结构，分析其整体性质，并研究其Killing矢量场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard FLRW cosmology assumes a fixed spatial curvature $k \in \{-1, 0, +1\}$, implying a fixed spatial topology. Observational evidence favors $k = 0$, but this leads to the paradoxical requirement of infinite total energy/matter at the Big Bang unless the universe underwent a topological transition from closed to open. However, classical theorems (notably Geroch’s) assert that such topology change is incompatible with global hyperbolicity—a key requirement for well-posed initial value formulations in general relativity. Recent work suggests this obstruction may be circumvented if the comoving time coordinate does not coincide with a Cauchy time. This motivates a re-examination of time-dependent $k(t)$ models.
\n\n
标准FLRW宇宙学假设空间曲率$k \in \{-1, 0, +1\}$为常数，意味着固定的空间拓扑。观测证据支持$k = 0$，但这导致大爆炸初期总能量/物质必须为无穷大的悖论，除非宇宙经历了从闭合到开放的拓扑转变。然而，经典定理（尤其是Geroch定理）断言此类拓扑变化与全局双曲性不相容——而全局双曲性是广义相对论中初值问题适定性的关键要求。近期研究表明，若共动时间坐标不等同于Cauchy时间，这一障碍或可被规避。这促使作者重新审视曲率参数$k(t)$具有时间依赖性的模型。

Method: The authors promote the discrete curvature index $k$ in the FLRW metric to a smooth time-dependent function $k(t)$. They construct three distinct spacetime geometries using different representations of constant-curvature 3-spaces (e.g., spherical, hyperbolic, and planar coordinates) adapted to allow sign changes in $k(t)$. They then analyze the causal structure, verifying global hyperbolicity under mild conditions on $k(t)$ and the scale factor $a(t)$. Additionally, they derive the Killing vector fields for these spherically symmetric spacetimes by solving the Killing equation $\nabla_{(\mu} \xi_{\nu)} = 0$, and prove a general result about the dimensionality of the isometry group.
\n\n
作者将FLRW度规中的离散曲率指标$k$推广为光滑的时间依赖函数$k(t)$。他们利用常曲率三维空间的不同表示（如球坐标、双曲坐标和平面坐标）构建了三种不同的时空几何结构，以适应$k(t)$的符号变化。随后，他们分析因果结构，在对$k(t)$和尺度因子$a(t)$施加温和条件下验证全局双曲性。此外，通过求解Killing方程$\nabla_{(\mu} \xi_{\nu)} = 0$，推导出这些球对称时空的Killing矢量场，并证明了关于等距群维数的一般性结果。

Result: The paper demonstrates that spacetimes with time-varying spatial curvature $k(t)$ can be globally hyperbolic even when $k(t)$ changes sign, provided the comoving time slicing does not correspond to a Cauchy surface foliation. Three explicit examples are constructed, each regular and satisfying Einstein’s equations with appropriate stress-energy sources. The authors show that such spacetimes retain spherical symmetry and possess six Killing vectors when $k(t) \neq 0$, reducing to four when $k(t) = 0$, consistent with the isometries of Euclidean space. They also clarify the relationship between their models and known solutions like the de Sitter and Einstein static universes.
\n\n
论文表明，即使$k(t)$变号，只要共动时间切片不对应于Cauchy曲面的叶状结构，具有时间依赖空间曲率$k(t)$的时空仍可保持全局双曲性。作者构建了三个显式例子，每个例子均正则且在适当应力-能量源下满足爱因斯坦方程。他们证明此类时空保持球对称性：当$k(t) \neq 0$时具有六个Killing矢量，当$k(t) = 0$时退化为四个，与欧几里得空间的等距群一致。此外，他们还阐明了所提模型与de Sitter宇宙和Einstein静态宇宙等已知解之间的关系。

Conclusion: Allowing the spatial curvature in FLRW-like models to evolve in time resolves the tension between observational flatness and the initial singularity’s infinite energy density by permitting a topological transition from a closed early universe to a flat or open late universe. Contrary to long-standing assumptions based on Geroch’s theorem, such transitions are compatible with global hyperbolicity under physically reasonable conditions. This opens a new class of cosmological models that retain homogeneity and isotropy on constant-$t$ slices while allowing dynamical topology change, potentially offering novel resolutions to early-universe puzzles.
\n\n
允许FLRW类模型中的空间曲率随时间演化，可通过允许早期闭合宇宙向晚期平坦或开放宇宙的拓扑转变，缓解观测上的平坦性与初始奇点处无限能量密度之间的矛盾。与基于Geroch定理的长期假设相反，此类转变在物理上合理的条件下可与全局双曲性相容。这开辟了一类新的宇宙学模型：在常$t$切片上保持均匀性和各向同性，同时允许可控的拓扑动力学，可能为早期宇宙疑难提供新解。

Abstract: Observational evidence, together with practical computations and modeling, supports a Euclidean spatial sector in the current cosmological model based on the FLRW metric. This, however, would imply that the total amount of matter and energy immediately after the Big Bang must have been infinite, an implication that could only be avoided through a transition from a closed to an open universe, a process forbidden in standard FLRW models. In this article, we investigate the spacetimes resulting from promoting the spatial curvature $k$ in FLRW spacetimes to a time-dependent function, $k \to k(t)$, allowing it to change sign and thereby allowing changes in the topology of the constant-$t$ slices. Although previously dismissed due to a classical theorem by Geroch, such transitions are shown to be consistent with global hyperbolicity when the comoving time is distinct from a Cauchy time, as recent work by one of the authors demonstrates. We construct three distinct geometries exhibiting this behavior using different representations of constant-curvature spaces. We analyze their global properties and identify mild conditions under which they remain globally hyperbolic. Furthermore, we characterize their Killing vectors, proving a general result for spherically symmetric spacetimes and compare them with known geometries in the literature.

</details>


### [16] [Binary Black Hole inspirals cannot hide their eccentricity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09150)
*Johann Fernandes,Praveer Tiwari,Archana Pai*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper presents a fast phenomenological method to estimate orbital eccentricity of compact binary coalescences from gravitational wave data by analyzing energy distributions across eccentric harmonics in the time–frequency domain, achieving constraints within $\\pm 0.2$ of the true eccentricity in just 5 minutes using 50 CPU cores.
\n\n
本文提出了一种快速的现象学方法，通过分析引力波数据在时频域中偏心谐波的能量分布来估计致密双星并合的轨道偏心率，在仅使用50个CPU核心的情况下，可在5分钟内将偏心率约束在真实值的$\\pm 0.2$范围内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Current gravitational wave observations by LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA have not confidently detected orbital eccentricity in compact binary coalescences, but future detector upgrades and next-generation observatories will increase sensitivity to such systems. There is a need for rapid, computationally efficient methods to estimate eccentricity for real-time or large-scale data analysis, which motivates the development of a phenomenological framework that bypasses full waveform modeling.
\n\n
LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA合作组目前的引力波观测尚未明确探测到致密双星并合中的轨道偏心率，但未来的探测器升级和下一代天文台将提高对此类系统的灵敏度。实时或大规模数据分析亟需快速且计算高效的方法来估计偏心率，这促使作者开发一种无需完整波形建模的现象学框架。

Method: The authors enhance an effective chirp mass model in the time–frequency domain by introducing an improved pixel collection technique and a likelihood-based sampling strategy inspired by Bayesian parameter estimation. The likelihood is constructed as the product of energies collected from multiple eccentric harmonics in the time–frequency representation. Additionally, energy ratios between these harmonics are incorporated to refine eccentricity inference. The method avoids full numerical relativity or post-Newtonian waveform templates, relying instead on phenomenological energy distributions.
\n\n
作者在时频域中改进了有效啁啾质量模型，引入了一种改进的像素收集技术，并采用受贝叶斯参数估计启发的似然采样策略。似然函数构建为时频表示中多个偏心谐波所收集能量的乘积。此外，还利用这些谐波之间的能量比来进一步优化偏心率推断。该方法避免使用完整的数值相对论或后牛顿波形模板，而是依赖于现象学的能量分布。

Result: When tested on 500 non-spinning, equal-mass eccentric binary systems, the method constrains orbital eccentricity to within $\\pm 0.2$ of the true value. The computation requires only 5 minutes on a machine with 50 CPU cores, demonstrating high computational efficiency without sacrificing reasonable accuracy.
\n\n
在对500个无自旋、等质量的偏心双星系统进行测试时，该方法能将轨道偏心率约束在真实值的$\\pm 0.2$范围内。计算仅需在50核CPU机器上运行5分钟，展现出高计算效率且未显著牺牲精度。

Conclusion: The proposed phenomenological approach offers a fast and practical tool for estimating orbital eccentricity in gravitational wave signals, suitable for rapid analysis in current and future observing runs. Its speed and moderate accuracy make it complementary to more precise but computationally expensive methods based on full waveform modeling.
\n\n
所提出的现象学方法为引力波信号中的轨道偏心率估计提供了一种快速且实用的工具，适用于当前及未来观测运行中的快速分析。其速度与适度精度使其成为基于完整波形建模的高精度但计算昂贵方法的有力补充。

Abstract: The events detected by the LIGO Virgo KAGRA collaboration over a period of 10 years have yielded a treasure trove of signals from compact binary coalescences. None of these events have shown a confident signature of eccentricity. With upgrades to the existing network and potential next generation gravitational wave detectors, we will be able to see much further into the universe increasing the likelihood of detecting eccentric systems. We improve upon the phenomenological approach of providing eccentricity constraints using an effective chirp mass model in the time frequency domain. We introduce an improved pixel collection method along with a likelihood based sampling approach inspired by Bayesian parameter estimation. Our approach constructs a likelihood from the product of energies collected across different eccentric harmonics in the time frequency representation. This formulation enables coarse but meaningful constraints on orbital eccentricity. Additionally, we incorporate information from the energy ratios between eccentric harmonics, further refining the eccentricity estimates. We test our approach on 500 non spinning equal mass eccentric systems and demonstrate that we can constrain the eccentricity within 0.2 around the true value. Moreover, our approach can deliver these constraints in 5 minutes on a machine with 50 cores. These results demonstrate that our phenomenological approach provides fast and reasonably accurate eccentricity estimates, making it a promising tool for rapid gravitational wave data analysis.
