### [17] [Shadows of quintessence black holes: spherical accretion, photon trajectories, and geodesic observers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09159)
*Ji-Wen Li,Zi-Liang Wang,Tao-Tao Sui*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates how a quintessence-like field modifies black hole shadow observables by accounting for accretion dynamics, photon geodesics, and—crucially—the motion of observers in non-asymptotically flat spacetimes. It shows that the apparent shadow size depends strongly on whether the observer is static or freely falling, with infalling observers measuring smaller angular radii due to relativistic aberration. Applying these results to M87$^\ast$, the authors find tighter constraints on the quintessence parameter for more negative equations of state, emphasizing that observer specification is essential in such spacetimes.
\n\n
本文研究了类quintessence场如何通过吸积流动力学、光子测地线以及——关键地——非渐近平直时空中的观测者运动来改变黑洞阴影可观测量。研究表明，表观阴影大小强烈依赖于观测者是静态还是自由下落：由于相对论性像差，下落观测者测得的角半径更小。将结果应用于M87$^\ast$，作者发现对于更负的状态方程，对quintessence参数的限制更强，强调在此类时空中必须明确指定观测者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard black hole shadow analyses assume static observers at spatial infinity, which is invalid in quintessence-corrected spacetimes that are not asymptotically flat. This necessitates a re-evaluation of shadow formation using physically motivated observers—specifically, freely falling (geodesic) observers—and a consistent treatment of how quintessence affects both spacetime geometry and observational signatures.
\n\n
标准黑洞阴影分析假设空间无穷远处的静态观测者，这在非渐近平直的quintessence修正时空中不再成立。因此，有必要使用物理上合理的观测者（特别是自由下落的测地线观测者）重新评估阴影形成过程，并一致处理quintessence如何同时影响时空几何和观测信号。

Method: The authors employ a perturbative expansion in the quintessence parameter to analytically compute key geometric quantities: event horizon $r_{\\rm H}$, photon sphere radius $r_{\\rm ph}$, innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) $r_{\\rm ISCO}$, and critical impact parameter $b_{\\rm crit}$. They model both static and spherically symmetric infalling accretion flows and calculate observed specific intensity maps for static and geodesic observers. The angular shadow radius is derived via ray tracing in the quintessence-modified Schwarzschild metric, incorporating relativistic Doppler and aberration effects for moving observers. Constraints on the quintessence parameter are obtained by comparing predicted shadow sizes with EHT measurements of M87$^\ast$.
\n\n
作者在quintessence参数中采用微扰展开，解析计算关键几何量：事件视界$r_{\\rm H}$、光子球半径$r_{\\rm ph}$、最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）$r_{\\rm ISCO}$和临界碰撞参数$b_{\\rm crit}$。他们建模了静态和球对称下落吸积流，并为静态与测地线观测者计算观测到的比强度图。角阴影半径通过在quintessence修正的Schwarzschild度规中进行光线追踪获得，并纳入运动观测者的相对论性多普勒和像差效应。通过将预测的阴影大小与EHT对M87$^\ast$的测量结果比较，获得对quintessence参数的限制。

Result: While $r_{\\rm ph}$ and $b_{\\rm crit}$ remain invariant spacetime properties, the observed angular shadow radius $\\theta_{\\rm sh}$ depends explicitly on the observer’s four-velocity and radial position. Freely infalling observers measure systematically smaller $\\theta_{\\rm sh}$ than static observers at the same $r$, while outgoing geodesic observers measure larger values—consistent with relativistic aberration. In non-asymptotically flat spacetimes, $b_{\\rm crit}$ alone cannot predict $\\theta_{\\rm sh}$; full observer-dependent ray tracing is required. For M87$^\ast$, more negative quintessence equations of state ($w < -1/3$) yield stronger observational bounds on the quintessence charge, with constraints largely robust across different observer models.
\n\n
尽管$r_{\\rm ph}$和$b_{\\rm crit}$仍是不变的时空属性，但观测到的角阴影半径$\\theta_{\\rm sh}$显式依赖于观测者的四速度和径向位置。在相同$r$处，自由下落观测者系统性地测得更小的$\\theta_{\\rm sh}$，而外向测地线观测者测得更大值——这与相对论性像差一致。在非渐近平直时空中，仅凭$b_{\\rm crit}$无法预测$\\theta_{\\rm sh}$；必须进行完整的依赖于观测者的光线追踪。对于M87$^\ast$，更负的quintessence状态方程（$w < -1/3$）对quintessence荷给出更强的观测限制，且该限制在不同观测者模型下基本稳健。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that observer prescription is not a mere technical detail but a central physical ingredient in black hole shadow modeling for non-asymptotically flat spacetimes. Neglecting the observer’s motion—especially in quintessence or dark energy scenarios—can lead to incorrect interpretations of shadow measurements. Future high-precision tests of gravity with EHT-like instruments must incorporate realistic observer trajectories to reliably constrain exotic fields near black holes.
\n\n
本研究表明，在非渐近平直时空的黑洞阴影建模中，观测者设定并非技术细节，而是核心物理要素。忽略观测者运动——尤其在quintessence或暗能量场景中——可能导致对阴影测量的错误解读。未来利用类似EHT的仪器进行高精度引力检验时，必须纳入真实的观测者轨迹，以可靠地限制黑洞附近的奇异场。

Abstract: The presence of a quintessence-like field can influence the black hole shadow through three primary mechanisms: the dynamics of accretion flows, the trajectories of photons, and the motion of observers. Unlike standard shadow analyses that assume a static observer at spatial infinity, the non-asymptotically flat nature of quintessence-corrected spacetimes motivates the consideration of freely falling (geodesic) observers. Using a perturbative approach, we derive analytical expressions for the event-horizon location, photon-sphere radius, innermost stable circular orbit, and critical impact parameter. We compute the observed intensity profiles for both static and infalling spherical accretion flows. We find that, although the photon-sphere radius and the critical impact parameter are invariant properties of the spacetime, the apparent angular size of the shadow depends sensitively on the observer's motion and location. Freely infalling observers systematically measure smaller angular radii than static observers at the same radius, whereas freely outgoing observers measure larger ones, in agreement with relativistic aberration. In contrast to the Schwarzschild case, the impact parameter alone is insufficient to characterize the observed angular structure in non-asymptotically flat spacetimes. Applying our results to the Event Horizon Telescope observation of M87$^\ast$, we show that more negative equations of state lead to stronger constraints on the quintessence parameter, largely independent of the observer prescription. Our analysis highlights the importance of carefully specifying the observer in shadow studies of non-asymptotically flat black-hole spacetimes.

</details>


### [18] [Quasinormal modes and greybody factors of magnetically charged de Sitter black holes probed by massless external fields in Einstein Euler Heisenberg gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09304)
*Ming Zhang,Guo-Xin Chen,Lei Zhang,Sheng-Yuan Li,Xufen Zhang,De-Cheng Zou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper computes quasinormal frequencies (QNFs) and greybody factors (GFs) for massless scalar and electromagnetic perturbations on magnetically charged de Sitter black holes in Euler-Heisenberg gravity, using AIM, WKB, and Bernstein spectral methods, and analyzes the dependence on magnetic charge $Q_{\mathrm{m}}$, cosmological constant $Λ$, coupling $ε$, and multipole number $l$.
\n\n
本文在Euler-Heisenberg引力框架下，针对磁荷de Sitter黑洞上的无质量标量场与电磁场微扰，利用渐近迭代法（AIM）、WKB方法和Bernstein谱方法计算了准正规模频率（QNFs）和灰体因子（GFs），并分析了磁荷 $Q_{\mathrm{m}}$、宇宙学常数 $Λ$、耦合参数 $ε$ 和多极矩数 $l$ 对其的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The study is motivated by the need to understand linear stability and radiation properties of black holes in nonlinear electrodynamics (specifically Euler-Heisenberg theory inspired by string theory) in de Sitter spacetime, where both magnetic charge and quantum corrections (via coupling $ε$) may significantly alter quasinormal mode spectra and greybody factors.
\n\n
该研究旨在理解在de Sitter时空中、受非线性电动力学（特别是受弦论启发的Euler-Heisenberg理论）修正的黑洞在线性微扰下的稳定性及其辐射特性，其中磁荷和通过耦合参数 $ε$ 引入的量子修正可能显著改变准正规模谱和灰体因子。

Method: The authors employ three complementary techniques: (1) the asymptotic iteration method (AIM) to numerically solve the perturbation equations; (2) the WKB approximation for both QNFs and greybody factor computations; and (3) the Bernstein spectral method as a high-precision validation tool specifically for the $l=0$ scalar sector where WKB fails. The background is a magnetically charged dS black hole in Euler-Heisenberg gravity with action modified by a coupling parameter $ε$.
\n\n
作者采用三种互补方法：(1) 渐近迭代法（AIM）用于数值求解微扰方程；(2) WKB近似用于计算QNFs和灰体因子；(3) Bernstein谱方法作为高精度验证工具，专门用于WKB失效的 $l=0$ 标量微扰情形。背景时空为Euler-Heisenberg引力中含磁荷的de Sitter黑洞，其作用量通过耦合参数 $ε$ 修正。

Result: The QNFs show dependence on $Q_{\mathrm{m}}$, $Λ$, $ε$, and $l$: increasing $Q_{\mathrm{m}}$ or $ε$ generally increases the damping rate (larger imaginary part), while larger $l$ leads to higher oscillation frequencies. AIM and WKB results agree well except for $l=0$, where Bernstein spectral method confirms the reliability of AIM. The greybody factor decreases with increasing $Q_{\mathrm{m}}$ or $ε$, indicating suppressed Hawking radiation transmission.
\n\n
QNFs依赖于 $Q_{\mathrm{m}}$、$Λ$、$ε$ 和 $l$：增大 $Q_{\mathrm{m}}$ 或 $ε$ 通常增强阻尼率（虚部增大），而更大的 $l$ 导致更高振荡频率。AIM与WKB结果在多数情况下吻合良好，但在 $l=0$ 情形下，Bernstein谱方法验证了AIM的可靠性。灰体因子随 $Q_{\mathrm{m}}$ 或 $ε$ 增大而减小，表明Hawking辐射透射被抑制。

Conclusion: The combined use of AIM, WKB, and Bernstein spectral methods provides a robust framework for studying QNMs in modified gravity with nonlinear electrodynamics. The results confirm that Euler-Heisenberg corrections and magnetic charge significantly affect both the quasinormal spectrum and greybody factors, offering insights into black hole stability and quantum-gravity-motivated extensions of general relativity in de Sitter space.
\n\n
AIM、WKB与Bernstein谱方法的联合使用为研究含非线性电动力学修正引力中的准正规模提供了稳健框架。结果表明，Euler-Heisenberg修正和磁荷显著影响准正规模谱与灰体因子，为de Sitter空间中黑洞稳定性及受量子引力启发的广义相对论推广提供了新见解。

Abstract: This paper investigates the perturbation dynamics of massless scalar and electromagnetic fields on magnetically charged de Sitter (dS) black holes within the framework of string-inspired Euler-Heisenberg (EH) gravity. We calculate the quasinormal frequencies (QNFs) and discuss the influences of black hole magnetic charge $Q_{\mathrm{m}}$, the cosmological constant $Λ$, coupling parameter $ε$ and multipole number $l$ on QNFs, emphasizing the relationships between these parameters and quasinormal modes (QNMs) behavior. We find that the results obtained through the asymptotic iteration method (AIM) are in good agreement with those obtained by the WKB method. Importantly, the Bernstein spectral method is employed as a rigorous cross-check for QNFs in the $l=0$ scalar perturbation sector, where the WKB approximation is often unreliable. The greybody factor (GFs) is calculated using WKB method. The effects of the parameters $Q_{\mathrm{m}}$ and $ε$ on the greybody factor are also studied.

</details>


### [19] [Deep Learning Search for Gravitational Waves from Compact Binary Coalescence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09386)
*Lorenzo Mobilia,Tito Dal Canton,Gianluca Maria Guidi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper proposes a hybrid gravitational-wave detection pipeline combining matched filtering with Convolutional Neural Networks (CNNs) to achieve high detection efficiency while reducing computational cost compared to traditional matched-filtering searches, especially in preparation for next-generation detectors like the Einstein Telescope.
\n\n
本文提出了一种混合引力波探测流程，将匹配滤波与卷积神经网络（Convolutional Neural Networks, CNNs）相结合，在相比传统匹配滤波搜索显著降低计算成本的同时保持高探测效率，尤其为爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）等下一代探测器时代做准备。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The computational burden of standard matched-filtering techniques is expected to become prohibitive with the increased data volumes and broader parameter-space coverage required by future gravitational-wave detectors such as the Einstein Telescope. There is a pressing need for alternative or complementary methods that maintain high detection performance while being computationally sustainable.
\n\n
标准匹配滤波技术的计算负担在未来引力波探测器（如爱因斯坦望远镜）所需的数据量和参数空间覆盖范围大幅增加的情况下预计将变得难以承受。因此迫切需要既能维持高探测性能又具备计算可持续性的替代或补充方法。

Method: The authors develop a hybrid approach that integrates concepts from matched filtering into a Convolutional Neural Network architecture. This method bypasses the conventional $χ^2$ veto test used in standard pipelines. It is trained and evaluated on simulated data containing Gaussian noise, transient noise (glitches), and physical signal features absent from the template bank—such as orbital eccentricity, spin-induced precession, and higher-order waveform modes.
\n\n
作者开发了一种混合方法，将匹配滤波的概念整合进卷积神经网络（CNN）架构中。该方法绕过了标准流程中常用的 $χ^2$ 拒绝检验。其训练与评估基于包含高斯噪声、瞬态噪声（glitches）以及模板库中未包含的物理信号特征（如轨道偏心率、自旋诱导进动和高阶波形模态）的模拟数据。

Result: The hybrid CNN–matched-filtering pipeline achieves detection efficiency comparable to that of a standard matched-filtering search across a range of realistic signal scenarios—including those with eccentricity, precession, and higher-order modes—while offering significantly improved computational efficiency and eliminating reliance on the $χ^2$ test.
\n\n
该混合CNN–匹配滤波流程在多种现实信号场景（包括具有偏心率、进动和高阶模态的情形）下实现了与标准匹配滤波搜索相当的探测效率，同时显著提升了计算效率，并无需依赖 $χ^2$ 检验。

Conclusion: Deep learning–assisted gravitational-wave searches, particularly hybrid architectures combining physical modeling with neural networks, can provide scalable and sustainable solutions for data analysis in the era of next-generation detectors without sacrificing sensitivity.
\n\n
深度学习辅助的引力波搜索——特别是结合物理建模与神经网络的混合架构——能够在不牺牲灵敏度的前提下，为下一代探测器时代的数据分析提供可扩展且可持续的解决方案。

Abstract: Gravitational wave searches rely on a combination of methods, including matched filtering, coherent analyses, and more recent machine learning based pipelines. For compact binary coalescences, where signals originate from the relativistic dynamics of compact objects, matched filtering remains a central element, but its computational cost will increase substantially with the data volumes and parameter-space coverage required by next-generation interferometers such as the Einstein Telescope. Developing complementary strategies that reduce computational load while preserving detection performance is therefore essential. We investigate a hybrid approach that combines matched-filtering concepts with Convolutional Neural Networks, enabling efficient signal searches without relying on the usual $χ^2$ rejection test. Using simulated data sets that include injected signals in Gaussian noise, transient noise, and physical effects not represented in template bank, such as eccentricity, precession and higher-order modes, we show that the method achieves a detection efficiency comparable to a standard matched-filtering search while offering a more resource efficient pipeline. These results indicate that deep learning assisted searches can support sustainable gravitational-wave data analysis in future detector eras.

### [20] [Relativistic Corrections to the Formation Rate of Extreme Mass-Ratio Inspirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09547)
*Chen Feng,Yong Tang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper develops a relativistically self-consistent analytic framework to estimate Extreme Mass-Ratio Inspiral (EMRI) event rates by incorporating general relativistic corrections to the loss-cone dynamics and plunge criteria. It finds that relativistic effects enhance EMRI rates by approximately a factor of 8 compared to Newtonian estimates, with greater enhancement for shallower stellar density profiles and independence from the central black hole mass.
\n\n
本文构建了一个相对论自洽的解析框架，用于估算极端质量比旋进（Extreme Mass-Ratio Inspiral, EMRI）事件率，通过引入对损失锥动力学和并合判据的广义相对论修正。研究发现，与牛顿力学估计相比，相对论效应使EMRI事件率提升约8倍，且在恒星密度轮廓更平缓时增强更显著，同时与中心黑洞质量无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Accurate estimation of EMRI event rates is crucial for predicting the detection prospects of space-based gravitational-wave observatories like LISA and Taiji. Previous Newtonian treatments neglect key relativistic features—such as energy-dependent loss-cone boundaries and the correct innermost stable orbit—that significantly affect whether a compact object undergoes an inspiral or a direct plunge. This motivates the development of a relativistically consistent formalism.
\n\n
精确估算EMRI事件率对于预测LISA和太极等空间引力波探测器的探测前景至关重要。以往的牛顿力学处理忽略了关键的相对论效应——例如能量依赖的损失锥边界和正确的最内稳定轨道——这些效应对致密天体是发生旋进还是直接并合具有决定性影响。这促使作者发展一个相对论自洽的理论框架。

Method: The authors generalize the standard loss-cone angular momentum $J_{\\rm lc}$ to an energy-dependent quantity $J_{\\rm lc}(E)$ in Schwarzschild spacetime and replace the Newtonian plunge pericenter with the relativistic minimum stable radius derived from general relativity. They integrate these corrections into a Fokker-Planck-type description of two-body relaxation and gravitational-wave-driven orbital decay, yielding a revised EMRI capture rate formula that accounts for relativistic orbital dynamics near the massive black hole.
\n\n
作者在史瓦西时空中将标准损失锥角动量 $J_{\\rm lc}$ 推广为能量依赖量 $J_{\\rm lc}(E)$，并用广义相对论导出的最小稳定半径替代牛顿力学中的并合近心距。他们将这些修正整合进描述二体弛豫与引力波驱动轨道衰减的福克-普朗克型方程中，从而得到一个计入大质量黑洞附近相对论轨道动力学的新EMRI俘获率公式。

Result: The relativistic treatment increases predicted EMRI event rates by roughly a factor of 8 relative to Newtonian calculations. This enhancement is more significant for shallower stellar density profiles (e.g., $\\rho \\propto r^{-\\gamma}$ with smaller $\\gamma$) and shows negligible dependence on the mass of the central massive black hole, highlighting the universality of relativistic corrections in EMRI formation.
\n\n
相对论处理使预测的EMRI事件率相较牛顿计算提升约8倍。这种增强在更平缓的恒星密度轮廓（例如 $\\rho \\propto r^{-\\gamma}$ 且 $\\gamma$ 较小）下更为显著，并且几乎不依赖于中心大质量黑洞的质量，凸显了相对论修正在EMRI形成中的普适性。

Conclusion: Relativistic effects—particularly the energy dependence of the loss-cone boundary and the correct identification of the plunge orbit via the minimum stable radius—are essential for accurate EMRI rate predictions. Neglecting them leads to severe underestimation of detectable events for missions like LISA and Taiji. The developed framework provides a robust, analytic tool for future population studies and detector sensitivity forecasts.
\n\n
相对论效应——特别是损失锥边界的能量依赖性以及通过最小稳定半径正确识别并合轨道——对准确预测EMRI事件率至关重要。忽略这些效应会导致对LISA和太极等任务可探测事件数的严重低估。所发展的框架为未来种群研究和探测器灵敏度预测提供了稳健的解析工具。

Abstract: Extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) are long-duration gravitational-wave sources in which a compact object gradually spirals into a massive black hole. Their formation is governed by the interplay between stochastic angular-momentum diffusion driven by two-body relaxation and the dissipative evolution caused by gravitational-wave emission, with the loss-cone boundary deciding whether an object undergoes an inspiral or a direct plunge. Building on this physical picture, we construct a relativistically self-consistent analytic framework for estimating EMRI event rates. In Schwarzschild spacetime, we generalize the standard loss-cone angular momentum to an energy-dependent quantity and revise the plunge pericenter by using the minimum stable radius derived from general relativity. Relative to the Newtonian treatment, we show that incorporating these relativistic effects increases the predicted EMRI rates by roughly a factor of 8. This enhancement becomes more pronounced for shallower stellar density profiles and is insensitive to the mass of the central massive black hole, which emphasizes that relativistic effects are essential for EMRI rate estimations that are relevant for space-based gravitational-wave detectors, such as LISA and Taiji.

</details>


### [21] [Dynamics of quadratic f(R) cosmology with a perfect fluid: Jordan and Einstein frames](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09667)
*Artur Alho,Margarida Lima,Filipe C. Mena*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies the global dynamics of spatially flat FLRW cosmologies in pure quadratic gravity theories (i.e., without Einstein–Hilbert term), using 3D regular dynamical systems in both Jordan and Einstein frames. It provides a complete phase-space characterization by analyzing monotonic functions, invariant boundaries, and non-hyperbolic fixed points, and clarifies which solutions are globally conformally related between frames.
\n\n
本文研究了纯二次引力理论（即不含Einstein–Hilbert项）在空间平坦FLRW宇宙学模型中的全局动力学行为，通过在Jordan frame和Einstein frame中构建三维正则动力系统，利用单调函数、不变边界和非双曲不动点的分析，给出了完整的相空间刻画，并阐明了哪些解在两个frame之间具有全局共形对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Quadratic gravity theories extend General Relativity by including higher-order curvature invariants like $R^2$, $R_{\mu\nu}R^{\mu\nu}$, and $R_{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}R^{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}$, which arise naturally in quantum gravity and early-universe cosmology. Understanding their cosmological dynamics—especially in the absence of the Einstein–Hilbert term—is crucial for assessing their viability and physical equivalence under conformal transformations. The motivation is to provide a rigorous, global phase-space analysis that resolves ambiguities about solution correspondence between the Jordan and Einstein frames.
\n\n
二次引力理论通过引入$R^2$、$R_{\mu\nu}R^{\mu\nu}$和$R_{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}R^{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}$等高阶曲率不变量来推广广义相对论，这些项在量子引力和早期宇宙学中自然出现。理解其宇宙学动力学——尤其是在不含Einstein–Hilbert项的情况下——对于评估其物理可行性以及在共形变换下不同frame之间的物理等价性至关重要。本文旨在通过严格的全局相空间分析，澄清Jordan frame与Einstein frame之间解的对应关系。

Method: The authors construct two global, regular 3-dimensional dynamical systems: one in the Jordan frame (based directly on the quadratic action) and another in the Einstein frame (obtained via a conformal transformation that maps the theory to GR with a scalar field). In the Jordan frame, they employ monotonicity arguments for the interior flow, analyze the 2D invariant boundary sets, and desingularize non-hyperbolic fixed points using techniques like blow-up or Poincaré compactification. In the Einstein frame, they exploit the skew-product structure of the state space (where the scalar field dynamics decouple partially) and similarly characterize boundary orbits. Asymptotic expansions of solutions near singularities or infinity are used to determine which Jordan-frame solutions admit a global conformal map to the Einstein frame.
\n\n
作者构建了两个全局且正则的三维动力系统：一个在Jordan frame（直接基于二次作用量），另一个在Einstein frame（通过共形变换将理论映射为含标量场的广义相对论）。在Jordan frame中，他们利用内流的单调性、分析二维不变边界集，并通过blow-up或Poincaré紧化等技术对非双曲不动点进行去奇点处理。在Einstein frame中，他们利用状态空间的skew-product结构（标量场动力学部分解耦），并同样刻画边界轨道。通过在奇点或无穷远处对解进行渐近展开，判断哪些Jordan frame解可全局共形映射到Einstein frame。

Result: The global phase portraits in both frames are fully characterized. In the Jordan frame, the monotonic function restricts the possible asymptotic behaviors, and all fixed points—including non-hyperbolic ones—are classified with their stability determined after desingularization. In the Einstein frame, the skew-product structure allows reduction to lower-dimensional subsystems, and the orbit structure on invariant boundaries is completely described. Crucially, the paper identifies a subset of Jordan-frame solutions that do not admit a global conformal extension to the Einstein frame due to singular behavior in the conformal factor, thereby resolving a key ambiguity in the physical interpretation of frame equivalence.
\n\n
两个frame中的全局相图均被完整刻画。在Jordan frame中，单调函数限制了可能的渐近行为，所有不动点（包括非双曲的）在去奇点后均被分类并确定其稳定性。在Einstein frame中，skew-product结构允许降维处理，且不变边界上的轨道结构被完全描述。关键的是，论文识别出一部分Jordan frame解由于共形因子的奇异行为而无法全局共形延拓到Einstein frame，从而澄清了frame等价性在物理解释中的关键模糊性。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that while the Jordan and Einstein frames are locally equivalent via conformal transformation, global equivalence fails for certain cosmological solutions in pure quadratic gravity. A complete dynamical systems analysis—combining monotonicity, boundary analysis, and desingularization—is essential to uncover this subtlety. This work establishes a rigorous framework for analyzing higher-order gravity theories and cautions against assuming global physical equivalence between conformally related frames without detailed dynamical scrutiny.
\n\n
研究表明，尽管Jordan frame与Einstein frame可通过共形变换局部等价，但在纯二次引力理论中，某些宇宙学解并不满足全局等价。必须结合单调性、边界分析和去奇点技术进行完整的动力系统分析，才能揭示这一微妙差异。本工作为高阶引力理论的分析建立了严格框架，并警示：在缺乏详细动力学检验的情况下，不应假设共形相关frame之间的全局物理等价性。

Abstract: We investigate the global dynamics of the field equations of (pure) quadratic theories of gravity which generalise Einstein's theory in spatially flat homogeneous and isotropic cosmological models with a perfect fluid. We introduce global and regular 3-dimensional dynamical systems' formulations, on both the Jordan frame and the conformally related Einstein frame. The analysis in the Jordan frame explores the monotonicity properties of the interior flow which, together with the characterisation of the orbit structure on the 2-dimensional invariant boundaries and the desingularisation of non-hyperbolic fixed points, provides a global description of the flow and its limit sets. In the Einstein frame, the analysis uses the skew-product structure of the Einstein state space and the characterisation of the orbit structure on the 2-dimensional invariant boundaries. Furthermore, by obtaining asymptotic expansions we identify the solutions that are global conformally mapped from the Jordan frame to the Einstein frame and those that are not.

### [22] [An asymptotic proof of the classical log soft graviton theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09844)
*Gianni Boschetti,Miguel Campiglia*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We derive the classical log soft graviton theorem using the asymptotic framework of Compère, Gralla, and Wei, relying only on Einstein equations near all infinities and their matching. The derivation is time-reversal covariant and includes incoming soft radiation; the standard asymmetric log soft factor emerges when incoming memory vanishes.
\n\n
我们利用Compère、Gralla和Wei的渐近框架，仅基于爱因斯坦方程在类时、类空和类光无穷远处的行为及其匹配条件，推导出经典对数软引力子定理。该推导在时间反演下完全协变，并包含入射软辐射；当入射记忆效应消失时，可恢复标准的不对称对数软因子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to provide a rigorous, fully covariant derivation of the classical log soft graviton theorem that clarifies the origin of the observed asymmetry between future and past hard scattering data. This asymmetry has been puzzling because it appears to conflict with time-reversal symmetry, and its root is traced to boundary conditions at spatial infinity.
\n\n
本文旨在提供一个严格且完全协变的经典对数软引力子定理推导，以阐明未来与过去硬散射数据之间观测到的不对称性的起源。这种不对称性令人困惑，因为它似乎与时间反演对称性相冲突，其根源被追溯到类空无穷远处的边界条件。

Method: The authors employ the asymptotic framework developed by Compère, Gralla, and Wei, which systematically describes the gravitational field near timelike ($i^\\pm$), spatial ($i^0$), and null ($\\mathscr{I}^\\pm$) infinity. They solve the Einstein equations in these regions and impose consistent matching conditions across the boundaries. The analysis is manifestly covariant under time reversal and explicitly includes contributions from both outgoing and incoming soft radiation.
\n\n
作者采用Compère、Gralla和Wei发展的渐近框架，该框架系统地描述了引力场在类时（$i^\\pm$）、类空（$i^0$）和类光（$\\mathscr{I}^\\pm$）无穷远处的行为。他们在这些区域求解爱因斯坦方程，并施加一致的边界匹配条件。该分析在时间反演下显式协变，并明确包含出射和入射软辐射的贡献。

Result: The derivation yields the classical log soft graviton theorem in a time-symmetric formulation. When incoming gravitational memory is absent, the result reduces to the standard log soft factor, which exhibits an asymmetry between future and past hard particles. This asymmetry is shown to originate from a discontinuity in the gravitational field at spatial infinity ($i^0$), a feature long recognized in the literature.
\n\n
该推导在时间对称形式下得到了经典对数软引力子定理。当不存在入射引力记忆效应时，结果退化为标准的对数软因子，该因子在未来的硬粒子与过去的硬粒子之间表现出不对称性。这种不对称性被证明源于类空无穷远（$i^0$）处引力场的不连续性，这是文献中早已认识到的特征。

Conclusion: The work demonstrates that the apparent time-asymmetry in the classical log soft graviton theorem is not fundamental but arises from boundary conditions at spatial infinity. The full, time-reversal-covariant treatment reveals that the soft theorem naturally incorporates both incoming and outgoing radiation, and the standard form is a special case under restricted boundary conditions.
\n\n
本工作表明，经典对数软引力子定理中表观的时间不对称性并非根本性的，而是源于类空无穷远处的边界条件。完整的、时间反演协变的处理揭示了软定理自然地同时包含入射和出射辐射，而标准形式是在特定边界条件下的一种特例。

Abstract: We present a derivation of the classical log soft graviton theorem within the asymptotic framework of Compère, Gralla, and Wei. The proof relies solely on Einstein equations near timelike, spatial, and null infinity, together with matching properties across these regions. The approach is fully covariant under time reversal and incorporates contributions from incoming soft radiation. In the absence of incoming memory one recovers the standard log soft factor, which features an asymmetry between future and past hard components. From an asymptotic perspective, the origin of this asymmetry lies in a long-known discontinuity of the gravitational field at spatial infinity.

### [23] [Globally stable, ghost-free hyperbolic square-root deformation of the Starobinsky model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09944)
*Andrei Galiautdinov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We introduce an exact, analytic deformation of the Starobinsky $f(R)$ model via a hyperbolic square-root ansatz for $f'(R) = \alpha R + \sqrt{\alpha^2 R^2 + 1}$ ($\alpha > 0$), which eliminates the strong-coupling singularity at $f'(R)=0$, recovers general relativity at low curvature, preserves the inflationary plateau at high curvature, and ensures global absence of ghosts and tachyons. The Einstein-frame scalar potential features an impenetrable wall at $\phi \to -\infty$, enabling non-singular bouncing cosmologies. Predictions for $N=60$ yield $n_s \simeq 0.967$ and $r \simeq 0.00083$, consistent with Planck and BICEP/Keck data.
\n\n
我们通过双曲平方根形式的 $f'(R) = \alpha R + \sqrt{\alpha^2 R^2 + 1}$（$\alpha > 0$）对 Starobinsky $f(R)$ 模型提出了一种精确解析的变形，消除了 $f'(R)=0$ 处的强耦合奇点，在低曲率下恢复广义相对论，在高曲率下保留暴胀平台，并确保全局无鬼态和快子。爱因斯坦标架下的标量势在 $\phi \to -\infty$ 处形成不可穿透的势垒，支持非奇异反弹宇宙学。对于 $N=60$，模型预言 $n_s \simeq 0.967$ 和 $r \simeq 0.00083$，与 Planck 和 BICEP/Keck 数据一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The standard quadratic Starobinsky model $f(R) = R + \alpha R^2$ suffers from a strong-coupling pathology when extended to negative curvatures due to the existence of a root in $f'(R)$, leading to a singular kinetic term for the scalaron and loss of predictivity. This motivates the construction of a modified $f(R)$ theory that retains the successful inflationary predictions while eliminating the problematic branch where $f'(R) \leq 0$, ensuring global hyperbolicity and stability.
\n\n
标准的二次 Starobinsky 模型 $f(R) = R + \alpha R^2$ 在延拓至负曲率区域时，由于 $f'(R)$ 存在零点，导致标量子（scalaron）动能项发散，出现强耦合问题并丧失可预测性。这促使作者构建一种修正的 $f(R)$ 理论，在保留成功暴胀预言的同时，消除 $f'(R) \leq 0$ 的病态分支，确保全局双曲性和稳定性。

Method: The authors propose a geometric ansatz for the derivative of the Lagrangian: $f'(R) = \alpha R + \sqrt{\alpha^2 R^2 + 1}$ with $\alpha > 0$, which is strictly positive for all real $R$. This defines an exact, analytic $f(R)$ function via integration. They analyze the resulting theory in both Jordan and Einstein frames, computing the scalaron mass squared $m_\phi^2 \propto f''(R)/[f'(R)]^3$, verifying its global positivity, and deriving the Einstein-frame potential $V(\phi)$ through a conformal transformation and scalar field redefinition. Inflationary observables ($n_s$, $r$) are computed using slow-roll approximations with $N=60$ e-folds.
\n\n
作者提出拉格朗日导数的几何形式：$f'(R) = \alpha R + \sqrt{\alpha^2 R^2 + 1}$（$\alpha > 0$），该式对所有实数 $R$ 严格为正。通过对该式积分得到精确解析的 $f(R)$ 函数。他们在 Jordan 标架和 Einstein 标架下分析该理论，计算标量子质量平方 $m_\phi^2 \propto f''(R)/[f'(R)]^3$ 并验证其全局正定性，并通过共形变换和标量场重定义导出 Einstein 标架势能 $V(\phi)$。利用慢滚近似和 $N=60$ 的 e-fold 数计算暴胀观测量（$n_s$, $r$）。

Result: The model yields a globally well-defined, ghost-free, and tachyon-free $f(R)$ gravity. It recovers GR as $R \to 0$, reproduces the Starobinsky inflationary plateau as $R \to +\infty$, and avoids the pathological branch as $R \to -\infty$ by ensuring $f'(R) \to 0^+$. The Einstein-frame potential $V(\phi) = \frac{1}{8\alpha} [ 1 - (1 + 2\sqrt{2/3}\phi) \exp(-2\sqrt{2/3}\phi) ] + \Lambda\exp(-2\sqrt{2/3}\phi)$ exhibits an impenetrable wall at $\phi \to -\infty$, enabling stable non-singular bounces. For $N=60$, it predicts $n_s \simeq 0.967$ and $r \simeq 0.00083$, lying within current observational bounds.
\n\n
该模型给出了一个全局良定义、无鬼态且无快子的 $f(R)$ 引力理论。当 $R \to 0$ 时恢复广义相对论，当 $R \to +\infty$ 时重现 Starobinsky 暴胀平台，并通过确保 $f'(R) \to 0^+$ 避免了 $R \to -\infty$ 时的病态分支。Einstein 标架势能 $V(\phi) = \frac{1}{8\alpha} [ 1 - (1 + 2\sqrt{2/3}\phi) \exp(-2\sqrt{2/3}\phi) ] + \Lambda\exp(-2\sqrt{2/3}\phi)$ 在 $\phi \to -\infty$ 处形成不可穿透的势垒，支持稳定的非奇异反弹。对于 $N=60$，预言 $n_s \simeq 0.967$ 和 $r \simeq 0.00083$，位于当前观测限制范围内。

Conclusion: The proposed hyperbolic square-root $f(R)$ model provides a theoretically robust and observationally viable extension of Starobinsky inflation that resolves the strong-coupling singularity while maintaining all desirable features: GR recovery, successful slow-roll inflation, and global stability. Its built-in energetic barrier in the Einstein frame offers a natural mechanism for non-singular cosmological scenarios, making it a compelling candidate for early- and late-time cosmology.
\n\n
所提出的双曲平方根 $f(R)$ 模型是对 Starobinsky 暴胀的一个理论稳健且观测可行的推广，解决了强耦合奇点问题，同时保留了所有理想特性：广义相对论恢复、成功的慢滚暴胀和全局稳定性。其 Einstein 标架中内建的能量势垒为非奇异宇宙学场景提供了自然机制，使其成为早期和晚期宇宙学的一个有力候选理论。

Abstract: We propose an exact, analytic deformation of the Starobinsky model governed by the strictly positive derivative of its Lagrangian, $f'(R) = αR + \sqrt{α^2 R^2 + 1}$, with $α> 0$. This geometric hyperbolic square-root ansatz is designed to eliminate the well-known strong-coupling singularity that arises in quadratic $f(R)$ gravity when $f'(R)=0$. The construction seamlessly recovers general relativity at low curvatures and preserves the successful slow-roll inflationary plateau at extreme positive curvatures. In the limit $R \to -\infty$, the derivative $f'(R)$ asymptotes to zero strictly from above, removing the pathological branch associated with the vanishing of $f'(R)$. This guarantees that the only admissible constant-curvature ($R=A$) solutions correspond to standard Einstein spaces with an effective cosmological constant $Λ_{\text{eff}} \equiv A/4$. The first and second derivatives of the action, as well as the scalaron mass squared, remain strictly positive globally, ensuring a perfectly ghost-free and tachyon-free cosmological evolution across the entire spacetime manifold. In the Einstein frame, the dynamics of the scalaron is governed by the globally defined potential $V(φ) = \frac{1}{8α} [ 1 - (1 + 2\sqrt{2/3}φ) \exp(-2\sqrt{2/3}φ) ] + Λ\exp(-2\sqrt{2/3}φ)$, which naturally establishes an impenetrable energetic wall as $φ\to -\infty$, offering a robust, globally stable mechanism for non-singular bouncing cosmologies. For $N = 60$ inflationary e-folds, the model predicts a scalar spectral index of $n_s \simeq 0.967$ and a strongly suppressed tensor-to-scalar ratio of $r \simeq 0.00083$, which position the proposed theory within the observationally favored parameter space of the Planck and BICEP/Keck Array baseline constraints.

</details>


### [24] [Strong deflection of massive particles via the geodesic deviation equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09946)
*Takahisa Igata,Yohsuke Takamori*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper formulates the strong deflection limit for timelike geodesic scattering in static, spherically symmetric, asymptotically flat spacetimes, showing that the logarithmic divergence of the deflection angle is governed by a radial instability exponent tied to local curvature and matter content.
\n\n
本文提出了静态、球对称、渐近平直时空下类时测地线散射的强偏折极限（strong deflection limit）表述，表明偏折角的对数发散由一个径向不稳定性指数（radial instability exponent）控制，该指数与局部曲率和物质内容相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The strong deflection limit has been well studied for null geodesics (e.g., photon rings), but a covariant and geometrically transparent formulation for timelike geodesics—relevant for massive particle orbits and gravitational lensing of massive objects—was lacking. The authors aim to fill this gap by linking the divergent behavior of the deflection angle to intrinsic geometric properties of the unstable circular orbit.
\n\n
强偏折极限在零测地线（如光子环）中已有深入研究，但针对类时测地线（与大质量粒子轨道及大质量物体引力透镜相关）尚缺乏协变且几何清晰的表述。作者旨在通过将偏折角的发散行为与不稳定圆轨道的内禀几何性质联系起来，填补这一空白。

Method: The authors use the geodesic deviation equation in a covariant manner to analyze trajectories near the unstable circular orbit. They define a radial instability exponent per unit azimuthal angle and relate it to the logarithmic coefficient in the deflection angle’s divergence as angular momentum approaches its critical value. They then express this exponent using local curvature invariants evaluated on the unstable orbit, leveraging the static and spherical symmetry of the spacetime.
\n\n
作者采用协变形式的测地线偏离方程（geodesic deviation equation）分析靠近不稳定圆轨道的轨迹。他们定义了单位方位角下的径向不稳定性指数，并将其与角动量趋近临界值时偏折角发散的对数系数关联。随后，利用时空的静态性和球对称性，将该指数用不稳定轨道上的局部曲率不变量表示。

Result: The logarithmic divergence coefficient of the deflection angle for timelike geodesics is shown to equal the radial instability exponent, which is expressible purely in terms of local curvature data on the unstable circular orbit. In general relativity, this reduces to a single scalar combination involving the static-frame energy density $\\rho$, radial pressure $p_r$, and tangential pressure $p_t$: specifically, $\\rho + p_r - 2p_t$.
\n\n
类时测地线偏折角的对数发散系数被证明等于径向不稳定性指数，该指数可完全用不稳定圆轨道上的局部曲率数据表达。在广义相对论中，这简化为一个仅包含静止系能量密度 $\\rho$、径向压强 $p_r$ 和切向压强 $p_t$ 的标量组合：即 $\\rho + p_r - 2p_t$。

Conclusion: The strong deflection limit for timelike geodesics admits a universal geometric description rooted in the local curvature and stability properties of the critical orbit. This provides a kinematic and geometric interpretation of relativistic scattering phenomena and reveals how matter content influences strong-field orbital dynamics through a simple local scalar in general relativity.
\n\n
类时测地线的强偏折极限具有普适的几何描述，其根源在于临界轨道的局部曲率与稳定性性质。这为相对论性散射现象提供了运动学与几何诠释，并揭示了在广义相对论中，物质内容如何通过一个简单的局部标量影响强场轨道动力学。

Abstract: We develop a formulation of the strong deflection limit for the scattering of particles following timelike geodesics in asymptotically flat, static, and spherically symmetric spacetimes. For fixed specific energy, as the angular momentum approaches its critical value from above, the particle passes arbitrarily close to the associated unstable circular orbit, undergoes many windings around it, and the deflection angle diverges logarithmically. Using the geodesic deviation equation, we show covariantly that the coefficient of this logarithmic divergence is determined by the radial instability exponent of the critical trajectory, defined per unit azimuthal angle. We express this instability exponent in terms of local curvature data on the unstable circular orbit, thereby providing both kinematic and geometric interpretations of the strong deflection limit. In general relativity, its matter dependence enters only through a single local scalar combination constructed from the static-frame energy density and the principal radial and tangential pressures.

</details>


### [25] [Interaction of the gravitational Hawking radiation and a static point mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09948)
*João P. B. Brito,Atsushi Higuchi,Luís C. B. Crispino*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper computes the finite response rate of a static point mass (supported by a string) outside a Schwarzschild black hole to Hawking gravitons in the Unruh state, showing that the black hole horizon provides a natural infrared (IR) cutoff absent in Rindler spacetime. The response vanishes for incoming thermal gravitons in the Hartle-Hawking state, making the total response identical in both quantum states—mirroring behavior seen in electromagnetism but not for scalar fields.
\n\n
本文计算了Schwarzschild黑洞外由弦支撑的静态质点在Unruh态下对Hawking引力子的响应率，结果有限，并表明黑洞视界提供了Rindler时空中所缺失的自然红外（IR）截断。在Hartle-Hawking态中，来自过去类光无穷远的热引力子引起的响应率为零，因此在Unruh态和Hartle-Hawking态下的总响应率相同——这一行为与电磁场中的静态电荷一致，但不同于无质量标量场的情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from understanding how quantum fields—specifically gravitons in the Unruh and Hartle-Hawking states—interact with localized stress-energy sources near black holes, and resolving the infrared (IR) divergences that plague analogous setups in Rindler spacetime. The authors aim to clarify whether black hole geometry naturally regulates such divergences and to compare the behavior across different quantum field types (gravitational, electromagnetic, scalar).
\n\n
动机源于理解量子场（特别是Unruh态和Hartle-Hawking态中的引力子）如何与黑洞附近局域化的应力-能量源相互作用，并解决Rindler时空中类似构型所面临的红外（IR）发散问题。作者旨在阐明黑洞几何是否能自然地调控此类发散，并比较不同量子场类型（引力、电磁、标量）的行为差异。

Method: The authors model a static point mass supported by a string as a classical stress-energy tensor $T_{\mu\nu}$ outside a Schwarzschild black hole. They compute its linear response to thermal gravitons using quantum field theory in curved spacetime, specifically evaluating the transition (response) rate via the Fourier transform of the symmetric two-point function of the linearized gravitational field in the Unruh and Hartle-Hawking states. The calculation leverages the known mode decomposition of gravitons in Schwarzschild spacetime and carefully handles the infrared behavior near the horizon.
\n\n
作者将由弦支撑的静态质点建模为Schwarzschild黑洞外部的经典应力-能量张量 $T_{\mu\nu}$。他们利用弯曲时空中的量子场论，通过计算线性化引力场在Unruh态和Hartle-Hawking态下的对称两点函数的Fourier变换，求得其对热引力子的线性响应（跃迁）率。该计算利用了Schwarzschild时空中引力子的已知模分解，并仔细处理了视界附近的红外行为。

Result: The total response rate of the stress-energy tensor to Hawking gravitons in the Unruh state is finite and given in closed form. Near the horizon, it matches the Rindler result but remains finite due to the black hole’s finite size acting as an IR cutoff. In the Hartle-Hawking state, the contribution from past null infinity vanishes, so the total response equals that in the Unruh state. This equality also holds for electromagnetic coupling but fails for a massless scalar field.
\n\n
应力-能量张量在Unruh态下对Hawking引力子的总响应率是有限的，并以闭合形式给出。在视界附近，其形式与Rindler结果一致，但由于黑洞有限尺度作为红外截断，结果保持有限。在Hartle-Hawking态中，来自过去类光无穷远的贡献为零，因此总响应率与Unruh态相同。这种等价性在电磁耦合中也成立，但在无质量标量场情形下不成立。

Conclusion: The Schwarzschild black hole geometry provides a physical infrared regulator for graviton-induced transitions of localized stress-energy sources, eliminating the IR divergence present in uniformly accelerated systems in flat spacetime. The equivalence of response rates in Unruh and Hartle-Hawking states for both gravitational and electromagnetic fields—but not scalar fields—suggests a deeper connection tied to gauge invariance and the tensor nature of the fields.
\n\n
Schwarzschild黑洞几何为局域应力-能量源在引力子诱导跃迁中提供了物理的红外调节机制，消除了平直时空中匀加速系统存在的红外发散。Unruh态与Hartle-Hawking态下引力场和电磁场响应率的等价性（而标量场不具备此性质）暗示了这与规范不变性及场的张量性质存在深层联系。

Abstract: We study the interaction of a stress-energy tensor describing a static point mass supported by a string outside a Schwarzschild black hole with the gravitons of the Hawking radiation. We derive a closed-form analytic expression for the total response rate of this stress-energy tensor to the thermal gravitons in the Unruh state, which models the quantum state in the spacetime of a spherically symmetric black hole formed by gravitational collapse. This response rate is finite in contrast with the infrared divergent response rate for a static point mass supported by a string in Rindler spacetime, i.e., a point mass accelerated uniformly by a string in Minkowski spacetime. By comparing the response rate near the black hole horizon with that in Rindler spacetime, we show that the size of the black hole acts as a natural infrared cutoff. We also find that the response rate of this stress-energy tensor to the thermal gravitons incoming from past null infinity in the Hartle-Hawking state vanishes. As a result, the total response rate of a static point mass (supported by a string) in the Unruh and Hartle-Hawking states for gravitons are identical. This is also the case for a static charge interacting with the electromagnetic field but not for a static source for a massless scalar field.

</details>

### [26] [Quotient Quiver Subtraction -- Classical Groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08774)
*Sam Bennett,Amihay Hanany,Guhesh Kumaran*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper generalizes quotient quiver subtraction—a combinatorial method for gauging Coulomb branch isometries in 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ theories—to include orthogonal and symplectic gauge groups using Type IIB brane setups with $\mathrm{O5}$ planes. The extended procedure modifies not only node subtraction but also the quiver’s graph structure, enabling new constructions of Higgs branches of higher-dimensional SCFTs.
\n\n
本文将商图减法（quotient quiver subtraction）——一种用于规范3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ 理论Coulomb分支等距群的组合方法——通过引入带有$\mathrm{O5}$平面的Type IIB膜构型，推广至包含$\mathrm{Sp}(n)$、$\mathrm{SO}(n)$以及耦合半超多重态的$\mathrm{Sp}(n)$规范群的情形。该扩展方法不仅涉及节点减法，还改变箭图（quiver）的图结构，从而为高维SCFT的Higgs分支提供了新的构造方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The original quotient quiver subtraction prescription applies only to unitary gauge groups and cannot directly handle orthogonal or symplectic isometry subgroups of the Coulomb branch. To broaden its applicability—particularly for constructing Higgs branches of superconformal field theories (SCFTs) in dimensions $>3$—the authors seek a systematic extension using physical brane realizations that naturally incorporate $\mathrm{O5}$ orientifold planes.
\n\n
原始的商图减法仅适用于酉规范群，无法直接处理Coulomb分支的正交或辛等距子群。为了拓展其适用范围——特别是用于构造维度$>3$的超共形场论（SCFT）的Higgs分支——作者借助能自然引入$\mathrm{O5}$定向平面的物理膜构型，寻求一种系统性的推广。

Method: The authors employ Type IIB string theory brane configurations involving D3, D5, NS5-branes, and $\mathrm{O5}$ orientifold planes to engineer 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ quiver gauge theories with unitary nodes. By analyzing how $\mathrm{O5}$ projections act on these brane systems, they derive modified quiver operations that correspond to gauging $\mathrm{Sp}(n)$, $\mathrm{SO}(n)$, or $\mathrm{Sp}(n)$ with a half-hypermultiplet. This goes beyond simple node subtraction: it involves changing edge orientations, identifying mirror-symmetric nodes, and altering the quiver’s Dynkin-type structure.
\n\n
作者采用包含D3、D5、NS5膜和$\mathrm{O5}$定向平面的Type IIB弦论膜构型，来构造具有酉节点的3d $\mathcal{N}=4$箭图规范理论。通过分析$\mathrm{O5}$投影对这些膜系统的作用，他们推导出对应于规范$\mathrm{Sp}(n)$、$\mathrm{SO}(n)$或带半超多重态的$\mathrm{Sp}(n)$的修正箭图操作。这一过程超越了简单的节点减法：它涉及改变边的方向、识别镜像对称节点，并改变箭图的Dynkin型结构。

Result: The extended prescription successfully gauges non-unitary Coulomb branch isometries by transforming the original unitary quiver into one with orthogonal or symplectic gauge groups, possibly coupled to half-hypermultiplets. This yields new brane-based constructions of the Higgs branches of certain 4d and 5d SCFTs, offering alternative geometric realizations consistent with known dualities.
\n\n
该扩展方法成功地通过将原始酉箭图变换为具有正交或辛规范群（可能耦合半超多重态）的箭图，实现了对非酉Coulomb分支等距群的规范。这为某些4d和5d SCFT的Higgs分支提供了新的基于膜的构造，给出了与已知对偶性一致的替代几何实现。

Conclusion: Quotient quiver subtraction can be systematically generalized beyond unitary groups using orientifolded brane setups. The resulting framework enriches the toolkit for studying 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ theories and their role as infrared descriptions of higher-dimensional SCFTs, particularly through their Higgs branches.
\n\n
商图减法可通过引入定向平面的膜构型被系统地推广至酉群之外的情形。所得框架丰富了研究3d $\mathcal{N}=4$理论及其作为高维SCFT红外描述（尤其是通过其Higgs分支）的工具集。

Abstract: Quotient quiver subtraction is a simple combinatorial prescription for gauging Coulomb branch isometry subgroups of 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ quiver gauge theories. This paper uses Type IIB brane constructions with $\mathrm{O5}$ planes to extend the prescription to gauge $\mathrm{Sp}(n),\;\mathrm{SO}(n)$, and $\mathrm{Sp}(n)$ coupled to a half-hypermultiplet Coulomb branch isometry subgroups of quivers with unitary gauge groups. The gauging procedure is no longer solely a subtraction -- additional steps change the graph type. The method is applied to provide alternative constructions of the Higgs branch of certain SCFTs in higher dimensions.

</details>


### [27] [A domain wall bound on anti-de Sitter vacua](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08779)
*Niccolò Cribiori,Antonia Paraskevopoulou,Thomas Van Riet*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper proposes a "domain wall bound" in anti-de Sitter (AdS) flux vacua by requiring that the tension of flux-changing domain walls exceeds the UV cutoff of the effective field theory. This yields an upper bound on the AdS radius and a corresponding lower bound on the gravitino mass, thereby supporting the gravitino conjecture and the AdS distance conjecture in the swampland program. The bound is tested in various string compactification scenarios, with classical flux vacua and LVS satisfying it, while racetrack and KKLT-like constructions face nontrivial constraints on scale hierarchies.
\n\n
本文通过要求通量改变的畴壁张力高于有效场论的紫外截断，提出了反德西特（AdS）通量真空中的“畴壁界”（domain wall bound）。这给出了AdS半径的上限和相应的引力微子质量下限，从而支持了沼泽地纲领中的引力微子猜想和AdS距离猜想。作者在多种弦紧化模型中检验了该界限：经典通量真空和LVS满足该界限，而racetrack和KKLT类构造在实现大尺度层级时受到非平凡约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the swampland program, which aims to distinguish consistent low-energy effective field theories that can be embedded in quantum gravity from those that cannot (the “swampland”). Two key conjectures—the gravitino mass conjecture and the anti-de Sitter distance conjecture—suggest that stable AdS vacua must have a gravitino mass bounded below and an AdS radius bounded above. The authors seek a physical mechanism rooted in domain wall dynamics to derive such bounds from first principles within controlled effective descriptions.
\n\n
动机源于沼泽地纲领（swampland program），其目标是区分可嵌入量子引力的低能有效场论与不可嵌入者（即“沼泽地”）。其中两个关键猜想——引力微子质量猜想和反德西特距离猜想——指出，稳定的AdS真空必须具有引力微子质量的下限和AdS半径的上限。作者试图从畴壁动力学出发，在可控的有效描述中基于第一性原理推导出此类界限。

Method: The method involves analyzing flux-changing domain walls interpolating between different AdS flux vacua in string theory compactifications. By imposing the consistency condition that the domain wall tension $T$ must satisfy $T > \Lambda_{\\text{UV}}^3$, where $\\Lambda_{\\text{UV}}$ is the ultraviolet cutoff of the effective field theory (typically set by the Kaluza-Klein or string scale), the authors derive an inequality relating the AdS radius $L_{\\text{AdS}}$ to the gravitino mass $m_{3/2}$. Using the relation $L_{\\text{AdS}}^{-1} \\sim m_{3/2}$ in supersymmetric AdS vacua, this leads to a lower bound on $m_{3/2}$, i.e., $m_{3/2} \\gtrsim \\Lambda_{\\text{UV}}^3 M_{\\text{Pl}}^{-2}$. The bound is then applied to explicit models: classical flux compactifications, racetrack superpotentials, Large Volume Scenario (LVS), and KKLT-like AdS vacua.
\n\n
方法包括分析弦论紧化中连接不同AdS通量真空的通量改变畴壁。通过施加一致性条件——畴壁张力 $T$ 必须满足 $T > \\Lambda_{\\text{UV}}^3$，其中 $\\Lambda_{\\text{UV}}$ 是有效场论的紫外截断（通常由Kaluza-Klein或弦尺度设定）——作者推导出AdS半径 $L_{\\text{AdS}}$ 与引力微子质量 $m_{3/2}$ 之间的不等式。利用超对称AdS真空中关系 $L_{\\text{AdS}}^{-1} \\sim m_{3/2}$，得到 $m_{3/2}$ 的下限，即 $m_{3/2} \\gtrsim \\Lambda_{\\text{UV}}^3 M_{\\text{Pl}}^{-2}$。随后将该界限应用于具体模型：经典通量紧化、racetrack超势、大体积场景（LVS）和KKLT类AdS真空。

Result: The domain wall bound is satisfied in classical flux vacua and the Large Volume Scenario (LVS), where the natural scales align with the derived inequality. However, in racetrack and KKLT-like AdS constructions, achieving parametrically large hierarchies between the AdS scale and the UV scale (e.g., $L_{\\text{AdS}}^{-1} \\ll \\Lambda_{\\text{UV}}$) conflicts with the bound unless model parameters are finely tuned. Thus, the bound imposes nontrivial constraints on the viability of such scenarios within the swampland framework.
\n\n
畴壁界在经典通量真空和大体积场景（LVS）中得以满足，其中自然尺度与所推导的不等式一致。然而，在racetrack和KKLT类AdS构造中，若试图实现AdS尺度与紫外尺度之间的参数化大层级（例如 $L_{\\text{AdS}}^{-1} \\ll \\Lambda_{\\text{UV}}$），则会与该界限冲突，除非对模型参数进行精细调节。因此，该界限对这些场景在沼泽地框架下的可行性施加了非平凡约束。

Conclusion: The domain wall bound provides a concrete, physically motivated derivation of the gravitino mass and AdS distance conjectures from the requirement of effective field theory consistency. It suggests that not all seemingly consistent low-energy AdS vacua can be completed in quantum gravity, reinforcing the swampland criteria. The analysis highlights tensions in popular moduli stabilization schemes like KKLT when attempting to engineer large scale separations, pointing toward deeper constraints in quantum gravity.
\n\n
畴壁界从有效场论一致性的要求出发，为引力微子质量和AdS距离猜想提供了具体且物理动机明确的推导。这表明并非所有看似自洽的低能AdS真空都能在量子引力中完成，从而强化了沼泽地判据。分析揭示了在KKLT等流行的模稳定化方案中，当试图构造大尺度分离时存在的张力，指向量子引力中更深层的约束。

Abstract: We consider anti-de Sitter flux vacua interpolated by flux-changing domain walls. Demanding that the tension of such a domain wall be above the ultraviolet cutoff of the effective description, we derive an upper bound on the anti-de Sitter radius, which we term domain wall bound. It translates into a lower bound on the gravitino mass, thus realizing the gravitino conjecture and the anti-de Sitter distance conjecture of the swampland program. We test the domain wall bound on several examples with a candidate hierarchy of scales: classical flux vacua, racetrack models, LVS and KKLT-like anti-de Sitter vacua. The classical flux vacua and LVS are found to be compatible with the bound. For racetrack and KKLT-like anti-de Sitter vacua, the bound poses a non-trivial constraint on achieving large hierarchies of scales.

</details>


### [28] [Interface Minimal Model Holography and Topological String Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08783)
*Davide Gaiotto,Keyou Zeng*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates 2d fermions coupled to 3d Chern-Simons gauge fields with $SU(N)$ gauge group, showing that the resulting interfaces correspond to $W_N$ minimal models. Using A-model Topological String Theory, the authors provide a holographic description and exploit exotic integrability to exactly match all sphere correlation functions of meson operators, thereby embedding Minimal Model Holography into String Theory.
\n\n
本文研究了与三维Chern-Simons规范场耦合的二维费米子系统，其中规范群为$SU(N)$且费米子处于基本表示。所得界面与$W_N$ minimal models密切相关。作者利用A-model Topological String Theory给出了该系统的全息描述，并借助其特殊的可积性（exotic integrability），精确匹配了介子算符在球面上的所有关联函数，从而将Minimal Model Holography嵌入到String Theory中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the holographic realization of 2d conformal field theories—specifically $W_N$ minimal models—arising from 3d Chern-Simons/fermion interfaces, and to embed such Minimal Model Holography within a concrete framework of string theory rather than as an isolated duality.
\n\n
动机在于理解由三维Chern-Simons/费米子界面所导出的二维共形场论（特别是$W_N$ minimal models）的全息实现，并将此类Minimal Model Holography嵌入到具体的String Theory框架中，而非仅作为一种孤立的对偶关系。

Method: The authors employ A-model Topological String Theory to construct a holographic dual of the 2d/3d interface system. They leverage the exotic integrability properties inherent in the model to compute and match sphere correlation functions of meson operators on both sides of the duality.
\n\n
作者采用A-model Topological String Theory构建二维/三维界面系统的全息对偶，并利用模型内禀的exotic integrability性质，在对偶两侧计算并匹配介子算符在球面上的关联函数。

Result: An exact holographic correspondence is established: all sphere correlation functions of meson operators in the 2d interface theory are matched with those computed in the A-model Topological String Theory dual, confirming that the interface realizes a $W_N$ minimal model and providing a string-theoretic embedding of Minimal Model Holography.
\n\n
建立了精确的全息对应：二维界面理论中介子算符在球面上的所有关联函数与A-model Topological String Theory对偶侧的计算结果完全匹配，证实该界面实现了$W_N$ minimal model，并为Minimal Model Holography提供了String Theory中的实现。

Conclusion: The work successfully embeds Minimal Model Holography into Topological String Theory by identifying a physical 2d/3d Chern-Simons–fermion interface whose holographic dual is governed by the A-model, with exact agreement of observables due to exotic integrability.
\n\n
本工作通过识别一个物理的二维/三维Chern-Simons–费米子界面，成功将Minimal Model Holography嵌入到Topological String Theory中；该界面的全息对偶由A-model支配，并因exotic integrability而实现可观测量的精确匹配。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of 2d fermions coupled to 3d Chern-Simons gauge fields. For $SU(N)$ gauge group and fermions in the fundamental representation, the resulting interfaces are closely related to $W_N$ minimal models. We give an holographic description of the interfaces within the A-model Topological String Theory. The model has exotic integrability properties, which allow us to propose an exact holographic match of all sphere correlation functions of meson operators. This construction embeds Minimal Model Holography in String Theory.

</details>


### [29] [A Covariant Formulation of Logarithmic Supertranslations at Spatial Infinity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08784)
*Florian Girelli,Simon Langenscheidt,Giulio Neri,Christopher Pollack,Celine Zwikel*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper proposes a new symplectic structure and conservative boundary conditions for asymptotically flat spacetimes at spatial infinity using a polyhomogeneous Beig-Schmidt expansion, revealing extended asymptotic symmetries beyond the BMS algebra that include regular log-translations and log-supertranslations. The associated charges are finite, conserved, and exhibit central extensions in their algebra, offering new physical observables relevant to null and timelike infinity.
\n\n
本文提出了一种新的辛结构和保守边界条件，用于在空间无穷远处的渐近平直时空，采用多齐次Beig-Schmidt展开，揭示了超出BMS代数的扩展渐近对称性，包括regular log-translations和log-supertranslations。相关电荷是有限且守恒的，其代数中存在中心扩张，为类光和类时无穷远处提供了新的物理可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to fully characterize the asymptotic symmetry structure of asymptotically flat spacetimes at spatial infinity, which has historically been less understood than at null infinity. Previous works either omitted logarithmic terms or restricted parity sectors, limiting the completeness of the symmetry algebra and its physical implications. This paper aims to resolve these gaps by incorporating both parities of log-supertranslations and introducing regular log-translations within a consistent phase space framework.
\n\n
动机源于需要完整刻画空间无穷远处渐近平直时空的渐近对称性结构，该结构在历史上比类光无穷远处的理解更不充分。以往工作要么忽略了对数项，要么限制了宇称分量，从而限制了对称代数及其物理含义的完整性。本文旨在通过在一个一致的相空间框架内同时纳入log-supertranslations的两种宇称并引入regular log-translations来解决这些不足。

Method: The authors employ a polyhomogeneous Beig-Schmidt expansion near spatial infinity to define boundary conditions that allow logarithmic terms in the metric. They construct a new symplectic structure compatible with these boundary conditions and derive the asymptotic symmetry algebra by analyzing residual diffeomorphisms preserving the structure. The associated charges are computed via covariant phase space methods, and their conservation and finiteness are verified. The algebra of charges is then examined for possible central extensions using Poisson bracket computations.
\n\n
作者在空间无穷远处采用多齐次Beig-Schmidt展开，定义允许度规中包含对数项的边界条件。他们构建了一个与这些边界条件兼容的新辛结构，并通过分析保持该结构的剩余微分同胚来推导渐近对称代数。相关电荷通过协变相空间方法计算，并验证其守恒性和有限性。随后通过泊松括号计算检验电荷代数中可能存在的中心扩张。

Result: The analysis yields an extended asymptotic symmetry algebra that includes the standard BMS supertranslations along with abelian sectors of regular log-translations and log-supertranslations. The corresponding charges are finite and conserved. Crucially, the charge algebra exhibits nontrivial central extensions: one between supertranslations and log-supertranslations, and another between singular translations and regular log-translations. Furthermore, the framework accommodates both even and odd parity log-supertranslations in a single phase space, unifying and extending prior approaches.
\n\n
分析得到了一个扩展的渐近对称代数，其中包含标准BMS超平移以及regular log-translations和log-supertranslations的阿贝尔子代数。相应电荷是有限且守恒的。关键的是，电荷代数表现出非平凡的中心扩张：一个存在于supertranslations与log-supertranslations之间，另一个存在于singular translations与regular log-translations之间。此外，该框架在单一相空间中同时容纳了偶宇称和奇宇称的log-supertranslations，统一并拓展了先前的方法。

Conclusion: The paper establishes a more complete and physically richer asymptotic symmetry structure at spatial infinity by incorporating logarithmic modes with both parities. The resulting centrally extended algebra suggests new gravitational memory effects and soft theorems, potentially linking spatial, null, and timelike infinities through novel observables encoded in the extended symmetry charges.
\n\n
本文通过纳入具有两种宇称的对数模，建立了空间无穷远处更完整且物理上更丰富的渐近对称结构。所得到的具有中心扩张的代数暗示了新的引力记忆效应和软定理，可能通过扩展对称电荷中编码的新可观测量，将空间、类光和类时无穷远联系起来。

Abstract: We investigate the asymptotic symmetries of asymptotically flat spacetimes at spatial infinity. We propose a new symplectic structure and conservative boundary conditions in a polyhomogeneous Beig-Schmidt expansion. The asymptotic symmetries extend the BMS algebra by abelian sectors, notably incorporating regular log-translations and log-supertranslations. The associated charges are finite and conserved, and we show that their algebra admits a central extension between supertranslations and log-supertranslations, and between the singular translations and regular log-translations. Our analysis is compatible with, and extends, both the work of arXiv:1106.4045 and arXiv:2211.10941 : it extends the former by incorporating log-supertranslations, and the latter by allowing both parities of the log-supertranslations in the same phase space. These newly identified symmetries at spatial infinity encode novel physical information that has not been revealed in other regions of asymptotically flat spacetimes, thereby opening the door to new observables to consider at null and timelike infinity.

</details>


### [30] [All-Loop Renormalization and the Phase of the de Sitter Wavefunction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08794)
*Alexander Farren,Ciaran McCulloch,Enrico Pajer,Xi Tong*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates that for shift-symmetric scalar fields in de Sitter space—a common approximation in inflationary models—the late-time wavefunction of the universe, though real at tree-level, acquires a universal imaginary part at all loop orders due to a renormalization-induced quantum anomaly. This imaginary component is fully determined by the wavefunction’s renormalization scale dependence, leading to an infinite set of consistency relations among correlators of massless fields and their conjugate momenta.
\n\n
本文证明，对于de Sitter空间中的shift-symmetric标量场（许多暴胀模型的良好近似），宇宙的晚期波函数在树图阶是实的，但由于重整化引起的量子反常，在所有圈图阶都会获得一个普适的虚部。该虚部完全由波函数对重整化标度的依赖所决定，从而导出无质量场及其共轭动量关联函数之间的一组无穷多致性关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from understanding how quantum effects in de Sitter space—particularly those arising from renormalization—impact the structure of the cosmological wavefunction. While tree-level computations for shift-symmetric scalars yield a purely real wavefunction consistent with symmetries like dilation invariance and the Bunch-Davies vacuum, quantum corrections can break this reality condition. The authors aim to uncover the precise nature of this breaking and its implications for observable correlations in the primordial universe.
\n\n
动机源于理解de Sitter空间中的量子效应（特别是由重整化引起的效应）如何影响宇宙学波函数的结构。尽管shift-symmetric标量场的树图计算给出一个纯实的波函数，与膨胀对称性和Bunch-Davies真空等对称性一致，但量子修正可能破坏这种实性条件。作者旨在揭示这种破坏的确切性质及其对原初宇宙可观测关联函数的影响。

Method: The authors employ a combination of symmetry principles (unitarity, locality, dilation isometry, and Bunch-Davies initial conditions) and renormalization group (RG) techniques within the framework of the late-time wavefunction formalism. They analyze the structure of loop corrections to the wavefunction for massless, shift-symmetric scalars in de Sitter, showing that the imaginary part arises as a quantum anomaly tied to RG flow. By leveraging the Callan–Symanzik equation adapted to the wavefunction, they derive a compact relation linking the imaginary part of the wavefunction to its scale dependence.
\n\n
作者结合对称性原理（幺正性、局域性、膨胀等距性和Bunch-Davies初态）与重整化群（RG）技术，在晚期波函数形式体系中进行分析。他们研究了de Sitter空间中无质量、shift-symmetric标量场波函数的圈图修正结构，表明其虚部作为与RG流相关的量子反常出现。通过将Callan–Symanzik方程推广到波函数框架，他们导出了一个紧凑关系，将波函数的虚部与其标度依赖性联系起来。

Result: The key result is that the imaginary part of the late-time wavefunction, $\\text{Im}\\,\\Psi$, is universally fixed by the derivative of the real part with respect to the renormalization scale $\\mu$: $$\\text{Im}\\,\\Psi = -\\frac{1}{2} \\frac{d}{d\\log\\mu} \\text{Re}\\,\\Psi,$$ to all orders in perturbation theory. This leads to an infinite hierarchy of relations among time-ordered and Wightman correlators involving fields and their conjugate momenta, explicitly verified at one-loop order for massless scalars in de Sitter.
\n\n
核心结果是：晚期波函数的虚部 $\\text{Im}\\,\\Psi$ 在所有微扰阶上被其实部对重整化标度 $\\mu$ 的导数普适地确定：$$\\text{Im}\\,\\Psi = -\\frac{1}{2} \\frac{d}{d\\log\\mu} \\text{Re}\\,\\Psi。$$ 这导致了涉及场及其共轭动量的时间序和Wightman关联函数之间的一组无穷多关系，作者在de Sitter空间中无质量标量场的一圈阶显式验证了这一点。

Conclusion: The paper establishes a deep connection between renormalization, quantum anomalies, and the analytic structure of the cosmological wavefunction in de Sitter. The derived relation not only resolves the tension between reality at tree-level and complexness at loop level but also provides powerful new consistency conditions for primordial correlators, offering a novel tool for the Cosmological Bootstrap program.
\n\n
本文建立了重整化、量子反常与de Sitter空间中宇宙学波函数解析结构之间的深刻联系。所导出的关系不仅解决了树图阶实性与圈图阶复性之间的张力，还为原初关联函数提供了强有力的新型一致性条件，为Cosmological Bootstrap计划提供了新工具。

Abstract: Cosmological observables of the primordial universe are encoded in the late-time field-theoretic wavefunction. For shift-symmetric scalars in de Sitter, a good approximation for many inflationary models, the wavefunction must be purely real at tree-level. This property is violated by a quantum anomaly in the process of renormalization. As a result, we show that the imaginary part of the wavefunction is fixed by its dependence on the renormalization scale to all loop orders in perturbation theory. This follows from unitarity, locality, dilation isometry and a Bunch-Davies state. The compact relation we uncover for the wavefunction implies an infinite set of relations among correlators of massless fields and their conjugate momenta, which we exemplify at one-loop order.

</details>


### [31] [Introduction to Generalized Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08798)
*Justin Kaidi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: These lecture notes provide a self-contained introduction to non-invertible symmetries, starting from higher-form symmetries and anomalies in $(1+1)$D, developing the mathematical framework of fusion categories, and extending to physical applications in $(3+1)$D quantum field theories.
\n\n
这些讲义提供了一个自包含的非可逆对称性（non-invertible symmetries）导论，从$(1+1)$维中的高形式对称性（higher-form symmetries）和反常（anomalies）出发，发展融合范畴（fusion categories）的数学框架，并延伸到$(3+1)$维量子场论中的物理应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to introduce non-invertible symmetries—a generalization beyond traditional group-like symmetries—using accessible tools for students and researchers unfamiliar with advanced topics like conformal field theory or lattice models, thereby bridging modern developments in quantum field theory with categorical mathematics.
\n\n
其动机是向不熟悉共形场论（conformal field theory）或格点模型（lattice models）等高级主题的学生和研究人员，介绍非可逆对称性——一种超越传统群类对称性的推广——从而将量子场论中的现代进展与范畴数学联系起来。

Method: The paper employs a pedagogical approach, beginning with foundational concepts such as higher-form symmetries and discrete gauge theories, then systematically building up to fusion categories, categorical gauging, and representation theory. It transitions from $(1+1)$D to $(3+1)$D systems to illustrate broader applicability.
\n\n
本文采用教学式方法，从高形式对称性（higher-form symmetries）和离散规范理论（discrete gauge theories）等基础概念出发，系统地构建融合范畴（fusion categories）、范畴化规范（categorical gauging）和表示论（representation theory），并从$(1+1)$维过渡到$(3+1)$维系统以展示更广泛的应用性。

Result: The notes establish a clear pathway from elementary symmetry concepts to the modern framework of non-invertible symmetries, demonstrating how fusion categories encode generalized symmetries and how these structures manifest physically in both low- and high-dimensional quantum field theories.
\n\n
这些讲义建立了一条从基本对称性概念到非可逆对称性现代框架的清晰路径，展示了融合范畴如何编码广义对称性，以及这些结构如何在低维和高维量子场论中体现物理效应。

Conclusion: Non-invertible symmetries represent a profound extension of the notion of symmetry in quantum field theory, best understood through the language of fusion categories; this framework unifies diverse phenomena across dimensions and offers new tools for analyzing phases and dualities.
\n\n
非可逆对称性代表了量子场论中对称性概念的深刻拓展，最好通过融合范畴的语言来理解；这一框架统一了跨维度的多种现象，并为分析相结构和对偶性（dualities）提供了新工具。

Abstract: These notes were prepared for a series of intensive lectures delivered at Hokkaido University, Nagoya University, Kyoto University, and Kyushu University.
  We begin with a brief review of higher-form symmetries, anomalies, and discrete gauge theories, before introducing non-invertible symmetries in $(1+1)$-dimensional systems. The basic structure of fusion categories is then discussed, including a discussion of categorical analogs of discrete gauging and representation theory. We subsequently turn to $(3+1)$-dimensional theories, where several physical applications of non-invertible symmetries are discussed. These notes are intended to be largely self-contained, and require no prior familiarity with subjects such as conformal field theory or lattice models.

### [32] [Crystal Melting, Triality and Partition Functions for Toric Calabi-Yau Fourfolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08815)
*Mario Carcamo,Sebastián Franco*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper extends crystal melting models for toric Calabi-Yau 4-folds, develops an algorithm to construct crystals from periodic quivers, studies their behavior under triality cascades, introduces stable variables that stabilize partition functions, and provides empirical data to guide the search for a generalization of cluster algebras in 2d (0,2) quiver theories.
\n\n
本文扩展了环面Calabi-Yau 4-fold的晶体熔化模型，开发了一种从周期箭图构造晶体的有效算法，研究了晶体在triality级联下的行为，引入了使配分函数稳定的“稳定变量”，并提供了经验数据以指导寻找适用于2d (0,2)箭图理论及其triality变换的cluster代数的物理推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to better understand crystal melting models associated with general toric Calabi-Yau 4-folds and their connection to 2d (0,2) supersymmetric quiver gauge theories. In particular, the authors aim to explore how these combinatorial models behave under triality—a 2d analog of Seiberg duality—and to generate concrete data (e.g., Hasse diagrams, partition functions) that could inform a physically motivated extension of cluster algebras beyond the standard 4d $\\mathcal{N}=1$ setting.
\n\n
动机源于更深入理解与一般环面Calabi-Yau 4-fold相关的晶体熔化模型及其与2d (0,2)超对称箭图规范理论的联系。作者特别希望探索这些组合模型在triality（即2d版本的Seiberg对偶）下的行为，并生成具体数据（如Hasse图、配分函数），以启发在标准4d $\\mathcal{N}=1$情形之外构建具有物理动机的cluster代数推广。

Method: The authors develop an efficient algorithm to construct 3D/4D crystal melting configurations directly from periodic quivers encoding the gauge theory data of 2d (0,1) or (0,2) theories. They analyze the action of triality on these crystals by tracking changes in the quiver, superpotential, and resulting crystal structure across a cascade. Key tools include computing partition functions $Z$, enumerating melting configurations, constructing Hasse diagrams of vacua, and identifying combinations of fugacities—called stable variables—that remain invariant or simplify under triality. The explicit geometry $Q^{1,1,1}$ serves as a testbed.
\n\n
作者开发了一种高效算法，直接从编码2d (0,1)或(0,2)理论规范数据的周期箭图构造3D/4D晶体熔化构型。他们通过追踪triality级联中箭图、超势和所得晶体结构的变化，分析triality对晶体的作用。关键工具包括计算配分函数$Z$、枚举熔化构型、构建真空的Hasse图，并识别在triality下保持不变或简化的fugacity组合——称为“稳定变量”。具体几何$Q^{1,1,1}$被用作测试平台。

Result: The paper demonstrates that crystal structures and their partition functions evolve predictably under periodic triality cascades. By introducing stable variables—specific combinations of Kähler parameters and flavor fugacities—the authors show that the partition function stabilizes along the cascade. They compute detailed data for the $Q^{1,1,1}$ example, including explicit Hasse diagrams, multiplicities of molten states, and stabilized partition functions. Moreover, the crystal partition function profile, when rewritten in terms of stable variables, exhibits universal or simplified behavior, suggesting hidden symmetries or invariants.
\n\n
本文表明，晶体结构及其配分函数在周期性triality级联下呈现可预测的演化。通过引入稳定变量（即Kähler参数与味fugacity的特定组合），作者证明配分函数在级联过程中趋于稳定。他们为$Q^{1,1,1}$例子计算了详细数据，包括显式的Hasse图、熔化态的多重性以及稳定的配分函数。此外，当用稳定变量重写时，晶体配分函数的“轮廓”展现出普适或简化的行为，暗示存在隐藏的对称性或不变量。

Conclusion: The work establishes a systematic framework for studying crystal melting models of toric Calabi-Yau 4-folds under triality, revealing stabilization mechanisms via stable variables. The empirical data generated strongly supports the existence of a generalized algebraic structure—beyond conventional cluster algebras—that governs 2d (0,2) triality. This paves the way for future theoretical developments linking combinatorial crystal models, supersymmetric gauge dynamics, and novel algebraic systems.
\n\n
本工作建立了在triality下研究环面Calabi-Yau 4-fold晶体熔化模型的系统框架，揭示了通过稳定变量实现的配分函数稳定机制。所生成的经验数据有力支持存在一种超越传统cluster代数的广义代数结构来支配2d (0,2) triality。这为未来将组合晶体模型、超对称规范动力学与新型代数系统相联系的理论发展铺平了道路。

Abstract: We extend the study of the recently introduced crystal melting models associated to toric Calabi-Yau 4-folds in several directions. In particular, we investigate in greater detail the structure of these models for general toric CY 4-folds and flavor configurations, using the explicit example of $Q^{1,1,1}$ to illustrate our ideas. To this end, we develop an efficient algorithm for constructing crystals based on periodic quivers. A central goal of this work is to understand the behavior of crystals and their partition functions under triality. We analyze the evolution of crystals along periodic triality cascades and generate detailed data for these systems, including Hasse diagrams, partition functions, and the multiplicities of melting configurations. We introduce the notion of stable variables and show that they lead to the stabilization of the partition functions along cascades. Finally, we define the profile of the crystal partition function and observe that, when expressed in terms of stable variables, it displays interesting behavior. A further motivation for this work is to generate empirical data that may guide the search for a physically motivated generalization of cluster algebras associated with $2d$ (0,2) quiver theories and their triality transformations.

</details>


### [33] [Universal Planar Abelian Duals for 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ Unitary CS-SQCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08842)
*Sergio Benvenuti,Riccardo Comi,Gabriel Pedde Ungureanu,Simone Rota,Anant Shri*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We construct a universal planar Abelian dual for 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ $U(N)_k$ SQCD with $F$ fundamentals, valid across the full $(N, F, k)$ parameter space (when supersymmetry is preserved). This extends beyond the previously known duality at $F = 2|k| + 2N$, providing a systematic framework to study infrared dynamics via mass deformations.
\n\n
我们为三维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ $U(N)_k$ SQCD（含 $F$ 个基本手征多重态）构建了一个普适的平面阿贝尔对偶理论，适用于整个 $(N, F, k)$ 参数空间（在超对称未破缺的前提下）。该结果超越了此前仅在 $F = 2|k| + 2N$ 处成立的对偶性，通过质量形变提供了一个系统研究红外动力学的框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Previous chiral-planar dualities were restricted to a special locus in parameter space ($F = 2|k| + 2N$), corresponding to a mass deformation of $\mathcal{N}=4$ mirror symmetry. A more general duality valid for arbitrary $(N, F, k)$ was needed to understand the full landscape of 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ gauge theories and their infrared behavior under generic deformations.
\n\n
此前的手征-平面对偶性仅限于参数空间中的特殊轨迹（$F = 2|k| + 2N$），对应于 $\mathcal{N}=4$ 镜像对称性的质量形变。为了理解三维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ 规范理论在任意 $(N, F, k)$ 下的完整结构及其在一般形变下的红外行为，亟需一个更普适的对偶描述。

Method: The authors develop a systematic algorithm to follow the renormalization group flow of the dual theory under generic real mass deformations. Starting from the known duality at $F = 2|k| + 2N$, they track how the dual quiver gauge theory evolves as masses are varied, thereby extending the duality to all allowed values of $(N, F, k)$. The resulting dual is a planar Abelian quiver gauge theory.
\n\n
作者发展了一套系统算法，用于追踪对偶理论在一般实质量形变下的重整化群流。他们从已知的 $F = 2|k| + 2N$ 处的对偶出发，跟踪当质量参数变化时对偶箭图规范理论的演化，从而将对偶性推广至所有允许的 $(N, F, k)$ 值。所得对偶理论是一个平面阿贝尔箭图规范理论。

Result: A universal planar Abelian quiver dual is established for all 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ $U(N)_k$ SQCD theories with unbroken supersymmetry. This dual provides a unified description of the infrared fixed points across the entire $(N, F, k)$ parameter space and demonstrates that the planar quiver structure persists under generic mass deformations.
\n\n
对于所有超对称未破缺的三维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ $U(N)_k$ SQCD 理论，建立了一个普适的平面阿贝尔箭图对偶。该对偶为整个 $(N, F, k)$ 参数空间中的红外不动点提供了统一描述，并表明平面箭图结构在一般质量形变下依然保持。

Conclusion: The planar Abelian quiver is not just a specific dual realization but a universal computational framework for analyzing 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ gauge dynamics. This work significantly broadens the scope of chiral-planar dualities and offers a powerful tool for exploring non-perturbative physics in three dimensions.
\n\n
平面阿贝尔箭图不仅是一个特定的对偶实现，更是分析三维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ 规范动力学的普适计算框架。这项工作极大拓展了手征-平面对偶性的适用范围，为探索三维非微扰物理提供了有力工具。

Abstract: We provide an explicit planar Abelian dual for three-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=2$ $U(N)_k$ SQCD with $F$ fundamental chiral multiplets. This construction covers the entire $(N, F, k)$ parameter space (provided supersymmetry is unbroken), offering a unified framework for the infrared physics of these theories. Our results generalize a recently discovered class of chiral-planar dualities, which were previously limited to the locus $F = 2|k| + 2N$, which is a mass deformation of $\mathcal{N}=4$ mirror symmetry plus a restricted set of additional mass deformations. By developing a systematic algorithm to track the flow of the dual theory under generic mass deformations, we establish the planar Abelian quiver not merely as a specific dual description, but as a universal tool for analyzing 3d gauge dynamics.
