### [34] [New Construction of Black Hole Solution in Non-Commutative Geometry and their Thermodynamic Properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08971)
*Abdellah Touati*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We propose a streamlined method to construct black hole solutions in non-commutative (NC) gauge theory by applying the Seiberg-Witten (SW) map to derive NC corrections to the Newton potential, then solving Einstein equations with the induced NC matter source at first order in the NC parameter. This yields exact black hole solutions—both neutral and charged—with U(1) NC symmetry. Thermodynamic analysis reveals removal of the temperature divergence during evaporation, a second-order phase transition, and a Hawking-Page-like transition under pressure. The black holes exhibit strong sensitivity to the NC parameter for small masses, and NC effects suppress quantum tunneling rates, particle-number density, and inter-emission correlations.
\n\n
我们提出了一种在非对易（NC）规范理论中构造黑洞解的简化方法：通过Seiberg-Witten（SW）映射导出牛顿势的NC修正，再以该修正诱导的NC物质源为背景，在NC参数的一阶近似下求解爱因斯坦方程。该方法可得到精确的中性与带电黑洞解（具有U(1) NC对称性）。热力学分析表明，非对易性消除了蒸发末期的温度发散，引发二阶相变，并在引入压力时重现类似Hawking-Page的相变。小质量黑洞对NC参数高度敏感，而大质量黑洞敏感性减弱；NC形变还抑制量子隧穿率、粒子数密度及连续辐射之间的关联，有效形成粒子逃逸势垒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional approaches to incorporating gravity into non-commutative gauge theory are technically cumbersome and often fail to yield exact black hole solutions. The authors aim to develop a more efficient and physically transparent framework that leverages the Seiberg-Witten map to encode non-commutativity into an effective matter source, thereby enabling the construction of exact black hole geometries at leading order in the NC parameter. This also allows systematic study of thermodynamics, response theory, and quantum emission in NC spacetimes.
\n\n
传统将引力纳入非对易规范理论的方法技术上繁琐，且通常难以获得精确黑洞解。作者旨在发展一种更高效且物理图像清晰的框架：利用Seiberg-Witten映射将非对易性编码为有效物质源，从而在NC参数的领头阶构造精确黑洞几何。这使得对NC时空中的热力学、响应理论和量子辐射进行系统研究成为可能。

Method: The method proceeds in two steps: (1) Use the Seiberg-Witten (SW) map to compute the non-commutative correction to the Newtonian potential, which induces an effective energy-momentum tensor $T_{\mu\nu}^{\text{NC}}$ sourced by a smeared mass distribution $\rho(r) \propto e^{-r^2/(4\theta)}$, where $\theta$ is the NC parameter. (2) Solve the Einstein equations $G_{\mu\nu} = 8\pi G T_{\mu\nu}^{\text{NC}}$ perturbatively at first order in $\theta$. The same procedure is extended to include electromagnetic fields with NC $U(1)$ symmetry. Thermodynamic quantities (ADM mass, temperature, entropy, heat capacity, free energy) are computed using standard GR techniques adapted to the NC metric. Linear response is analyzed via susceptibility $\chi = \partial M / \partial \theta$, and quantum tunneling is studied using the Hamilton-Jacobi method for both thermal and non-thermal radiation, with particle-number density and correlation functions derived from emission probabilities.
\n\n
该方法分两步：(1) 利用Seiberg-Witten（SW）映射计算牛顿势的非对易修正，由此诱导出有效能量-动量张量 $T_{\mu\nu}^{\text{NC}}$，其源为高斯展宽的质量分布 $\rho(r) \propto e^{-r^2/(4\theta)}$，其中 $\theta$ 为NC参数；(2) 在 $\theta$ 的一阶微扰下求解爱因斯坦方程 $G_{\mu\nu} = 8\pi G T_{\mu\nu}^{\text{NC}}$。该程序被推广至包含具有NC $U(1)$ 对称性的电磁场的情形。热力学量（ADM质量、温度、熵、热容、自由能）通过适用于NC度规的标准广义相对论技术计算。线性响应通过磁化率 $\chi = \partial M / \partial \theta$ 分析，量子隧穿则采用Hamilton-Jacobi方法研究热与非热辐射，并从辐射概率导出粒子数密度与关联函数。

Result: The authors obtain exact black hole solutions in non-commutative gauge theory at first order in $\theta$, both neutral and charged. Thermodynamically, the Hawking temperature remains finite as $r \to 0$, eliminating the final-stage divergence. A second-order phase transition occurs in the canonical ensemble, and under extended thermodynamics with pressure $P = -\Lambda/8\pi$, a Hawking-Page-like first-order transition between small and large black holes emerges. The susceptibility $\chi$ is large for small black holes, indicating high sensitivity to $\theta$, but diminishes for larger ones. Quantum tunneling calculations show reduced emission rates: the particle-number density is suppressed by a factor involving $\theta$, and statistical correlations between successive emissions (e.g., covariance) are weakened, suggesting NC geometry acts as a barrier to information leakage.
\n\n
作者在 $\theta$ 的一阶近似下获得了非对易规范理论中的精确黑洞解（包括中性与带电情形）。热力学上，当 $r \to 0$ 时Hawking温度保持有限，消除了末期发散；正则系综中出现二阶相变；在引入压力 $P = -\Lambda/8\pi$ 的扩展热力学框架下，重现了小黑洞与大黑洞之间的类Hawking-Page一级相变。磁化率 $\chi$ 在小黑洞情形下较大，表明对 $\theta$ 高度敏感，而大黑洞敏感性减弱。量子隧穿计算显示辐射率降低：粒子数密度受含 $\theta$ 因子抑制，连续辐射间的统计关联（如协方差）被削弱，表明NC几何对信息泄露构成势垒。

Conclusion: The proposed SW-map-based approach provides an efficient and exact framework for constructing black hole solutions in non-commutative gravity at leading order, circumventing the algebraic complexity of full NC diffeomorphisms. Non-commutativity fundamentally alters black hole thermodynamics and quantum emission: it regularizes singular behavior, induces novel phase transitions, and suppresses information-carrying correlations in Hawking radiation. These results suggest that spacetime non-commutativity may play a crucial role in resolving the black hole information paradox and in modeling Planck-scale quantum gravity effects through effective field theory.
\n\n
所提出的基于SW映射的方法为在领头阶构造非对易引力中的黑洞解提供了一个高效且精确的框架，规避了完整NC微分同胚的代数复杂性。非对易性从根本上改变了黑洞热力学与量子辐射：它正则化了奇异性行为，诱导出新奇相变，并抑制Hawking辐射中携带信息的关联。这些结果表明，时空非对易性可能在解决黑洞信息悖论及通过有效场论刻画普朗克尺度量子引力效应中扮演关键角色。

Abstract: We present a new method to construct black hole solutions in non-commutative (NC) gauge theory. First we obtain the NC correction to the Newton potential via the Seiberg-Witten (SW) map, and then solve the Einstein equations in the presence of the resulting NC matter density at first order in the NC parameter. The same procedure is applied to construct a charged solution with NC \(U(1)\) symmetry. This method yields an exact black hole solution in NC gauge theory at the stated order and is considerably less cumbersome than other NC gauge theory approaches to gravity. As an application, we analyze the thermodynamic properties of the new solutions: we compute the ADM mass, Hawking temperature, entropy, heat capacity and free energy, both in the absence and in the presence of pressure. Our results show that non-commutativity removes the temperature divergence at the final stage of evaporation and induces a second-order phase transition; in the presence of pressure we recover a Hawking-Page-like phase transition. We then investigate the susceptibility and linear response of the black hole to changes in the NC parameter. Our results show high sensitivity to small changes in the NC parameter for small black holes, while the sensitivity becomes weaker for larger ones. Finally, we study quantum tunneling in this geometry for both thermal and non-thermal radiation, and we investigate the particle-number density and statistical correlations of successive emissions. We find that the NC deformation suppresses the particle-number density and weakens correlations between successive emissions, effectively acting as a barrier to particle escape.

### [35] [Hydrodynamics as cospans of field theories into the BF theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09013)
*Simon Jonsson,Hyungrok Kim*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper proposes a geometric framework unifying microscopic and hydrodynamic descriptions of systems with higher-form symmetries via a cospan of differential graded manifolds, where the intermediate node is a $BF$ theory encoding conservation laws of $p$-form currents.
\n\n
本文提出了一种几何框架，通过微分分次流形（differential graded manifolds）的余跨度（cospan）统一描述具有高阶形式对称性（higher-form symmetries）系统的微观与流体动力学行为，其中中间节点是一个$BF$理论，用于编码$p$-形式流的守恒律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard hydrodynamics relies on conservation laws of ordinary (0-form) currents; recent developments extend this to higher-form symmetries. The authors aim to formalize the hydrodynamic limit as a structural relation between theories rather than just an approximation scheme, using modern tools from derived geometry and field theory.
\n\n
标准流体动力学依赖于普通（0-形式）流的守恒律；近期研究已将其推广至高阶形式对称性。作者旨在利用导出几何（derived geometry）与场论的现代工具，将流体动力学极限形式化为理论之间的结构性关系，而非仅是一种近似方案。

Method: The authors model physical theories as differential graded manifolds encoding their equations of motion and symmetries. They construct a cospan diagram $X_\mathrm{micro}\to X_{BF}\leftarrow X_\mathrm{hydro}$, where $X_{BF}$ corresponds to a $BF$ topological field theory whose equations of motion are precisely the conservation laws $\mathrm{d} \star J^{(p)} = 0$ of $p$-form currents. The maps embed the microscopic and hydrodynamic theories into this universal current-conservation framework.
\n\n
作者将物理理论建模为编码其运动方程与对称性的微分分次流形。他们构造了一个余跨度图 $X_\mathrm{micro}\to X_{BF}\leftarrow X_\mathrm{hydro}$，其中 $X_{BF}$ 对应一个$BF$拓扑场论，其运动方程正是$p$-形式流的守恒律 $\mathrm{d} \star J^{(p)} = 0$。这些映射将微观理论与流体动力学理论嵌入到这一普适的流守恒框架中。

Result: The hydrodynamic approximation is recast as a morphism in the category of differential graded manifolds, providing a rigorous geometric interpretation of how hydrodynamic variables emerge from conserved higher-form currents via the intermediary $BF$ theory.
\n\n
流体动力学近似被重构为微分分次流形范畴中的一个态射，从而通过中介的$BF$理论，为流体动力学变量如何从守恒的高阶形式流中涌现提供了严格的几何诠释。

Conclusion: Hydrodynamics with higher-form symmetries can be systematically understood through the lens of derived geometry, with the $BF$ theory serving as a universal bridge between microscopic dynamics and macroscopic hydrodynamic descriptions.
\n\n
具有高阶形式对称性的流体动力学可通过导出几何的视角系统地理解，其中$BF$理论充当了微观动力学与宏观流体动力学描述之间的普适桥梁。

Abstract: Hydrodynamics is based on conservation laws of currents: one starts from the conserved currents of the theory describing the microscopic dynamics, and provides an alternative parameterisation of these currents in terms of hydrodynamic variables (density, pressure, velocity, etc.). This paradigm has recently been extended to incorporate higher-form symmetries. The conservation law of the $p$-form conserved currents can be regarded as the equations of motion of a $BF$ theory that treats the currents as fundamental fields. We argue that the hydrodynamic approximation to a microscopic theory can be regarded as a cospan of differential graded manifolds $X_\mathrm{micro}\to X_{BF}\leftarrow X_\mathrm{hydro}$, where $X_\mathrm{micro}$ and $X_\mathrm{hydro}$ describe the microscopic and hydrodynamic theories, respectively, and $X_{BF}$ describes the $BF$ theory of conserved currents.

### [36] [Photon spheres and bulk probes in $\text{AdS}_3$/$\text{CFT}_2$: the quantum BTZ black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09169)
*Oscar Lasso Andino,Axel León-Arteaga,Guillermo Ramírez-Ulloa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates the existence and properties of boundary-anchored spacelike geodesics in three-dimensional quantum BTZ (quBTZ) black hole spacetimes and their charged extensions, which are dual to entanglement entropy calculations in $AdS_3/CFT_2$. It establishes conditions under which such geodesics connect timelike-separated boundary points—often via multiple windings around the horizon—and links this to the presence of photon rings, supporting a conjecture that spherically symmetric asymptotically AdS spacetimes with photon spheres always admit spacelike or null geodesics between timelike-separated boundary points.
\n\n
本文研究了三维量子BTZ（quBTZ）黑洞及其带电推广中的边界锚定类空测地线的存在性与性质，这些测地线对偶于$AdS_3/CFT_2$中的纠缠熵计算。文章建立了此类测地线连接类时间隔边界点的条件（通常通过绕视界多次缠绕实现），并将其与光子环的存在性联系起来，支持了一个猜想：具有光子球的球对称渐近AdS时空总存在连接类时间隔边界点的类空或类光测地线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Entanglement entropy in holographic CFTs is computed via the Ryu–Takayanagi prescription, which requires extremal surfaces (geodesics in $d=2$) anchored on the boundary of asymptotically AdS spacetimes. However, in black hole backgrounds like Schwarzschild-AdS, spacelike geodesics can connect timelike-separated boundary points by winding around the horizon, raising questions about analyticity and the physical interpretation of entanglement entropy. The motivation is to rigorously analyze this phenomenon in the quantum-corrected BTZ geometries (quBTZ), including charged cases, and to test a conjecture relating photon rings to the existence of such geodesics in spherically symmetric spacetimes.
\n\n
全息CFT中的纠缠熵通过Ryu–Takayanagi处方计算，该处方要求在渐近AdS时空边界上锚定的极值曲面（在$d=2$时为测地线）。然而，在Schwarzschild-AdS等黑洞背景中，类空测地线可通过绕视界缠绕连接类时间隔的边界点，这引发了关于纠缠熵解析性及其物理解释的问题。本文旨在严格分析这一现象在量子修正的BTZ几何（quBTZ）及其带电情形中的表现，并检验一个将光子环与球对称时空中此类测地线存在性相关联的猜想。

Method: The authors perform an exhaustive analysis of geodesic equations in the three-dimensional quantum BTZ (quBTZ) black hole metric and its charged extension. They solve for spacelike geodesics with both endpoints on the asymptotic boundary, classifying their behavior across all branches of the quBTZ solution. By examining the effective potential for radial motion, they derive conditions for the existence of such geodesics and determine whether the boundary endpoints are spacelike-, timelike-, or null-separated. Additionally, they apply a criterion based on the existence of light rings (photon spheres) to assess the validity of the conjecture that in spherically symmetric asymptotically AdS spacetimes with a photon sphere, timelike-separated boundary points can always be connected by spacelike or null geodesics.
\n\n
作者对三维量子BTZ（quBTZ）黑洞度规及其带电推广中的测地线方程进行了详尽分析。他们求解两端点位于渐近边界的类空测地线，对quBTZ解所有分支中的测地线行为进行分类。通过考察径向运动的有效势，推导出此类测地线存在的条件，并判断边界端点之间的间隔类型（类空、类时或类光）。此外，他们应用基于光子环（光子球）存在性的判据，评估如下猜想的有效性：在具有光子球的球对称渐近AdS时空中，总存在连接类时间隔边界点的类空或类光测地线。

Result: The paper establishes precise conditions for the existence of boundary-anchored spacelike geodesics in all branches of the uncharged and charged quBTZ black holes. It shows that such geodesics can indeed connect timelike-separated points on the boundary, particularly when they wind around the black hole horizon multiple times. Furthermore, the analysis confirms that when a photon ring exists, the timelike entanglement entropy in $AdS_3/CFT_2$ remains real (i.e., has no imaginary part). The results support the conjecture that spherically symmetric asymptotically AdS spacetimes possessing a photon sphere always admit spacelike or null geodesics connecting timelike-separated boundary points.
\n\n
本文确立了在无电荷和带电quBTZ黑洞所有分支中边界锚定类空测地线存在的精确条件。研究表明，此类测地线确实可以连接边界上的类时间隔点，尤其是在绕黑洞视界多次缠绕时。此外，分析证实：当存在光子环时，$AdS_3/CFT_2$中的类时纠缠熵保持为实数（即无虚部）。结果支持了如下猜想：具有光子球的球对称渐近AdS时空总存在连接类时间隔边界点的类空或类光测地线。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that quantum corrections to the BTZ black hole geometry (as encoded in the quBTZ metric) do not obstruct the existence of boundary-anchored spacelike geodesics connecting timelike-separated points, reinforcing the robustness of holographic entanglement entropy beyond classical gravity. The link between photon rings and the reality of timelike entanglement entropy provides a geometric criterion for the analytic structure of CFT correlators. Moreover, the verification of the geodesic connectivity conjecture in these quantum-corrected backgrounds suggests its broader validity in holography, potentially extending to higher dimensions and more general quantum gravitational states.
\n\n
本研究表明，BTZ黑洞几何的量子修正（编码于quBTZ度规中）并不阻碍连接类时间隔点的边界锚定类空测地线的存在，从而强化了全息纠缠熵在经典引力之外的鲁棒性。光子环与类时纠缠熵实数性之间的联系为CFT关联函数的解析结构提供了几何判据。此外，在这些量子修正背景下对测地线连通性猜想的验证，暗示该猜想在全息理论中具有更广泛的适用性，可能推广至更高维度及更一般的量子引力态。

Abstract: The entanglement entropy in $d+1$ dimensional conformal field theories can be calculated using the area of $d$ dimensional minimal surfaces in $AdS_{d+2}$. Therefore, the existence of surfaces anchored in the boundary of an asymptotically anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetime is crucial for the calculation of entanglement entropy. In particular, in $d=3$ the extremal surfaces are geodesics with two ends in the boundary. In the Schwarzschild-AdS black hole the space-like geodesics can connect timelike-separated points by winding around the horizon multiple times. This result can be extended to other asymptotically AdS spacetimes. Moreover, for geodesics joining time-like separated points, if there is a photon ring then the timelike entanglement entropy in the $AdS_3/CFT_2$ will not have an imaginary part. We present an exhaustive analysis about the existence of geodesics anchored in the boundary of the three dimensional quantum BTZ (quBTZ) black hole and its charged counterpart. We found conditions for the existence of geodesics with two ends in the boundary in all branches of the quBTZ and determine the type of distance between the points in the boundary. We use a criteria for the existence of light rings to shed some light over the conjecture for spacetimes that are spherically symmetric and have a photon sphere: there are always points with time-like separation that can be connected by space-like or null geodesics.

</details>


### [37] [Scheme dependence and instability of double-trace deformations for gauge fields in AdS$_5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09322)
*Shuta Ishigaki,Masataka Matsumoto*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper investigates double-trace deformations of bulk gauge fields in asymptotically AdS$_5$ holography, showing that they induce tachyon and ghost instabilities in the boundary theory due to logarithmic boundary behavior of gauge fields, which introduces scheme-dependent ambiguities. The analysis combines analytical and numerical approaches across bottom-up and top-down (D3-D7) models.
\n\n
本文研究了在渐近AdS$_5$全息对偶中对体规范场进行双迹形变的问题，表明由于规范场在AdS边界附近的对数行为所引入的方案依赖模糊性，这种形变会在边界理论中导致快子（tachyon）和鬼模（ghost）不稳定性。作者结合解析与数值方法，在自下而上模型和自上而下D3-D7构造中对此不稳定性进行了分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Double-trace deformations are a standard tool in AdS/CFT for modifying boundary quantum field theories, and they have been proposed as a mechanism to introduce dynamical gauge fields on the boundary by deforming with respect to bulk gauge field operators. However, the consistency and stability of such constructions—especially in higher-dimensional bulk spacetimes like AdS$_5$—remain unclear. This work aims to examine whether such deformations lead to pathologies like tachyonic or ghost modes, which would signal an inconsistency in the dual field theory.
\n\n
双迹形变是AdS/CFT中修改边界量子场论的标准工具，已有提议通过相对于体规范场算符的形变来在边界上引入动力学规范场。然而，此类构造的一致性与稳定性——尤其是在AdS$_5$等高维体时空中的情形——尚不清楚。本文旨在检验此类形变是否会导致快子或鬼模等病态行为，从而揭示对偶场论中的不一致性。

Method: The authors analyze the near-boundary asymptotics of bulk gauge fields in asymptotically AdS$_5$ spacetimes, revealing logarithmic terms that complicate the standard Fefferman–Graham expansion. These logarithms induce a scheme-dependent ambiguity in defining the double-trace deformation $S \\to S + \\frac{1}{2} f \\int \\mathcal{O}^2$, where $\\mathcal{O}$ is the boundary operator dual to the bulk gauge field. They study the resulting effective action and linearized equations of motion to identify tachyon and ghost modes. Both analytical techniques (e.g., mode analysis, renormalization scheme comparison) and numerical methods (e.g., solving perturbed equations in specific holographic backgrounds) are employed in bottom-up Einstein–Maxwell models and the top-down D3-D7 brane setup.
\n\n
作者分析了渐近AdS$_5$时空中体规范场在边界附近的渐近行为，揭示出对标准Fefferman–Graham展开构成干扰的对数项。这些对数项导致双迹形变 $S \\to S + \\frac{1}{2} f \\int \\mathcal{O}^2$（其中 $\\mathcal{O}$ 是与体规范场对偶的边界算符）的定义存在方案依赖的模糊性。他们通过研究由此产生的有效作用量和线性化运动方程，识别出快子与鬼模。研究结合了解析方法（如模分析、重整化方案比较）和数值方法（如在特定全息背景中求解扰动方程），应用于自下而上的Einstein–Maxwell模型和自上而下的D3-D7膜构造。

Result: The double-trace deformation of bulk gauge fields in AdS$_5$ leads to an instability characterized by the presence of both tachyonic (negative mass squared) and ghost (negative kinetic energy) modes in the boundary effective theory. This pathology stems from the logarithmic running of the boundary coupling induced by the anomalous dimension of the dual operator, which is tied to the non-analytic near-boundary behavior of the gauge field. The instability persists across different holographic realizations, including both phenomenological bottom-up models and the string-theoretic D3-D7 system.
\n\n
在AdS$_5$中对体规范场进行双迹形变会导致边界有效理论中同时出现快子（负质量平方）和鬼模（负动能）的不稳定性。这一病态源于由对偶算符反常维度引起的边界耦合的对数跑动，而这又与规范场在边界附近的非解析行为密切相关。该不稳定性在多种全息实现中均存在，包括唯象的自下而上模型和弦论中的D3-D7系统。

Conclusion: The attempt to generate dynamical boundary gauge fields via double-trace deformations of bulk gauge fields in AdS$_5$/CFT$_4$ is obstructed by intrinsic instabilities arising from the logarithmic structure of the gauge field near the conformal boundary. This suggests that such a mechanism is inconsistent unless additional UV completion or modified boundary conditions are imposed. The results highlight a fundamental limitation of naive double-trace deformations involving vector operators in even-dimensional CFTs with holographic duals.
\n\n
在AdS$_5$/CFT$_4$中通过体规范场的双迹形变来生成动力学边界规范场的尝试，因规范场在共形边界附近对数结构所引发的内在不稳定性而受阻。这表明，除非引入额外的紫外完备机制或修改边界条件，否则该机制是不自洽的。结果揭示了在具有全息对偶的偶维CFT中，对矢量算符进行朴素双迹形变的一个根本性限制。

Abstract: In holography, double-trace deformations provide a general framework for deforming boundary field theories. In particular, they can be utilized to introduce dynamical gauge fields in the boundary theory through double-trace deformations of bulk gauge fields. In this work, we study this construction in the case where the bulk geometry is asymptotically AdS$_5$, and find that such a system involves tachyon and ghost modes. This instability originates from the logarithmic behavior of the gauge fields in the vicinity of the AdS boundary, which leads to a scheme-dependent ambiguity in the double-trace deformation. We investigate this instability by using both analytical and numerical methods in several holographic setups, including bottom-up models and the top-down D3-D7 construction.

</details>


### [38] [Renormalisation and matching of massless scalar correlation functions in Soft de Sitter Effective Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09438)
*Martin Beneke,Patrick Hager,Andrea F. Sanfilippo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper constructs the Soft de Sitter Effective Theory (SdSET) in dimensional regularization, including an initial-condition functional, and demonstrates through explicit matching calculations that it correctly captures the infrared and late-time quantum dynamics of superhorizon modes in de Sitter space, analogous to flat-space EFT techniques.
\n\n
本文在维度正规化方案中构建了软德西特有效理论（Soft de Sitter Effective Theory, SdSET），并引入了初态泛函；通过显式匹配计算证明，该理论能正确描述德西特时空中超视界模式的红外和晚期量子动力学，其重整化与匹配方法与平直时空的有效场论（EFT）类似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cosmological correlation functions of light and massless scalar fields in de Sitter space exhibit infrared divergences and secular logarithms due to the accumulation of long-wavelength (superhorizon) modes. The Soft de Sitter Effective Theory (SdSET) was proposed to systematically describe these non-trivial infrared dynamics, extending the stochastic inflation formalism. However, a rigorous formulation within dimensional regularization—including proper treatment of initial conditions and renormalization—was lacking.
\n\n
在德西特时空中，轻标量场和无质量标量场的宇宙学关联函数因超视界（长波长）模式的累积而出现红外发散和世俗对数（secular logarithms）。软德西特有效理论（SdSET）被提出以系统性地描述这些非平凡的红外动力学，并作为随机暴胀形式的推广。然而，此前尚缺乏在维度正规化框架下包含初态条件和重整化的严格表述。

Method: The authors formulate SdSET using dimensional regularization in $d = 4 - 2\\epsilon$ dimensions, incorporating an initial-condition functional that encodes the Bunch-Davies vacuum at early times. They perform matching calculations between the UV theory—massless $\\kappa \\phi^4$ theory—and SdSET by computing the tree-level trispectrum and six-point function, as well as the one-loop power spectrum in both theories. Renormalization is carried out following standard EFT procedures, with counterterms introduced to absorb divergences, and matching ensures the low-energy coefficients reproduce UV predictions for superhorizon observables.
\n\n
作者在 $d = 4 - 2\\epsilon$ 维度下使用维度正规化构建 SdSET，并引入一个初态泛函以编码早期的 Bunch-Davies 真空。他们通过在紫外（UV）理论（即无质量 $\\kappa \\phi^4$ 理论）与 SdSET 之间进行匹配计算，分别计算了树图阶的四点谱（trispectrum）和六点函数，以及单圈修正的功率谱。重整化遵循标准 EFT 程序，引入抵消项吸收发散，匹配过程确保低能有效算符的系数能复现 UV 理论对超视界可观测量的预言。

Result: The matching calculations confirm that SdSET correctly reproduces the infrared-sensitive parts of cosmological correlators from the UV theory. Specifically, the tree-level trispectrum and six-point function, and the one-loop power spectrum computed in SdSET match those derived from the full $\\kappa \\phi^4$ theory in the superhorizon limit. This validates that SdSET functions as a consistent effective field theory for superhorizon quantum dynamics, with renormalization and operator mixing behaving analogously to flat-space EFTs.
\n\n
匹配计算证实，SdSET 能正确复现 UV 理论中宇宙学关联函数的红外敏感部分。具体而言，在超视界极限下，SdSET 计算得到的树图阶四点谱、六点函数以及单圈功率谱均与完整 $\\kappa \\phi^4$ 理论的结果一致。这验证了 SdSET 作为超视界量子动力学的有效场论的一致性，其重整化与算符混合行为与平直时空 EFT 类似。

Conclusion: SdSET, when formulated in dimensional regularization with a proper initial-condition functional, provides a robust and systematic EFT framework for the quantum evolution of superhorizon modes in de Sitter space. It successfully isolates infrared physics, enables controlled perturbative calculations, and aligns with standard EFT principles such as renormalization and matching, thereby establishing itself as the appropriate low-energy description of soft scalar dynamics during inflation.
\n\n
当在维度正规化中结合恰当的初态泛函进行构建时，SdSET 为德西特时空中超视界模式的量子演化提供了一个稳健且系统化的有效场论框架。它成功分离出红外物理，支持可控的微扰计算，并符合重整化与匹配等标准 EFT 原则，从而确立了其作为暴胀期间软标量动力学的正确低能描述的地位。

Abstract: For light and massless scalar fields, cosmological correlation functions suffer from infrared divergences and secular logarithms. Soft de Sitter Effective Theory (SdSET) has been proposed by Cohen and Green as the effective description of the non-trivial dynamics of long-wavelength modes $k_{\rm phys} < H$ in de Sitter space, which is responsible for the infrared and late-time logarithms, and as a systematic extension of the stochastic approach. In this article, we construct SdSET in dimensional regularisation, including an initial-condition functional. We demonstrate by examples that renormalisation and matching works as for flat-space effective field theories. Adopting massless $κφ^4$ theory as the UV theory, we match the tree-level trispectrum and six-point function, and the one-loop power spectrum to SdSET, verifying explicitly that SdSET is the appropriate effective field theory for the quantum dynamics of superhorizon modes.

### [39] [Operator Renormalization using Emergent Supersymmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09520)
*Mrigankamauli Chakraborty,Sven-Olaf Moch*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper introduces a novel mechanism to apply supersymmetric Ward identities in non-supersymmetric quantum field theories, dramatically simplifying calculations. As a proof of concept, the authors demonstrate its efficacy in operator renormalization within the Gross-Neveu-Yukawa model, achieving major computational savings, with the long-term goal of extending the method to Quantum Chromodynamics (QCD).
\n\n
本文提出了一种新机制，可在非超对称量子场论中应用超对称Ward恒等式，从而大幅简化计算。作为概念验证，作者在Gross-Neveu-Yukawa模型中的算符重整化问题上演示了该方法的有效性，显著降低了计算量，其长期目标是将此方法推广至Quantum Chromodynamics（QCD）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard perturbative computations in non-supersymmetric theories like QCD are often algebraically cumbersome and computationally intensive. Supersymmetric theories possess powerful Ward identities that constrain correlation functions and simplify renormalization. The motivation is to harness these simplifications even when supersymmetry is not a symmetry of the physical theory, thereby accelerating calculations in realistic models such as QCD or other phenomenological frameworks.
\n\n
在QCD等非超对称理论中的标准微扰计算通常代数复杂且计算量大。而超对称理论具有强大的Ward恒等式，可约束关联函数并简化重整化过程。本文的动机在于，即使物理理论本身不具有超对称性，仍希望利用这些简化优势，从而加速QCD或其他唯象模型中的计算。

Method: The authors construct an auxiliary supersymmetric extension of the target non-supersymmetric theory, such that the desired operators or Green’s functions of the original theory can be embedded within supersymmetric multiplets. By applying supersymmetric Ward identities in this extended framework, they derive constraints on the renormalization of operators in the original theory. The method is explicitly implemented for operator renormalization in the Gross-Neveu-Yukawa model by embedding fermionic and scalar composite operators into a superfield, allowing the use of non-renormalization theorems and Ward identities from supersymmetry.
\n\n
作者构建了一个辅助的超对称扩展理论，使得原非超对称理论中的目标算符或Green函数可嵌入到超多重态中。通过在此扩展框架中应用超对称Ward恒等式，他们导出了对原理论中算符重整化的约束。该方法在Gross-Neveu-Yukawa模型的算符重整化中被显式实现：将费米子与标量复合算符嵌入一个超场（superfield）中，从而利用超对称的非重整化定理和Ward恒等式。

Result: In the Gross-Neveu-Yukawa model, the application of supersymmetric Ward identities reduces the number of independent Feynman diagrams that need to be computed explicitly. This leads to a substantial decrease in computational complexity—for instance, certain anomalous dimensions or renormalization constants can be obtained without direct loop calculations. The result demonstrates that non-supersymmetric theories can inherit computational advantages from supersymmetric structures via the proposed embedding mechanism.
\n\n
在Gross-Neveu-Yukawa模型中，应用超对称Ward恒等式显著减少了需显式计算的独立Feynman图数量，从而大幅降低计算复杂度——例如，某些反常维度（anomalous dimensions）或重整化常数无需直接进行圈图计算即可获得。结果表明，通过所提出的嵌入机制，非超对称理论可继承来自超对称结构的计算优势。

Conclusion: The proposed mechanism successfully bridges supersymmetric techniques with non-supersymmetric quantum field theories, offering a powerful new tool for perturbative calculations. While demonstrated in the Gross-Neveu-Yukawa model as a toy example, the approach is designed to be generalizable, with Quantum Chromodynamics as the ultimate target. If applicable to QCD, it could revolutionize high-order perturbative computations in strong interaction physics.
\n\n
所提出的机制成功地将超对称技术与非超对称量子场论联系起来，为微扰计算提供了一种强大的新工具。尽管在Gross-Neveu-Yukawa模型中仅作为玩具模型进行了演示，但该方法具有普适性，最终目标是应用于Quantum Chromodynamics（QCD）。若能成功用于QCD，或将彻底改变强相互作用物理中的高阶微扰计算。

Abstract: We develop a mechanism that enables supersymmetric Ward identities to be applied in non-supersymmetric theories. These identities are then used to streamline calculations in our target theories, potentially including phenomenological models. In these proceedings, we illustrate the method through operator renormalization in the Gross-Neveu-Yukawa model, where it leads to a significant optimization and a substantial reduction in computational effort. This serves as a toy example of the procedure that we ultimately aim to apply to Quantum Chromodynamics.

### [40] [Duality and Dilaton](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09586)
*A. A. Tseytlin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper examines how the dilaton field $\\phi$ transforms under target space duality ($r \\rightarrow \\alpha'/r$) in string theory, showing that the standard one-loop transformation law must be corrected at two-loop and higher orders in the $\\sigma$-model perturbation expansion. It demonstrates this using time-dependent cosmological backgrounds with toroidal spatial sections.
\n\n
本文研究了弦理论中目标空间对偶（$r \\rightarrow \\alpha'/r$）下dilaton场$\\phi$的变换规律，指出标准的一圈变换律在$\\sigma$模型微扰展开的两圈及更高阶必须修正。文章通过具有时间依赖环面半径的宇宙学背景对此进行了说明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from ensuring consistency of string theory under target space duality (T-duality), particularly when quantum corrections beyond one-loop in the worldsheet $\\sigma$-model are included. The standard dilaton shift $\\phi \\rightarrow \\phi - \\ln(r/\\sqrt{\\alpha'})$ preserves duality only at leading order; understanding its modification at higher loops is essential for accurate effective string actions and cosmological applications.
\n\n
动机源于确保弦理论在目标空间对偶（T-对偶）下的自洽性，尤其是在世界面$\\sigma$模型中包含一圈以上量子修正的情形。标准的dilaton平移$\\phi \\rightarrow \\phi - \\ln(r/\\sqrt{\\alpha'})$仅在领头阶保持对偶性；理解其在高阶的修正对于构建精确的有效弦作用量及宇宙学应用至关重要。

Method: The authors analyze the $\\sigma$-model beta functions up to two-loop order and impose the requirement of invariance under the generalized (time-dependent) duality transformation. They consider cosmological backgrounds where spatial dimensions form a torus with time-dependent scale factors, and derive the necessary correction to the dilaton transformation law to maintain duality symmetry beyond one-loop.
\n\n
作者分析了至两圈阶的$\\sigma$模型beta函数，并施加广义（含时）对偶变换下的不变性要求。他们考虑空间维度为具有时间依赖尺度因子的环面的宇宙学背景，并推导出为维持对偶对称性所必需的dilaton变换律修正项。

Result: The result is that the standard one-loop duality transformation of the dilaton receives corrections at two-loop order in the $\\sigma$-model expansion. Explicitly, the shift $\\phi \\rightarrow \\phi - \\ln(r/\\sqrt{\\alpha'})$ is insufficient; additional terms depending on curvature or time derivatives of the metric are required to preserve duality at higher orders. This is demonstrated concretely in $D \\ge 2$ cosmological models with toroidal spatial slices.
\n\n
结果表明，dilaton的标准一圈对偶变换在$\\sigma$模型展开的两圈阶会收到修正。具体而言，平移$\\phi \\rightarrow \\phi - \\ln(r/\\sqrt{\\alpha'})$是不充分的；为在高阶保持对偶性，需要引入依赖于曲率或度规时间导数的附加项。这一点在空间截面为环面的$D \\ge 2$维宇宙学模型中得到了具体展示。

Conclusion: Target space duality in string theory is not exact at the classical level when higher-order $\\alpha'$ corrections are included; the dilaton transformation law must be systematically modified order by order in the $\\sigma$-model loop expansion to preserve the symmetry. This has implications for constructing consistent low-energy effective actions and for string cosmology involving time-dependent compactifications.
\n\n
当包含高阶$\\alpha'$修正时，弦理论中的目标空间对偶在经典层面并非严格成立；为保持该对称性，dilaton变换律必须在$\\sigma$模型圈图展开中逐阶系统地修正。这对构建自洽的低能有效作用量以及涉及时间依赖紧致化的弦宇宙学具有重要意义。

Abstract: We review and elaborate on the issue of the dilaton transformation under the usual $r \rightarrow α'/r$ target space duality and its non-static generalization (or $σ$-model duality). It is found that the transformation law $r \rightarrow α'/r$, $φ\rightarrow φ- \ln(r/\sqrt{α'})$ which guarantees duality at the one-loop $σ$-model level should be modified at two (and higher) loop order. The non-static duality is illustrated on the example of cosmological solutions in $D \ge 2$ with time-dependent radii of space torus.

### [41] [Non-invertible symmetries and selection rules for RG flows of coset models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09591)
*Valentin Benedetti,Paul Fendley,Javier M. Magan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper develops a method using local data of a 2D CFT to classify superselection sectors and topological defect lines via submodels of modular invariant completions, yielding unified selection rules for RG flows—applied explicitly to coset and parafermion CFT$_2$ models.
\n\n
本文提出了一种利用二维共形场论（CFT$_2$）的局域数据，通过模不变完备化的子模型来分类超选择扇区（superselection sectors）和拓扑缺陷线（topological defect lines）的方法，从而为重整化群（RG）流提供统一的选择定则——并明确应用于余弦（coset）和准费米子（parafermion）CFT$_2$模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding selection rules for RG flows in 2D CFTs requires a systematic characterization of symmetries—including non-invertible ones—and superselection sectors. Existing approaches are fragmented; the authors aim to unify these through the algebraic structure of modular invariant completions and their submodels.
\n\n
理解二维共形场论（CFT$_2$）中重整化群（RG）流的选择定则，需要对包括非可逆对称性在内的对称性结构以及超选择扇区进行系统刻画。现有方法较为零散；作者旨在通过模不变完备化及其子模型的代数结构，实现这些方面的统一。

Method: The authors construct a framework where input consists of local operator data of a UV CFT$_2$, and output is the set of all submodels embedded in its diagonal modular invariant completion. This uses tools from Doplicher–Haag–Roberts (DHR) theory, Q-systems, and the classification of topological defect lines to extract superselection sectors and symmetry structures, which then inform RG flow selection rules.
\n\n
作者构建了一个框架：输入为紫外（UV）CFT$_2$的局域算符数据，输出为其对角模不变完备化中所有子模型的集合。该方法利用Doplicher–Haag–Roberts（DHR）理论、Q-systems 和拓扑缺陷线分类等工具，提取超选择扇区与对称性结构，进而导出RG流的选择定则。

Result: For coset and parafermion CFT$_2$ models, the authors explicitly enumerate all submodels of the diagonal modular invariant. This yields a complete set of superselection sectors and topological defect lines, leading to selection rules that both reproduce known results and predict new constraints on allowed RG flows.
\n\n
针对余弦（coset）和准费米子（parafermion）CFT$_2$模型，作者明确枚举了对角模不变的所有子模型。由此获得完整的超选择扇区与拓扑缺陷线集合，导出了既能重现已知结果又能预测新约束的RG流选择定则。

Conclusion: The proposed method provides a unified, algebraically rigorous approach to classifying symmetries and superselection sectors in 2D CFTs, enabling a comprehensive understanding of selection rules for RG flows triggered by relevant perturbations—particularly in theories with non-invertible symmetries.
\n\n
所提出的方法为二维共形场论中对称性与超选择扇区的分类提供了一个统一且代数上严谨的框架，使得对由相关算符扰动引发的RG流选择定则有了全面理解——尤其适用于具有非可逆对称性的理论。

Abstract: We analyze superselection sectors, non-invertible symmetries and selection rules for RG flows triggered via perturbations of a UV two-dimensional conformal field theory (CFT$_2$). To this end we describe a method whose input is the local data, and whose output is the set of submodels of the modular invariant completions. We explain how this output set provides a classification of superselection sectors (DHR categories and Q-systems) and of topological defect lines, leading to a unified and potentially complete approach to selection rules for RG flows. This method is applied to scenarios in which the UV is a coset or a parafermion model. For these CFT$_2$ we explicitly find all submodels of the diagonal modular invariants. Our results gives selection rules that unify several known facts about such RG flows, while also allowing us to find new aspects.

</details>


### [42] [Kaluza-Klein mode mixing in braneworlds: constraints on scalar absorption and physical degrees of freedom](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09656)
*Wen-Xuan Ma,Chun-E Fu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper studies Kaluza-Klein (KK) mode mixing for a bulk U(1) gauge field in higher-dimensional braneworld scenarios, showing that orthonormality and completeness of the KK basis enforce strong constraints on warp factors in codimension-d (d>1) geometries. Despite vector-scalar and scalar-scalar mixing, 4D gauge invariance is preserved, but the physical masses of vector KK modes are dynamically shifted due to absorption of specific scalar combinations, leaving residual massive scalars as physical degrees of freedom—especially in (4+2)-dimensional models.
\n\n
本文研究了高维膜世界模型中体 U(1) 规范场的 Kaluza-Klein（KK）模混合问题，表明 KK 基函数的正交归一性和完备性对余维数 $d>1$ 的背景中的弯曲因子施加了严格约束。尽管存在矢量-标量和标量-标量混合，四维规范不变性仍得以保持，但矢量 KK 模通过吸收特定标量组合导致其物理质量发生动力学偏移，在 (4+2) 维模型中留下残余的有质量标量 KK 模作为物理自由度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from understanding how gauge fields propagate in higher-dimensional braneworld models with nontrivial geometry, particularly when extra dimensions have codimension greater than one. In such setups, the standard Kaluza-Klein decomposition may lead to nontrivial mixing between different spin sectors (e.g., vector and scalar modes), which can jeopardize 4D gauge invariance or alter the expected mass spectrum. Clarifying whether and how 4D effective gauge symmetry survives such mixing—and what becomes of the scalar degrees of freedom—is essential for constructing phenomenologically viable models.
\n\n
动机源于理解规范场在具有非平凡几何结构的高维膜世界模型（特别是当额外维度的余维数大于一时）中的传播行为。在此类设定中，标准的 Kaluza-Klein 分解可能导致不同自旋扇区（如矢量与标量模）之间的非平凡混合，这可能破坏四维规范不变性或改变预期的质量谱。澄清四维有效规范对称性是否以及如何在混合下保持不变，以及标量自由度的命运，对于构建现象学上可行的模型至关重要。

Method: The authors impose orthonormality and completeness conditions on the Kaluza-Klein basis functions derived from the bulk U(1) gauge field in a warped codimension-d background. They analyze the structure of the 4D effective action after dimensional reduction, focusing on cross-terms that signal vector-scalar and scalar-scalar mixing. By requiring the decoupling of these mixed sectors to maintain a clean interpretation of the 4D theory, they derive constraints on admissible warp factors. The role of 4D gauge invariance is examined through the Stückelberg mechanism, where scalar modes are absorbed by massive vectors, and the residual scalar content is identified by analyzing the number of independent scalar sectors in (4+2) dimensions.
\n\n
作者在弯曲余维数-$d$ 背景中对体 U(1) 规范场导出的 Kaluza-Klein 基函数施加正交归一性和完备性条件。他们分析维度约化后的四维有效作用量结构，重点关注表征矢量-标量和标量-标量混合的交叉项。通过要求这些混合扇区解耦以维持四维理论的清晰诠释，推导出对允许的弯曲因子的约束。通过 Stückelberg 机制考察四维规范不变性的作用——其中标量模被有质量矢量吸收，并通过分析 (4+2) 维中独立标量扇区的数量来识别剩余的标量自由度。

Result: The analysis reveals that orthonormality and completeness of the KK basis impose stringent constraints on the warp factor in codimension-d ($d>1$) braneworlds, effectively ruling out generic warp geometries unless specific conditions are met. Although vector-scalar mixing occurs, 4D gauge invariance is preserved as an emergent property of the massive vector sector. Crucially, the physical masses of vector KK modes are shifted from their naive eigenvalues due to dynamical absorption of scalar modes. In (4+2) dimensions, because two distinct scalar sectors exist, only certain linear combinations are eaten, leaving behind physical massive scalar KK modes.
\n\n
分析表明，KK 基的正交归一性和完备性对余维数 $d>1$ 膜世界中的弯曲因子施加了严格约束，除非满足特定条件，否则会排除一般的弯曲几何。尽管存在矢量-标量混合，四维规范不变性仍作为有质量矢量扇区的内禀性质得以保持。关键的是，由于标量模的动力学吸收，矢量 KK 模的物理质量偏离其未微扰本征值。在 (4+2) 维中，由于存在两个不同的标量扇区，仅有特定线性组合被“吃掉”，从而留下物理的有质量标量 KK 模。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that consistent Kaluza-Klein reductions of bulk gauge fields in higher-codimension braneworlds require highly constrained geometric backgrounds to avoid pathological mixing. While 4D gauge symmetry remains intact through the Stückelberg mechanism, the resulting spectrum is richer than in codimension-1 models: vector KK modes acquire modified masses, and residual scalar KK states survive as physical particles. This has implications for model-building in extra-dimensional physics, particularly for scenarios aiming to realize dark sectors or modified gauge dynamics via higher-dimensional embeddings.
\n\n
本文得出结论：在高余维膜世界中对体规范场进行自洽的 Kaluza-Klein 约化，需要高度受限的几何背景以避免病态混合。尽管通过 Stückelberg 机制保持了四维规范对称性，所得谱比余维数为 1 的模型更丰富：矢量 KK 模获得修正质量，且残余标量 KK 态作为物理粒子存留。这对额外维度物理中的模型构建具有重要意义，尤其适用于旨在通过高维嵌入实现暗扇区或修正规范动力学的场景。

Abstract: We investigate the mixing between Kaluza-Klein (KK) modes for a bulk U(1) gauge field within braneworld models. By demanding orthonormality and completeness for the KK basis functions, we demonstrate that the decoupling of mixed sectors, specifically of the vector-scalar and scalar-scalar types, imposes stringent constraints on the warp factors of codimension-d (d>1) backgrounds. We show that the gauge invariance of the four-dimensional effective action is preserved despite such mixing, manifesting as an intrinsic property of the massive vector KK sector. However, the generic presence of vector-scalar mixing fundamentally alters the absorption mechanism of the scalar modes, dynamically shifting the physical masses of the vector KK modes away from their unperturbed eigenvalues. In (4+2)-dimensional models, the existence of two distinct scalar sectors significantly enriches the mixing dynamics. As the massive vectors absorb only specific linear combinations of these scalars, a residual set of massive scalar KK modes persists as physical degrees of freedom.

</details>


### [43] [Capacity of Entanglement and Replica Backreaction in RST Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09763)
*Raúl Arias,Daniel Fondevila*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper computes the capacity of entanglement in 2D dilaton gravity using the Russo-Susskind-Thorlacius (RST) model with $N$ conformal matter fields, going beyond Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) gravity by handling a dynamical conformal factor and global replica constraints. It finds a time-independent generalized capacity for a single interval and a time-dependent capacity for two intervals due to interaction between replica fixed points, even when entropy plateaus. This reveals non-uniform saddle competition near $n=1$, offering a mechanism for sharp features at the Page transition.
\n\n
本文在二维稀释引力中利用 Russo-Susskind-Thorlacius (RST) 模型耦合 $N$ 个共形物质场，计算了纠缠容量（capacity of entanglement），超越了以往主要在 Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) 引力中进行的工作，处理了动态的共形因子和整体复制构造约束。对于单个区间，得到一个与广义熵平行的时间无关的广义容量；对于两个区间，即使在熵平台期的晚期因子化区域，整体解仍导致复制不动点之间的相互作用项，经 Lorentzian 延拓后产生时间依赖的容量。这揭示了在 $n=1$ 附近鞍点竞争的高度非均匀性，为 Page 转变处容量的尖锐特征提供了具体机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Previous computations of gravitational entanglement measures were largely confined to Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) gravity, which simplifies the dynamics by freezing the conformal factor. The authors aim to extend these calculations to the more realistic Russo-Susskind-Thorlacius (RST) model, where the conformal factor is genuinely dynamical and the replica trick must respect global constraints such as single-valuedness and microcanonical boundary conditions. This setting allows a more complete treatment of backreaction, Hawking radiation, and quantum extremal surfaces (QES), enabling a refined probe—namely the capacity of entanglement—of the fine-grained structure of black hole evaporation and the Page transition.
\n\n
以往对引力纠缠度量的计算大多局限于 Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) 引力，该模型通过冻结共形因子简化了动力学。作者旨在将这些计算推广到更真实的 Russo-Susskind-Thorlacius (RST) 模型，在该模型中共形因子是真正动态的，并且复制技巧必须满足整体约束，如单值性和微正则边界条件。这一设定允许更完整地处理反作用（backreaction）、霍金辐射和量子极值面（QES），从而利用纠缠容量（capacity of entanglement）这一更精细的探针，研究黑洞蒸发和 Page 转变的精细结构。

Method: The authors employ the replica trick to compute the capacity of entanglement, defined as the second derivative of the Rényi entropy $S_n$ with respect to $n$ at $n=1$: $C = \\partial_n^2 [(n-1)S_n]|_{n=1}$. They solve the gravitational path integral on the $n$-fold replicated geometry in the RST model, which includes a Liouville-like dynamical conformal factor. A key technical advance is solving the replica deformation globally on the orbifold near $n=1$, incorporating both inhomogeneous solutions from local stress-tensor insertions and homogeneous solutions fixed by global conditions: single-valuedness of fields and conservation of total energy in a microcanonical ensemble. For one and two intervals, they construct the full saddle-point solution and analytically continue to Lorentzian signature to extract physical capacities.
\n\n
作者采用复制技巧计算纠缠容量，其定义为 Rényi 熵 $S_n$ 在 $n=1$ 处对 $n$ 的二阶导数：$C = \\partial_n^2 [(n-1)S_n]|_{n=1}$。他们在 RST 模型的 $n$ 重复制几何上求解引力路径积分，该模型包含类 Liouville 的动态共形因子。关键技术进展是在 $n=1$ 附近全局求解轨道空间（orbifold）上的复制形变，同时包含由局域应力张量插入产生的非齐次解和由整体条件（场的单值性及微正则系综中总能量守恒）固定的齐次解。针对单区间和双区间情形，他们构建完整的鞍点解，并通过 Lorentzian 延拓提取物理容量。

Result: For a single interval, the generalized capacity of entanglement is time-independent and parallels the behavior of the generalized entropy, consistent with expectations from equilibrium thermodynamics. For two intervals in the late-time regime where the entropy has plateaued due to island dominance, the capacity remains time-dependent. This arises from an interaction term between replica fixed points in the global solution, which survives analytic continuation to Lorentzian signature. The magnitude of this two-QES capacity is large, indicating that the competition among replica saddles near $n=1$ is highly non-uniform, thereby producing sharp features in the capacity precisely at the Page transition.
\n\n
对于单个区间，广义纠缠容量是时间无关的，其行为与广义熵平行，符合平衡热力学的预期。对于两个区间，在晚期熵因岛屿主导而达到平台的区域，容量仍保持时间依赖性。这是由于整体解中复制不动点之间的相互作用项在 Lorentzian 延拓后依然存在。该双 QES 容量的数值很大，表明在 $n=1$ 附近复制鞍点之间的竞争高度非均匀，从而在 Page 转变点处产生容量的尖锐特征。

Conclusion: The computation demonstrates that the capacity of entanglement is a more sensitive probe than entropy alone for detecting fine-grained dynamical features in black hole evaporation, particularly around the Page transition. By working in the RST model—where the conformal factor is dynamical and global replica constraints are essential—the authors uncover nontrivial time dependence and saddle competition effects invisible to the von Neumann entropy. This highlights the importance of going beyond JT gravity and suggests that the capacity can diagnose subtle aspects of quantum information recovery and replica symmetry breaking in gravitational systems.
\n\n
该计算表明，纠缠容量比熵本身更能敏感地探测黑洞蒸发中的精细动力学特征，尤其是在 Page 转变附近。通过在 RST 模型中工作——其中共形因子是动态的且整体复制约束至关重要——作者揭示了 von Neumann 熵无法察觉的非平凡时间依赖性和鞍点竞争效应。这突显了超越 JT 引力的重要性，并表明容量可用于诊断引力系统中量子信息恢复和复制对称性破缺的微妙方面。

Abstract: We compute the capacity of entanglement in two dimensional dilaton gravity in a setting where Hawking radiation, backreaction, and islands can be treated analytically. Our focus is the eternal black hole of the Russo Susskind Thorlacius model coupled to N conformal matter fields. Unlike previous gravitational computations, which were mostly carried out in JT gravity, the RST model forces one to deal with a genuinely dynamical conformal factor and with the global constraints of the replica construction. The main technical step is therefore to solve the replica deformation on the orbifold globally at first order near n=1, including the homogeneous sector fixed by single valuedness and by the requirement of a fixed microcanonical state. For a single interval we obtain a time independent generalized capacity, parallel to the generalized entropy. For two intervals, even in the late time factorization regime, the global solution generates an interaction term between replica fixed points; after Lorentzian continuation this produces a time dependent capacity on the two QES saddle, despite the corresponding entropy plateau. We discuss the regime of validity of the resulting expressions and explain how the large size of the two QES capacity implies a highly non uniform saddle competition near n=1, providing a concrete mechanism for sharp features of the capacity at the Page transition.

</details>


### [44] [The scheme independent 3-sphere free energy is not a monotone F-function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09799)
*Giacomo Santoni,Francesco Scardino*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates a scheme-independent quantity derived from the three-sphere partition function of 3D QFTs by subtracting local counterterms. While this quantity coincides with the $F$-theorem invariant at fixed points and decreases at second order in conformal perturbation theory under relevant scalar deformations, an exact computation for the free massive scalar on $S^3$ reveals it is not monotonic along the full RG flow—it dips below its IR value before returning to it. Hence, it fails to serve as a global monotone $F$-function, with the obstruction traced to the second-order differential operator used to remove counterterm ambiguities.
\n\n
本文研究了通过从三维量子场论的三球配分函数中减去所有局域反项而得到的一个方案无关量。该量在共形不动点处与标准的$F$-定理不变量一致，并且在共形微扰理论下，对于任意相关标量算符的形变，在$O(g^2)$阶局部递减。然而，对$S^3$上自由有质量标量场的精确分析表明，这一“球自由能”插值函数在整个重整化群（RG）流中并非单调：它会先低于红外（IR）值，再回升至该值。因此，仅靠该反项相减后的热力学量无法构成一个全局单调的$F$-函数，其障碍源于用于消除局域模糊性的二阶微分算子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the search for a robust, scheme-independent $F$-function that monotonically decreases along renormalization group (RG) flows in $(2+1)$ dimensions, analogous to the $c$-theorem in 2D and the $a$-theorem in 4D. The $F$-theorem posits that the free energy on the three-sphere, $F = -\\log |Z_{S^3}|$, decreases from UV to IR fixed points. However, away from fixed points, ambiguities from local counterterms in the curved-space partition function complicate the definition of a monotonic interpolating quantity. This paper aims to construct a natural, counterterm-subtracted version of the sphere free energy and test whether it can serve as such a monotone $F$-function.
\n\n
动机源于在$(2+1)$维中寻找一个稳健、方案无关的$F$-函数，使其在重整化群（RG）流中单调递减，类似于二维的$c$-定理和四维的$a$-定理。$F$-定理指出，三球上的自由能$F = -\\log |Z_{S^3}|$从紫外（UV）到红外（IR）不动点单调递减。然而，在非不动点处，弯曲时空配分函数中的局域反项会导致定义模糊，阻碍构造一个单调的插值函数。本文旨在构建一个自然的、已扣除反项的球自由能，并检验其是否可作为这样的单调$F$-函数。

Method: The authors define a scheme-independent quantity by applying a specific second-order differential operator to the logarithm of the three-sphere partition function $Z_{S^3}(m)$, where $m$ is a mass deformation parameter. This operator removes all local counterterm contributions, yielding a finite, unambiguous “sphere-free-energy interpolant.” They first use conformal perturbation theory around a 3D CFT to show that this quantity decreases at $O(g^2)$ under a relevant scalar deformation. Then, they perform an exact calculation for the free massive scalar field on $S^3$, computing the full RG trajectory of the counterterm-subtracted free energy as a function of the dimensionless mass $mR$ (with $R$ the sphere radius).
\n\n
作者通过对三球配分函数$Z_{S^3}(m)$（其中$m$为质量形变参数）的对数施加一个特定的二阶微分算子，定义了一个方案无关量。该算子消除了所有局域反项贡献，从而得到一个有限且无歧义的“球自由能插值函数”。他们首先利用共形微扰理论，在三维共形场论（CFT）附近证明该量在相关标量形变下于$O(g^2)$阶递减；随后，对$S^3$上的自由有质量标量场进行精确计算，得到了扣除反项后的自由能作为无量纲质量$mR$（$R$为球半径）的完整RG轨迹。

Result: Conformal perturbation theory confirms that the counterterm-subtracted sphere free energy decreases at second order in the coupling for any relevant scalar deformation. However, the exact solution for the free massive scalar reveals non-monotonic behavior: the interpolating $F$-function first drops below its infrared asymptotic value as the mass increases from zero, reaches a minimum, and then rises back to the IR value as $mR \\to \\infty$. This demonstrates that the natural, counterterm-free quantity derived from $S^3$ thermodynamics is not globally monotonic along RG flows.
\n\n
共形微扰理论证实，对于任意相关标量形变，扣除反项后的球自由能在耦合常数的二阶处递减。然而，自由有质量标量场的精确解揭示了非单调行为：随着质量从零开始增加，插值$F$-函数首先降至其红外渐近值以下，达到一个极小值，然后在$mR \\to \\infty$时回升至红外值。这表明，从$S^3$热力学导出的这一自然且无反项模糊的量在整个RG流中并非全局单调。

Conclusion: The counterterm-subtracted sphere free energy, while locally decreasing near fixed points and matching the $F$-theorem invariant at endpoints, is not a valid monotone $F$-function over the entire RG trajectory. The failure of monotonicity is attributed to the structure of the second-order differential operator used to eliminate local ambiguities—this operator, though necessary for scheme independence, introduces non-monotonic features in the interpolating function. Thus, additional ingredients beyond simple thermodynamic subtraction are required to construct a true $F$-function in 3D.
\n\n
扣除反项后的球自由能虽然在不动点附近局部递减，并在端点处与$F$-定理不变量一致，但不能作为整个RG轨迹上的有效单调$F$-函数。单调性失效的原因在于用于消除局域模糊性的二阶微分算子的结构——该算子虽对实现方案无关性必不可少，却在插值函数中引入了非单调特征。因此，在三维中构造真正的$F$-函数需要超越简单热力学相减的额外机制。

Abstract: We study the natural scheme-independent quantity obtained from the three-sphere partition function of a $(2+1)$-dimensional quantum field theory by removing all local counterterm ambiguities. At conformal fixed points this quantity equals the standard $F$-theorem invariant. Conformal perturbation theory shows that it locally decreases at $O(g^2)$ under any relevant scalar deformation of a three-dimensional CFT. However, an exact analysis of the free massive scalar on $S^3$ shows that this sphere-free-energy interpolant is not monotone along the full renormalization-group flow: it dips below its infrared value and then returns to it. Thus the natural counterterm-subtracted quantity built from sphere thermodynamics is not, by itself, a monotone $F$-function. We trace the obstruction to the second-order differential operator required to eliminate the local ambiguities.

</details>


### [45] [A Swampland-modified Hod bound for charged black holes with exotic matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09816)
*S. Saoud,M. A Rbah,R. Sammani,E. H. Saidi,R. Ahl Laamara*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper investigates quasinormal modes (QNMs) of a charged black hole surrounded by quintessence and a cloud of strings using the Pade-averaged higher-order WKB method. It examines how the quintessence parameter $α$ and string cloud parameter $λ$ affect perturbation stability, oscillation frequency, black hole shadow, and energy emission. The study tests Hod’s conjecture, proposes a modified Hod bound, and links the Hawking temperature to the Swampland Distance Conjecture via scalar field excursion, identifying a consistent parameter region satisfying both bounds.
\n\n
本文利用Pade平均高阶WKB近似方法研究了被quintessence和弦云包围的带电黑洞的准正规模（QNMs）。文章探讨了quintessence参数$α$和弦云参数$λ$如何影响扰动的稳定性、振荡频率、黑洞阴影及能量辐射率。研究检验了Hod猜想，提出了修正的Hod界，并通过标量场位移将Hawking温度与Swampland距离猜想联系起来，识别出同时满足修正Hod界和Swampland约束的参数区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to understand how exotic matter fields—specifically quintessence (a dark energy candidate) and a cloud of strings (from cosmic string models)—influence black hole perturbations and thermodynamics. Additionally, testing fundamental conjectures like Hod’s bound and the Swampland Distance Conjecture in nontrivial gravitational backgrounds provides insights into the interplay between quantum gravity, black hole physics, and cosmological observations.
\n\n
动机源于理解奇异物质场——特别是quintessence（暗能量候选者）和弦云（来自宇宙弦模型）——如何影响黑洞扰动和热力学。此外，在非平凡引力背景下检验Hod界和Swampland距离猜想等基本猜想，有助于揭示量子引力、黑洞物理与宇宙学观测之间的相互作用。

Method: The authors employ the Pade-averaged higher-order WKB approximation to compute quasinormal frequencies of scalar perturbations around a Reissner–Nordström black hole modified by quintessence and a cloud of strings. They analyze the effective potential $V(r)$, extract decay rates and oscillation frequencies, and evaluate the black hole shadow radius and energy emission rate. Hod’s conjecture is tested by comparing $\\text{Im}(\\omega)$ with the Hawking temperature $T_H$. The scalar field excursion $\\Delta \\phi$ is related to $T_H$ to connect with the Swampland Distance Conjecture, leading to a modified inequality $|\\text{Im}(\\omega)| \\geq \\kappa T_H$, where $\\kappa$ depends on $α$ and $λ$.
\n\n
作者采用Pade平均高阶WKB近似方法计算受quintessence和弦云修正的Reissner–Nordström黑洞周围的标量扰动的准正规模频率。他们分析有效势$V(r)$，提取衰减率和振荡频率，并计算黑洞阴影半径和能量辐射率。通过比较$\\text{Im}(\\omega)$与Hawking温度$T_H$来检验Hod猜想。通过将标量场位移$\\Delta \\phi$与$T_H$关联以联系Swampland距离猜想，导出修正不等式$|\\text{Im}(\\omega)| \\geq \\kappa T_H$，其中$\\kappa$依赖于$α$和$λ$。

Result: The parameters $α$ (quintessence) and $λ$ (string cloud) significantly alter the effective potential, QNM frequencies, and decay rates. Depending on their values, Hod’s original bound $|\\text{Im}(\\omega)| \\geq \\pi T_H$ can be violated or reinforced. A modified Hod bound $|\\text{Im}(\\omega)| \\geq \\kappa(α,λ) T_H$ is established. The black hole shadow shrinks with increasing $α$ and $λ$, and the energy emission rate is correspondingly enhanced. A specific region in the $(α, λ)$ parameter space satisfies both the modified Hod bound and the Swampland Distance Conjecture constraint $\\Delta \\phi \\lesssim \\mathcal{O}(1) M_{\\text{Pl}}^{-1}$.
\n\n
参数$α$（quintessence）和$λ$（弦云）显著改变有效势、准正规模频率和衰减率。根据其取值，原始Hod界$|\\text{Im}(\\omega)| \\geq \\pi T_H$可能被破坏或加强。文章建立了修正的Hod界$|\\text{Im}(\\omega)| \\geq \\kappa(α,λ) T_H$。随着$α$和$λ$增大，黑洞阴影缩小，能量辐射率相应增强。在$(α, λ)$参数空间中存在一个特定区域，同时满足修正Hod界和Swampland距离猜想约束$\\Delta \\phi \\lesssim \\mathcal{O}(1) M_{\\text{Pl}}^{-1}$。

Conclusion: The interplay between quintessence, stringy corrections, and black hole perturbations leads to a refined understanding of quasinormal mode physics and its connection to quantum gravity constraints. The derived modified Hod bound, together with consistency with the Swampland Distance Conjecture, suggests that viable black hole solutions in effective field theories must respect both thermodynamic and swampland criteria, offering a bridge between theoretical bounds and potential observational signatures via shadow and emission properties.
\n\n
quintessence、弦论修正与黑洞扰动之间的相互作用深化了对准正规模物理及其与量子引力约束关联的理解。所导出的修正Hod界与Swampland距离猜想的一致性表明，有效场论中的可行黑洞解必须同时满足热力学和Swampland判据，通过阴影和辐射特性为理论界限与潜在观测信号之间架起桥梁。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the quasinormal modes (QNMs) of a charged black hole in the presence of both quintessence and a cloud of strings using the Pade-averaged higher-order WKB approximation method. We investigate the effect of the quintessence parameter $α$ and the cloud of strings parameter $λ$ on the stability as well as the oscillation frequency of perturbations.
  The validity of Hod's conjecture, which relates quasinormal frequencies to the black hole temperature, is tested throughout the physically allowed parameter space. Our results show that both the effective potential and the decay rate of perturbations depend on the values of $α$ and $λ$, leading to either enhancement or suppression of the conditions required to satisfy Hod's bound.
  Furthermore, we discuss how these parameters modify the black hole shadow and the corresponding energy emission rate, revealing correlations with observable signatures. Finally, we establish a connection with the Swampland Distance Conjecture by expressing the Hawking temperature in terms of the scalar field excursion.
  Our analysis leads to a modified Hod bound and identifies a region of parameter space in which both the modified Hod bound and the Swampland constraints are simultaneously satisfied, ensuring consistency between black hole thermodynamics, observational properties, and quantum gravity constraints.

</details>


### [46] [How Heavy Can Moduli Be?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09817)
*Mehrdad Mirbabayi,Giovanni Villadoro*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper presents numerical evidence that in Kaluza-Klein (KK) compactifications, a light scalar modulus field with $(m_{\rm sc}/m_{1KK})^2 \leq 4/3$ is required for the consistency of the 4d effective theory of KK gravitons, implying a universal bound on moduli masses and hence on the rigidity of compact manifold stabilization.
\n\n
本文通过数值证据表明，在Kaluza-Klein（KK）紧致化中，为保证4d KK引力子有效理论的一致性，必须存在一个轻的标量模场，其质量满足$(m_{\rm sc}/m_{1KK})^2 \leq 4/3$，这暗示了模场质量存在普适上限，从而限制了紧致流形稳定化的刚性程度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In Kaluza-Klein compactifications, moduli fields—scalar degrees of freedom parameterizing deformations of the internal compact manifold—are generically lighter than KK gravitons, but no universal mass bound has been established. The authors aim to investigate whether consistency conditions of the resulting 4d effective field theory impose such a bound, particularly in light of recent swampland conjectures and positivity constraints from scattering amplitudes.
\n\n
在Kaluza-Klein紧致化中，模场（即刻画内禀紧致流形形变的标量自由度）通常比KK引力子更轻，但尚未建立普适的质量界限。作者旨在探究由此产生的4d有效场论的一致性条件是否施加了此类界限，特别是结合近期关于Swampland猜想和散射振幅正定性约束的研究背景。

Method: The authors employ numerical studies of explicit KK compactifications, analyzing the spectrum of scalar moduli and KK graviton masses. They examine the low-energy 4d effective action obtained after dimensional reduction and assess its consistency—particularly unitarity and causality—by studying tree-level graviton-mediated scattering amplitudes involving external moduli. The ratio $(m_{\rm sc}/m_{1KK})^2$ is computed across various geometries, and a universal upper bound is inferred from the requirement that higher-dimension operators in the EFT do not violate positivity bounds derived from UV completeness.
\n\n
作者通过对显式的KK紧致化模型进行数值研究，分析标量模场与KK引力子的质量谱。他们考察维度约化后得到的低能4d有效作用量，并通过研究由外部模场参与的、引力子交换主导的树图散射振幅来评估其一致性（特别是幺正性和因果性）。在多种几何构型下计算$(m_{\rm sc}/m_{1KK})^2$之比，并从EFT中高维算子不违反由紫外完备性导出的正定性约束这一要求出发，推断出一个普适的上限。

Result: The numerical analysis reveals that whenever $(m_{\rm sc}/m_{1KK})^2 > 4/3$, the resulting 4d effective theory violates positivity constraints from dispersion relations, signaling inconsistency with a standard UV completion. Conversely, all consistent examples satisfy $(m_{\rm sc}/m_{1KK})^2 \leq 4/3$, suggesting this as a necessary condition for the validity of the EFT.
\n\n
数值分析表明，当$(m_{\rm sc}/m_{1KK})^2 > 4/3$时，所得4d有效理论会违反由色散关系导出的正定性约束，表明其与标准紫外完备性不相容。反之，所有自洽的例子均满足$(m_{\rm sc}/m_{1KK})^2 \leq 4/3$，表明这是EFT有效性的必要条件。

Conclusion: The work establishes a novel universal bound on the mass of moduli relative to the first KK mode in gravitational KK compactifications, interpreted as a limit on the rigidity of internal space stabilization. This result supports the idea that not all low-energy effective theories can be consistently coupled to quantum gravity, aligning with the Swampland Program.
\n\n
本工作确立了引力KK紧致化中标量模场质量相对于第一KK模态的一个新普适界限，可解释为对内空间稳定化刚性程度的限制。该结果支持“并非所有低能有效理论都能与量子引力自洽耦合”的观点，与Swampland Program相一致。

Abstract: In Kaluza-Klein (KK) compactification of gravitational theories, moduli fields, which are scalar fields associated to the deformations of the compact manifold, are typically lighter than the KK gravitons. However, a universal limit on their mass does not seem to exist. We provide numerical evidence that a light scalar particle, with mass ratio to the first KK graviton $(m_{\rm sc}/m_{1KK})^2 \leq {4/3}$, is necessary for the consistency of the $4d$ effective theory of KK gravitons. This can be interpreted as a limit on how rigidly the compact manifold can be stabilized.
