### [47] [Equilibrium Partition Function of Non-Relativistic CFTs in Harmonic Trap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09856)
*Eunwoo Lee*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper studies the equilibrium partition function of non-relativistic conformal field theories (NRCFTs) in harmonic traps using harmonic quantization. It identifies universal pole structures in $\\log Z$ at leading hydrodynamic order, with residues governed by the equation of state, and explores a less universal large-angular-momentum regime where centrifugal forces nearly cancel the trap.
\n\n
本文研究了谐振子势阱中非相对论共形场论（NRCFT）的平衡配分函数，采用谐振量子化方法。在流体动力学主导阶下，$\\log Z$ 表现出由物态方程决定的普适极点结构；在大角动量极限下，离心效应几乎抵消势阱，此时极点残差依赖于 $μ/T$ 和 $ω/T$，普适性减弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the thermodynamic structure of non-relativistic conformal field theories under harmonic confinement—a setup directly relevant to cold-atom experiments—by analyzing the analytic properties of the equilibrium partition function in the presence of rotation and trapping potentials.
\n\n
动机在于理解谐振子势阱中非相对论共形场论（NRCFT）的热力学结构——该设定直接关联冷原子实验——通过分析存在旋转与势阱时平衡配分函数的解析性质。

Method: The authors employ harmonic quantization to compute the equilibrium partition function $Z(ω, Ω_a, μ, T)$ for NRCFTs. They first perform a hydrodynamic expansion at leading order, linking $\\log Z$ to the equation of state. Then they examine the limit $Ω_a \\to ω$, where centrifugal effects dominate, using effective field theory and symmetry arguments to extract the pole structure and residue dependence.
\n\n
作者采用谐振量子化方法计算 NRCFT 的平衡配分函数 $Z(ω, Ω_a, μ, T)$。首先在主导阶进行流体动力学展开，将 $\\log Z$ 与物态方程联系起来；随后考察 $Ω_a \\to ω$ 极限（离心效应主导），利用有效场论和对称性论证提取极点结构及其残差依赖。

Result: At leading hydrodynamic order, $\\log Z$ has simple poles at $ω^2 = Ω_a^2$ with residues given by a universal function of $μ/T$. In the large-angular-momentum limit $Ω_a \\to ω$, the poles persist but the residues become non-universal, depending on both $μ/T$ and $ω/T$. Explicit results are provided for unitary Fermi gases in harmonic traps.
\n\n
在流体动力学主导阶，$\\log Z$ 在 $ω^2 = Ω_a^2$ 处具有简单极点，其残差由 $μ/T$ 的普适函数给出。在大角动量极限 $Ω_a \\to ω$ 下，极点依然存在，但残差失去普适性，依赖于 $μ/T$ 和 $ω/T$。文中给出了谐振子势阱中幺正费米气体的具体结果。

Conclusion: The equilibrium partition function of NRCFTs in harmonic traps encodes universal thermodynamic information through its pole structure in the hydrodynamic regime, while deviations from universality arise in the centrifugal-dominated limit. This provides a bridge between theoretical predictions and experimental observables in rotating cold-atom systems.
\n\n
谐振子势阱中 NRCFT 的平衡配分函数通过其在流体动力学区域的极点结构编码了普适热力学信息，而在离心力主导极限下普适性被打破。这为理论预测与旋转冷原子系统中的实验观测量之间建立了桥梁。

Abstract: We investigate the equilibrium partition function of non-relativistic conformal field theories in harmonic quantization. We first analyze the hydrodynamic regime and show that, at leading order, the partition function exhibits a universal structure determined by the equation of state: the logarithm of the partition function develops simple poles in $ω^2-Ω_a^2$, where $ω$ is the harmonic trapping frequency and $Ω_a$ are angular velocities acting as chemical potentials for angular momentum. The corresponding residue is determined by a single-variable function of $μ/T$, with $μ$ the particle-number chemical potential and $T$ the temperature.
  We then study the large-angular-momentum limit $Ω_a\toω$. In this regime centrifugal effects nearly cancel the trapping potential, and the logarithm of the partition function again exhibits simple poles in $ω^2-Ω_a^2$, but with a less universal residue depending separately on $μ/T$ and $ω/T$. As explicit examples we analyze superfluid systems realizable in cold-atom experiments, in particular fermions at unitarity confined in a harmonic trap.

</details>


### [48] [Dynamics and interaction of solitons in the BPS limit and their internal modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09887)
*S. Navarro-Obregón*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This thesis investigates soliton dynamics in 1D and 2D field theories—focusing on kinks, oscillons, vortices, and sphalerons—by constructing effective models via the collective coordinate method to capture essential internal and radiation degrees of freedom. Key advances include incorporating genuine radiation modes into collective coordinates, generalizing Samols' moduli space metric for Abelian-Higgs vortices with vibrational modes, discovering semi-BPS sphalerons, and proposing a dynamic stabilization mechanism driven by oscillatory internal modes.
\n\n
本论文研究了一维和二维场论中的孤子动力学，重点关注扭结（kinks）、振荡子（oscillons）、涡旋（vortices）和瞬子（sphalerons），通过集体坐标法（collective coordinate method）构建有效模型，以捕捉内部模和辐射模等关键自由度。主要进展包括：首次在集体坐标框架中引入真实的辐射模；通过引入振动自由度，推广了Abelian-Higgs模型中局部涡旋的Samols模空间度规；发现并分析了一类新的“半BPS瞬子”（semi-BPS sphalerons）；并提出了一种由振荡内部模驱动的动力学稳定机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Field theories describing solitons possess infinitely many degrees of freedom, making analytical treatment and predictive modeling difficult. Understanding the role of internal modes—especially their coupling to radiation and influence on stability—is crucial for capturing nontrivial soliton dynamics beyond static or rigid approximations. The motivation is to develop tractable yet faithful effective descriptions that bridge numerical simulations and analytical insight, particularly in lower-dimensional settings as a foundation for 3D generalizations.
\n\n
描述孤子的场论具有无穷多自由度，使得解析处理和预测建模极为困难。理解内部模（internal modes）的作用——特别是其与辐射的耦合及其对稳定性的影响——对于超越静态或刚性近似、捕捉非平凡孤子动力学至关重要。本研究旨在发展既简洁又忠实的有效描述，以连接数值模拟与解析洞察，尤其以低维模型为基础，为三维理论的推广奠定基础。

Method: The primary methodology is the collective coordinate method, extended to include both internal vibrational modes and genuine radiation modes—departing from traditional truncations that neglect radiative backreaction. Perturbative techniques complement this approach. For vortices in the Abelian-Higgs model, the moduli space approximation is generalized by incorporating vibrational degrees of freedom into Samols’ metric framework. Numerical simulations of the full field theory inform and validate the effective models.
\n\n
主要方法是集体坐标法（collective coordinate method），并加以扩展以同时包含内部振动模和真实的辐射模——突破了传统截断中忽略辐射反作用的局限。微扰技术作为补充手段。对于Abelian-Higgs模型中的涡旋，通过将振动自由度纳入Samols度规框架，推广了模空间（moduli space）近似。完整场论的数值模拟用于指导并验证有效模型。

Result: Key results include: (1) the first consistent inclusion of genuine radiation modes within the collective coordinate formalism; (2) a generalized Samols-type moduli space metric for local vortices that accounts for vibrational excitations; (3) the identification and analysis of a new class of solutions termed semi-BPS sphalerons; and (4) a detailed study showing that oscillatory internal modes can delay or suppress sphaleron decay, leading to a proposed dynamic stabilization mechanism shown to be robust across broader classes of models.
\n\n
主要成果包括：(1) 首次在集体坐标形式体系中一致地引入了真实的辐射模；(2) 推广了适用于局部涡旋的Samols型模空间度规，使其能描述振动激发；(3) 发现并分析了一类新解——“半BPS瞬子”（semi-BPS sphalerons）；(4) 详细研究表明，振荡内部模可延缓或抑制瞬子衰变，由此提出了一种动力学稳定机制，并证明该机制在更广泛的模型中具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: The thesis demonstrates that effective models incorporating both internal and radiative degrees of freedom provide a powerful framework for understanding complex soliton dynamics. The dynamic stabilization mechanism mediated by internal modes reveals a novel pathway to enhance soliton longevity, with potential implications for cosmological and high-energy physics scenarios where metastable topological configurations play a role. The methodologies developed offer a scalable approach toward analyzing three-dimensional solitonic systems.
\n\n
本论文表明，同时包含内部模与辐射模的有效模型为理解复杂孤子动力学提供了强大框架。由内部模介导的动力学稳定机制揭示了一种增强孤子寿命的新途径，对宇宙学和高能物理中涉及亚稳拓扑构型的场景具有潜在意义。所发展的方法为分析三维孤子系统提供了可扩展的路径。

Abstract: The main objective of this thesis has been to analyse soliton dynamics in detail, with special attention paid to the role of the internal modes associated with these configurations. Specifically, the thesis has focused on the study of one- and two-dimensional models, with the aim of developing a solid basis that can then be extended to the study in three-dimensional theories. This thesis concentrates on the study of kinks, oscillons, vortices, and sphalerons. Nevertheless, field theories constitute systems with an infinite number of degrees of freedom, which poses challenges both for obtaining analytical results and for predictive modeling. To address these challenges, this thesis employs the construction of effective models that retain the essential degrees of freedom required to capture the phenomenology observed in numerical simulations of the full theory, using the well-known collective coordinate method. In addition, other complementary mathematical tools, such as perturbative techniques, have also been employed. Among the main achievements of this doctoral thesis, it is worth highlighting the introduction, for the first time, of genuine radiation modes within the collective coordinate framework. Furthermore, a generalisation of Samols' moduli space metric for local vortices in the Abelian-Higgs model has been developed through the incorporation of vibrational degrees of freedom. Additionally, a new class of sphalerons that we have coined semi-BPS sphalerons has been identified and analysed. Finally, the role of oscillatory internal modes in the decay process of sphalerons has been studied in detail, leading to the proposal of a dynamic stabilisation mechanism. This mechanism has been further explained and extended to more general models, demonstrating the robustness and potential applicability of this phenomenon to physically relevant theories.

</details>


### [49] [One-loop mass corrections of interacting string states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09935)
*Lorenzo Grimaldi,Massimo Bianchi,Maurizio Firrotta*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper computes one-loop mass corrections for massive string states in the first Regge trajectory of the NS-NS sector in Type-II string theories, addressing both real (IR-divergent) and imaginary (decay width) parts using vertex operator constructions, elliptic function identities, and the $i\varepsilon$-prescription for modular integral regularization. Numerical results are provided up to level $N=4$.
\n\n
本文计算了Type-II弦理论NS-NS扇区中第一Regge轨迹上大质量弦态的单圈质量修正，通过顶点算符构造、椭圆函数性质以及弦理论中的$i\\varepsilon$-处方处理模积分的红外发散，同时提取了与树图衰变宽度相关的虚部。数值结果给出至能级$N=4$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Massive string states in the free theory exhibit exponential degeneracy, but become unstable once interactions (via non-zero string coupling $g_s$) are introduced. Understanding their decay and mass shifts at quantum level is essential for connecting perturbative string spectra to physical observables. The one-loop mass correction encodes both the decay width (imaginary part) and radiative corrections (real part), yet the latter suffers from IR divergences that require careful regularization—motivating a systematic study within controlled sectors like the first Regge trajectory in Type-II theories.
\n\n
自由弦理论中的大质量态具有指数级简并性，但一旦引入相互作用（即非零弦耦合$g_s$），这些态变得不稳定。在量子层面理解其衰变与质量移动对连接微扰弦谱与物理可观测量至关重要。单圈质量修正同时包含衰变宽度（虚部）和辐射修正（实部），但后者存在红外发散，需谨慎正则化——这促使在Type-II理论的第一Regge轨迹等可控扇区中开展系统研究。

Method: The authors focus on states in the first Regge trajectory of the NS-NS sector in Type-II string theory. They explicitly construct the corresponding vertex operators for levels up to $N=4$. Using properties of elliptic functions on the torus, they evaluate the worldsheet integral over the insertion point of the vertex operators in closed form. The remaining integral over the modular parameter $\\tau$ of the torus is IR-divergent; this is regularized via the $i\\varepsilon$-prescription adapted to string theory, which effectively shifts pole locations in the complex $\\tau$-plane. The imaginary part of the resulting amplitude is related to the tree-level two-particle decay rate via the optical theorem.
\n\n
作者聚焦于Type-II弦理论NS-NS扇区中第一Regge轨迹上的态。他们显式构造了直至能级$N=4$的相应顶点算符。利用环面上椭圆函数的性质，以闭合形式计算了顶点算符插入点的世界面积分。剩余的环面模参数$\\tau$积分存在红外发散，通过弦理论中的$i\\varepsilon$-处方进行正则化，该方法有效移动了复$\\tau$平面上的极点位置。所得振幅的虚部通过光学定理与树图双粒子衰变率相关联。

Result: Closed-form expressions for the one-loop mass corrections (both real and imaginary parts) are obtained for NS-NS states in the first Regge trajectory up to level $N=4$. The imaginary part matches the expected decay width into two lower-mass states at tree level. The real part, after $i\\varepsilon$-regularization of the modular integral, yields finite numerical values for the mass shift, demonstrating the feasibility of renormalizing IR divergences in this context.
\n\n
获得了第一Regge轨迹上NS-NS态直至能级$N=4$的单圈质量修正（实部与虚部）的闭合表达式。虚部与树图下衰变为两个低质量态的预期衰变宽度一致。实部在通过$i\\varepsilon$-处方正则化模积分后，给出了有限的质量移动数值结果，证明了在此背景下重整化红外发散的可行性。

Conclusion: The study provides a concrete framework for computing quantum corrections to massive string state masses, handling both decay widths and IR-divergent radiative corrections in a controlled setting. The use of the $i\\varepsilon$-prescription in the modular domain offers a viable regularization scheme, and the explicit results up to $N=4$ lay groundwork for higher-level analyses and potential connections to effective field theory or black hole physics via the string spectrum.
\n\n
本研究为计算大质量弦态质量的量子修正提供了一个具体框架，在可控设定下同时处理衰变宽度与红外发散的辐射修正。在模空间中使用$i\\varepsilon$-处方提供了一种可行的正则化方案，而直至$N=4$的显式结果为更高能级的分析以及通过弦谱与有效场论或黑洞物理的潜在联系奠定了基础。

Abstract: The free string spectrum is highly degenerate, with a degeneracy that grows exponentially with the mass. Turning on a non-vanishing string coupling $g_s$ introduces interactions, rendering massive string states unstable and allowing them to decay into lower-mass states, with mixing constrained by Lorentz invariance. This behavior is expected already at one-loop level. The imaginary part of the one-loop mass correction is related to the width of the decay into two lower-mass states at tree level, whereas the real part is generally IR-divergent and needs regularization and renormalization. The analysis simplifies for states in the first Regge trajectory. In particular, we consider the one-loop mass corrections for these states in the NS-NS sector of Type-II string theories. We explicitly construct the related vertex operators and exploit the properties of elliptic functions in order to obtain a closed form expression for the integral over the insertion point. We further regularize the divergences of the integral over the modular parameter of the torus by means of the $i\varepsilon$-prescription in string theory. Finally we extract numerical results for the mass correction up to level $N=4$.

</details>


### [50] [Generalised Cluster Adjacency for Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09965)
*Mattia Capuano,Livia Ferro,Tomasz Lukowski,Alessandro Palazio,Yao-Qi Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper investigates the cluster algebraic structure of wavefunction coefficients in massless scalar theories in de Sitter space, introducing a stronger "ordered single cluster condition" for path graphs and extending cluster-like structures to general tree graphs via tubes and tubings.
\n\n
本文研究了de Sitter宇宙学中无质量标量理论的波函数系数的cluster代数结构，针对路径图引入了更强的“有序单cluster条件”，并通过tube和tubing将类似的cluster结构推广到一般树图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to uncover deeper algebraic structures—specifically cluster algebras—that govern the analytic properties of cosmological wavefunction coefficients, thereby enabling more powerful bootstrap methods beyond standard locality and unitarity constraints.
\n\n
动机是揭示支配宇宙学波函数系数解析性质的更深层代数结构（特别是cluster代数），从而超越标准的局域性和幺正性约束，实现更强大的bootstrap方法。

Method: The authors analyze the symbol alphabet of wavefunction coefficients for the $n$-site path graph $P_n$, identifying that all letters in each symbol word belong to a single cluster of the $A_{2n-3}$ cluster algebra, with additional ordering constraints. They formalize this as the "ordered single cluster condition." For general tree graphs, they use combinatorial structures called tubes and tubings to define analogous cluster-like algebras.
\n\n
作者分析了$n$-点路径图$P_n$的波函数系数的symbol字母表，发现每个symbol词中的所有字母都属于$A_{2n-3}$ cluster代数中的同一个cluster，并满足额外的顺序约束。他们将此形式化为“有序单cluster条件”。对于一般树图，他们利用称为tube和tubing的组合结构来定义类似的cluster代数。

Result: The paper establishes that wavefunction coefficients for path graphs obey the ordered single cluster condition—a stricter version of cluster adjacency—and demonstrates that tree graphs admit a cluster-like structure based on tubes and tubings, enabling a symbol bootstrap approach for cosmological correlators.
\n\n
本文证明了路径图的波函数系数满足有序单cluster条件——一种比cluster邻接更强的约束——并表明树图可通过tube和tubing支持类似的cluster结构，从而为宇宙学关联函数提供symbol bootstrap方法。

Conclusion: The results suggest that cluster algebraic structures, particularly through the ordered single cluster condition and tubing-based generalizations, provide a powerful organizing principle for wavefunction coefficients in de Sitter cosmology, opening new avenues for the Cosmological Bootstrap program.
\n\n
结果表明，cluster代数结构（特别是通过有序单cluster条件及基于tubing的推广）为de Sitter宇宙学中的波函数系数提供了强有力的组织原则，为Cosmological Bootstrap计划开辟了新路径。

Abstract: In this paper we study the cluster algebraic properties of wavefunction coefficients for massless scalar theories in de Sitter cosmology. We show that the symbol of the wavefunction coefficient of the $n$-site path graph $P_n$ obeys a generalisation of cluster adjacency, where all letters in a given word belong to the same cluster of an $A_{2n-3}$ algebra, with certain additional constraints on the order of the letters. We call this property the ordered single cluster condition, and provide its physical interpretation. This condition is stronger than the usual cluster adjacency obeyed by neighbouring letters, and imposes stronger constraints for the symbol bootstrap. We also show how any tree graph satisfies a cluster-like structure in terms of tubes and tubings on the underlying graph, which allows for a similar bootstrap approach.

</details>


### [51] [Does hot QCD have a conformal manifold in the chiral limit?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09977)
*Shi Chen,Aleksey Cherman,Robert D. Pisarski*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: Recent lattice QCD results indicate a second-order chiral phase transition for $N_f \ge 2$ massless flavors. The paper uses 't Hooft anomaly matching at general imaginary baryon chemical potential $θ_B = iμ_B/T$ to constrain possible critical CFT descriptions, identifying only three minimal scenarios. The favored scenario for $N_f \ge 3$ (and possibly $N_f = 2$) involves a conformal manifold of $θ_B$-dependent universality classes with an exactly marginal operator tied to baryon density, going beyond standard Ginzburg-Landau theory.
\n\n
近期格点QCD结果表明，对于 $N_f \\ge 2$ 个无质量味，手征相变是二级的。本文利用在一般虚重子化学势 $θ_B = iμ_B/T$ 下的't Hooft反常匹配来约束可能的临界CFT描述，仅留下三种最小情形。对于 $N_f \\ge 3$（可能也包括 $N_f = 2$）最合理的情形超越了Ginzburg-Landau理论，其特征是一个依赖于 $θ_B$ 的共形流形（conformal manifold），其中包含一个与重子密度相关的精确边际算符（exactly marginal operator）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lattice simulations show that the finite-temperature chiral phase transition in QCD with $N_f \ge 2$ massless quark flavors is second-order, implying an underlying critical point described by a conformal field theory (CFT). However, the precise nature of this CFT remains unclear. The authors aim to narrow down viable CFT candidates by exploiting symmetry and anomaly constraints, particularly the 't Hooft anomaly associated with chiral symmetry and baryon number at nonzero imaginary baryon chemical potential $θ_B$.
\n\n
格点模拟表明，在具有 $N_f \\ge 2$ 个无质量夸克味的QCD中，有限温度下手征相变是二级的，这意味着存在一个由共形场论（CFT）描述的临界点。然而，该CFT的确切性质尚不清楚。作者旨在通过利用对称性和反常约束（特别是与手征对称性和重子数相关的't Hooft反常，在非零虚重子化学势 $θ_B$ 下）来缩小可行的CFT候选者范围。

Method: The authors apply 't Hooft anomaly matching across the chiral phase transition at general $θ_B = iμ_B/T$. This anomaly, which involves the chiral symmetry and the $U(1)_B$ baryon symmetry, must be reproduced by any candidate infrared CFT. By analyzing how the anomaly constrains the possible operator content and global symmetries of the CFT, they classify consistent scenarios. They particularly focus on whether the CFT can support a conformal manifold parameterized by $θ_B$, requiring an exactly marginal operator whose coupling is conjugate to $θ_B$ (i.e., related to baryon density).
\n\n
作者在一般的 $θ_B = iμ_B/T$ 下应用手征相变处的't Hooft反常匹配。该反常涉及手征对称性和 $U(1)_B$ 重子对称性，任何候选的红外CFT都必须重现这一反常。通过分析该反常如何约束CFT可能的算符内容和整体对称性，他们对自洽的情形进行了分类。他们特别关注CFT是否能支持一个由 $θ_B$ 参数化的共形流形（conformal manifold），这要求存在一个精确边际算符（exactly marginal operator），其耦合与 $θ_B$ 共轭（即与重子密度相关）。

Result: The 't Hooft anomaly at general $θ_B$ severely restricts possible CFT descriptions, leaving only three minimal consistent scenarios. For $N_f \ge 3$, the most plausible scenario is one where the critical theory is not described by a conventional Ginzburg-Landau paradigm but instead possesses a conformal manifold: a continuous family of CFTs labeled by $θ_B$, connected by an exactly marginal deformation associated with the baryon density operator. This implies the critical exponents depend continuously on $θ_B$. The same scenario may also apply to $N_f = 2$.
\n\n
在一般 $θ_B$ 下的't Hooft反常严重限制了可能的CFT描述，仅留下三种最小的自洽情形。对于 $N_f \\ge 3$，最合理的情形是：临界理论不由传统的Ginzburg-Landau范式描述，而是拥有一个共形流形（conformal manifold）——即一族由 $θ_B$ 标记的连续CFT，通过一个与重子密度算符相关的精确边际形变（exactly marginal deformation）相互连接。这意味着临界指数会随 $θ_B$ 连续变化。同一情形也可能适用于 $N_f = 2$。

Conclusion: The interplay between 't Hooft anomalies and the physics of the QCD chiral phase transition at nonzero imaginary chemical potential provides a powerful tool to classify possible critical theories. The analysis points toward a non-Ginzburg-Landau criticality for $N_f \ge 3$, characterized by a $θ_B$-dependent conformal manifold with an exactly marginal operator dual to baryon density. This suggests a richer critical structure than previously assumed and offers concrete predictions for lattice studies at imaginary chemical potential.
\n\n
't Hooft反常与非零虚化学势下QCD手征相变物理之间的相互作用，为分类可能的临界理论提供了强有力的工具。分析指出，对于 $N_f \\ge 3$，临界行为超越了Ginzburg-Landau范式，其特征是一个依赖于 $θ_B$ 的共形流形（conformal manifold），其中包含一个与重子密度对偶的精确边际算符（exactly marginal operator）。这表明临界结构比先前假设的更为丰富，并为在虚化学势下的格点研究提供了具体的预测。

Abstract: Recent lattice evidence suggests the chiral phase transition in QCD is second-order for $N_f \ge 2$ massless flavors. We constrain CFT descriptions of a critical line in temperature $T$ and imaginary baryon chemical potential $θ_B = iμ_B/T$. An 't Hooft anomaly at general $θ_B$ constrains the transition even at $θ_B = 0$, leaving only three minimal scenarios. The best-motivated scenario for $N_f\ge3$, and perhaps also $N_f = 2$, is beyond Ginzburg-Landau, featuring a conformal manifold of $θ_B$-dependent universality classes with an exactly marginal operator related to baryon density.

</details>

### [52] [Binary Black Holes population synthesis based on the current LVK observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08785)
*Mehdi El Bouhaddouti,Ilias Cholis,Muhsin Aljaf*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper analyzes LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) gravitational-wave data from 2015–2024 to test whether binary black hole (BBH) mergers originate solely from first-generation stellar collapse (power-law mass distribution), or if a significant fraction arises from hierarchical mergers (second-generation black holes) and/or primordial black holes (PBHs). Strong statistical evidence ($-2\Delta \ln \mathcal{L} = -150$, $\ln \mathrm{BF} = 71$) favors a mixed population model combining power-law and hierarchical merger components, with a roughly one-to-one ratio between them. A third PBH component is also statistically preferred.
\n\n
本文分析了2015–2024年LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA（LVK）引力波数据，以检验双黑洞（BBH）并合事件是否仅源于第一代恒星坍缩（幂律质量分布），还是部分来自等级并合（第二代黑洞）和/或原初黑洞（PBHs）。统计证据强烈支持混合种群模型（$-2\Delta \ln \mathcal{L} = -150$，$\ln \mathrm{BF} = 71$），该模型结合了幂律分布与等级并合成分，两者比例约为1:1。加入第三种原初黑洞（PBH）成分也受到统计偏好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to understand the astrophysical origins of the growing catalog of binary black hole mergers detected by LVK. Specifically, the observation of very massive black holes challenges models based solely on first-generation stellar collapse, which predicts a power-law mass distribution with an upper mass gap. Hierarchical mergers in dense environments (e.g., globular clusters, AGN disks) or primordial black holes could explain these outliers, necessitating a population-level statistical test to disentangle formation channels.
\n\n
动机源于理解LVK探测到的日益增长的双黑洞并合事件的天体物理起源。特别是，超大质量黑洞的观测对仅基于第一代恒星坍缩的模型构成挑战，后者预测具有上限质量间隙的幂律质量分布。密集环境（如球状星团、活动星系核盘）中的等级并合或原初黑洞（PBHs）可能解释这些异常值，因此需要在种群层面进行统计检验以区分不同形成通道。

Method: The authors perform a Bayesian model comparison using the full LVK BBH catalog (2015–early 2024). They construct three population models: (1) a single power-law mass distribution representing first-generation (1g) black holes from stellar collapse; (2) a two-component mixture of 1g black holes (power-law) and second-generation (2g) black holes from hierarchical mergers, whose mass distribution peaks at higher masses (~35–50 $M_\odot$); and (3) a three-component model adding a primordial black hole (PBH) population merging in dark matter halos or the intergalactic medium. They compute log-likelihood differences ($-2\Delta \ln \mathcal{L}$) and log-Bayes factors ($\ln \mathrm{BF}$) to compare model evidences.
\n\n
作者使用完整的LVK双黑洞目录（2015–2024年初）进行贝叶斯模型比较。他们构建了三种种群模型：(1) 单一幂律质量分布，代表来自恒星坍缩的第一代（1g）黑洞；(2) 两成分混合模型，包含1g黑洞（幂律分布）和来自等级并合的第二代（2g）黑洞，其质量分布峰值位于更高质量处（~35–50 $M_\odot$）；(3) 三成分模型，额外加入在暗物质晕或星系际介质中并合的原初黑洞（PBH）种群。通过计算对数似然差（$-2\Delta \ln \mathcal{L}$）和对数贝叶斯因子（$\ln \mathrm{BF}$）来比较模型证据。

Result: The analysis finds strong statistical preference for the two-component model over the single power-law model, with $-2\Delta \ln \mathcal{L} = -150$ and $\ln \mathrm{BF} = 71$, indicating decisive evidence for hierarchical mergers. The inferred ratio of 1g (power-law) to 2g (hierarchical) black holes is approximately 1:1. Furthermore, extending to a three-component model that includes a PBH population is also statistically favored, suggesting that PBHs may contribute non-negligibly to the observed merger rate.
\n\n
分析发现两成分模型相比单一幂律模型具有强烈统计偏好，$-2\Delta \ln \mathcal{L} = -150$ 且 $\ln \mathrm{BF} = 71$，表明存在等级并合的决定性证据。推断出的第一代（幂律）与第二代（等级）黑洞比例约为1:1。此外，包含原初黑洞（PBH）种群的三成分模型也受到统计偏好，表明PBHs可能对观测到的并合率有不可忽略的贡献。

Conclusion: The observed population of binary black hole mergers cannot be explained by first-generation stellar-origin black holes alone. A significant fraction—comparable in number—must originate from hierarchical mergers, likely occurring in dense dynamical environments. Additionally, the data provide tentative support for a subpopulation of primordial black holes contributing to the merger events. These findings have profound implications for understanding black hole formation channels, the role of dense stellar systems, and the potential cosmological origin of some compact objects.
\n\n
观测到的双黑洞并合种群无法仅由第一代恒星起源黑洞解释。相当大一部分（数量级相当）必须源于等级并合，很可能发生在致密动力学环境中。此外，数据为原初黑洞（PBHs）子种群对并合事件的贡献提供了初步支持。这些发现对理解黑洞形成通道、致密星系统的作用以及某些致密天体的宇宙学起源具有深远意义。

Abstract: The ongoing observations from ground based gravitational-wave observatories have led to the detection of more than a hundred merger events between black holes. We use the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) observations from 2015 to early 2024, to test the population synthesis of these merging binaries; which will allow us to probe the formation mechanisms and environments of these black holes. We test if the current sample of binary black holes can be explained only by the merger of black holes coming from the collapse of the cores of massive stars, i.e. as just first generation black holes merging with each other. Those black holes' masses will roughly follow a power-law distribution. We also test if in addition to the merger between first generation black holes, there is evidence for a second population of black hole binaries in which at least one the binaries' members is the product of an earlier merger between black holes. These binaries are typically referred to as signals of hierarchical mergers. Such a population can possibly explain the observation of very massive black hole binaries by the LVK collaboration. We find that the LVK observations give a statistical preference in log-likelihood of up to $- 2 Δln\mathcal{L} = -150$ or in log-Bayes factor of up to $ln\textrm{BF} = 71$, for the full sample of black hole binaries originating from a combination of black holes following a power-law distribution and black holes from hierarchical mergers. The ratio of black holes following a power-law mass-distribution to a mass-distribution expected from hierarchical mergers is found to be as high as one-to-one. We also consider that some of the LVK black hole merging binaries are the result of primordial black holes (PBHs), merging inside dark matter halos and in the intergalactic medium. Adding a third population is preferred. [abridged]

</details>


### [53] [Detecting Axion-like particles using Cosmic Variance Cancellation with CMB and Radio surveys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08808)
*Harsh Mehta,Anaya Dixit,Suvodip Mukherjee,Joseph Silk*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper proposes using Cosmic Variance Cancellation (CVC) with multi-frequency observations from the Simons Observatory (SO) and Square Kilometre Array (SKA) to significantly improve constraints on axion-like particles (ALPs) by exploiting the spectral dependence of CMB photon–ALP resonant conversion in galaxy clusters. The method leverages cross-correlations between microwave and radio bands to suppress cosmic variance, yielding tighter bounds on the ALP signal—especially for low-mass ALPs—and offers a robust way to validate or reject false detections based on frequency behavior.
\n\n
本文提出利用宇宙方差消除（Cosmic Variance Cancellation, CVC）方法，结合Simons Observatory（SO）和Square Kilometre Array（SKA）的多频段观测，通过探测星系团中CMB光子与轴子类粒子（ALP）共振转换的谱依赖性，显著提升对ALP的限制。该方法利用微波与射电波段之间的互相关以抑制宇宙方差，尤其对低质量ALP信号约束更强，并可通过不同频段中信号的频率行为有效排除虚假探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Axion-like particles (ALPs) are well-motivated dark matter candidates that can induce distortions in the CMB spectrum via resonant photon–ALP conversion in the magnetic fields of galaxy clusters. Traditional searches using auto-spectra from single experiments suffer from cosmic variance, limiting sensitivity—particularly for low-mass ALPs ($m_a \sim 10^{-14} \, \mathrm{eV}$) whose signals peak at radio frequencies. The blackbody nature of the CMB implies that such conversions imprint a characteristic spectral signature across both microwave and radio bands, motivating a multi-frequency cross-correlation strategy to cancel cosmic variance and enhance detection power.
\n\n
轴子类粒子（ALP）是理论上有充分动机的暗物质候选者，其在星系团磁场中可引发CMB光子的共振转换，从而在CMB谱上留下畸变信号。传统基于单实验自谱（auto-spectra）的搜寻受限于宇宙方差，尤其对低质量ALP（$m_a \sim 10^{-14} \, \mathrm{eV}$）——其信号在射电波段最强——灵敏度不足。CMB的黑体谱特性表明，此类转换会在微波与射电波段留下具有特征谱形的信号，这促使作者采用多频段互相关策略以消除宇宙方差，提升探测能力。

Method: The authors employ Cosmic Variance Cancellation (CVC), a technique that exploits the fact that the same underlying large-scale structure (here, galaxy clusters) sources ALP-induced distortions observed in multiple frequency bands. By cross-correlating maps from SO (microwave) and SKA (radio), they construct estimators for the normalized ALP signal ratio that are insensitive to sample variance. The analysis assumes knowledge of cluster electron density and magnetic field profiles, and models the frequency-dependent conversion probability $P_{\gamma \leftrightarrow a}(\nu, z)$, which scales with $g_{a\gamma}^2$ and depends on the ALP mass $m_a$. Forecasts are performed for clusters up to redshift $z = 1$, comparing the statistical uncertainty in the inferred signal ratio using auto-spectra alone versus CVC-enhanced cross-spectra.
\n\n
作者采用宇宙方差消除（CVC）技术，利用同一底层大尺度结构（此处为星系团）在多个频段中产生的ALP诱导畸变信号具有共同起源这一事实。通过交叉关联SO（微波）与SKA（射电）的天图，构建对归一化ALP信号比的估计量，使其对样本方差不敏感。分析中假设已知星系团的电子密度与磁场轮廓，并建模频率依赖的转换概率 $P_{\gamma \leftrightarrow a}(\nu, z)$，该概率正比于 $g_{a\gamma}^2$ 并依赖于ALP质量 $m_a$。研究对红移 $z = 1$ 以内的星系团进行预测，比较仅使用自谱与采用CVC增强的互谱在推断信号比时的统计不确定性。

Result: Using auto-spectra from galaxy clusters up to $z = 1$, the standard deviation in the inferred normalized ALP signal ratio is $5.9 \times 10^{-2}$ for $m_a = 10^{-14} \, \mathrm{eV}$. With CVC applied to cross-correlations between SO and SKA bands, this improves dramatically to $1.0 \times 10^{-2}$. The gain arises because CVC cancels the dominant cosmic variance contribution, allowing the measurement to be limited by instrumental noise rather than sample variance. The method is particularly effective for low-mass ALPs, whose conversion signals are stronger and spectrally distinct across microwave and radio frequencies.
\n\n
对于质量 $m_a = 10^{-14} \, \mathrm{eV}$ 的ALP，仅使用红移 $z = 1$ 以内星系团的自谱时，归一化ALP信号比的推断标准差为 $5.9 \times 10^{-2}$；而应用CVC对SO与SKA波段进行互相关后，该值显著改善至 $1.0 \times 10^{-2}$。性能提升源于CVC消除了主导的宇宙方差贡献，使测量精度由仪器噪声而非样本方差所限制。该方法对低质量ALP尤为有效，因其转换信号更强且在微波与射电频段具有显著不同的谱形。

Conclusion: Cosmic Variance Cancellation provides a powerful and universal probe of ALP-induced CMB spectral distortions by leveraging their unique frequency dependence across microwave and radio observations. This approach not only enhances sensitivity—particularly for low-mass ALPs—but also offers a consistency test: any claimed ALP detection must reproduce the predicted spectral shape across bands, thereby guarding against false positives. Future joint analyses of SO and SKA data could thus deliver stringent new constraints on the photon–ALP coupling $g_{a\gamma}$ and ALP mass $m_a$.
\n\n
宇宙方差消除（CVC）通过利用ALP诱导CMB谱畸变在微波与射电波段的独特频率依赖性，提供了一种强大且普适的探测手段。该方法不仅显著提升了灵敏度（尤其对低质量ALP），还提供了自洽性检验：任何声称的ALP探测都必须在不同频段复现预测的谱形，从而有效防范假阳性。因此，未来对SO与SKA数据的联合分析有望对光子–ALP耦合常数 $g_{a\gamma}$ 和ALP质量 $m_a$ 给出严格的新限制。

Abstract: Axions and axion-like particles (ALPs) arise naturally in many extensions of the Standard Model and are among the well-motivated candidates for dark matter. In the presence of magnetic fields of galaxy clusters, Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) photons can convert to ALPs, with the efficiency of the process governed by the cluster electron density and magnetic field profiles, the photon--ALP coupling strength ($g_{aγ}$), as well as the frequency ($ν$) of the photon at the redshift of the cluster. The CMB blackbody spectrum suggests that this resonant conversion also takes place at radio wavelengths, following the spectral behaviour of the ALP distortion signal. This opens a new window to search for ALPs using cosmic variance cancellation (CVC), with multi-frequency tracers of the same phenomenon in CMB photon--ALP resonant conversion. The constraints on the ALP signal ratios from different combinations of microwave and radio bands of the Simons Observatory (SO) and the Square Kilometre Array (SKA) can be significantly improved using CVC compared to the case of using auto-only spectra from the two experiments. With the large number of galaxy clusters that will be observed by SO and SKA, we will be able to obtain much more information using CVC, especially for low-mass ALPs with stronger signals. Using the auto-only spectra from galaxy clusters up to redshift $z = 1$ for inference of the normalized ratio parameter, we obtain a standard deviation of $5.9 \times 10^{-2}$ for an ALP mass $m_a = 10^{-14} \, \mathrm{eV}$, which improves to $1 \times 10^{-2}$ using CVC. This method provides a universal probe of the ALP distortion signal using its spectral dependence and can also invalidate false detections of the ALP signal based on its frequency behaviour in different bands.

</details>


### [54] [Statistical consistency of sign-switching vacuum energy with cosmological observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09270)
*Sehjal Khandelwal,Abraão J. S. Capistrano,Suresh Kumar*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper evaluates consistency between cosmological datasets in $\\Lambda$CDM and its sign-switching extension $\\Lambda_{\\rm s}$CDM using both Gaussian and exact non-Gaussian diagnostics. It finds that Gaussian tension metrics can overstate inconsistencies, while non-Gaussian parameter shifts reveal strong agreement between CMB and BAO data. $\\Lambda_{\\rm s}$CDm slightly improves geometric compatibility at intermediate redshifts, but reduced parameter tensions do not guarantee better predictive performance—underscoring the need for exact, non-Gaussian, and predictive consistency tests.
\n\n
本文使用高斯和精确非高斯一致性诊断方法，评估了 $\\Lambda$CDM 及其符号切换扩展模型 $\\Lambda_{\\rm s}$CDM 中不同宇宙学数据集之间的一致性。研究发现，常用的高斯张力指标在结合宽泛的非高斯后验与紧约束数据集时会显著夸大不一致性；而精确的非高斯参数偏移则表明 CMB 与 BAO 观测在两种模型中高度一致。$\\Lambda_{\\rm s}$CDM 在中等红移处略微改善了几何兼容性，但参数层面张力的降低并不必然意味着预测一致性的提升——这凸显了采用精确、非高斯且具有预测性的诊断方法对稳健评估宇宙学模型一致性的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Current cosmological analyses often rely on Gaussian approximations to quantify tensions between datasets, which may be inadequate when posteriors are significantly non-Gaussian. This can lead to misleading conclusions about model consistency or the need for new physics. The authors aim to address this by employing exact non-Gaussian consistency diagnostics and evaluating predictive adequacy in late-time observables within both standard $\\Lambda$CDM and its $\\Lambda_{\\rm s}$CDM extension.
\n\n
当前宇宙学分析常依赖高斯近似来量化数据集之间的张力，但在后验分布显著非高斯的情况下，这种做法可能不充分，从而导致关于模型一致性或新物理需求的误导性结论。作者旨在通过引入精确的非高斯一致性诊断方法，并在标准 $\\Lambda$CDM 及其 $\\Lambda_{\\rm s}$CDM 扩展模型中评估晚期可观测量的预测充分性，以解决这一问题。

Method: The authors constrain $\\Lambda$CDM and $\\Lambda_{\\rm s}$CDM using a combination of CMB data (Planck, ACT, SPT), BAO measurements from DESI DR2, and low-redshift Type Ia supernovae from PantheonPlus+SH0ES. They compare Gaussian tension estimators (e.g., differences in best-fit parameters normalized by uncertainties) with exact non-Gaussian diagnostics based on full posterior distributions. Additionally, they assess predictive consistency by examining how well early-universe-inferred parameters predict late-time geometric probes.
\n\n
作者利用 CMB 数据（Planck、ACT、SPT）、DESI DR2 的 BAO 测量以及 PantheonPlus+SH0ES 的低红移 Ia 型超新星数据，对 $\\Lambda$CDM 和 $\\Lambda_{\\rm s}$CDM 模型进行约束。他们将高斯张力估计量（例如，以不确定性归一化的最佳拟合参数差异）与基于完整后验分布的精确非高斯诊断方法进行比较。此外，他们还通过检验早期宇宙推断的参数对晚期几何探针的预测能力，来评估模型的预测一致性。

Result: Gaussian tension metrics are shown to overestimate inconsistencies when applied to combinations of broad non-Gaussian posteriors and tightly constrained datasets. In contrast, exact non-Gaussian parameter shift diagnostics indicate excellent agreement between CMB and BAO data in both $\\Lambda$CDM and $\\Lambda_{\\rm s}$CDM. The $\\Lambda_{\\rm s}$CDM model yields modest improvements in geometric compatibility at intermediate redshifts, but this does not translate into significantly better predictive consistency for late-time observables.
\n\n
研究表明，当应用于宽泛的非高斯后验与紧约束数据集的组合时，高斯张力指标会高估不一致性。相比之下，精确的非高斯参数偏移诊断显示，在 $\\Lambda$CDM 和 $\\Lambda_{\\rm s}$CDM 两种模型中，CMB 与 BAO 数据之间具有极佳的一致性。$\\Lambda_{\\rm s}$CDM 模型在中等红移处对几何兼容性有轻微改善，但这并未转化为对晚期可观测量显著更优的预测一致性。

Conclusion: Robust assessment of cosmological model consistency requires moving beyond Gaussian approximations to include exact, non-Gaussian, and predictive diagnostics. While extensions like $\\Lambda_{\\rm s}$CDM may alleviate some parameter-level tensions, such improvements do not automatically ensure better predictive performance. Therefore, consistency evaluations must incorporate both statistical rigor and predictive validity across cosmic epochs.
\n\n
对宇宙学模型一致性的稳健评估必须超越高斯近似，纳入精确、非高斯且具有预测性的诊断方法。尽管像 $\\Lambda_{\\rm s}$CDM 这样的扩展模型可能缓解某些参数层面的张力，但此类改进并不自动保证预测性能的提升。因此，一致性评估必须同时兼顾统计严谨性与跨宇宙时期的预测有效性。

Abstract: We assess dataset agreement and late-time predictive adequacy in $Λ$CDM and its sign-switching extension, $Λ_{\rm s}$CDM, using a suite of Gaussian and exact non-Gaussian consistency diagnostics. Both models are constrained with cosmic microwave background measurements from Planck, ACT, and SPT, baryon acoustic oscillation data from DESI DR2, and low-redshift Type Ia supernova data from PantheonPlus+SH0ES. We find that commonly used Gaussian tension metrics can significantly overstate inconsistencies when broad, non-Gaussian posteriors are combined with tightly constrained datasets. In contrast, the exact non-Gaussian parameter shift indicates excellent consistency between CMB and BAO observations in both models. The $Λ_{\rm s}$CDM extension modestly improves geometric compatibility at intermediate redshifts, although reductions in parameter-level tension do not necessarily imply improved predictive consistency. These results highlight the importance of exact, non-Gaussian, and predictive diagnostics for robust assessments of cosmological model consistency.

</details>


### [55] [Constraints on Neutrino Mass with Void Weak Lensing Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09278)
*Wenshuo Xu,Cheng Zhao,Chen Su,Huanyuan Shan,Yu Liu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper demonstrates that the void-shear cross-correlation (void lensing) provides a competitive and independent probe of the total neutrino mass $M_\\nu$, yielding constraints of $\\sigma(M_\\nu)=0.096\\,{\\rm eV}$ without shape noise and $\\sigma(M_\\nu)=0.340\\,{\\rm eV}$ with Stage-III-like shape noise. A linear relationship between the void lensing signal and $M_\\nu$ is identified, and forward modeling from void density profiles is validated across cosmologies.
\n\n
本文表明，空洞-剪切交叉关联（空洞透镜效应）为总中微子质量 $M_\\nu$ 提供了一个具有竞争力且独立的探针，在无形状噪声时约束为 $\\sigma(M_\\nu)=0.096\\,{\\rm eV}$，在采用第三阶段（Stage-III-like）形状噪声时为 $\\sigma(M_\\nu)=0.340\\,{\\rm eV}$。研究发现空洞透镜信号与 $M_\\nu$ 之间存在明显的线性关系，并验证了从不同宇宙学模型下的空洞密度轮廓进行前向建模的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cosmic voids encode complementary cosmological information compared to overdense regions like halos. Massive neutrinos suppress structure growth on small scales, which affects both the abundance and internal profiles of voids. The void lensing effect—i.e., the weak gravitational lensing induced by underdense regions—offers a direct probe of the total matter distribution, including contributions from both cold dark matter and neutrinos. This work aims to quantify how precisely void lensing can constrain the total neutrino mass $M_\\nu$, especially in light of upcoming large-scale galaxy surveys.
\n\n
宇宙空洞相比致密区域（如晕）编码了互补的宇宙学信息。大质量中微子会抑制小尺度上的结构增长，从而影响空洞的丰度和内部轮廓。空洞透镜效应——即由欠密区域引起的弱引力透镜——提供了对总物质分布（包括冷暗物质和中微子贡献）的直接探针。本工作旨在量化空洞透镜效应对总中微子质量 $M_\\nu$ 的约束能力，特别是在即将到来的大规模星系巡天背景下。

Method: The authors use cosmological N-body simulations with varying total neutrino masses. Voids are identified using the DIVE void finder applied to the combined dark matter and neutrino particle distributions. Density profiles of these voids are extracted. Mock shear catalogs are generated via ray-tracing through the simulation boxes to compute the void-shear cross-correlation (i.e., the stacked tangential shear profile around voids). They analyze the dependence of this lensing signal on $M_\\nu$, perform forward modeling of the signal from the measured density profiles using the Born approximation, and assess statistical uncertainties under idealized and realistic (Stage-III-like) observational conditions.
\n\n
作者使用具有不同总中微子质量的宇宙学 N-body 模拟。利用 DIVE 空洞搜寻器在联合的暗物质与中微子粒子分布上识别空洞，并提取其密度轮廓。通过在模拟盒子中进行光线追踪生成模拟剪切星表，计算空洞-剪切交叉关联（即围绕空洞的堆叠切向剪切轮廓）。他们分析该透镜信号对 $M_\\nu$ 的依赖性，使用 Born 近似从前测得的密度轮廓对信号进行前向建模，并在理想化和现实（第三阶段类）观测条件下评估统计不确定性。

Result: The void lensing signal shows a clear linear anti-correlation with total neutrino mass: larger $M_\\nu$ leads to shallower voids and weaker lensing signals. In the absence of shape noise, the constraint on $M_\\nu$ reaches $\\sigma(M_\\nu)=0.096\\,{\\rm eV}$; with Stage-III-like shape noise ($\\sigma_e \\simeq 0.3$), it degrades to $\\sigma(M_\\nu)=0.340\\,{\\rm eV}$. Forward modeling based on void density profiles accurately reproduces the measured lensing signal across different cosmologies, confirming its reliability for inference.
\n\n
空洞透镜信号与总中微子质量呈现明显的线性负相关：更大的 $M_\\nu$ 导致更浅的空洞和更弱的透镜信号。在无形状噪声情况下，对 $M_\\nu$ 的约束达到 $\\sigma(M_\\nu)=0.096\\,{\\rm eV}$；在第三阶段类形状噪声（$\\sigma_e \\simeq 0.3$）下，退化为 $\\sigma(M_\\nu)=0.340\\,{\\rm eV}$。基于空洞密度轮廓的前向建模能准确复现不同宇宙学模型下的测量透镜信号，证实了其用于推断的可靠性。

Conclusion: Void lensing is a promising and independent cosmological probe of the total neutrino mass. Its sensitivity arises from the impact of massive neutrinos on the matter distribution within and around voids. The validated forward modeling framework enables its application to real data from galaxy surveys. Combining void lensing with other probes (e.g., CMB, galaxy clustering, cluster counts) could significantly improve constraints on $M_\\nu$ and help break parameter degeneracies.
\n\n
空洞透镜效应是探测总中微子质量的一个有前景且独立的宇宙学探针。其灵敏度源于大质量中微子对空洞内外物质分布的影响。已验证的前向建模框架使其可应用于真实星系巡天数据。将空洞透镜与其他探针（如 CMB、星系成团性、星系团计数）结合，可显著提升对 $M_\\nu$ 的约束并帮助打破参数简并。

Abstract: Cosmic voids, the underdense regions of the Large Scale Structure (LSS), provide cosmological information highly complementary to that obtained from overdense regions. In this work, we investigate the constraining power of the void-shear cross-correlation (void lensing effect) on the total neutrino mass. Based on cosmological simulations with varying neutrino masses, we identify voids with the DIVE void finder and obtain their density profiles from the underlying dark matter and neutrino distributions. We then generate mock shear catalogues through ray-tracing and measure the corresponding void lensing signals. Our results show that void lensing yields an independent constraint on total neutrino mass as $σ(M_ν)=0.096\,{\rm eV}$ in the absence of shape noise, and $σ(M_ν)=0.340\,{\rm eV}$ when adopting a Stage-III-like shape noise ($σ_e \simeq 0.3$). Moreover, we find a clear linear relationship between the void lensing signal and neutrino mass. We further validate the forward modelling of the void lensing signal from the void density profiles across different cosmologies, demonstrating its accuracy and potential for future applications. These findings highlight void lensing as a promising probe of massive neutrinos and motivate its applications to galaxy survey data as well as the combination with other cosmological observables.

</details>


### [56] [Mock Catalogs of Strongly Lensed Gravitational Waves via A Halo Model Approach with Ground-based Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09289)
*Youkai Li,Kai Liao,Mingqi Sun,Lilan Yang,Xuheng Ding,Marek Biesiada,Tonghua Liu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper constructs a realistic mock catalog of strongly lensed gravitational wave (GW) events for third-generation detectors like Einstein Telescope (ET) and Cosmic Explorer (CE), incorporating a composite lens mass model with dark matter halos, galaxies, and subhalos. It forecasts hundreds of detectable lensed events per year—including doublets, quadruplets, subhalo-lensed systems, and rare complete image configurations with detectable central images—and provides public access to the GW-LMC dataset to support future lensing searches.\n\n
本文构建了一个面向第三代引力波探测器（如Einstein Telescope和Cosmic Explorer）的强透镜引力波事件模拟星表，采用了包含暗物质晕、星系及子晕的复合透镜质量模型。研究预测每年可探测到数百个透镜事件——包括双像、四像、子晕透镜系统以及罕见的具有可探测中心像的完整成像构型，并公开发布了GW-LMC数据集以支持未来的透镜搜寻。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: With the imminent deployment of third-generation GW observatories (e.g., ET and CE), the expected detection rate of strongly lensed GWs will increase dramatically. However, existing mock catalogs often rely on simplified lens models that neglect substructure (e.g., subhalos) or fail to capture rare but informative configurations such as complete image systems with a detectable central image. A physically motivated, high-fidelity mock catalog is essential to develop robust statistical methods for identifying and confirming lensed GW signals in real data.\n\n
随着第三代引力波天文台（如ET和CE）即将部署，强透镜引力波的预期探测率将急剧上升。然而，现有的模拟星表通常依赖简化的透镜模型，忽略了子结构（如subhalos），或未能捕捉到稀有但信息丰富的构型（例如具有可探测中心像的完整成像系统）。一个基于物理动机且高保真的模拟星表对于开发稳健的统计方法以在真实数据中识别和确认透镜引力波信号至关重要。

Method: The authors generate the Gravitational Waves-Lensing Mock Catalog (GW-LMC) by combining: (1) a composite lens mass model that includes main dark matter halos, galaxy-scale lenses, and subhalos; (2) three distinct GW source populations (binary black holes, binary neutron stars, and neutron star–black hole binaries); and (3) four detector network configurations (including ET+CE) with Earth rotation effects accounted for. They simulate full lensing configurations—doublets, quadruplets, triplets, quintuplets—and specifically flag systems where the central image is above the detection threshold. Detection criteria are applied based on signal-to-noise ratio (SNR), with both strict (all images detectable) and relaxed (at least one image detectable) thresholds. They also study dependencies on lens and stellar evolution models.\n\n
作者通过结合以下要素生成了引力波-透镜模拟星表（GW-LMC）：(1) 一个包含主暗物质晕、星系尺度透镜和subhalos的复合透镜质量模型；(2) 三类不同的引力波源种群（双黑洞、双中子星、中子星-黑洞双星）；(3) 四种探测器网络构型（包括ET+CE），并考虑地球自转效应。他们模拟了完整的透镜构型——双像、四像、三像、五像——并特别标记出中心像高于探测阈值的系统。基于信噪比（SNR）应用探测判据，包括严格条件（所有像均可探测）和宽松条件（至少一个像可探测）。他们还研究了透镜模型和恒星演化模型对结果的影响。

Result: For the ET+CE network, the authors predict ~400 double-image and ~36 quadruple-image lensed GW events per year. Among these, ~107 are lensed by subhalos and ~20 are complete systems (triplets or quintuplets) with a detectable central image—unlike in optical lensing where the central image is typically demagnified below observability. They also forecast ~360 high-magnification ($\\mu > 3$) events annually. Under a relaxed detection criterion (only one image above threshold), the total number of detectable lensed events rises to ~617 per year. The study further quantifies how variations in lens mass modeling and stellar evolution prescriptions affect event rates, SNR pair distributions, and time-delay distributions.\n\n
对于ET+CE网络，作者预测每年约有400个双像和36个四像透镜引力波事件。其中约107个由subhalos透镜产生，约20个为具有可探测中心像的完整系统（三像或五像）——这与光学透镜不同，后者中心像通常因去放大而不可观测。他们还预测每年约有360个高放大率（$\\mu > 3$）事件。在宽松探测判据下（仅需一个像超过阈值），每年可探测的透镜事件总数上升至约617个。研究还量化了透镜质量模型和恒星演化模型的变化对事件率、SNR对分布及时延分布的影响。

Conclusion: This work provides the first comprehensive, physically motivated mock catalog of strongly lensed GWs that includes substructure and rare complete-image configurations. The results offer critical statistical priors for future lensing searches with third-generation detectors and demonstrate that lensed GWs—especially those involving subhalos or central images—can serve as powerful probes of small-scale structure in the universe. The public release of GW-LMC enables community-wide development of lensing identification pipelines.\n\n
本工作提供了首个包含子结构和稀有完整成像构型的、基于物理动机的强透镜引力波综合模拟星表。其结果为第三代探测器未来的透镜搜寻提供了关键的统计先验，并表明透镜引力波——尤其是涉及subhalos或中心像的事件——可作为探测宇宙小尺度结构的有力探针。GW-LMC的公开发布将促进社区广泛开发透镜识别流程。

Abstract: As plans for the construction of third-generation gravitational wave (GW) detectors advance, research into strongly lensed GWs has become increasingly critical. It is anticipated that hundreds of multi-image lensed GWs will be detected annually. We present a comprehensive suite of lensed GW mock catalog derived from a composite lens mass model incorporating dark matter halos, galaxies, and subhalos. We analyze three source populations with four detector network configurations considering the earth rotation. Our simulations encompass not only conventional doublets and quadruplets but also subhalo-lensed events, highly magnified systems, and complete three or five image systems with a detectable central image, a feature distinct from optical lensing. For the joint ET+CE network, we forecast an annual detection rate of approximately 400 doublets and 36 quadruplets. Notably, this population includes roughly 107 events lensed by subhalos and 20 complete systems with detectable central images. Furthermore, we analyze high-magnification events ($μ> 3$), predicting approximately 360 such cases. Under a more relaxed selection criterion that requires only at least one lensed signal to exceed the detection threshold, we estimate a total of approximately 617 lensed events. We also investigate the impact of variations in lens mass models and stellar evolution models on event rates, as well as the distributions of SNR pairs and time delays. These results establish a more physically grounded statistical prior for the future identification and authentication of lensed GW signals. The Gravitational Waves-Lensing Mock Catalog (GW-LMC) have been made publicly available.

</details>


### [57] [Reliable Tests of Faint-end UV Luminosity Functions in Strong Lensing Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09308)
*Jiashuo Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This thesis tests ultralight bosonic dark matter ($\psi$DM) against standard cold dark matter by searching for a faint-end turnover in the high-redshift galaxy luminosity function using strong lensing in MACS J0416. After mitigating severe contamination from low-redshift interlopers—using HST/JWST data and machine learning—it finds no evidence for such a turnover, placing a lower bound of $m_\psi > 2.97 \times 10^{-22} \, \text{eV}$ (95% CL). This limit is interpreted as constraining an effective de Broglie scale in a multi-component $\psi$DM scenario.
\n\n
本论文通过在MACS J0416强引力透镜场中搜寻高红移星系光度函数的暗端截断（faint-end turnover），检验超轻玻色子暗物质（$\psi$DM）与标准冷暗物质模型。在利用HST/JWST数据和机器学习方法有效缓解低红移前景星系严重污染后，未发现该截断信号，从而给出$\psi$DM粒子质量下限$m_\psi > 2.97 \times 10^{-22} \, \text{eV}$（95%置信度）。该限制被解释为对多组分$\psi$DM模型中主导集体引力行为的有效德布罗意尺度的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The fundamental particle nature of dark matter remains unknown despite its dominance in the cosmic mass budget. Ultralight bosonic dark matter ($\psi$DM) with mass $\sim 10^{-22}$ eV predicts quantum pressure that suppresses small-scale structure, manifesting as a faint-end turnover in the high-redshift galaxy luminosity function. Strong gravitational lensing by massive clusters like MACS J0416 enables probing intrinsically faint galaxies where this signature should appear. However, reliable detection requires addressing severe contamination from low-redshift galaxies misidentified as high-redshift due to similar spectral energy distributions (SEDs), which could obscure or mimic the turnover signal.
\n\n
尽管暗物质占据宇宙总质量的约85%，其基本粒子性质仍未知。质量约为$10^{-22}$ eV的超轻玻色子暗物质（$\psi$DM）因量子压效应会抑制小尺度结构形成，这应在高红移星系光度函数的暗端表现为截断（turnover）。MACS J0416等大质量星系团的强引力透镜效应可放大极暗弱星系，使其成为探测该信号的理想场所。然而，可靠探测需解决低红移星系因光谱能量分布（SED）相似而被误判为高红移星系的严重污染问题，此类前景污染可能掩盖或伪造截断信号。

Method: The analysis focuses on the Hubble Frontier Fields (HFF), particularly MACS J0416, combining deep HST and JWST photometry to construct cleaner high-redshift galaxy samples at $3.5 \leq z \leq 5.5$ and $6 \leq z \leq 10$. Photometric redshift catalogs are critically assessed, revealing $\sim 50\%$ contamination by low-z interlopers in the $z \sim 4–5.5$ range. Interloper mitigation employs: (1) direct identification via high-resolution HST+JWST imaging and SED fitting, and (2) machine learning techniques for fields lacking supplementary data. The corrected luminosity functions are then used to test for the predicted $\psi$DM-induced faint-end turnover. Constraints on the boson mass $m_\psi$ are derived by comparing observed galaxy counts with theoretical predictions incorporating quantum pressure effects. The interpretation is extended to a multi-component $\psi$DM framework, where the bound is associated with an effective de Broglie wavelength $\lambda_{\rm dB} \propto 1/m_\psi$ governing collective behavior.
\n\n
分析聚焦于哈勃前沿场（HFF），特别是MACS J0416，结合深度HST与JWST测光数据构建更纯净的$3.5 \leq z \leq 5.5$和$6 \leq z \leq 10$高红移星系样本。研究评估了现有测光红移星表，发现$z \sim 4–5.5$区间约50%的星系实为低红移前景污染。前景污染缓解方法包括：(1) 利用高分辨率HST+JWST成像与SED拟合直接识别；(2) 对缺乏补充数据的天区采用机器学习技术。修正后的光度函数用于检验$\psi$DM模型预言的暗端截断。通过将观测星系数密度与包含量子压效应的理论预测对比，导出玻色子质量$m_\psi$的限制。该限制进一步被推广至多组分$\psi$DM框架，其中约束对应于主导集体引力行为的有效德布罗意波长$\lambda_{\rm dB} \propto 1/m_\psi$。

Result: The study finds no statistically significant evidence for a faint-end turnover in the high-redshift galaxy luminosity function within the strong lensing field of MACS J0416. This non-detection translates into a lower bound on the ultralight boson mass of $m_\psi > 2.97 \times 10^{-22} \, \text{eV}$ at 95% confidence level. Additionally, it is demonstrated that existing HFF photometric redshift catalogs suffer from $\sim 50\%$ contamination by low-redshift interlopers in the $3.5 \leq z \leq 5.5$ range, highlighting the necessity of deep multi-wavelength data or machine learning for reliable sample selection.
\n\n
研究在MACS J0416强引力透镜场的高红移星系光度函数中未发现具有统计显著性的暗端截断信号。该非探测结果转化为对超轻玻色子质量的下限约束：$m_\psi > 2.97 \times 10^{-22} \, \text{eV}$（95%置信度）。此外，研究证实现有HFF测光红移星表在$3.5 \leq z \leq 5.5$区间存在约50%的低红移前景污染，凸显了深度多波段数据或机器学习方法对可靠样本选取的必要性。

Conclusion: The absence of a faint-end turnover in the corrected high-redshift galaxy samples rules out ultralight bosonic dark matter with mass below $2.97 \times 10^{-22} \, \text{eV}$ as the dominant component. This represents one of the strongest constraints on $\psi$DM from galaxy counts at high redshift. The work underscores the critical impact of interloper contamination on small-scale structure probes and validates the combined use of HST/JWST data and machine learning for robust cosmological inference. Furthermore, the constraint is interpreted not merely as a particle mass limit but as a bound on an effective de Broglie scale in a potentially multi-component $\psi$DM universe, suggesting that even in complex dark sector scenarios, the collective quantum behavior is constrained by observations of early galaxy formation.
\n\n
修正后的高红移星系样本中缺乏暗端截断信号，排除了质量低于$2.97 \times 10^{-22} \, \text{eV}$的超轻玻色子作为主导暗物质成分的可能性。这是目前基于高红移星系计数对$\psi$DM最严格的限制之一。本工作强调了前景污染对小尺度结构探针的关键影响，并验证了HST/JWST数据与机器学习结合在稳健宇宙学推断中的有效性。此外，该约束不仅被视为粒子质量上限，更被解释为对潜在多组分$\psi$DM宇宙中有效德布罗意尺度的限制，表明即使在复杂的暗物质模型中，早期星系形成观测仍能约束其集体量子行为。

Abstract: Dark matter comprises ~85% of the entire mass of the Universe, but the fundamental nature of its constituent particles remains elusive. In this thesis, I test for two competitive dark matter models: the conventional heavy particle paradigm, and dark matter being ultralight bosons of mass $\sim 10^{-22}$eV ($ψ$DM). More specifically, I test for the faint-end turnover induced by $ψ$DM models, exploiting the strong lensing power by massive galaxy clusters to probe intrinsically fainter magnitudes. A key challenge for such an analysis would be contamination by low-z galaxies sharing similar observed SEDs as high-z galaxies. As I will demonstrate, such a contamination issue is generally severe and may wash out the faint-end turnover signatures. I also show that $\sim 50\%$ of the purported $3.5\leq z\leq 5.5$ galaxies within existing photometric redshift catalogs constructed for Hubble Frontier Fields (HFF) are in fact low-z interlopers. Luckily, individual mitigation of interlopers can be achieved with the combination of deep HST and JWST observations. For fields without supplementary data, machine learning methods will be shown useful in preserving the mitigating power. Cleaner $3.5\leq z\leq 5.5$ and $6\leq z\leq 10$ samples are derived for a more reliable test in strong lensing field of MACS J0416, with which I found no evidence for faint-end turnovers, leading to a constraint on the $ψ$DM mass of $>2.97\times10^{-22}$eV at 95\% confidence. This constraint will also be interpreted in an scheme where dark matter is composed of multiple particle copies, where I argue the derived mass bound is likely on an effective de Broglie scale governing the collective behavior of the entire $ψ$DM budget under gravitational equilibrium established.

</details>


### [58] [Hidden Vela Supercluster Revealed by First Hybrid Redshift & Peculiar Velocity Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09339)
*A. M. Hollinger,H. M. Courtois,R. C. Kraan-Korteweg,J. Mould,S. H. A. Rajohnson*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper presents a hybrid reconstruction method combining 65,518 galaxy peculiar velocity measurements from the CF4++ catalogue with 8,283 new redshifts—especially 2,176 deep HI redshifts from MeerKAT—in the southern Zone of Avoidance (ZOA, |b| ≤ 10°). This approach fills a critical ~20% gap in whole-sky large-scale structure maps and reveals the Vela supercluster as a dominant mass concentration rivaling Shapley, with total mass $33.8 \\times 10^{16} M_\\odot$, radius 70 $h^{-1}$ Mpc, and distance 189 $h^{-1}$ Mpc.
\n\n
本文提出了一种混合重建方法，结合了CF4++目录中的65,518个星系本动速度测量值与8,283个新的红移数据——特别是来自MeerKAT的2,176个深度HI红移数据，覆盖南天“回避区”（Zone of Avoidance, ZOA, |b| ≤ 10°）。该方法填补了全天大尺度结构图中约20%的关键空白，并揭示Vela超星系团是一个主导性的质量集中区，其总质量达$33.8 \\times 10^{16} M_\\odot$，特征半径为70 $h^{-1}$ Mpc，距离为189 $h^{-1}$ Mpc，可与Shapley超星系团相媲美。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Milky Way's Galactic plane obscures ~20% of the extragalactic sky due to dust and stellar foregrounds, creating a major incompleteness in whole-sky maps of large-scale structure—particularly severe for peculiar velocity catalogs. This hampers robust inference of cosmic flows and their relation to the underlying mass-density field, especially in the southern Zone of Avoidance (ZOA).
\n\n
银河系银道面由于尘埃和恒星前景遮挡了约20%的河外天空，在全天大尺度结构图中造成重大缺失，尤其严重影响本动速度样本的完整性。这阻碍了对宇宙流及其与底层质量密度场关系的可靠推断，尤其是在南天“回避区”（Zone of Avoidance, ZOA）。

Method: The authors develop a hybrid reconstruction methodology that fuses peculiar velocity data from the CF4++ catalogue (65,518 galaxies) with newly acquired redshift data near the southern ZOA (|b| ≤ 10°), including 2,176 high-sensitivity interferometric HI redshifts from the SARAO MeerKAT telescope. This enables coverage of the innermost 3°-wide strip of the ZOA to unprecedented depth, overcoming traditional observational limitations.
\n\n
作者开发了一种混合重建方法，融合了CF4++目录中的本动速度数据（65,518个星系）与在南天回避区（|b| ≤ 10°）新获得的红移数据，其中包括来自SARAO MeerKAT望远镜的2,176个高灵敏度干涉仪HI红移数据。这使得能够以前所未有的深度覆盖ZOA最内侧3°宽的区域，克服了传统观测限制。

Result: The hybrid reconstruction reveals the Vela supercluster as a dominant mass overdensity in the southern ZOA, with total mass $33.8 \\times 10^{16} M_\\odot$, characteristic radius of 70 $h^{-1}$ Mpc, double-core morphology, and distance of 189 $h^{-1}$ Mpc. It rivals the Shapley concentration in mass and exceeds the combined mass of Laniakea and the Great Attractor region, thereby reshaping our understanding of gravitational sources in the southern sky.
\n\n
混合重建揭示Vela超星系团是南天回避区中的主导性质量超密度结构，其总质量为$33.8 \\times 10^{16} M_\\odot$，特征半径为70 $h^{-1}$ Mpc，具有双核形态，距离为189 $h^{-1}$ Mpc。其质量可与Shapley超星系团相媲美，并超过Laniakea和巨引源（Great Attractor）区域的总质量，从而重塑了我们对南天引力源的理解。

Conclusion: This work provides the most complete and dynamically consistent map of the southern Zone of Avoidance to date by integrating peculiar velocities and deep redshift surveys. It demonstrates that hybrid reconstruction techniques are essential for next-generation large-scale structure analyses, particularly in obscured regions, and establishes Vela as a key gravitational anchor in the local Universe.
\n\n
本工作通过整合本动速度与深度红移巡天，提供了迄今为止最完整且动力学自洽的南天回避区地图。研究表明，混合重建技术对于下一代大尺度结构分析至关重要，尤其适用于被遮蔽区域，并确立了Vela超星系团作为本地宇宙中一个关键引力锚点的地位。

Abstract: A large fraction of the extragalactic sky is obscured by foreground dust and stars along the plane of the Milky Way, leaving a major gap (~ 20%) in whole-sky maps of large-scale structures -- an incompleteness that is even more severe for peculiar velocity samples. This has long limited an unambiguous interpretation of observed cosmic flows and their connection to the underlying mass-density field.
  We present a new hybrid reconstruction methodology which combines 65,518 galaxy peculiar velocity distances from the CF4++ catalogue (Courtois2025) with 8283 new galaxy redshifts observed near the southern Galactic plane (|b| <= 10 degrees) Zone of Avoidance. A major advance is the inclusion of 2176 high-sensitivity, interferometric HI redshifts obtained with the SARAO MeerKAT telescope which for the first time provide coverage of the innermost 3degrees-wide strip of the southern ZOA and to unprecedented depth.
  This hybrid redshifts & peculiar velocities approach yields a substantially revised view of the inferred overdensities in and around the ZOA. In particular, the Vela supercluster emerges as a dominant mass concentration, rivaling the Shapley concentration and exceeding the mass associated with Laniakea and the Great Attractor region. With a total mass of 33.8 10^16 Msol, a characteristic radius of 70 hmpc, and a double core morphology at a distance of 189 hmpc, Vela dominates the mass budget and gravitational influence of the southern Zone of Avoidance. These results provide the most complete and dynamically consistent picture to date of the southern Zone of Avoidance and demonstrate the transformative potential of hybrid reconstruction techniques tailored for the next generation of large-scale surveys.

### [59] [Pure Natural Inflation Passes the ACT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09413)
*Cristóbal Zenteno Gatica,Alexandros Papageorgiou,Matteo Fasiello*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: Pure natural inflation remains viable under current CMB constraints from the Atacama Cosmology Telescope, with a non-trivial fraction of its parameter space allowed under both instantaneous and standard reheating assumptions. A phenomenological extension is also analyzed and its viable region mapped.
\n\n
纯自然暴胀模型在Atacama宇宙微波背景（CMB）望远镜的最新观测限制下仍然可行，在瞬时再热和标准再热假设下，其参数空间的一个非平凡部分被保留。本文还分析了该模型的一个唯象学推广，并绘制了其可行参数区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to test the viability of pure natural inflation—a theoretically well-motivated single-field inflation model derived from top-down considerations—against the latest high-resolution CMB data from the Atacama Cosmology Telescope (ACT), which provides tighter constraints on primordial power spectra and inflationary parameters than previous datasets.
\n\n
动机在于利用Atacama宇宙微波背景（CMB）望远镜提供的最新高分辨率数据，检验纯自然暴胀（一种源于自上而下理论构造、具有坚实理论动机的单场暴胀模型）的可行性。ACT数据对原初功率谱和暴胀参数施加了比以往更严格的限制。

Method: The authors compare predictions of the pure natural inflation potential $V(\\phi) = \\Lambda^4 \\left[1 + \\cos(\\phi/f)\\right]$ with CMB constraints by computing the scalar spectral index $n_s$ and tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$ across the model’s parameter space. They consider two reheating scenarios: instantaneous reheating and standard reheating with typical equation-of-state assumptions. They also extend the analysis to a phenomenological generalization of the potential and map regions consistent with ACT data.
\n\n
作者通过计算纯自然暴胀势 $V(\\phi) = \\Lambda^4 \\left[1 + \\cos(\\phi/f)\\right]$ 所预言的标量谱指数 $n_s$ 和张量-标量比 $r$，将其与CMB观测限制进行对比。他们考虑了两种再热情形：瞬时再热和基于典型物态方程假设的标准再热。此外，他们还将分析扩展到该势能的一个唯象学推广形式，并绘制出与ACT数据一致的参数区域。

Result: A non-trivial portion of the parameter space of pure natural inflation is found to be compatible with ACT CMB constraints under both reheating assumptions. The analysis also identifies viable regions in the extended phenomenological model, demonstrating that natural inflation remains observationally viable despite increasingly stringent CMB bounds.
\n\n
研究发现，在两种再热假设下，纯自然暴胀模型的参数空间中存在一个非平凡的部分与ACT的CMB限制相容。分析还确定了推广唯象模型中的可行区域，表明尽管CMB限制日益严格，自然暴胀模型仍具有观测可行性。

Conclusion: Pure natural inflation is not ruled out by current CMB data and retains predictive and theoretical appeal. Its compatibility with ACT observations supports continued investigation into axion-inspired inflationary models and their extensions within fundamental physics frameworks.
\n\n
纯自然暴胀并未被当前CMB数据排除，仍具有理论吸引力和预测能力。其与ACT观测的兼容性支持在基础物理框架内继续探索受轴子启发的暴胀模型及其推广形式。

Abstract: Pure natural inflation is a compelling effectively single-field model of inflation stemming from a top-down approach to the acceleration mechanism. In this short letter we show that such model is compatible with the latest CMB constraints from the Atacama Cosmology Telescope. Under both the instantaneous reheating hypothesis and standard assumptions for reheating, we rule in a non-trivial fraction of the parameter space. We apply our analysis also to a phenomenological extension of the model and chart its viable parameter space.

</details>


### [60] [Exploring the $S_8$ Tension: Insights from the CatNorth 1.5-Million Quasar Candidates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09457)
*Jin Qin,Xue-Bing Wu,Yuming Fu,Haojie Xu,Yuxuan Pang,Yun-Hao Zhang,Pengjie Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper measures the cosmological parameter $S_8$ using quasar candidates from the CatNorth catalog and Planck CMB lensing data, finding values consistent with Planck 2018 at $z<1.5$ and lower values at $z>1.5$, suggesting reduced evidence for the $S_8$ tension when using this sample.
\n\n
本文利用CatNorth类星体候选样本和Planck CMB透镜数据测量宇宙学参数$S_8$，发现在$z<1.5$时与Planck 2018结果一致，而在$z>1.5$时数值偏低，表明使用该样本时$S_8$张力的证据减弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The persistent $\sim3\sigma$ tension in $S_8$ between high-redshift CMB and low-redshift weak lensing measurements motivates a re-examination using alternative tracers like quasars, which can probe large-scale structure across broad redshift ranges and potentially reveal whether the discrepancy stems from systematics or new physics beyond $Λ$CDM.
\n\n
$S_8$在高红移CMB与低红移弱引力透镜测量之间存在持续约$3\sigma$的张力，促使研究者使用类星体等替代示踪体重新检验该问题。类星体可跨越宽红移范围探测大尺度结构，有助于判断该差异源于系统误差还是超出$Λ$CDM的新物理。

Method: The authors perform auto- and cross-correlation analyses between the CatNorth 1.5 million quasar candidate catalog and Planck DR4 CMB lensing maps. To mitigate spatial incompleteness-induced systematics, they develop a machine-learning-based selection function that suppresses spurious large-scale power excess. They measure $S_8$ in multiple redshift bins ($z<1.5$, $z>1.5$, and volume-limited subsamples) using these correlation functions within a standard cosmological inference framework.
\n\n
作者对CatNorth包含150万类星体候选体的星表与Planck DR4 CMB透镜图进行自相关和互相关分析。为减轻空间不完整性引起的系统误差，他们开发了一种基于机器学习的选择函数，有效抑制了大尺度上的虚假功率谱超量。他们在标准宇宙学推断框架下，利用这些关联函数在多个红移区间（$z<1.5$、$z>1.5$及体积限制子样本）中测量$S_8$。

Result: For $z<1.5$, the analysis yields $S_8 = 0.844^{+0.058}_{-0.056}$, consistent with Planck 2018 ($S_8=0.834\pm0.016$) and lower than a previous Quaia-based result. At $z>1.5$, $S_8=0.724^{+0.058}_{-0.054}$, likely affected by incompleteness or foregrounds. Volume-limited samples show $S_8 = 0.835^{+0.053}_{-0.049}$ ($z<2$), $0.824^{+0.061}_{-0.062}$ ($0.4<z<1.5$), and $0.789^{+0.062}_{-0.062}$ ($1.5<z<2.5$), indicating less tension overall.
\n\n
在$z<1.5$时，分析得到$S_8 = 0.844^{+0.058}_{-0.056}$，与Planck 2018结果（$S_8=0.834\pm0.016$）一致，且低于先前基于Quaia样本的结果。在$z>1.5$时，$S_8=0.724^{+0.058}_{-0.054}$，可能受样本不完整或前景污染影响。体积限制样本显示：$S_8 = 0.835^{+0.053}_{-0.049}$（$z<2$）、$0.824^{+0.061}_{-0.062}$（$0.4<z<1.5$）和$0.789^{+0.062}_{-0.062}$（$1.5<z<2.5$），整体上$S_8$张力减弱。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that using a large, high-purity quasar catalog with a robust ML-based selection function can produce $S_8$ constraints aligned with CMB results at low redshifts, reducing the apparent tension. However, high-redshift measurements remain vulnerable to observational systematics, highlighting the need for improved completeness and foreground mitigation in future surveys.
\n\n
研究表明，使用高纯度大样本类星体星表并结合基于机器学习的稳健选择函数，可在低红移处获得与CMB结果一致的$S_8$约束，从而缓解明显的张力。然而，高红移测量仍易受观测系统误差影响，凸显未来巡天需改进样本完备性与前景抑制技术。

Abstract: The parameter $S_8$, a key probe of cosmic structure growth, exhibits a persistent $\sim3σ$ tension between high-redshift measurements from cosmic microwave background (CMB) anisotropies and low-redshift weak gravitational lensing observations. This discrepancy may indicate either unaccounted systematic effects or new physics beyond the standard $Λ$CDM cosmology. In this work, we constrain $S_8$ using the high purity CatNorth 1.5 million quasar candidate catalog and the {\it Planck} DR4 CMB lensing data across the broad redshift ranges through auto-correlation and cross-correlation analyses. To address the spatial incompleteness, we develop a machine-learning-based selection function that effectively suppresses the systematics-induced power spectrum excess on large scales. Our robust low-redshift measurements at $z<1.5$ yield $S_8 = 0.844^{+0.058}_{-0.056}$, consistent with the {\it Planck} 2018 CMB anisotropies constraints of $S_8=0.834\pm0.016$ but lower than the $0.879^{+0.055}_{-0.055}$ reported by a previous work using the Quaia quasar candidate catalog. However, for high-redshift faint quasars at $z>1.5$, we find a lower value of $S_8=0.724^{+0.058}_{-0.054}$, likely due to the sample incompleteness and/or the foreground contamination. Further tests on the volume-limited samples exhibit a consistent trend: $S_8 = 0.835^{+0.053}_{-0.049}$ for $z < 2$, $0.824^{+0.061}_{-0.062}$ for $0.4 < z < 1.5$, and a lower value of $0.789^{+0.062}_{-0.062}$ for the higher redshift range of $1.5 < z < 2.5$. While future data may refine these results, our current measurements based on a large sample of quasar candidates show less evidence of the $S_8$ tension.
