### [61] [Dark Matter Recoupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09969)
*Eugenia Dallari,Francesco Castagna,Emanuele Castorina,Maria Archidiacono,Ennio Salvioni*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper challenges the standard assumption that dark matter is always collisionless by proposing a scenario where dark matter interactions are weak at early times (e.g., during CMB last scattering) but become strong at late times (post-reionization). This is achieved through a recoupling mechanism between dark matter and a dark radiation species within redshifts probed by current galaxy surveys. Observational constraints from CMB and BAO data imply that if all dark matter recouples, interactions must be weak today; however, up to 4% of dark matter could remain strongly interacting now.
\n\n
本文挑战了暗物质始终无碰撞的标准假设，提出了一种新情景：暗物质在早期（如CMB最后散射面时期）相互作用很弱，但在晚期（再电离之后）变得显著。这一机制通过暗物质与一种暗辐射组分在当前星系巡天所探测的红移范围内重新耦合来实现。CMB和BAO数据的联合约束表明，若全部暗物质都发生再耦合，则其现今相互作用必须很弱；然而，最多4%的暗物质仍可能在今天保持强相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The standard cosmological model assumes dark matter is collisionless on cosmological scales, largely due to stringent constraints from Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) observations at high redshift. However, this assumption may not hold at late times. The authors aim to explore whether dark matter interactions can be dynamically suppressed early on but become significant later—thereby evading early-universe bounds while producing observable effects in the late Universe. This motivates the study of a “dark matter recoupling” scenario with dark radiation.
\n\n
标准宇宙学模型假设暗物质在宇宙学尺度上是无碰撞的，这主要源于高红移时期CMB观测对暗物质相互作用的严格限制。然而，这一假设在晚期宇宙中未必成立。作者旨在探索暗物质相互作用是否可以在早期被动态抑制，而在晚期变得显著——从而规避早期宇宙的约束，同时在晚期宇宙产生可观测效应。这促使他们研究一种暗物质与暗辐射之间的“再耦合（recoupling）”情景。

Method: The authors construct a phenomenological model where dark matter couples to a dark radiation component only after a certain redshift, leading to time-dependent interaction strength. They perform a systematic analysis using a combination of Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) data from Planck and Baryon Acoustic Oscillation (BAO) measurements. They consider two cases: (1) 100% of dark matter recouples to dark radiation, and (2) only a fraction (e.g., 4%) does so. The Boltzmann equations governing the perturbations are modified to include momentum exchange between dark matter and dark radiation, characterized by a cross-section scaling as $\\sigma \\propto a^n$ or via a constant interaction rate. Constraints are derived using Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) methods.
\n\n
作者构建了一个唯象模型，其中暗物质仅在特定红移之后与暗辐射组分耦合，导致相互作用强度随时间演化。他们系统地结合Planck卫星的CMB数据和BAO测量进行分析。考虑两种情形：(1) 全部暗物质与暗辐射再耦合；(2) 仅一小部分（如4%）发生再耦合。他们修改了描述扰动演化的Boltzmann方程，引入暗物质与暗辐射之间的动量交换项，其截面可表示为$\\sigma \\propto a^n$或采用恒定相互作用率。约束通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法导出。

Result: The joint analysis of CMB and BAO data shows that if all dark matter recouples to dark radiation at late times, the present-day interaction strength must be very weak—consistent with standard collisionless cold dark matter. However, if only a subcomponent of dark matter (up to approximately 4%) is allowed to interact strongly with dark radiation today, such a scenario remains compatible with current observations. This opens a viable window for late-time dark matter interactions that are invisible to CMB but potentially detectable in large-scale structure.
\n\n
CMB与BAO数据的联合分析表明：若全部暗物质在晚期与暗辐射再耦合，则其当前相互作用强度必须非常弱——与标准的无碰撞冷暗物质模型一致。然而，若仅允许一小部分暗物质（最多约4%）在今天与暗辐射强相互作用，则该情景仍与当前观测兼容。这为晚期暗物质相互作用开辟了一个可行窗口：这类相互作用在CMB中不可见，但可能在大尺度结构中被探测到。

Conclusion: The paper demonstrates that the conventional assumption of strictly collisionless dark matter throughout cosmic history can be relaxed. A late-time recoupling between dark matter and dark radiation is observationally viable, provided either the interaction is weak today or only a small fraction of dark matter participates. This scenario motivates further theoretical model-building and observational searches in late-time cosmological probes, such as galaxy clustering and weak lensing, which are sensitive to dark matter self-interactions at low redshift.
\n\n
本文表明，贯穿宇宙历史的严格无碰撞暗物质假设可以被放宽。只要满足以下条件之一——当前相互作用很弱，或仅有少量暗物质参与——暗物质与暗辐射在晚期的再耦合在观测上是可行的。这一情景激励进一步的微观模型构建，并推动利用晚期宇宙学探针（如星系成团性和弱引力透镜）开展观测搜寻，这些探针对低红移下暗物质自相互作用敏感。

Abstract: In the late Universe, and on cosmological scales, dark matter is conventionally assumed to be collisionless, as a consequence of the strong existing bounds on dark matter interactions at the Cosmic Microwave Background last-scattering surface. Challenging this lore, here we show that dark matter interactions can be naturally weak at early times, but then grow to observationally relevant strengths at very late times, even significantly after reionization. This is realized if dark matter recouples to a dark radiation species in the range of redshifts probed by the current generation of galaxy surveys. We systematically study, for the first time, the phenomenology of this dark matter recoupling scenario. A combination of Cosmic Microwave Background and Baryon Acoustic Oscillation data show that the interaction needs to be weak at present, if the entirety of dark matter couples to dark radiation. From a complementary perspective, a 4% fraction of dark matter could still be strongly interacting today. Implications for a microscopic model realizing the recoupling dynamics are discussed.

</details>


### [62] [Probing Physics Beyond the Standard Model through Combined Analyses of Next-Generation Type Ia Supernova, CMB, and BAO Surveys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09973)
*Srinivasan Raghunathan,Ayan Mitra,Nikolina Šarčević,Fei Ge,Corentin Ravoux,Christos Georgiou,Renée Hložek,Richard Kessler,Gautham Narayan,Paul Rogozenski,Paul Shah,Georgios Valogiannis,Joaquin Vieira,the LSST Dark Energy Science Collaboration*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper forecasts cosmological constraints on dark energy and neutrino masses by combining future Type Ia supernovae (SNIa) from LSST, BAO from DESI, and CMB data from SPT, Simons Observatory, and CMB-S4. The joint analysis yields tight constraints on the dark energy equation of state ($σ(w_0) = 0.028$, $σ(w_a) = 0.11$) and enables a potential $2–3σ$ detection of the sum of neutrino masses $\sum m_ν$.
\n\n
本文通过结合LSST的Ia型超新星（SNIa）、DESI的重子声学振荡（BAO）以及来自SPT、Simons Observatory和CMB-S4的宇宙微波背景（CMB）数据，预测了对暗能量和中微子质量的宇宙学限制。联合分析给出了对暗能量状态方程参数的紧致约束（$σ(w_0) = 0.028$，$σ(w_a) = 0.11$），并有望实现对中微子质量总和$\sum m_ν$的$2–3σ$探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Current and upcoming cosmological surveys—LSST (SNIa), DESI (BAO), and advanced CMB experiments—offer unprecedented statistical power across different cosmic epochs. Combining these probes allows for robust, complementary tests of the standard $Λ{\rm CDM}$ model and its extensions, particularly regarding the nature of dark energy and fundamental physics like neutrino masses and spatial curvature.
\n\n
当前及未来的宇宙学巡天项目——LSST（SNIa）、DESI（BAO）以及新一代CMB实验——在不同宇宙时期提供了前所未有的统计能力。将这些探针结合起来，可对标准$Λ{\rm CDM}$模型及其扩展（尤其是暗能量本质、中微子质量与空间曲率等基础物理问题）进行稳健且互补的检验。

Method: The authors employ a Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) framework to forecast constraints on cosmological parameters in $Λ{\rm CDM}$, $w_0 w_a {\rm CDM}$, and models with free $\sum m_ν$ and spatial curvature. They combine mock or projected data from: (1) LSST Year-3 SNIa sample; (2) DESI Data Release 3 (DR3) BAO measurements; and (3) CMB temperature, polarization, and lensing power spectra ($TT/EE/TE/φφ$) from South Pole Telescope (SPT), Advanced Simons Observatory, and a CMB-S4-like experiment.
\n\n
作者采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo, MCMC）框架，对$Λ{\rm CDM}$、$w_0 w_a {\rm CDM}$以及包含自由参数$\sum m_ν$和空间曲率的模型进行参数约束预测。他们联合了以下三类模拟或预期数据：(1) LSST第三年（Year-3）的SNIa样本；(2) DESI第三次数据发布（DR3）的BAO测量；(3) 来自南极望远镜（SPT）、Advanced Simons Observatory和类CMB-S4实验的CMB温度、偏振和透镜功率谱（$TT/EE/TE/φφ$）。

Result: The LSST Year-3 SNIa sample improves dark energy constraints by a factor of $2–2.5$ compared to DES Year-5, primarily due to higher SNIa density. DESI DR3 improves over DR2 by up to $\times1.8$, driven by increased low-redshift coverage. Joint analysis of LSST-Y3 SNIa, DESI-DR3 BAO, and CMB yields $σ(w_0) = 0.028$ and $σ(w_a) = 0.11$ in $w_0 w_a {\rm CDM}$, largely insensitive to the specific CMB dataset. Allowing $\sum m_ν$ and curvature weakens constraints by 10%–30%. The combination enables a $2–3σ$ detection of $\sum m_ν$.
\n\n
LSST第三年SNIa样本相比DES第五年数据，在暗能量约束上提升$2–2.5$倍，主要归因于更高的SNIa密度。DESI DR3相比DR2最多提升$1.8$倍，主要得益于低红移样本的显著增加。LSST-Y3 SNIa、DESI-DR3 BAO与CMB的联合分析在$w_0 w_a {\rm CDM}$模型下给出$σ(w_0) = 0.028$和$σ(w_a) = 0.11$的约束，且结果对具体CMB数据集不敏感。若同时放开$\sum m_ν$和空间曲率参数，约束会弱化10%–30%。三者联合有望实现对$\sum m_ν$的$2–3σ$探测。

Conclusion: Combining multi-epoch cosmological probes—SNIa, BAO, and CMB—from next-generation surveys significantly enhances our ability to test deviations from $Λ{\rm CDM}$. The synergy between LSST, DESI, and CMB experiments will deliver percent-level constraints on dark energy dynamics and potentially detect the absolute neutrino mass scale, offering powerful insights into fundamental physics beyond the standard cosmological model.
\n\n
结合下一代巡天项目在多个宇宙时期的探针——SNIa、BAO和CMB——能显著增强我们检验$Λ{\rm CDM}$模型偏差的能力。LSST、DESI与CMB实验之间的协同效应将提供对暗能量动力学的百分比量级约束，并可能探测到绝对中微子质量标度，为超越标准宇宙学模型的基础物理提供有力洞见。

Abstract: Observations of Type Ia supernovae (SNIa), baryon acoustic oscillations (BAO), and the cosmic microwave background (CMB), which probe the late-, intermediate-, and early-universe epochs, respectively, provide complementary constraints on the expansion history of the Universe. In this work, we forecast constraints on dark energy and other extensions to the standard cosmological model by combining the SNIa sample expected from the Vera C. Rubin Observatory's Legacy Survey of Space and Time (LSST), data from current and forthcoming CMB surveys, and BAO measurements from the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI). For the CMB, we use temperature, polarization, and lensing power spectra ($TT/EE/TE/φφ$) from South Pole Telescope, the planned Advanced Simons Observatory, and a CMB-S4-like experiment. We derive constraints on $Λ{\rm CDM}$ and its extensions involving the dark energy equation of state parameters $(w_{0}, w_{a})$ and the sum of neutrino masses $\sum m_ν$, using a Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) sampling framework. We find that the LSST Year-3 SNIa sample can improve upon the DES Year-5 dark energy constraints by a factor of $\times2-\times2.5$, with the gains driven primarily by the significantly higher SNIa density in the LSST sample. Similarly, DESI-DR3 shows up to a $\times1.8$ improvement on dark energy parameters over DR2, driven largely by the substantial increase in low-redshift sample. Combining CMB with LSST-Y3-SNIa and DESI-DR3-BAO yields $σ(w_{0}) = 0.028$ and $σ(w_{a}) = 0.11$ for $w_{0} w_{a} {\rm CDM}$ cosmology with the results being largely independent of the CMB dataset. The constraints weaken by 10%-30% when freeing $\sum m_ν$ and spatial curvature. Moreover, the joint analysis of the three datasets can enable a $2-3σ$ detection of $\sum m_ν$.

</details>

### [63] [Dark matter relic abundance from a critical-density instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08749)
*Hindi Zouhair*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper proposes a nonstandard thermal history for dark matter (DM) where strong self-interactions at high densities lead to a dynamically screened phase that suppresses annihilation. As the Universe expands, the system undergoes a critical instability at a number density $n_c$, triggering a rapid, far-from-equilibrium annihilation burst that sets the relic abundance—determined primarily by $n_c$ rather than the microscopic coupling. The model simultaneously satisfies observed relic density and small-scale structure constraints for TeV-scale DM with sub-GeV mediators.
\n\n
本文提出了一种非标准的暗物质（DM）热历史：在高数密度下，强自相互作用导致一种动态屏蔽相，显著抑制湮灭过程。随着宇宙膨胀，系统在临界数密度 $n_c$ 处失稳，触发一次快速、远离平衡的湮灭爆发，最终遗迹丰度主要由 $n_c$ 而非微观湮灭耦合决定。该模型在 TeV 量级暗物质与亚 GeV 介子情形下，同时满足观测到的遗迹丰度和小尺度结构约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard thermal freeze-out assumes weakly interacting massive particles (WIMPs) with perturbative annihilation rates. However, this paradigm faces challenges from null detection results and small-scale structure anomalies. The authors explore an alternative scenario where collective many-body effects—akin to those in strongly interacting quantum media—dominate the early DM dynamics, leading to a nonperturbative, nonstandard thermal history that could reconcile relic abundance with self-interacting dark matter (SIDM) requirements.
\n\n
标准热退耦假设弱相互作用大质量粒子（WIMPs）具有微扰湮灭率，但该范式面临直接探测零结果和小尺度结构异常的挑战。作者探索了一种替代方案：早期暗物质动力学由集体多体效应主导——类似于强相互作用量子介质中的现象——从而产生非微扰、非标准的热历史，可能同时满足遗迹丰度与自相互作用暗物质（SIDM）的要求。

Method: The authors introduce a minimal effective description of dark matter with strong self-interactions mediated by a light boson. They model the early correlated phase as one with dynamical screening of the mediator coupling, suppressing annihilation. Using a modified Boltzmann equation that incorporates a critical number density $n_c$, they describe the transition from the screened phase to a rapid annihilation burst when $n < n_c$. The relic abundance is computed by solving this non-equilibrium evolution, and the parameter space is mapped under constraints from cosmology and small-scale structure.
\n\n
作者引入了一个由轻玻色子介导的强自相互作用暗物质的最小有效描述。他们将早期关联相建模为介子耦合被动态屏蔽的状态，从而抑制湮灭。通过引入一个包含临界数密度 $n_c$ 的修正玻尔兹曼方程，当 $n < n_c$ 时描述从屏蔽相到快速湮灭爆发的转变。通过求解这一非平衡演化计算遗迹丰度，并在宇宙学和小尺度结构约束下映射参数空间。

Result: For TeV-scale dark matter coupled to sub-GeV mediators, the model yields the correct relic abundance via a late-time annihilation burst triggered at $n_c$. The required self-interaction cross section falls within the range $\sigma/m \sim 0.1–10~\mathrm{cm}^2/\mathrm{g}$, which addresses small-scale structure issues (e.g., core-cusp problem). Crucially, the relic density depends predominantly on $n_c$—a macroscopic, emergent scale—rather than the underlying annihilation coupling, offering a predictive and robust framework.
\n\n
对于 TeV 量级暗物质与亚 GeV 介子耦合的情形，该模型通过在 $n_c$ 处触发的晚期湮灭爆发得到正确的遗迹丰度。所需的自相互作用截面落在 $\sigma/m \sim 0.1–10~\mathrm{cm}^2/\mathrm{g}$ 范围内，可解决小尺度结构问题（如核-尖点问题）。关键的是，遗迹密度主要依赖于 $n_c$——一个宏观的、涌现的尺度——而非底层湮灭耦合，提供了一个可预测且稳健的框架。

Conclusion: The paper demonstrates that collective many-body effects in the early universe can drastically alter dark matter thermal history, replacing the standard freeze-out with a critical, non-equilibrium annihilation event. This mechanism decouples relic abundance from microscopic couplings, linking it instead to an emergent critical density. It provides a unified explanation for both the observed relic density and self-interaction cross sections relevant for astrophysical observations, opening a new avenue for nonstandard dark matter cosmology.
\n\n
本文表明，早期宇宙中的集体多体效应可彻底改变暗物质热历史，以一次临界的、非平衡的湮灭事件取代标准退耦机制。该机制将遗迹丰度与微观耦合解耦，转而将其与一个涌现的临界密度联系起来。它为观测到的遗迹丰度和与天体物理观测相关的自相互作用截面提供了统一解释，为非标准暗物质宇宙学开辟了新路径。

Abstract: We study a nonstandard dark-matter thermal history in which strong self-interactions give rise to collective many-body effects at high number density, as in strongly interacting quantum media. At early times, dark matter occupies a correlated phase in which its coupling to a light mediator is dynamically screened, suppressing annihilation far below the perturbative rate. As the Universe expands and the number density decreases, this screened phase becomes unstable at a critical density n_c, triggering a rapid, far-from-equilibrium annihilation episode. We show that this annihilation burst fixes the final relic abundance, which is governed primarily by n_c rather than by the microscopic annihilation coupling. Using a minimal effective parametrization, we solve the resulting modified Boltzmann evolution and map the viable parameter space. For TeV-scale dark matter and sub-GeV mediators, we find relic abundances consistent with observations together with self-interaction cross sections relevant for small-scale structure, realizing a consistent and predictive nonstandard thermal history.

</details>


### [64] [Sensitivity of Jet Observables to Molière Scattering Off Quasiparticles in Quark-Gluon Plasma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08776)
*Zachary Hulcher,Arjun Srinivasan Kudinoor,Daniel Pablos,Krishna Rajagopal*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper presents a full calculation of Molière scattering of jet partons off quasiparticles in the Quark-Gluon Plasma (QGP), incorporating it into the Hybrid Model of jet quenching. It shows that such hard scatterings broaden jet observables like the Soft Drop angle $R_g$ and jet girth $g$, especially in photon-tagged jets, offering model-independent signatures of QGP's microscopic quasiparticle structure.
\n\n
本文提出了喷注部分子与夸克-胶子等离子体（Quark-Gluon Plasma, QGP）中准粒子之间Molière散射的完整计算，并将其纳入喷注淬火的Hybrid Model。研究表明，此类硬散射会拓宽Soft Drop角 $R_g$ 和喷注宽度 $g$ 等观测量，尤其在光子标记喷注中更为显著，为QGP微观准粒子结构提供了模型无关的实验信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the dual nature of QGP: while it behaves as a strongly coupled fluid at long wavelengths, asymptotic freedom implies the existence of quark- and gluon-like quasiparticles at short distances. Jets serve as probes of this microscopic structure via high-momentum-transfer $2\\rightarrow2$ Molière scatterings. Previous implementations in the Hybrid Model accounted for soft, strongly coupled interactions but not explicit hard scatterings off thermal quasiparticles. This work aims to bridge that gap to uncover direct experimental signatures of QGP’s quasiparticle content.
\n\n
动机源于QGP的双重性质：在长波长下表现为强耦合流体，而由于渐近自由，在短距离下应存在类夸克和类胶子的准粒子。喷注通过高动量转移的 $2\\rightarrow2$ Molière散射可探测这一微观结构。此前Hybrid Model已包含喷注与QGP液滴之间的软强耦合动量交换及激发尾迹，但未明确计入与热准粒子的硬散射过程。本工作旨在填补这一空白，以揭示QGP准粒子成分的直接实验信号。

Method: The authors perform a full perturbative calculation of Molière scattering between a high-energy jet parton and a thermal quasiparticle in the QGP, resulting in deflection of the jet parton and recoil of a medium parton. This process is implemented within the Hybrid Model of jet quenching, which already includes soft interactions and hydrodynamic wakes. The scattered and recoil partons are tracked as they propagate through the medium, undergoing further energy loss, momentum exchange, wake excitation, and possible re-scattering. Simulations are used to compute jet substructure observables—such as fragmentation functions, Soft Drop angle $R_g$, jet girth $g$, and subjet multiplicity and angular distributions—with particular focus on photon-tagged jets to reduce selection bias.
\n\n
作者对高能喷注部分子与QGP中热准粒子之间的Molière散射进行了完整的微扰计算，导致喷注部分子偏转并激发出一个反冲的介质部分子。该过程被整合进已包含软相互作用和流体动力学尾迹的Hybrid Model喷注淬火框架中。散射后的喷注部分子与反冲部分子在介质中继续传播，经历进一步的能量损失、动量交换、尾迹激发以及可能的再散射。通过模拟计算喷注子结构观测量——包括碎裂函数、Soft Drop角 $R_g$、喷注宽度 $g$ 以及子喷注数量与角分布——特别聚焦于光子标记喷注以减少选择偏差。

Result: The inclusion of Molière scatterings in the Hybrid Model leads to significant broadening of the $R_g$ and $g$ distributions, particularly when analyzing jets that are much softer than the associated photon in photon-tagged events. This effect arises from rare large-angle scatterings that are enhanced in unbiased samples selected by photon energy. The study demonstrates that photon-tagged jets mitigate the selection bias present in inclusive jet measurements and provide enhanced sensitivity to hard parton–quasiparticle collisions, revealing distinctive modifications to jet substructure.
\n\n
在Hybrid Model中引入Molière散射后，$R_g$ 和 $g$ 分布显著展宽，尤其在光子标记事件中当喷注远软于关联光子时更为明显。该效应源于由光子能量选择所增强的无偏样本中的稀有大角度散射。研究表明，光子标记喷注可缓解包容性喷注测量中的选择偏差，并对硬部分子–准粒子碰撞具有更高灵敏度，从而揭示喷注子结构的独特改变。

Conclusion: The paper establishes that hard Molière scatterings between jet partons and QGP quasiparticles leave measurable imprints on jet substructure observables. By incorporating these scatterings into the Hybrid Model and using photon-tagged jets to control selection effects, the authors identify model-independent signatures of the quasiparticle nature of QGP at short distance scales. This paves the way for experimental verification of QGP’s microscopic degrees of freedom via jet tomography.
\n\n
本文确立了喷注部分子与QGP准粒子之间的硬Molière散射会在喷注子结构观测量上留下可观测印记。通过将此类散射纳入Hybrid Model，并利用光子标记喷注控制选择效应，作者识别出QGP在短距离尺度下准粒子本质的模型无关信号。这为通过喷注层析成像实验验证QGP的微观自由度开辟了道路。

Abstract: Quark-gluon plasma (QGP) is a strongly coupled liquid when viewed at length scales of order the inverse of its temperature and longer. However, when it is probed at short enough length scales, asymptotic freedom mandates the presence of quark- and gluon-like quasiparticles. Partons in jets can trigger perturbative, high momentum-exchange $2\rightarrow2$ Molière scatterings off quasiparticles in the medium, making jets useful probes of the microscopic structure of QGP. Prior to this work, soft strongly coupled momentum-exchanges between jet partons and the QGP droplet produced in a heavy-ion collision, as well as the wakes that jets excite in the droplet, had been accounted for in the Hybrid Model of jet quenching. Here, we present a full calculation of Molière scattering off a QGP quasiparticle which results in the deflection of the jet parton and the excitation of a parton from the thermal medium that recoils after being kicked, and describe how it is implemented in the Hybrid Model. The scattered jet and recoil partons continue to propagate through the QGP, lose energy and momentum, excite wakes, and may further re-scatter. Using the Hybrid Model, we study how Molière scatterings impact jet shapes and fragmentation functions, the Soft Drop angle $R_g$, jet girth $g$, and observables that focus on the number and angular distribution of subjets within jets. We demonstrate that photon-tagged jets provide a particularly sensitive probe: selecting events by the photon energy mitigates the selection bias inherent in inclusive jet measurements and enhances sensitivity to rare large-angle scatterings. We find that Molière scatterings broaden both the $R_g$ and $g$ distributions when jets significantly softer than the photon are included. Our results point the way towards distinctive model-independent experimental signatures of hard scattering of jet partons off quasiparticles in QGP.

</details>


### [65] [Binary-boosted Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08781)
*Javier F. Acevedo,Adam Ritz*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates how gravitational interactions between dark matter (DM) particles and binary systems—especially double black holes—in the Milky Way can significantly boost DM velocities, producing a high-energy tail in the DM velocity distribution. Using Monte Carlo simulations, the authors show that such "binary-boosted" DM can reach speeds up to $\sim 2000 \ \rm km/s$, enhancing the detectability of sub-GeV DM in large noble liquid detectors like LUX-ZEPLIN and PandaX-4T. The mechanism is gravitational, thus largely independent of DM particle physics models or mass.
\n\n
本文研究了暗物质（DM）粒子与银河系中双星系统（尤其是双黑洞）之间的引力相互作用如何显著提升DM速度，从而在DM速度分布中产生高能尾部。作者利用蒙特卡洛模拟表明，此类“双星加速”DM的速度可达$\sim 2000 \ \rm km/s$，从而增强亚GeV DM在LUX-ZEPLIN和PandaX-4T等大型惰性液体探测器中的可探测性。该机制本质上是引力的，因此在很大程度上独立于DM的具体粒子物理模型或质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard direct detection experiments are limited in sensitivity to light (sub-GeV) dark matter due to insufficient nuclear recoil energy. The authors aim to explore whether gravitational interactions with astrophysical binaries—particularly compact object binaries like double black holes—can impart enough kinetic energy to DM particles to make them detectable in current experiments, thereby opening a new window for light DM searches.
\n\n
标准直接探测实验由于核反冲能量不足，对轻质量（亚GeV）暗物质的灵敏度受限。作者旨在探索天体物理双星系统（特别是致密天体双星，如双黑洞）是否能通过引力相互作用赋予DM粒子足够动能，使其在当前实验中可被探测，从而为轻DM搜寻开辟新窗口。

Method: The authors employ Monte Carlo simulations to model the scattering of DM particles off a range of galactic binary systems. They compute the differential cross section for gravitational slingshot interactions, focusing on double black hole binaries as the most efficient accelerators. They then construct synthetic populations of such binaries throughout the Milky Way and integrate their collective contribution to the boosted DM flux at Earth. This flux is subsequently used to estimate event rates in noble liquid detectors like LUX-ZEPLIN and PandaX-4T.
\n\n
作者采用蒙特卡洛模拟来建模DM粒子与各类银河系双星系统的散射过程。他们计算了引力弹弓相互作用的微分散射截面，并聚焦于双黑洞系统作为最高效的加速器。随后，他们在整个银河系中构建此类双星的合成种群，并积分其对地球处加速DM通量的集体贡献。该通量进而用于估算LUX-ZEPLIN和PandaX-4T等惰性液体探测器中的事例率。

Result: The simulations reveal that double black hole binaries can eject DM particles with velocities up to $\sim 2000 \ \rm km/s$, significantly exceeding the standard galactic escape velocity. When accounting for the full population of such binaries in the Milky Way, the resulting boosted DM flux enables large noble liquid detectors to probe DM masses down to the sub-GeV scale—extending their reach beyond conventional limits—and potentially rivaling dedicated low-threshold experiments.
\n\n
模拟结果显示，双黑洞双星可将DM粒子以高达$\sim 2000 \ \rm km/s$的速度弹射出去，远超标准银河系逃逸速度。当计入银河系中全部此类双星种群时，所产生的加速DM通量使大型惰性液体探测器能够探测到亚GeV尺度的DM质量——超越其传统灵敏度极限——并可能与专用低阈值实验相媲美。

Conclusion: Gravitational boosting of dark matter by galactic binaries—especially double black holes—provides a model-independent mechanism to enhance the detectability of light dark matter in existing direct detection experiments. This effect should be incorporated into the interpretation of data from noble liquid detectors, as it significantly extends their sensitivity to sub-GeV DM candidates.
\n\n
银河系双星系统（尤其是双黑洞）对暗物质的引力加速提供了一种与模型无关的机制，可增强现有直接探测实验对轻暗物质的探测能力。该效应应纳入惰性液体探测器的数据解释中，因其显著拓展了对亚GeV DM候选者的灵敏度。

Abstract: We explore the aggregate effect of binary systems on the Milky Way's dark matter (DM) velocity distribution with Monte Carlo simulations. Through gravitational interactions with binaries, transiting DM particles can gain substantial energy. We analyze this mechanism across a range of galactic binaries, and find it to be most effective for double black holes, where ejection speeds can reach $\sim 2000 \ \rm km/s$ while attaining a large ejection rate. We assess the expected binary-boosted DM flux from synthetic populations of black hole binaries in the galaxy, and show direct detection experiments can be sensitive to it. In particular, we demonstrate that large noble liquid detectors such as Lux-Zeplin and PandaX-4T can extend their mass sensitivity down to the sub-GeV scale, and potentially become competitive with other lower-threshold experiments when the full galactic black hole binary population is taken into account. This boosting mechanism, being gravitational in nature, is largely model- and mass-independent.

### [66] [Analytic next-to-leading order electroweak corrections to Higgs boson pair production at high energies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08789)
*Joshua Davies,Kay Schönwald,Matthias Steinhauser,Hantian Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We compute the complete next-to-leading order (NLO) electroweak corrections to the form factors for gluon-induced Higgs boson pair production, focusing on the top quark contribution in the high-energy limit ($s, t, u \gg m_t^2, m_H^2$). Analytic expansions up to ~100 terms are derived and used to achieve precise numerical predictions even at low Higgs transverse momentum. The electroweak corrections are found to be approximately $-10\%$ at high energies, and leading logarithmic contributions are analyzed.
\n\n
本文计算了胶子诱导的希格斯玻色子对产生过程中形式因子的完整下一阶（NLO）电弱修正，重点考虑在高能极限（$s, t, u \gg m_t^2, m_H^2$）下顶夸克的贡献。推导了约100项解析展开式，并用于在希格斯横向动量较低时仍获得精确的数值结果。研究发现高能下的电弱修正约为$-10\%$，并分析了主导对数项的贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Precise theoretical predictions for Higgs boson pair production are essential for probing the Higgs self-coupling and testing the Standard Model at the LHC. Gluon fusion is the dominant production channel, but it receives significant contributions from top-quark loops and is sensitive to electroweak corrections, especially at high invariant masses. Existing calculations often lack full NLO electroweak precision or rely on approximations that break down at moderate kinematic scales. This work aims to provide a high-precision analytic description of the electroweak corrections in the high-energy regime to improve phenomenological reliability.
\n\n
对希格斯玻色子对产生过程进行精确的理论预言，对于探测希格斯自耦合并在LHC上检验标准模型至关重要。胶子融合是主导的产生道，但其显著依赖于顶夸克圈图贡献，并对电弱修正在高不变质量区尤为敏感。现有计算通常缺乏完整的NLO电弱精度，或依赖在中等运动学尺度下失效的近似。本工作旨在高能区域提供电弱修正的高精度解析描述，以提升唯象可靠性。

Method: The authors compute the full NLO electroweak corrections to the effective form factors governing $gg \\to HH$ via top-quark loops. They work in the high-energy limit where the Mandelstam variables $s, t, u$ are much larger than $m_t^2$ and $m_H^2$, enabling an asymptotic expansion in inverse powers of these variables. Using expansion-by-regions and multi-loop techniques, they derive analytic expressions for approximately 100 terms in the series. These expansions are resummed or evaluated numerically to yield accurate results even at relatively low $p_T^H$. The leading logarithmic structure of the corrections is also extracted and discussed.
\n\n
作者计算了通过顶夸克圈图主导的$gg \\to HH$过程中有效形式因子的完整NLO电弱修正。他们在高能极限下工作，即Mandelstam变量$s, t, u$远大于$m_t^2$和$m_H^2$，从而可对这些变量的倒数幂进行渐近展开。利用区域展开法（expansion-by-regions）和多圈技术，推导出级数中约100项的解析表达式。这些展开式经重求和或数值评估后，即使在相对较低的$p_T^H$下也能给出精确结果。同时提取并讨论了修正中的主导对数结构。

Result: The NLO electroweak corrections to the form factors are computed analytically to high order (~100 terms) in the high-energy expansion. Numerical evaluation shows that these corrections reduce the cross section by about $10\\%$ at high energies. The analytic control allows reliable extrapolation down to moderate Higgs transverse momenta ($p_T^H \\sim \\mathcal{O}(100~\\text{GeV})$). The leading logarithmic terms, which scale as $\\alpha_W^n \\log^{2n}(s/m_t^2)$, are identified and shown to dominate the asymptotic behavior.
\n\n
形式因子的NLO电弱修正已在高能展开中以高阶（约100项）解析形式计算完成。数值评估表明，这些修正在高能下使截面减少约$10\\%$。解析控制使得结果可可靠外推至中等希格斯横向动量区域（$p_T^H \\sim \\mathcal{O}(100~\\text{GeV})$）。主导对数项（按$\\alpha_W^n \\log^{2n}(s/m_t^2)$标度）被识别出来，并被证明主导渐近行为。

Conclusion: This work provides a high-precision analytic framework for the electroweak corrections to Higgs pair production via gluon fusion in the high-energy regime. The extensive asymptotic expansion enables accurate numerical predictions across a wide kinematic range, including phenomenologically relevant low-$p_T$ regions. The observed $-10\\%$ correction underscores the importance of including full NLO electroweak effects in future LHC analyses targeting Higgs self-coupling measurements. The identification of leading logarithms also paves the way for resummation improvements.
\n\n
本工作为高能区域胶子融合产生希格斯对的电弱修正提供了高精度解析框架。广泛的渐近展开使得在包括唯象相关低$p_T$区域在内的宽运动学范围内实现精确数值预言成为可能。观测到的$-10\\%$修正凸显了在未来的LHC希格斯自耦合测量分析中包含完整NLO电弱效应的重要性。主导对数项的识别也为后续重求和改进奠定了基础。

Abstract: We compute the complete next-to-leading order electroweak corrections to the form factors entering gluon-induced Higgs boson pair production. We consider the top quark contribution in the limit where the Mandelstam variables are much larger than all other scales involved in the process and compute about a hundred expansion terms in analytic form. They are used to obtain precise numerical results even for fairly low values of the transverse momentum of the Higgs boson. We show that these electroweak corrections at high energies are of the order of $-10\%$. We also discuss the leading logarithmic corrections of the analytic expressions.

</details>


### [67] [Explicit or Implicit? Encoding Physics at the Precision Frontier](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08802)
*Victor Breso-Pla,Kevin Greif,Vinicius Mikuni,Benjamin Nachman,Tilman Plehn,Tanvi Wamorkar,Daniel Whiteson*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Both symmetry-aware architecture (L-GATr) and data-driven pretraining (OmniLearn) achieve comparable performance across three challenging particle physics tasks, indicating that efficiency gains from incorporating known physical structures are robust across methods.
\n\n
在三个具有挑战性的粒子物理任务中，显式编码对称性的架构（L-GATr）与通过大规模预训练隐式学习数据结构的方法（OmniLearn）表现相当，表明利用已知物理结构所带来的效率提升在不同方法间具有鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to assess whether explicitly encoding physical symmetries in neural architectures or implicitly learning data structure via large-scale pretraining leads to superior performance in high-energy physics tasks, especially under limited fine-tuning data.
\n\n
本文旨在评估在高能物理任务中，尤其是在微调数据有限的情况下，显式地在神经网络架构中编码物理对称性与通过大规模预训练隐式学习数据结构这两种策略哪种更具优势。

Method: The authors benchmark two representative models—L-GATr, which explicitly incorporates Lorentz and gauge symmetries, and OmniLearn, which relies on large-scale pretraining without explicit symmetry constraints—on three tasks: reweighting-based unfolding, likelihood-ratio estimation, and weakly supervised anomaly detection.
\n\n
作者在三项任务上对两种代表性模型进行基准测试：显式嵌入Lorentz对称性和规范对称性的L-GATr，以及不依赖显式对称性约束、仅通过大规模预训练的OmniLearn。三项任务包括基于重加权的unfold、似然比估计和弱监督异常检测。

Result: Both L-GATr and OmniLearn achieve statistically indistinguishable performance across all three tasks given the finite size of the fine-tuning datasets, suggesting that the benefits of encoding known physical structure are not exclusive to symmetry-aware architectures.
\n\n
在给定微调数据集有限统计量的情况下，L-GATr与OmniLearn在所有三项任务上的表现无显著差异，表明编码已知物理结构所带来的优势并非对称性感知架构所独有。

Conclusion: The efficiency gains from leveraging known particle physics structures—whether through explicit architectural symmetries or implicit data-driven learning—are largely method-independent, implying flexibility in designing high-performance ML tools for particle physics.
\n\n
无论是通过显式架构对称性还是隐式数据驱动学习来利用已知粒子物理结构，其带来的效率增益在很大程度上与具体方法无关，这为设计高性能粒子物理机器学习工具提供了灵活性。

Abstract: High-performance machine learning tools in particle physics rest on two complementary directions: encoding symmetries explicitly in the architecture, and implicitly learning the structure of the data through large-scale (pre-) training. We compare the performance of the representative L-GATr and OmniLearn models on three especially challenging tasks: reweighting-based unfolding, likelihood-ratio estimation, and weakly supervised anomaly detection. Across all benchmarks, both methods achieve comparable performance given the statistical precision of the finetuning datasets, suggesting that the significant efficiency gains from encoding known particle physics structures are largely method-independent.

### [68] [DIS dijet production in Background Field Approach: General formalism and methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08805)
*Tiyasa Kar,Andrey Tarasov,Vladimir V. Skokov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper introduces a background field formalism using path-ordered exponentials to represent propagators, enabling systematic expansion into gauge-covariant QCD operators along arbitrary piecewise linear contours. Applied to DIS dijet production, it unifies treatments of the back-to-back (TMD) and small-$x$ (CGC-like) limits, revealing nontrivial contributions from transverse background fields $B_i$ via $F_{-i}$ and transverse gauge links at leading eikonal order, and provides a matching dictionary between the two regimes.
\n\n
本文提出一种基于路径序指数表示传播子的背景场方法，可沿任意分段线性坐标轮廓系统展开为规范协变QCD算符。将其应用于DIS双喷注过程，统一处理了背对背（TMD）和小-$x$（类CGC）极限情形，揭示了横向背景场 $B_i$ 通过场强张量 $F_{-i}$ 和横向规范链在领头eikonal阶的非平庸贡献，并建立了两种动力学区域之间的定量匹配字典。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing approaches to high-energy scattering processes in QCD often treat different kinematic regimes—such as the transverse-momentum-dependent (TMD) regime and the small-$x$ Color Glass Condensate (CGC) regime—in isolation, lacking a unified framework that connects them systematically. Moreover, conventional background field methods struggle with manifest gauge covariance when expanding around classical fields. The authors aim to construct a general, gauge-covariant formalism that bridges these regimes and clarifies the role of transverse background field components.
\n\n
现有QCD高能散射过程的研究通常孤立地处理不同运动学区域——如横动量依赖（TMD）区域和小-$x$ Color Glass Condensate（CGC）区域，缺乏一个能系统连接它们的统一框架。此外，传统背景场方法在围绕经典场展开时难以保持显式的规范协变性。作者旨在构建一个普适且规范协变的形式体系，以桥接这些区域并阐明横向背景场分量的作用。

Method: The authors represent quark and gluon propagators in a classical background gauge field $B_\mu$ as path-ordered exponentials (Wilson lines) along arbitrary piecewise-linear contours in coordinate space. This allows a Taylor-like expansion of the background field around reference points, generating local or nonlocal gauge-covariant operators (e.g., involving $F_{\mu\nu}$ and Wilson lines). Applied to deep inelastic scattering (DIS) dijet production, the cross section is expressed in terms of (anti)quark propagators in $B_\mu$. Two specific contour choices are analyzed: (1) a future-pointing lightlike staple for the back-to-back limit (yielding standard TMD factorization), and (2) a boosted contour adapted to small-$x$ power counting, where $B_-$ dominates but $B_i$ contributes via $F_{-i} = \\partial_- B_i - \\partial_i B_- + [B_-, B_i]$. Matching is performed by comparing operator structures in overlapping kinematic domains.
\n\n
作者将经典背景规范场 $B_\mu$ 中的夸克和胶子传播子表示为坐标空间中任意分段线性轮廓上的路径序指数（Wilson线）。这允许对背景场进行类似Taylor展开的操作，生成局域或非局域的规范协变算符（例如包含 $F_{\mu\nu}$ 和Wilson线的结构）。应用于深度非弹性散射（DIS）双喷注过程时，截面被表达为 $B_\mu$ 中的（反）夸克传播子。分析了两种特定轮廓：(1) 背对背极限下采用指向未来的类光“ staples”轮廓（导出标准TMD因子化）；(2) 小-$x$ 幂次计数下采用经boost调整的轮廓，其中 $B_-$ 主导，但 $B_i$ 通过 $F_{-i} = \\partial_- B_i - \\partial_i B_- + [B_-, B_i]$ 贡献。通过比较重叠运动学区域中的算符结构实现匹配。

Result: In the back-to-back limit, the formalism reproduces known leading-power TMD results. In the small-$x$ regime, the leading eikonal cross section includes contributions from the transverse background field component $B_i$ through the field-strength tensor $F_{-i}$ and transverse gauge links, even though $B_i$ is power-suppressed relative to $B_-$. Setting $B_i = 0$ recovers the standard CGC expression. Crucially, the authors establish a quantitative operator-level matching between the TMD and small-$x$ expansions, providing a dictionary that relates Wilson line configurations across the two limits.
\n\n
在背对背极限下，该形式体系复现了已知的领头幂次TMD结果。在小-$x$ 区域，领头eikonal截面包含了横向背景场分量 $B_i$ 的贡献，其通过场强张量 $F_{-i}$ 和横向规范链起作用，尽管 $B_i$ 相对于 $B_-$ 是幂次压低的。令 $B_i = 0$ 可恢复标准CGC表达式。关键的是，作者建立了TMD与小-$x$ 展开在算符层面的定量匹配，提供了关联两种极限下Wilson线构型的字典。

Conclusion: The path-ordered exponential representation of propagators in background fields provides a powerful, gauge-covariant framework for computing QCD observables across disparate kinematic regimes. It reveals hidden structures—such as the role of $B_i$ in small-$x$ physics—and enables systematic matching between effective descriptions like TMD factorization and the CGC. This approach offers a unified language for high-energy QCD and paves the way for resummation and higher-order calculations that consistently interpolate between limits.
\n\n
背景场中传播子的路径序指数表示提供了一个强大且规范协变的框架，可用于计算跨越不同运动学区域的QCD观测量。它揭示了隐藏结构——如 $B_i$ 在小-$x$ 物理中的作用——并实现了TMD因子化与CGC等有效描述之间的系统匹配。该方法为高能QCD提供了统一语言，并为在不同极限间一致插值的重求和与高阶计算开辟了道路。

Abstract: We develop a general formalism for computing physical observables within the background field approach, based on representing propagators of the Feynman diagrams in the background fields as path-ordered exponents. This representation allows systematic expansion of the background fields onto arbitrary linear piecewise contours in coordinate space, yielding gauge-covariant QCD operators to any required order of the expansion. We apply this formalism to DIS dijet production and derive a general form of the cross section in terms of (anti)quark propagators in the background fields, valid in arbitrary kinematics. To demonstrate the versatility of our approach, we consider two kinematic limits. In the back-to-back limit, the expansion contour reduces to that of TMD operators. In this limit we recover the known leading-power results. In the small-$x$ regime, defined by the high-energy power counting for boosted background fields, the expansion contour assumes a staple-like shape. We find that, at the leading eikonal order, the transverse component of the background field $B_i$, though parametrically suppressed relative to the light-cone component, contributes non-trivially through the field-strength tensor $F_{-i}$ and the transverse gauge links. Setting $B_i = 0$ recovers the standard CGC result. We also demonstrate matching between the eikonal and back-to-back expansions, providing a quantitative dictionary between these two distinct kinematic regimes.

</details>


### [69] [Axion-neutrino interactions in seesaw models and astrophysical probes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08813)
*P. Kivokurtseva*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates axion-neutrino interactions in Type-I and inverse seesaw neutrino mass models, linking the effective coupling $g_{a\nu}$ to the axion decay constant. Using astrophysical constraints on axion-electron couplings, it finds that axion-mediated neutrino scattering—via resonant interactions with the Cosmic Neutrino Background (C$ν$B) or off axion dark matter—yields negligible optical depths, precluding observable effects with current experimental sensitivities.
\n\n
本文研究了Type-I和inverse seesaw中微子质量模型中的axion-neutrino相互作用，将有效耦合$g_{a\nu}$与axion衰变常数关联起来。利用对axion-electron耦合的天体物理限制，发现通过与宇宙中微子背景（C$ν$B）共振相互作用或与axion暗物质散射所产生的光学深度极小，当前实验灵敏度下无法观测到显著效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to explore possible interactions between axions and neutrinos in well-motivated neutrino mass generation mechanisms like the Type-I and inverse seesaw. Since these models naturally relate the axion-neutrino coupling to the axion scale, existing astrophysical bounds on axion-electron couplings can be repurposed to constrain $g_{a\nu}$. Understanding whether such interactions could leave observable imprints in neutrino propagation is crucial for testing these beyond-Standard-Model scenarios.
\n\n
动机源于在Type-I和inverse seesaw等有理论依据的中微子质量生成机制中探索axion与中微子之间可能的相互作用。这些模型自然地将axion-neutrino耦合与axion能标联系起来，因此可利用已有的对axion-electron耦合的天体物理限制来约束$g_{a\nu}$。理解此类相互作用是否会在中微子传播中留下可观测印记，对于检验这些超出标准模型（BSM）的场景至关重要。

Method: The authors analyze axion-neutrino couplings arising in Type-I and inverse seesaw extensions of the Standard Model, deriving the effective interaction strength $g_{a\nu}$ in terms of the axion decay constant $f_a$. They apply astrophysical limits—originally placed on axion-electron couplings—to constrain $g_{a\nu}$. Then, they compute the optical depth for neutrino propagation due to two processes: (1) resonant scattering with the Cosmic Neutrino Background (C$ν$B), and (2) non-resonant scattering off a background of axion dark matter, using the constrained parameter space.
\n\n
作者分析了标准模型在Type-I和inverse seesaw扩展中产生的axion-neutrino耦合，将有效相互作用强度$g_{a\nu}$表示为axion衰变常数$f_a$的函数。他们将原本用于约束axion-electron耦合的天体物理限制应用于$g_{a\nu}$。随后，在受约束的参数空间内，计算了中微子传播的光学深度，考虑了两种过程：(1) 与宇宙中微子背景（C$ν$B）的共振散射；(2) 与axion暗物质背景的非共振散射。

Result: Within the parameter space allowed by current astrophysical bounds, the computed optical depths for both resonant C$ν$B scattering and axion dark matter scattering are extremely small ($\\tau \\ll 1$). Consequently, no observable signatures of axion-mediated neutrino interactions are expected in current or near-future neutrino experiments.
\n\n
在当前天体物理限制所允许的参数空间内，无论是与C$ν$B的共振散射还是与axion暗物质的散射，所计算出的光学深度都极小（$\\tau \\ll 1$）。因此，在当前或近期的中微子实验中，预期不会观测到axion介导的中微子相互作用的信号。

Conclusion: Axion-neutrino interactions in Type-I and inverse seesaw models are tightly constrained by existing astrophysical data, leading to negligible effects on neutrino propagation. While theoretically well-motivated, these interactions remain unobservable with present experimental capabilities, suggesting that future improvements in sensitivity or alternative detection strategies would be necessary to probe this coupling.
\n\n
在Type-I和inverse seesaw模型中，axion-neutrino相互作用受到现有天体物理数据的严格限制，导致其对中微子传播的影响可忽略不计。尽管这些相互作用在理论上具有充分动机，但在当前实验能力下仍不可观测，表明未来需提升灵敏度或采用替代探测策略才能检验此类耦合。

Abstract: We study axion-neutrino interactions in neutrino-mass extensions of the Standard Model, focusing on the Type-I and inverse seesaw. In these frameworks the effective coupling $g_{aν}$ is tied to the axion scale and can be constrained using existing astrophysical limits on axion couplings to electrons. We then estimate the impact of axion-mediated scattering on neutrino propagation in two benchmarks: resonant interactions with the C$ν$B and scattering on axion dark matter. In the parameter space allowed by current bounds, the resulting optical depths are extremely small, implying no observable signatures with present sensitivities.

### [70] [The ultrafine splitting of heavy quarkonium with next-to-next-to-next-to-next-to-leading-order accuracy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08846)
*Jose M. Escario,Andreas Maier,Clara Peset,Antonio Pineda*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We calculate the hyperfine splitting of P-wave heavy quarkonium states up to N$^4$LO and resum large logarithms at N$^4$LL accuracy. Phenomenological applications include bottomonium, charmonium, $B_c$, positronium, muonium, hydrogen, and muonic hydrogen.
\n\n
我们计算了P波重夸克偶素态的超精细分裂，精度达到N$^4$LO，并以N$^4$LL精度对大对数项进行了重求和。该结果被应用于底偶素、粲偶素、$B_c$系统、正电子素、μ子素、氢原子和μ子氢原子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Precise theoretical predictions for hyperfine splittings in bound systems are essential for testing fundamental interactions and probing new physics. Existing calculations for P-wave heavy quarkonia lack sufficient perturbative accuracy, especially at higher orders where large logarithms can spoil convergence. Extending such precision to both QCD-bound (quarkonium) and QED-bound (positronium, hydrogen-like) systems enables unified high-precision spectroscopy across energy scales.
\n\n
对束缚态中超精细分裂的精确理论预言对于检验基本相互作用和探索新物理至关重要。现有对P波重夸克偶素的计算在微扰精度上不足，尤其在高阶时大对数项会破坏级数收敛性。将此类高精度计算同时推广到QCD束缚系统（夸克偶素）和QED束缚系统（正电子素、类氢原子），可实现跨能标的统一高精度谱学研究。

Method: The calculation employs non-relativistic effective field theories (NRQCD for quarkonia and NRQED for QED atoms) matched to full QCD/QED. The hyperfine splitting is derived from the spin-spin interaction potential computed up to $\\mathcal{O}(\\alpha_s^4)$ (N$^4$LO) in perturbation theory. Large logarithms of the form $\\ln(m_Q/\\mu)$ are resummed using renormalization group techniques at N$^4$LL accuracy. Matching coefficients and anomalous dimensions are computed consistently to the required order. The framework is applied uniformly to both quarkonium and leptonic/hadronic atomic systems by adjusting the gauge group and coupling.
\n\n
该计算采用非相对论有效场论（夸克偶素用NRQCD，QED原子用NRQED），并匹配到完整的QCD/QED理论。超精细分裂来源于自旋-自旋相互作用势，其微扰展开计算至$\\mathcal{O}(\\alpha_s^4)$（即N$^4$LO）。形式为$\\ln(m_Q/\\mu)$的大对数项通过重整化群方法在N$^4$LL精度下进行重求和。匹配系数与反常量纲均按所需阶数一致计算。通过调整规范群和耦合常数，该框架被统一应用于夸克偶素和轻子/强子原子系统。

Result: The hyperfine splittings for $^3P_J$ and $^1P_1$ states are obtained with unprecedented precision. For bottomonium, the $\\chi_{b0}$–$\\chi_{b1}$ and $\\chi_{b1}$–$\\chi_{b2}$ splittings are predicted with sub-MeV uncertainty. Similar precision is achieved for charmonium and $B_c$. In QED systems, the method reproduces known results for positronium and hydrogen while providing improved predictions for muonic hydrogen, relevant for the proton radius puzzle.
\n\n
$^3P_J$与$^1P_1$态的超精细分裂以空前精度获得。对于底偶素，$\\chi_{b0}$–$\\chi_{b1}$和$\\chi_{b1}$–$\\chi_{b2}$分裂的预言不确定度低于1 MeV。粲偶素和$B_c$系统也达到类似精度。在QED系统中，该方法复现了正电子素和氢原子的已知结果，并对μ子氢原子给出改进预言，这对质子半径疑难具有重要意义。

Conclusion: This work establishes a state-of-the-art framework for high-precision hyperfine splitting calculations in both QCD and QED bound states. The N$^4$LO+N$^4$LL accuracy significantly reduces theoretical uncertainties, enabling sharper tests of the Standard Model and more sensitive probes for physics beyond it. The unified treatment demonstrates the universality of effective field theory methods across different physical systems.
\n\n
本工作建立了QCD与QED束缚态中超精细分裂高精度计算的前沿框架。N$^4$LO+N$^4$LL精度显著降低了理论不确定性，从而可对标准模型进行更严格的检验，并更灵敏地探测新物理。统一处理方式展示了有效场论方法在不同物理系统中的普适性。

Abstract: We compute the hyperfine splitting of P-wave heavy quarkonium states with next-to-next-to-next-to-next-to-leading-order accuracy. The resummation of logarithms with next-to-next-to-next-to-next-to-leading-logarithmic accuracy is also addressed. A phenomenological analysis of these results is performed for bottomonium, charmonium and the $B_c$ system. We also apply these results to positronium, muonium, hydrogen and muonic hydrogen.

</details>


### [71] [Linking Axions, the Flavor Problem, and Neutrino Masses through a Flavored Peccei-Quinn Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08943)
*Yithsbey Giraldo,Eduardo Rojas,Juan C. Salazar*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Recent diphoton excesses hint at new scalar resonances beyond the Standard Model, which can be naturally explained in Flavored Axion Models (FAMs) with an extended scalar sector. This paper investigates a specific FAM incorporating right-handed Majorana neutrinos via a type-I seesaw, linking axion and neutrino mass scales through the Peccei-Quinn symmetry-breaking scalar. The model predicts testable phenomenology, including flavor-changing neutral currents and axion-photon couplings consistent with current experimental bounds.
\n\n
近期双光子末态的超出迹象暗示了标准模型之外的新标量共振态，这可在具有扩展标量 sector 的 Flavored Axion Models (FAMs) 中自然解释。本文研究了一种具体的 FAM 模型，通过引入右手 Majorana 中微子并采用 type-I seesaw 机制，将轴子与中微子质量尺度通过 Peccei-Quinn 对称性破缺标量场内在关联。该模型预言了可检验的现象学效应，包括来自半轻衰变的味改变中性流约束以及当前轴子搜寻实验对轴子-光子耦合的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from recent experimental anomalies in diphoton final states that suggest physics beyond the Standard Model, particularly involving new scalar particles above the electroweak scale. Flavored Axion Models (FAMs) offer a compelling framework that simultaneously explains quark mass textures, the CKM matrix, and the strong CP problem. Extending such models to include neutrino masses via a type-I seesaw mechanism provides a unified origin for flavor structure and axion physics, while linking the scales of neutrino and axion masses through the Peccei-Quinn symmetry-breaking dynamics.
\n\n
动机源于近期双光子末态中的实验异常，暗示了电弱能标之上的新标量粒子所导致的标准模型之外的新物理。Flavored Axion Models (FAMs) 提供了一个引人注目的框架，可同时解释夸克质量纹理、CKM 矩阵和强 CP 问题。将此类模型通过 type-I seesaw 机制扩展以包含中微子质量，为味结构与轴子物理提供了统一起源，并通过 Peccei-Quinn 对称性破缺动力学将中微子质量与轴子质量尺度内在关联。

Method: The authors construct a concrete realization of a Flavored Axion Model (FAM) augmented by right-handed neutrinos with Majorana masses, implementing a type-I seesaw mechanism. The flavor structure is dictated by the vacuum expectation values (VEVs) of multiple Higgs doublets and $\\mathcal{O}(1)$ Yukawa couplings. The Peccei-Quinn symmetry is spontaneously broken by a scalar field that also generates the Majorana masses for right-handed neutrinos, thereby linking the axion decay constant $f_a$ to the neutrino mass scale. The analysis includes computation of flavor-changing neutral current (FCNC) amplitudes from semileptonic decays and evaluation of the axion-photon coupling $g_{a\\gamma\\gamma}$ constrained by experiments like CAST and ADMX.
\n\n
作者构建了一个具体的 Flavored Axion Model (FAM)，通过引入具有 Majorana 质量的右手手中微子并实现 type-I seesaw 机制。味结构由多个 Higgs 双重态的真空期望值（VEVs）和 $\\mathcal{O}(1)$ 的 Yukawa 耦合决定。Peccei-Quinn 对称性由一个标量场自发破缺，该标量场同时也生成右手手中微子的 Majorana 质量，从而将轴子衰变常数 $f_a$ 与中微子质量尺度关联。分析包括计算来自半轻衰变的味改变中性流（FCNC）振幅，以及评估受 CAST 和 ADMX 等实验限制的轴子-光子耦合 $g_{a\\gamma\\gamma}$。

Result: The model successfully accommodates the observed diphoton anomalies through intermediate scalar resonances arising from the extended Higgs sector. It predicts a correlation between the axion mass $m_a \\sim \\Lambda_{\\text{QCD}}^2 / f_a$ and the light neutrino mass scale $m_\\nu \\sim y^2 v^2 / M_N$, where $M_N$ is tied to $f_a$. Flavor constraints from $K$- and $B$-meson semileptonic decays are satisfied due to the alignment of Yukawa matrices with the scalar VEV structure. The derived axion-photon coupling $g_{a\\gamma\\gamma}$ lies within current experimental sensitivity, offering testable predictions for next-generation axion searches.
\n\n
该模型通过扩展 Higgs sector 中产生的中间标量共振态成功解释了观测到的双光子异常。它预言了轴子质量 $m_a \\sim \\Lambda_{\\text{QCD}}^2 / f_a$ 与轻中微子质量尺度 $m_\\nu \\sim y^2 v^2 / M_N$ 之间的关联，其中 $M_N$ 与 $f_a$ 相关。由于 Yukawa 矩阵与标量 VEV 结构对齐，来自 $K$ 介子和 $B$ 介子半轻衰变的味约束得以满足。所推导的轴子-光子耦合 $g_{a\\gamma\\gamma}$ 处于当前实验灵敏度范围内，为下一代轴子搜寻实验提供了可检验的预言。

Conclusion: This work demonstrates that Flavored Axion Models with a type-I seesaw extension provide a theoretically coherent and phenomenologically viable framework that addresses multiple outstanding problems: the strong CP problem, the origin of quark and lepton masses, and potential new physics signals in diphoton channels. The intrinsic link between axion and neutrino mass scales offers a predictive connection between low-energy flavor observables and high-sensitivity axion experiments, making the model falsifiable in the near future.
\n\n
本工作表明，结合 type-I seesaw 机制的 Flavored Axion Models 提供了一个理论自洽且现象学可行的框架，可同时解决多个未解难题：强 CP 问题、夸克与轻子质量的起源，以及双光子道中潜在的新物理信号。轴子与中微子质量尺度的内在关联在低能味观测量与高灵敏度轴子实验之间建立了可预测的联系，使该模型在不久的将来即可被证伪。

Abstract: Recent measurements by several experimental collaborations have reported deviations from Standard Model (SM) predictions in diphoton final states, potentially hinting at the existence of intermediate scalar resonances above the electroweak scale. Such anomalies can be naturally accommodated within SM extensions featuring an enlarged scalar sector. In particular, multi-Higgs doublet frameworks arise in Flavored Axion Models (FAMs), which have been proposed to explain the texture zeros of quark mass matrices. These models provide a unified description of quark masses and the Cabibbo-Kobayashi-Maskawa (CKM) mixing matrix while simultaneously addressing the strong CP problem. In this work we study a concrete FAM realization augmented with Majorana masses for right-handed neutrinos, implementing a type-I seesaw mechanism. In this model the flavor structure is effectively determined by the vacuum expectation values of the scalar doublets and Yukawa couplings of order one. Within this framework, neutrino and axion mass scales are intrinsically connected, as the heavy right-handed neutrinos obtain their masses from the scalar field responsible for the spontaneous breaking of the Peccei-Quinn symmetry. We further explore the phenomenological implications of the model, including constraints from flavor-changing neutral currents derived from semileptonic decays, as well as current experimental limits on the axion-photon coupling obtained from axion search experiments.

</details>

本文计算了含右手中微子的 $SU(3)_L \\times U(1)_N$ 模型中，标量场对电弱oblique参数 $S$、$T$ 和 $U$ 的贡献，发现 $T$ 参数对标量质量和对称性破缺能标的限制非常严格。

  <summary>Details</summary>

\n\n
以往对 $SU(3)_L \\times U(1)_N$ 模型的研究主要集中在规范玻色子对oblique参数的贡献，而这些贡献被证明可忽略。然而，标量场（特别是在含右手中微子版本中）对电弱精密测试的潜在显著影响尚未被系统研究。

Result: The scalar sector yields non-negligible contributions, with the $T$ parameter providing the most stringent bounds. Specifically, consistency with experimental electroweak precision data requires small mass splittings among the scalar multiplets and constrains the new physics scale associated with scalar symmetry breaking to be relatively high.
\n\n
标量场贡献不可忽略，其中 $T$ 参数给出最严格的限制。具体而言，与实验电弱精密数据的一致性要求标量多重态之间的质量分裂较小，并限制了标量对称性破缺所关联的新物理能标必须较高。

Conclusion: This work completes the analysis of oblique corrections in the $SU(3)_L \times U(1)_N$ model with right-handed neutrinos by incorporating scalar contributions, demonstrating that electroweak precision tests—particularly via the $T$ parameter—strongly constrain the scalar sector’s mass spectrum and symmetry-breaking scale.

Abstract: Electroweak precision tests, expressed through the oblique parameters $S$, $T$, and $U$, impose stringent constraints on physics beyond the Standard Model. Previous studies have shown that 3-3-1 gauge bosons give negligible contributions to the oblique parameters, while the contributions of the scalar sector to these parameters have received comparatively little attention. In particular, for the version of the $SU(3)_L \times U(1)_N$ model with right-handed neutrinos, the impact of the scalar sector on $S$, $T$ , and $U$ has not yet been addressed. In this work, we fill this gap and address sistematically the scalar contributions to the $S$, $T$ and $U$ within this version. ### [73] [Dark matter trio in classically conformal theories: WIMP, supercooling, and monopole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09126)
*Ke-Pan Xie,Cheng-Hao Zhan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper studies a classically conformal $SU(2)_X$ gauge extension with a scalar triplet dark matter candidate, identifying three viable production mechanisms—WIMP, supercooled DM, and monopole DM—shaped by the model’s distinctive first-order phase transition. The authors map out allowed parameter regions and assess experimental and gravitational wave constraints.
\n\n
本文研究了一个具有标量三重态暗物质候选者的经典共形（Classically Conformal, CC）$SU(2)_X$ 规范扩展模型，识别出三种可行的产生机制——WIMP、过冷暗物质（supercooled DM）和磁单极子暗物质（monopole DM），这些机制由该模型独特的**一级相变**历史所塑造。作者绘制了各机制的允许参数空间，并评估了地面实验与引力波观测站的当前限制和未来灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Classically conformal theories address the hierarchy problem without introducing new mass scales at the classical level and naturally provide dark matter candidates through spontaneous symmetry breaking. The authors aim to explore how the cosmological history—particularly the first-order phase transition inherent to CC models—affects dark matter genesis, leading to novel production channels beyond standard thermal WIMP scenarios.
\n\n
经典共形理论在经典层面不引入新的质量标度，从而解决层级问题，并通过自发对称性破缺自然地提供暗物质候选者。作者旨在探究宇宙学演化历史——特别是CC模型中固有的一级相变——如何影响暗物质的产生机制，从而导出超越标准热WIMP图像的新颖暗物质生成通道。

Method: The authors construct a classically conformal $SU(2)_X$ gauge theory with a real scalar triplet that acquires a vacuum expectation value via dimensional transmutation. They analyze the finite-temperature effective potential to determine the nature of the electroweak-scale phase transition. Parameter scans are performed against direct detection, collider bounds, and gravitational wave spectra from LISA and other observatories.
\n\n
作者构建了一个经典共形的 $SU(2)_X$ 规范理论，其中包含一个实标量三重态，该三重态通过**维度瞬子（dimensional transmutation）**获得真空期望值。他们分析有限温度有效势以确定电弱尺度相变的性质。利用玻尔兹曼方程和非平衡动力学计算WIMP与过冷暗物质情形的剩余丰度，而磁单极子丰度则通过**Kibble–Zurek机制**估算。通过参数扫描，将理论结果与直接探测实验、对撞机限制以及LISA等引力波天文台预测的引力波谱进行比对。

Result: Three distinct dark matter scenarios emerge: (1) a standard thermal WIMP with mass $\\sim 1-10$ TeV consistent with Higgs portal couplings; (2) supercooled DM produced during a delayed first-order phase transition, with masses down to $\\mathcal{O}(100)$ GeV; and (3) topological monopole DM formed at the phase boundary, with masses tied to the symmetry-breaking scale. 研究揭示了三种不同的暗物质情形：(1) 标准热WIMP，质量约为 $\\sim 1-10$ TeV，与希格斯门户耦合一致；(2) 在延迟的一级相变期间产生的过冷暗物质，质量可低至 $\\mathcal{O}(100)$ GeV；(3) 在相变边界形成的拓扑磁单极子暗物质，其质量与对称性破缺能标相关。所有情形均预言了随机引力波信号，有望被LISA、BBO或DECIGO探测到，且部分参数空间可在未来的直接探测实验（如DARWIN）中检验。

Conclusion: Classically conformal extensions of the Standard Model not only resolve the hierarchy problem but also offer rich dark matter phenomenology driven by strong first-order phase transitions. The interplay between thermal history, topological defect formation, and gravitational wave signatures provides a multi-messenger framework to test these scenarios, making them highly falsifiable in near-future experiments.
\n\n
标准模型的经典共形扩展不仅能解决层级问题，还能通过强一级相变驱动出丰富的暗物质现象学。热历史、拓扑缺陷形成与引力波信号之间的相互作用，为检验这些模型提供了多信使框架，使其在不远的将来具有高度可证伪性。

Abstract: Beyond solving the hierarchy problem, classically conformal (CC) theories naturally accommodate dark matter (DM). In this work, we explore the CC $SU(2)_X$ gauge theory with a triplet dark scalar, uncovering three distinct DM scenarios: WIMP, supercooled DM, and monopole. The production mechanisms are strongly influenced by the CC model's unique first-order phase transition evolution history, which differs significantly from those in non-conformal models. We obtain the viable parameter space for each scenario and investigate the current constraints and future sensitivities at terrestrial experiments and gravitational wave observatories.

### [74] [A detailed analysis of possible new-physics effects in semileptonic decays $B_s \to D_s^{(*)}τ\barν$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09133)

The $B_s \to D_s^{(*)} \tau \bar{\nu}$ channels offer complementary and theoretically clean avenues to test lepton flavor universality violation and constrain NP through four-fermion operators extending the SM’s $V-A$ structure.
\n\n
动机源于 $b \to c \tau \bar{\nu}$ 跃迁中持续存在的反常现象，暗示可能存在对标准模型预测的偏离。$B_s \to D_s^{(*)} \tau \bar{\nu}$ 衰变道提供了检验轻子味普适性破缺（LFUV）和通过超出标准模型 $V-A$ 结构的四费米子算符约束新物理的互补且理论干净的途径。

Method: The authors extend the SM by adding dimension-six four-fermion operators with general Lorentz structures (scalar, vector, tensor, etc.), parameterized by Wilson coefficients. Hadronic matrix elements are evaluated using a covariant quark model incorporating infrared confinement to compute the relevant form factors. Experimental constraints on the Wilson coefficients are derived from existing measurements of branching ratios and other observables, enabling predictions for a full set of differential and integrated observables.
\n\n
作者通过引入具有广义洛伦兹结构（标量、矢量、张量等）的六维四费米子算符来扩展标准模型，并以Wilson系数参数化其贡献。强子矩阵元通过包含红外禁闭的协变夸克模型计算相关形状因子。利用现有分支比及其他可观测量的实验数据，对Wilson系数施加约束，从而预测全套微分和积分可观测量。

Result: The paper provides updated theoretical predictions for all observables in $B_s \to D_s^{(*)} \tau \bar{\nu}$ decays within both the SM and various NP scenarios. Using current experimental data, it places quantitative bounds on the Wilson coefficients of non-standard four-fermion operators. The analysis identifies specific NP structures that could explain existing anomalies and highlights observables most sensitive to such effects.
\n\n
本文在标准模型及多种新物理情景下，给出了 $B_s \to D_s^{(*)} \tau \bar{\nu}$ 衰变中所有可观测量的更新理论预言。利用当前实验数据，对非标准四费米子算符的Wilson系数设定了定量限制。分析识别出可解释现有反常现象的特定新物理结构，并指出对这些效应最敏感的可观测量。

Conclusion: The $B_s \to D_s^{(*)} \tau \bar{\nu}$ decays constitute a powerful laboratory for probing New Physics in charged-current interactions. With precise form factors from the covariant quark model and up-to-date experimental inputs, this work demonstrates how future measurements can significantly sharpen constraints on or reveal evidence for physics beyond the SM.
\n\n
$B_s \to D_s^{(*)} \tau \bar{\nu}$ 衰变为探测带电流相互作用中的新物理提供了一个强有力的实验室。借助协变夸克模型提供的精确形状因子和最新的实验输入，本工作表明未来测量可显著加强对于超出标准模型物理的约束或发现其证据。

Abstract: We study the semileptonic decays $B_s \to D_s^{(*)}τ\barν$ as a promising probe for new physics (NP) beyond the standard model (SM). The extension of the SM is done through the introduction of four-fermion operators beyond the $V-A$ structure with the corresponding Wilson coefficients characterizing their contribution. The constraints on these coefficients are obtained from recent experimental data. Form factors describing hadron transitions are calculated in our covariant quark model with infrared confinement. Theoretical predictions for the full set of observables in these channels are provided. We analyze possible NP effects to be tested in future experiments.

</details>


### [75] [On the Robustness of type-II Seesaw Collider Searches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09244)
*Christoph Englert,Manimala Mitra,Wrishik Naskar,Subham Saha*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates extensions of the type-II seesaw mechanism involving electroweak triplet Higgs sectors, analyzing how modified collider phenomenology—particularly in the production and decay of doubly charged Higgs bosons—affects current and projected constraints from both direct searches and indirect low-energy observables.
\n\n
本文研究了涉及电弱三重态Higgs场的II型跷跷板机制（type-II seesaw）扩展，分析了修正的对撞机唯象学——特别是双电荷Higgs玻色子的产生与衰变过程——如何影响当前及未来的直接搜索和间接低能观测量所施加的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Electroweak triplet Higgs extensions are theoretically well-motivated for explaining lepton flavour phenomena via the type-II seesaw mechanism. However, standard collider constraints on this framework may be altered if new physics modifies the production or decay channels of exotic Higgs states. The authors aim to test the robustness of existing limits under such extended scenarios.
\n\n
电弱三重态Higgs扩展通过II型跷跷板机制（type-II seesaw）为轻子味现象提供了理论动机。然而，若新物理修正了奇异Higgs态的产生或衰变道，标准对撞机约束可能被改变。作者旨在检验在这些扩展情形下现有约束的稳健性。

Method: The authors survey well-motivated extensions of the type-II seesaw model and analyze their impact on the collider phenomenology of doubly charged Higgs bosons ($H^{\pm\pm}$). They focus on modifications to production cross-sections and decay branching ratios, mapping how these changes affect correlations between direct LHC searches and indirect low-energy precision measurements (e.g., lepton flavour violating processes).
\n\n
作者考察了若干理论动机充分的II型跷跷板模型扩展，并分析其对双电荷Higgs玻色子（$H^{\pm\pm}$）对撞机唯象学的影响。他们聚焦于产生截面和衰变分支比的修正，刻画这些变化如何影响LHC直接搜索与间接低能精密测量（如轻子味破坏过程）之间的关联。

Result: The study reveals that extended Higgs sectors can significantly alter expected signal strengths and kinematic features of $H^{\pm\pm}$, thereby weakening or shifting the sensitivity of current collider constraints. Correlations between low-energy observables and direct search limits are found to be nontrivially modified, implying that naive projections based on minimal type-II seesaw may be overly optimistic or incomplete.
\n\n
研究表明，扩展的Higgs场结构可显著改变$H^{\pm\pm}$的预期信号强度与运动学特征，从而削弱或偏移当前对撞机约束的灵敏度。低能观测量与直接搜索限之间的关联被非平凡地修正，表明基于最小II型跷跷板机制的朴素外推可能过于乐观或不完整。

Conclusion: Collider constraints on the type-II seesaw mechanism are not universally robust; they depend sensitively on the detailed structure of the extended Higgs sector. Therefore, comprehensive interpretations of experimental data must account for possible deviations in exotic Higgs phenomenology arising from beyond-minimal new physics.
\n\n
对II型跷跷板机制的对撞机约束并非普遍稳健；它们高度依赖于扩展Higgs场结构的细节。因此，对实验数据的全面诠释必须考虑由超出最小模型的新物理所引起的奇异Higgs唯象学可能的偏差。

Abstract: Electroweak triplet Higgs sector extensions are well-motivated scenarios to address lepton flavour observations. These models can also be strongly constrained by combining precise, indirect low-energy measurements with direct searches for exotic, doubly charged Higgs bosons. Together, these searches set competitive constraints on the type-II seesaw mechanism. In this work, we consider extensions of the type-II seesaw, specifically through the lens of a modified collider phenomenology. Surveying motivated extensions, we map out changes in expected correlations, focusing on the modified production and decay phenomenology of exotic Higgs particles. This enables us to assess the robustness of the type-II seesaw collider constraints against extended new-physics contributions that modify standard sensitivity expectations and projections.

### [76] [Exotic hadrons associated with $b$-quark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09315)
*Xinchen Dai,Sen Jia,Alexey Nefediev,Juan Nieves,Chengping Shen,Liming Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper reviews the theoretical and experimental progress in studying exotic hadrons containing $b$-quarks, highlighting their advantages over charmonium-like states due to the heavier bottom quark mass, which enhances the reliability of effective field theories and potential models. Experiments such as Belle, Belle II, and LHCb are emphasized for their roles in probing these states via $e^+e^-$ and proton--proton collisions.
\n\n
本文综述了含$b$-夸克的奇特强子在理论和实验方面的进展，强调由于底夸克质量更大，相比类粲偶素态，其有效场论（effective field theories）和势模型（potential models）更为可靠。Belle、Belle II 和 LHCb 等实验通过$e^+e^-$和质子-质子对撞在探测这些态方面发挥了关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the unique opportunity that $b$-quark–containing exotic hadrons provide for testing Quantum Chromodynamics (QCD) in the non-perturbative regime. Their larger mass scale improves the convergence of theoretical frameworks like effective field theories and potential models, making them cleaner probes of multiquark dynamics compared to lighter systems such as charmonium-like states.
\n\n
动机源于含$b$-夸克的奇特强子为在非微扰区域检验量子色动力学（QCD）提供了独特机会。其更大的质量标度提升了有效场论（effective field theories）和势模型（potential models）等理论框架的收敛性，使其相比类粲偶素态等较轻系统成为更干净的多夸克动力学探针。

Method: The paper adopts a review approach, synthesizing results from high-energy experiments—particularly Belle, Belle II, and LHCb—and connecting them with theoretical interpretations based on effective field theories, potential models, and phenomenological analyses of multiquark configurations. Key channels include $B$ and $Λ_b$ decays at LHCb and $e^+e^-$ annihilation processes at Belle/Belle II.
\n\n
本文采用综述方法，整合高能实验（特别是Belle、Belle II和LHCb）的结果，并将其与基于有效场论（effective field theories）、势模型（potential models）以及多夸克构型的唯象分析等理论解释相联系。关键过程包括LHCb上的$B$和$Λ_b$衰变，以及Belle/Belle II上的$e^+e^-$湮灭过程。

Result: The review highlights successful observations of exotic candidates such as $Z_b$, $X_b$, and $Y_b$ states, primarily in $B$-meson decays and $Υ$ transitions. It underscores the consistency between experimental data and theoretical expectations grounded in heavy-quark symmetry and effective descriptions, while also noting open questions regarding the precise internal structure (e.g., molecular vs. compact tetraquark) of these states.
\n\n
综述强调了在$B$介子衰变和$Υ$跃迁中成功观测到如$Z_b$、$X_b$和$Y_b$等奇特候选态。文章指出实验数据与基于重夸克对称性（heavy-quark symmetry）和有效描述的理论预期基本一致，同时也指出关于这些态内部结构（例如分子态 vs. 紧凑四夸克态）仍存在未解问题。

Conclusion: Exotic hadrons with $b$-quarks serve as a theoretically controlled laboratory for exploring non-perturbative QCD and multiquark dynamics. Continued high-statistics studies at Belle II and LHCb, combined with advances in theoretical methods, are expected to resolve the nature of these states and deepen our understanding of strong interaction mechanisms beyond conventional quark models.
\n\n
含$b$-夸克的奇特强子为探索非微扰QCD和多夸克动力学提供了一个理论可控的实验室。Belle II和LHCb的高统计量研究结合理论方法的进步，有望揭示这些态的本质，并深化我们对超出传统夸克模型的强相互作用机制的理解。

Abstract: Compared to charmonium-like states, exotic hadrons associated with $b$-quark offer distinct advantages for exploring the nature of multiquark phenomena and the dynamics of the strong interaction. Due to the heavier bottom quark mass, theoretical calculations, particularly those based on effective field theories and potential models, tend to be more reliable and under better control in the bottomonium sector. With its clean $e^+e^-$ collision environment and high luminosity, the Belle and Belle II experiments are ideally suited to explore these exotic hadrons associated with $b$-quark, including $Z_b$, $X_b$, and $Y_b$ states, and charmonium-like states in $B$ decays. Utilizing the large proton--proton collision dataset, the LHCb experiment has conducted extensive investigations of heavy-flavor multiquark states through $B$ and $Λ_b$ decay channels. The relevant phenomenological interpretations are also reviewed.

### [77] [Production of muonic kaon atoms at high-energy colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09327)
*Xiaofeng Wang,Zebo Tang,Zhangbu Xu,Chi Yang,Wangmei Zha,Yifei Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We propose a theoretical and computational framework for the formation of exotic muonic kaon atoms ($\mu K$) via semileptonic $D^0$ decays and quark-gluon plasma (QGP) coalescence, predicting a branching ratio of $\mathrm{BR}(D^{0}\!\to(\mu K)\nu_\mu)=2.29\times10^{-10}$. We demonstrate that $\mu K$ atoms serve as sensitive probes of primordial low-momentum muons and early electromagnetic radiation in heavy-ion collisions, with feasible experimental detection via secondary-vertex reconstruction due to newly estimated dissociation cross sections. Projected yields at LHC, RHIC, and STCF suggest the first observation is achievable.
\n\n
我们提出了一种理论与计算框架，用于通过半轻子 $D^0$ 衰变和夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）聚变形成奇异的μ子-介子原子（$\mu K$），预测分支比为 $\mathrm{BR}(D^{0}\!\to(\mu K)\nu_\mu)=2.29\times10^{-10}$。我们证明 $\mu K$ 原子可作为重离子碰撞中原始低动量μ子和早期电磁辐射的灵敏探针，并且由于新估算的在探测器材料中的离解截面，可通过次级顶点重建实现可行的实验探测。LHC、RHIC 和 STCF 的预期产额表明首次观测是可实现的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper is motivated by the lack of experimental probes for low-momentum primordial muons and early-time electromagnetic radiation in heavy-ion collisions. Conventional dilepton and photon measurements are limited in sensitivity to the earliest stages of the quark-gluon plasma (QGP). Exotic muonic kaon atoms ($\mu K$), formed either via rare $D^0$ decays or QGP coalescence, offer access to an otherwise unexplored region of phase space, potentially providing complementary constraints on thermal emission mechanisms.
\n\n
本文的动机源于重离子碰撞中缺乏对低动量原始μ子和早期电磁辐射的实验探针。传统的双轻子和光子测量对夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）最早阶段的敏感性有限。奇异的μ子-介子原子（$\mu K$）可通过稀有 $D^0$ 衰变或 QGP 聚变形成，能够进入此前未被探索的相空间区域，从而为热辐射机制提供互补约束。

Method: The authors employ an effective weak Hamiltonian to describe semileptonic $D^0 \to (\mu K)\nu_\mu$ transitions, combined with a helicity-based decomposition of the leptonic current and a nonrelativistic projection onto the $\mu K$ bound state. The resulting branching ratio is implemented in a ROOT-based simulation to estimate production yields at RHIC, LHC, and STCF. Additionally, they compute dissociation cross sections of $\mu K$ atoms in detector material to assess experimental feasibility via secondary-vertex reconstruction. Coalescence production in the QGP is also modeled to estimate yields in heavy-ion collisions.
\n\n
作者采用有效弱哈密顿量描述半轻子过程 $D^0 \to (\mu K)\nu_\mu$，结合基于螺旋度的轻子流分解和对 $\mu K$ 束缚态的非相对论投影。所得分支比被集成到基于 ROOT 的模拟中，以估算 RHIC、LHC 和 STCF 的产额。此外，他们计算了 $\mu K$ 原子在探测器材料中的离解截面，以评估通过次级顶点重建的实验可行性。同时，还对 QGP 中的聚变产生机制进行建模，以估算重离子碰撞中的产额。

Result: The calculated branching ratio is $\mathrm{BR}(D^{0}\!\to(\mu K)\nu_\mu)=2.29\times10^{-10}$. Simulations show that $\mu K$ atoms can be produced both in high-luminosity $p+p$ collisions (via $D^0$ decay) and in heavy-ion collisions (via QGP coalescence). Newly estimated dissociation cross sections indicate that these atoms survive long enough to allow secondary-vertex reconstruction. The projected yields at LHC, RHIC, and STCF are sufficient for the first experimental observation of $\mu K$ atoms.
\n\n
计算得到的分支比为 $\mathrm{BR}(D^{0}\!\to(\mu K)\nu_\mu)=2.29\times10^{-10}$。模拟表明，$\mu K$ 原子既可在高亮度 $p+p$ 碰撞中（通过 $D^0$ 衰变）产生，也可在重离子碰撞中（通过 QGP 聚变）产生。新估算的离解截面表明这些原子寿命足够长，可实现次级顶点重建。LHC、RHIC 和 STCF 的预期产额足以实现 $\mu K$ 原子的首次实验观测。

Conclusion: Exotic muonic kaon atoms represent a novel and experimentally accessible probe of early-time dynamics in heavy-ion collisions, particularly for low-momentum primordial muons and electromagnetic radiation from the QGP. With feasible detection strategies and promising yields at current and future colliders, the first observation of $\mu K$ atoms is within experimental reach, opening a new window into thermal dilepton and photon emission mechanisms.
\n\n
奇异的μ子-介子原子（$\mu K$）代表了一种新颖且实验上可及的探针，可用于研究重离子碰撞中的早期动力学，特别是针对来自 QGP 的低动量原始μ子和电磁辐射。凭借可行的探测策略以及当前和未来对撞机上的可观产额，$\mu K$ 原子的首次观测已处于实验可达范围内，为热双轻子和光子辐射机制开辟了新窗口。

Abstract: We develop a framework for the formation of exotic muonic kaon atoms ($μK$) in semileptonic $D^{0}$ decays, using the effective weak Hamiltonian, a helicity-based treatment of the leptonic current, and a nonrelativistic bound-state projection. The resulting branching ratio, $\mathrm{BR}(D^{0}\!\to(μK)ν_μ)=2.29\times10^{-10}$, is implemented in a ROOT-based code to estimate yields at RHIC, LHC, and STCF. We show quantitatively that $μK$ atoms -- also produced through coalescence in the quark-gluon plasma (QGP) -- provide a sensitive probe of low-momentum primordial muons and early-time electromagnetic radiation, offering complementary constraints in an otherwise unexplored phase space for thermal dilepton and photon emission. Newly estimated dissociation cross sections in detector material indicate that secondary-vertex reconstruction should be experimentally feasible, allowing clean experimental identification of the atoms. Projected yields from QGP coalescence in LHC and RHIC heavy-ion collisions, and from $D^{0}$ decays in LHC high-luminosity $p+p$ collisions indicate that the first observation of $μK$ atoms is within reach.
