### [78] [Extracting freeze-out conditions in beam energy scan via functional QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09336)
*Yi Lu,Christian S. Fischer,Fei Gao,Yu-xin Liu,Jan M. Pawlowski*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper establishes a connection between theoretical QCD predictions and experimental heavy-ion collision data by matching ratios of baryon number susceptibilities from functional QCD with proton cumulants measured in experiments. This matching uniquely determines the freeze-out temperature and chemical potential at each collision energy. Using these self-consistently determined freeze-out parameters, the authors predict the kurtosis along the freeze-out line, finding good agreement with existing data and identifying a peak near 5 GeV that signals the QCD critical end point.
\n\n
本文通过将泛函QCD方法计算的重子数susceptibility比值与实验中提取的质子累积量进行匹配，建立了理论QCD预言与重离子碰撞实验数据之间的联系。这种匹配在每个碰撞能量下唯一确定了冻结参数（温度和化学势）。利用这些自洽确定的冻结参数，作者预测了冻结线上的峰度（kurtosis），与现有实验数据定量吻合，并在约5 GeV处发现一个峰结构，表明QCD临界端点（critical end point）的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Fluctuations of conserved charges, such as baryon number, are sensitive probes of the QCD phase structure and can be computed precisely in theoretical frameworks like functional QCD. Simultaneously, high-precision measurements of proton number cumulants in heavy-ion collisions provide experimental access to these fluctuations. However, a direct comparison is nontrivial because theory computes baryon fluctuations while experiments measure proton fluctuations. The motivation is to bridge this gap by assuming that the ratios of low-order susceptibilities are universal enough to allow matching, thereby enabling a self-consistent determination of the chemical freeze-out parameters and a prediction for higher-order cumulants like kurtosis, which may reveal the QCD critical end point.
\n\n
守恒荷（如重子数）的涨落是探测QCD相结构的灵敏探针，可在泛函QCD等理论框架中精确计算。同时，重离子碰撞中质子数累积量的高精度测量为这些涨落提供了实验途径。然而，直接比较并不简单，因为理论计算的是重子涨落，而实验测量的是质子涨落。本文的动机在于假设低阶susceptibility比值具有足够的普适性，从而允许理论与实验匹配，由此实现对化学冻结参数的自洽确定，并进一步预测高阶累积量（如峰度kurtosis），以揭示QCD临界端点。

Method: The authors employ functional methods in QCD (e.g., Dyson-Schwinger equations or functional renormalization group) to compute the lowest-order baryon number susceptibilities $\\chi_1^B$, $\\chi_2^B$, etc., as functions of temperature $T$ and baryon chemical potential $\\mu_B$. They form ratios such as $\\chi_1^B/\\chi_2^B$ and compare them with the corresponding ratios of proton number cumulants ($C_1/C_2$, etc.) measured in heavy-ion collision experiments at various beam energies $\\sqrt{s_{NN}}$. For each collision energy, they identify the unique $(T, \\mu_B)$ point where the theoretical and experimental ratios coincide—this defines the freeze-out point. Using this determined freeze-out line, they then compute the theoretical prediction for the kurtosis, defined as $\\kappa \\sigma^2 = \\chi_4^B / \\chi_2^B$, along the same line.
\n\n
作者采用QCD中的泛函方法（如Dyson-Schwinger方程或泛函重整化群）计算最低阶重子数susceptibility（如$\\chi_1^B$、$\\chi_2^B$等）作为温度$T$和重子化学势$\\mu_B$的函数。他们构建比值（如$\\chi_1^B/\\chi_2^B$），并与不同束流能量$\\sqrt{s_{NN}}$下重离子碰撞实验中测得的质子数累积量比值（如$C_1/C_2$等）进行比较。对于每个碰撞能量，他们找出理论与实验比值一致的唯一点$(T, \\mu_B)$——该点即为冻结点。利用由此确定的冻结线，他们进一步计算沿该线的峰度理论预言，定义为$\\kappa \\sigma^2 = \\chi_4^B / \\chi_2^B$。

Result: The comparison yields a self-consistent freeze-out line in the QCD phase diagram, parameterized by collision energy. Along this line, the predicted kurtosis $\\kappa \\sigma^2 = \\chi_4^B / \\chi_2^B$ shows quantitative agreement with available experimental data for proton kurtosis, despite the mismatch between baryons (theory) and protons (experiment). Notably, the kurtosis exhibits a pronounced peak at a collision energy of approximately 5 GeV, which the authors interpret as a signature of the QCD critical end point.
\n\n
比较结果在QCD相图中得到了一条自洽的冻结线，由碰撞能量参数化。沿此线，预测的峰度$\\kappa \\sigma^2 = \\chi_4^B / \\chi_2^B$与现有质子峰度实验数据定量吻合，尽管理论（重子）与实验（质子）存在不匹配。值得注意的是，峰度在约5 GeV的碰撞能量处出现显著峰值，作者将其解释为QCD临界端点的信号。

Conclusion: By matching low-order fluctuation ratios from functional QCD with experimental proton cumulants, the study provides a robust method to determine the chemical freeze-out parameters across beam energies. The resulting prediction for the kurtosis not only validates the approach through agreement with data but also offers compelling evidence for the existence of the QCD critical end point near 5 GeV collision energy. This demonstrates the power of combining first-principles QCD calculations with fluctuation observables in heavy-ion collisions.
\n\n
通过将泛函QCD的低阶涨落比值与实验质子累积量匹配，本研究提供了一种稳健的方法来确定不同束流能量下的化学冻结参数。由此得到的峰度预言不仅通过与数据的一致性验证了该方法，还为QCD临界端点存在于约5 GeV碰撞能量附近提供了有力证据。这展示了将第一性原理QCD计算与重离子碰撞中的涨落观测量相结合的强大能力。

Abstract: Fluctuations of conserved charges provide a link between high quality theoretical results and precision measurements of heavy ion collisions. We compare results for ratios of the lowest order baryon number susceptibilities from functional QCD approaches to proton number cumulants extracted from experiments. We find that they meet at a specific temperature and chemical potential for each collision energy. This is indicative of the respective freeze-out point. From this self-consistent determination of the freeze-out parameters we extract a prediction for the kurtosis on the freeze-out line. We find quantitative agreement with experimental data where available, despite comparing apples (baryons) with oranges (protons). At a collision energy around 5 GeV, our kurtosis exhibits a peak structure indicative of the critical end point of QCD.

</details>


### [79] [Scattering of $Λ_{c}Λ_{c}$ and $Λ_{c}\barΛ_{c}$ in chiral effective field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09404)
*Zhe Liu,Hao Xu,Zhan-Wei Liu,Xiang Liu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper studies $S$-wave scattering in $Λ_cΛ_c$ and $Λ_c\bar{Λ}_c$ systems using chiral effective field theory (χEFT) up to next-to-leading order (NLO). Contact low-energy constants are fixed by lattice QCD data at unphysical pion mass, then extrapolated to physical pion mass. The $Λ_cΛ_c$ interaction in the $I(J^P)=0(0^+)$ channel is repulsive, while $Λ_c\bar{Λ}_c$ shows attractive interactions in both $I(J^{PC})=0(0^{-+})$ and $0(1^{--})$ channels, supporting bound-state formation—especially stronger in the $0(1^{--})$ channel. Two-pion exchange spin-spin terms cause significant mass splitting between these channels.
\n\n
本文在次领头阶（NLO）的幺正手征有效场论（χEFT）框架下研究了 $Λ_cΛ_c$ 和 $Λ_c\bar{Λ}_c$ 系统的 $S$ 波散射。通过拟合非物理π介子质量下的格点QCD相移数据确定接触项低能常数，并外推至物理π介子质量。结果表明，$I(J^P)=0(0^+)$ 的 $Λ_cΛ_c$ 通道呈现排斥相互作用；而 $Λ_c\bar{Λ}_c$ 在 $I(J^{PC})=0(0^{-+})$ 和 $0(1^{--})$ 通道均表现出吸引作用，支持束缚态形成，其中 $0(1^{--})$ 通道吸引力更强。此外，双π交换引起的自旋-自旋项对相互作用贡献显著，导致这两个 $Λ_c\bar{Λ}_c$ 通道之间出现明显的质量劈裂。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the nature of baryon-baryon and baryon-antibaryon interactions involving charm quarks is crucial for exploring exotic hadronic matter and testing QCD in the non-perturbative regime. While lattice QCD provides first-principles results, it is often limited to unphysical quark masses. A systematic framework like chiral effective field theory (χEFT) allows for controlled extrapolation to the physical point and prediction of observables not yet accessible on the lattice, such as $Λ_c\bar{Λ}_c$ scattering.
\n\n
理解含粲夸克的重子-重子及重子-反重子相互作用对于探索奇异强子物质和检验非微扰QCD至关重要。虽然格点QCD提供了第一性原理结果，但通常受限于非物理夸克质量。手征有效场论（χEFT）等系统性框架可实现对物理点的受控外推，并预测格点上尚不可及的观测量（如 $Λ_c\bar{Λ}_c$ 散射）。

Method: The authors employ a unified chiral effective field theory (χEFT) framework up to next-to-leading order (NLO) for both $Λ_cΛ_c$ and $Λ_c\bar{Λ}_c$ systems. The contact interactions are parameterized by low-energy constants (LECs), which are fitted to existing lattice QCD data for the $Λ_cΛ_c$ $S$-wave phase shift at an unphysical pion mass ($m_π ≈ 410$ MeV). The two-pion exchange contributions, including spin-spin and tensor terms, are included at NLO. After fixing the LECs, the theory is extrapolated to the physical pion mass ($m_π ≈ 140$ MeV) to predict phase shifts and potentials for both systems, particularly for the $Λ_c\bar{Λ}_c$ channels where no lattice data exist.
\n\n
作者采用统一的次领头阶（NLO）手征有效场论（χEFT）框架处理 $Λ_cΛ_c$ 和 $Λ_c\bar{Λ}_c$ 系统。接触相互作用由低能常数（LECs）参数化，并通过拟合非物理π介子质量（$m_π ≈ 410$ MeV）下格点QCD给出的 $Λ_cΛ_c$ $S$ 波相移数据来确定。NLO阶包含双π交换贡献，包括自旋-自旋项和张量项。在固定LECs后，将理论外推至物理π介子质量（$m_π ≈ 140$ MeV），以预测两个系统的相移和势，特别是尚无格点数据的 $Λ_c\bar{Λ}_c$ 通道。

Result: At the physical pion mass, the $I(J^P)=0(0^+)$ $Λ_cΛ_c$ interaction is repulsive, consistent with lattice QCD. For $Λ_c\bar{Λ}_c$, attractive potentials are found in both $I(J^{PC})=0(0^{-+})$ and $0(1^{--})$ channels, each capable of forming a bound state. The attraction is stronger in the $0(1^{--})$ channel. The two-pion exchange spin-spin interaction generates a significant mass splitting between these two channels, highlighting its crucial role in the dynamics.
\n\n
在物理π介子质量下，$I(J^P)=0(0^+)$ 的 $Λ_cΛ_c$ 相互作用为排斥，与格点QCD一致。对于 $Λ_c\bar{Λ}_c$，在 $I(J^{PC})=0(0^{-+})$ 和 $0(1^{--})$ 两个通道中均发现吸引势，均可形成束缚态，其中 $0(1^{--})$ 通道吸引力更强。双π交换的自旋-自旋相互作用在这两个通道间产生显著的质量劈裂，凸显其在动力学中的关键作用。

Conclusion: Chiral effective field theory provides a consistent and predictive framework for charm baryon interactions. Using lattice QCD input, the study successfully describes $Λ_cΛ_c$ scattering and predicts novel bound states in the $Λ_c\bar{Λ}_c$ system. The strong attraction in the $0(1^{--})$ channel and the sizable mass splitting due to two-pion exchange suggest that $Λ_c\bar{Λ}_c$ bound states could be observable in future experiments, offering new probes of QCD in the heavy-quark sector.
\n\n
手征有效场论为粲重子相互作用提供了自洽且具预测能力的框架。借助格点QCD输入，本研究成功描述了 $Λ_cΛ_c$ 散射，并预言了 $Λ_c\bar{Λ}_c$ 系统中新的束缚态。$0(1^{--})$ 通道中的强吸引力以及双π交换导致的显著质量劈裂表明，$Λ_c\bar{Λ}_c$ 束缚态可能在未来的实验中被观测到，为探索重夸克区的QCD提供新探针。

Abstract: We investigate the $S$-wave scatterings of $Λ_cΛ_c$ and $Λ_{c}\bar Λ_{c}$ systems within a unified chiral effective field theory framework up to next-to-leading order. The contact low-energy coupling constants are determined by fitting to the lattice QCD results for the $Λ_cΛ_c$ scattering phase shift at an unphysical pion mass. After extrapolating to the physical pion mass, we find a repulsive interaction in the $I(J^P)=0(0^{+})$ $Λ_cΛ_c$ channel, consistent with the lattice QCD simulation. On the $Λ_{c}\bar Λ_{c}$ side, using the fitted contact low-energy constants, we predict the phase shifts and potentials for $Λ_c \barΛ_c$ scattering in the $I(J^{PC})=0(0^{-+})$ and $0(1^{--})$ channels. Attractive interactions are found in both channels, each allowing for the formation of bound states. In particular, the attraction in the $0(1^{--})$ $Λ_c \barΛ_c$ channel is stronger. In addition, our analysis reveals that the spin-spin term caused by the two-pion exchange contributes significantly to the interactions, leading to a distinct mass splitting between the $0(0^{-+})$ and $0(1^{--})$ $Λ_c \barΛ_c$ channels.

</details>


### [80] [Beyond QED: Electroweak and hadronic extensions of McMule](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09443)
*Sophie Kollatzsch*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: McMule is a Monte Carlo framework for computing higher-order QED corrections in low-energy lepton processes; recent upgrades include electroweak effects via low-energy EFT and non-perturbative hadronic contributions using disperon QED, with applications to experiments like MOLLER.
\n\n
McMule 是一个用于计算低能轻子过程中高阶 QED 修正的蒙特卡洛框架；近期升级包括通过低能有效场论（EFT）纳入电弱效应，以及利用 disperon QED 方法引入非微扰强子贡献，并已应用于 MOLLER 等实验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Precision measurements in low-energy lepton scattering and decays demand high-order radiative corrections. Standard perturbative QED is insufficient when electroweak or non-perturbative hadronic effects become relevant. McMule addresses this by systematically incorporating such effects within consistent theoretical frameworks—low-energy EFT for electroweak corrections and disperon QED for hadronic vacuum polarisation and pion form factors.
\n\n
低能轻子散射与衰变中的精密测量需要高阶辐射修正。当电弱效应或非微扰强子效应变得重要时，标准微扰 QED 不再足够。McMule 通过在一致的理论框架内系统地纳入这些效应来解决此问题——使用低能有效场论（EFT）处理电弱修正，使用 disperon QED 处理强子真空极化与 π 介子形状因子。

Method: The paper employs two complementary theoretical approaches: (1) a low-energy effective field theory (EFT) to capture electroweak corrections below the weak scale, enabling systematic inclusion of $\\gamma$-$Z$ mixing; and (2) disperon QED, which combines OpenLoops (for automated one-loop amplitudes) with dispersion relations and EFT to model non-perturbative hadronic vacuum polarisation and pion electromagnetic form factors in loop diagrams. Careful matching between OpenLoops and the EFT expansion ensures consistency in power counting and infrared behavior.
\n\n
本文采用两种互补的理论方法：(1) 使用低能有效场论（EFT）捕捉弱标度以下的电弱修正，从而系统地纳入 $\\gamma$-$Z$ 混合效应；(2) disperon QED 方法，将 OpenLoops（用于自动计算单圈振幅）与色散关系及 EFT 相结合，以在圈图中建模非微扰强子真空极化与 π 介子电磁形状因子。通过仔细匹配 OpenLoops 与 EFT 展开，确保幂次计数和红外行为的一致性。

Result: The extended McMule framework successfully incorporates both electroweak and non-perturbative hadronic effects at NNLO precision. Applied to the MOLLER experiment, it reveals that the choice of model for non-perturbative $\\gamma$-$Z$ mixing significantly impacts the predicted asymmetry, highlighting the need for consistent EFT-based treatment. The disperon QED implementation demonstrates how OpenLoops can be aligned with EFT power counting without double-counting or violating analyticity.
\n\n
扩展后的 McMule 框架成功在 NNLO 精度下纳入了电弱与非微扰强子效应。将其应用于 MOLLER 实验表明，非微扰 $\\gamma$-$Z$ 混合所采用的模型对预测的不对称性有显著影响，凸显了基于 EFT 的一致处理的必要性。disperon QED 的实现展示了如何在不重复计数或破坏解析性的前提下，使 OpenLoops 与 EFT 幂次展开保持一致。

Conclusion: McMule’s recent advances establish a robust, EFT-consistent framework for precision predictions in low-energy lepton physics, bridging perturbative QED, electroweak corrections, and non-perturbative hadronic effects. This paves the way for reliable theoretical inputs to next-generation parity-violating electron scattering experiments like MOLLER.
\n\n
McMule 的最新进展建立了一个稳健且符合 EFT 的框架，用于低能轻子物理中的精密预言，成功衔接了微扰 QED、电弱修正与非微扰强子效应。这为 MOLLER 等下一代宇称破坏电子散射实验提供了可靠的理论输入。

Abstract: McMule is a Monte Carlo framework developed to advance the low-energy precision frontier by providing QED corrections to leptonic scattering and decay processes, currently up to next-to-next-to-leading order. Recent developments have extended its capabilities in two important directions: the systematic inclusion of electroweak effects at low energies within the low-energy effective field theory [arXiv:2507.17652], and the incorporation of pion form factors and the non-perturbative hadronic vacuum polarisation in loop amplitudes through a combination of OpenLoops and effective field theory techniques, referred to as disperon QED [arXiv:2512.10709]. I will provide an overview of McMule and discuss these recent extensions and their applications. In particular, I will illustrate the impact of the model used for non-perturbative $γ$-$Z$ mixing effects in the context of the MOLLER experiment and highlight the subtlety involved in consistently aligning OpenLoops with its effective field theory expansion in disperon QED.

### [81] [Vector-like dark matter within an alternative left-right symmetric model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09444)
*Yassine Bouzeraib,Mohamed Sadek Zidi,Geneviève Bélanger*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study a left-right symmetric model extended by an extra $SU(2)$ gauge group with vector-like leptons, where the neutral component serves as a stable TeV-scale dark matter candidate. Its stability arises from a discrete parity symmetry, and interactions with the Standard Model occur via vector and vector-like lepton portals. We constrain the model using relic density, collider limits, and direct/indirect detection data, and explore future sensitivities of XLZD and CTA.
\n\n
我们研究了一种通过额外的 $SU(2)$ 规范群和矢量型轻子扩展的左右对称模型，其中中性组分作为稳定的 TeV 量级暗物质候选者。其稳定性源于离散宇称对称性，与标准模型的相互作用通过矢量门户（vector portal）和矢量型轻子门户（vector-like lepton portal）实现。我们利用遗迹密度、对撞机限制以及直接/间接探测数据约束该模型，并探讨了 XLZD 和 CTA 对未来参数空间的探测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to address the nature of dark matter within a theoretically motivated extension of the Standard Model—specifically, the left-right symmetric model augmented by a new non-abelian $SU(2)$ gauge symmetry. The inclusion of vector-like leptons under this new symmetry offers a natural framework for a stable dark matter candidate without introducing ad hoc stabilizing mechanisms, while maintaining testability through multiple experimental channels.
\n\n
本文旨在在标准模型的一个理论动机明确的扩展框架内——即通过新增非阿贝尔 $SU(2)$ 规范对称性扩展的左右对称模型——探讨暗物质的本质。在此新对称性下引入矢量型轻子，为稳定的暗物质候选者提供了一个自然框架，无需引入特设的稳定机制，同时保持了多通道实验可检验性。

Method: The authors construct a model with an extended gauge group $SU(2)_L \\times SU(2)_R \\times SU(2)_X$, where the new $SU(2)_X$ is associated with vector-like leptons in its fundamental representation. A discrete parity symmetry is imposed to prevent mixing between vector-like and Standard Model leptons, thereby ensuring dark matter stability. The dark matter candidate is the neutral component of the $SU(2)_X$ triplet. Interactions with the visible sector proceed via s-channel exchange of the $W^{\\prime\\pm}$ boson (vector portal) and t-channel exchange of the charged vector-like lepton $E^{\\pm}$ (vector-like lepton portal). The analysis includes relic density calculations, collider constraints on $W^{\\prime\\pm}$ and $E^{\\pm}$ masses, and comparisons with current direct (LZ) and indirect (Fermi-LAT) detection limits. Future sensitivities of XLZD and CTA are also projected.
\n\n
作者构建了一个具有扩展规范群 $SU(2)_L \\times SU(2)_R \\times SU(2)_X$ 的模型，其中新的 $SU(2)_X$ 与处于其基本表示下的矢量型轻子相关联。通过施加离散宇称对称性，禁止矢量型轻子与标准模型轻子之间的混合，从而确保暗物质的稳定性。暗物质候选者是 $SU(2)_X$ 三重态的中性组分。与可见扇区的相互作用通过 $W^{\\prime\\pm}$ 玻色子的 s-道交换（矢量门户）和带电矢量型轻子 $E^{\\pm}$ 的 t-道交换（矢量型轻子门户）进行。分析包括遗迹密度计算、对 $W^{\\prime\\pm}$ 和 $E^{\\pm}$ 质量的对撞机约束，并与当前直接探测（LZ）和间接探测（Fermi-LAT）限制进行比较，同时预测了 XLZD 和 CTA 的未来灵敏度。

Result: The model yields a viable TeV-scale dark matter candidate consistent with the observed relic abundance. Parameter regions satisfying all current constraints—collider bounds on $W^{\\prime\\pm}$ and $E^{\\pm}$, LZ direct detection limits, and Fermi-LAT indirect detection—are identified. The complementarity between direct and indirect detection strategies is demonstrated, with projections showing that future multi-ton experiments like XLZD and the CTA telescope will probe significant portions of the remaining parameter space.
\n\n
该模型产生了一个与观测到的遗迹丰度一致的可行 TeV 量级暗物质候选者。已识别出满足所有当前约束条件的参数区域——包括对 $W^{\\prime\\pm}$ 和 $E^{\\pm}$ 的对撞机限制、LZ 直接探测上限以及 Fermi-LAT 间接探测约束。研究表明直接与间接探测策略具有互补性，预测显示未来的多吨级实验（如 XLZD）和 CTA 望远镜将探测剩余参数空间的大部分区域。

Conclusion: This work demonstrates that extending the left-right symmetric model with an additional $SU(2)$ gauge group and vector-like leptons provides a theoretically well-motivated and phenomenologically viable dark matter framework. The dark matter candidate is naturally stable due to a discrete symmetry, interacts through two distinct portals, and lies at the TeV scale—within reach of next-generation direct and indirect detection experiments. The model exemplifies how particle physics beyond the Standard Model can simultaneously address symmetry restoration, neutrino mass origins, and dark matter.
\n\n
本工作表明，在左右对称模型中引入额外的 $SU(2)$ 规范群和矢量型轻子，可构建一个理论动机充分且现象学上可行的暗物质框架。该暗物质候选者因离散对称性而自然稳定，通过两种不同门户与可见扇区相互作用，且质量位于 TeV 量级——处于下一代直接与间接探测实验的可及范围之内。该模型展示了超越标准模型的粒子物理如何同时解决对称性恢复、中微子质量起源和暗物质问题。

Abstract: We investigate an extension of the left-right symmetric model featuring an additional non-abelian $SU(2)$ gauge symmetry. The particle content is augmented by one generation of vector-like leptons transforming under the fundamental representation of this new gauge group. We demonstrate that the neutral component of the vector-like lepton multiplet naturally provides a viable and stable dark matter candidate. Stability is ensured by imposing a discrete parity symmetry that forbids mixing between the vector-like leptons and the Standard Model leptons. As a consequence, the dark sector interacts with the visible sector exclusively through the vector portal (via s-channel processes) and the vector-like lepton portal (via t-channel processes). In our analysis, we incorporate collider constraints on the mass of the first-generation extra charged gauge boson $W^{\prime\pm}$, while assuming that additional scalar states are decoupled from the relevant energy scale for simplicity. We identify the regions of parameter space consistent with the observed relic abundance, collider bounds on the charged partner $E^{\pm}$, current direct detection limits from the LZ experiment and indirect detection constraints from Fermi-LAT. We find viable dark matter with a mass at the TeV scale. We show the complementarity of direct and indirect searches in probing the remaining parameter space of the model, in particular comparing the prospects of multi-ton direct detection experiments such as XLZD and of the CTA telescope.

### [82] [Joint Bayesian analysis of soft and high-$p_\perp$ probes yields tighter constraints on QGP properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09584)
*Marko Djordjevic,Dusan Zigic,Igor Salom,Magdalena Djordjevic*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper performs a joint Bayesian calibration of bulk quark-gluon plasma (QGP) parameters by simultaneously fitting low-$\pt$ bulk observables and high-$\pt$ jet tomography within a unified medium evolution framework. The inclusion of high-$\pt$ data significantly improves constraints on bulk properties compared to low-$\pt$-only analyses.
\n\n
本文通过在统一的介质演化框架内同时拟合低-$\pt$体观测量和高-$\pt$喷注层析（jet tomography），对夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）的体参数进行联合贝叶斯校准。与仅使用低-$\pt$数据的分析相比，引入高-$\pt$数据显著改善了对体参数的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to overcome limitations of traditional low-$\pt$-only Bayesian calibrations of QGP bulk properties, which fail to describe high-$\pt$ observables like anisotropic flow $v_2(\pt)$ and nuclear modification factor $R_{\mathrm{AA}}(\pt)$. By incorporating high-$\pt$ tomographic probes into the calibration, the authors aim to achieve more robust and precise constraints on the underlying medium evolution and transport coefficients.
\n\n
动机在于克服传统仅基于低-$\pt$观测量的QGP体性质贝叶斯校准的局限性——这类方法无法描述高-$\pt$观测量（如各向异性流 $v_2(\pt)$ 和核修正因子 $R_{\mathrm{AA}}(\pt)$）。通过将高-$\pt$层析探针纳入校准过程，作者旨在对介质演化和输运系数获得更稳健、更精确的约束。

Method: The method combines \textsc{TRENTo}+\textsc{VISHNU} for low-$\pt$ bulk evolution with \textsc{DREENA-A} for high-$\pt$ energy loss calculations. Temperature profiles from the hydrodynamic simulation are fed into \textsc{DREENA-A} to compute light and heavy flavor $R_{\mathrm{AA}}(\pt)$ and $v_2(\pt)$. A Gaussian process emulator is constructed to accelerate likelihood evaluations, enabling efficient Hamiltonian Monte Carlo (HMC) sampling of both the low-$\pt$-only and joint (low+high-$\pt$) posterior distributions.
\n\n
方法结合了用于低-$\pt$体演化的 \textsc{TRENTo}+\textsc{VISHNU} 框架与用于高-$\pt$能量损失计算的 \textsc{DREENA-A} 模型。将流体力学模拟得到的温度剖面输入 \textsc{DREENA-A}，以计算轻味与重味强子的 $R_{\mathrm{AA}}(\pt)$ 和 $v_2(\pt)$。构建高斯过程（Gaussian process）代理模型以加速似然函数评估，从而实现对低-$\pt$单独后验分布和联合（低+高-$\pt$）后验分布的高效哈密顿蒙特卡洛（Hamiltonian Monte Carlo, HMC）采样。

Result: The low-$\pt$-only calibration underpredicts high-$\pt$ elliptic flow $v_2(\pt)$, indicating missing physics or inconsistent parameter inference. In contrast, the joint calibration successfully describes both low- and high-$\pt$ observables simultaneously. Crucially, the joint analysis yields significantly tighter posterior constraints on bulk QGP parameters—such as initial entropy density and shear viscosity—demonstrating the constraining power of high-$\pt$ tomography.
\n\n
仅使用低-$\pt$数据的校准低估了高-$\pt$椭圆流 $v_2(\pt)$，表明存在物理缺失或参数推断不一致。相比之下，联合校准能同时成功描述低-$\pt$和高-$\pt$观测量。关键的是，联合分析对QGP体参数（如初始熵密度和剪切粘滞系数）给出了显著更紧致的后验约束，证明了高-$\pt$层析的强大约束能力。

Conclusion: High-$\pt$ jet tomography provides essential complementary information to low-$\pt$ bulk observables for constraining QGP properties. Joint Bayesian calibration across momentum scales is necessary for a consistent and precise extraction of medium parameters, paving the way for more rigorous multi-messenger studies of the quark-gluon plasma.
\n\n
高-$\pt$喷注层析为约束QGP性质提供了对低-$\pt$体观测量至关重要的补充信息。跨动量尺度的联合贝叶斯校准对于一致且精确地提取介质参数是必要的，为开展更严格的夸克-胶子等离子体多信使研究铺平了道路。

Abstract: To extract bulk QGP properties, we perform a joint Bayesian calibration of bulk-medium parameters using low-$\pt$ bulk and high-$\pt$ tomography within a common medium evolution. Low-$\pt$ observables are computed with \textsc{TRENTo}+\textsc{VISHNU}; temperature profiles are passed to \textsc{DREENA-A} to predict light/heavy $R_{\mathrm{AA}}(\pt)$ and $v_2(\pt)$. Gaussian-process emulation enables Hamiltonian Monte Carlo sampling of the low-$\pt$-only and joint posteriors. The low-$\pt$-only case underpredicts high-$\pt$ anisotropy; the joint calibration matches both sectors and markedly tightens bulk-parameter constraints, demonstrating the added power of high-$\pt$ data.

</details>


### [83] [Circumstellar Medium of Supernovae as New Probes for Feebly-interacting Particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09615)
*Yu Cheng,Chui-Fan Kong,Yen-Hsun Lin,Meng-Ru Wu,Seokhoon Yun*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper proposes using the circumstellar medium (CSM) around core-collapse supernovae (CCSNe) as a detector for feebly-interacting particles (FIPs). FIPs from the proto-neutron star can decay in the CSM before shock breakout, depositing energy that creates a photosphere and emits precursor blackbody radiation. Non-detection of such emission in SN 2023ixf yields new constraints on MeV-scale dark photons, surpassing previous CCSN limits and probing uncharted parameter space. Dust sublimation by FIP energy injection provides an additional diagnostic for future Galactic supernovae.
\n\n
本文提出利用核心坍缩超新星（CCSNe）周围的致密星周介质（CSM）作为微弱相互作用粒子（FIPs）的探测器。来自原中子星的FIPs可在激波突破前于CSM中衰变并沉积能量，形成光球并产生前驱黑体辐射。对SN 2023ixf早期观测中未发现此类辐射，由此对MeV尺度暗光子设定了比以往CCSN限制更强的新约束，并探索了此前未被覆盖的参数空间。FIP能量注入导致的尘埃升华还可为未来银河系超新星提供稳健诊断手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Current astrophysical probes of feebly-interacting particles (FIPs)—such as dark photons—are limited by uncertainties in stellar environments and observational systematics. Core-collapse supernovae (CCSNe) offer extreme conditions where FIPs may be copiously produced in the proto-neutron star, but traditional bounds rely on energy-loss arguments that saturate quickly. The authors aim to exploit the dense, confined circumstellar medium (CSM) surrounding some CCSNe as a target where FIP decays can produce observable electromagnetic signatures, thereby accessing previously inaccessible regions of FIP parameter space.
\n\n
目前对微弱相互作用粒子（FIPs）——如暗光子——的天体物理探针受限于恒星环境的不确定性和观测系统误差。核心坍缩超新星（CCSNe）提供了极端条件，其中FIPs可能在原中子星中大量产生，但传统限制依赖于能量损失论证，且很快达到饱和。作者旨在利用某些CCSNe周围致密、受限的星周介质（CSM）作为靶区，使FIP衰变产生可观测的电磁信号，从而探索此前无法触及的FIP参数空间。

Method: The authors model FIP production in the proto-neutron star via thermal processes, followed by propagation through the stellar envelope and subsequent decay within the dense circumstellar medium (CSM). They compute the deposited energy from FIP decays, which heats and ionizes the CSM, forming a photosphere that emits blackbody radiation prior to shock breakout. Using early-time photometric data from SN 2023ixf, they derive upper limits on precursor luminosity and translate these into constraints on the kinetic mixing parameter $\\epsilon$ of MeV-scale dark photons. They also analyze FIP-induced dust sublimation as a complementary signature for future nearby supernovae.
\n\n
作者通过热过程建模原中子星中的FIP产生，随后模拟其穿过恒星包层并在致密星周介质（CSM）中衰变的过程。他们计算FIP衰变沉积的能量，该能量加热并电离CSM，形成一个在激波突破前发射黑体辐射的光球。利用SN 2023ixf的早期测光数据，他们推导出前驱辐射光度的上限，并将其转化为对MeV尺度暗光子动能混合参数$\\epsilon$的限制。他们还分析了FIP诱导的尘埃升华作为未来邻近超新星的补充信号。

Result: The non-detection of excess precursor emission in SN 2023ixf leads to new upper limits on the kinetic mixing parameter $\\epsilon$ for dark photons with masses $m_{A'} \\sim \\mathcal{O}(1{-}100)$ MeV, significantly improving upon existing core-collapse supernova bounds. These constraints exclude regions of parameter space not probed by laboratory experiments, beam dumps, or other astrophysical sources. Additionally, the authors show that FIP-induced dust sublimation within $\\sim 10^{16}$ cm of the progenitor could produce observable infrared echoes in future Galactic supernovae, offering a robust secondary probe.
\n\n
SN 2023ixf中未探测到过量前驱辐射，从而对质量$m_{A'} \\sim \\mathcal{O}(1{-}100)$ MeV的暗光子动能混合参数$\\epsilon$设定了新的上限，显著优于现有的核心坍缩超新星限制。这些约束排除了实验室实验、束流倾倒实验及其他天体物理源尚未探测的参数区域。此外，作者指出，在距离前身星约$\\sim 10^{16}$ cm范围内的FIP诱导尘埃升华可在未来的银河系超新星中产生可观测的红外回光，提供一种稳健的次级探针。

Conclusion: This work establishes the circumstellar medium of core-collapse supernovae as a powerful new arena for probing feebly-interacting particles through their electromagnetic decay products. By leveraging early-time observations and dust sublimation effects, it opens a multi-messenger window into the MeV-scale dark sector, complementing terrestrial experiments and setting competitive, sometimes superior, constraints on dark photon models.
\n\n
本工作确立了核心坍缩超新星的星周介质作为通过电磁衰变产物探测微弱相互作用粒子（FIPs）的一个全新有力平台。通过结合早期观测与尘埃升华效应，它为探索MeV尺度暗区打开了一个多信使窗口，可与地面实验互补，并对暗光子模型设定了具有竞争力甚至更优的限制。

Abstract: We propose a novel strategy to probe feebly-interacting particles (FIPs) by exploiting the dense, confined circumstellar medium (CSM) surrounding core-collapse supernovae (CCSNe). FIPs produced in the proto-neutron star can deposit substantial visible energy into the CSM via decay prior to the shock breakout from the progenitor star. This energy injection heats and ionizes the CSM, establishing a FIP-induced photosphere that generates distinctive precursor blackbody emission. Using early-time observations of SN 2023ixf, we translate the non-detection of excessive precursor luminosity into stringent new constraints on MeV-scale dark photons as an exemplary model. Our results significantly extend existing CCSN bounds and exclude previously unexplored regions of parameter space. We further demonstrate that the FIP-induced dust sublimation offers robust diagnostics for future Galactic SNe, opening a new avenue to explore the dark sector.

### [84] [JLab and J-PARC for the J/{\ensuremathψ} Production at the Threshold](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09622)
*Igor I. Strakovsky,Jung Keun Ahn,William J. Briscoe,Misha G. Ryskin,Axel Schmid*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: New threshold measurements from 007 and CLAS12 for $γ~p\to p~J/ψ$ and $γ^\ast~p\to p~J/ψ$ reactions, combined with prior GlueX data, refine the determination of the $J/ψ$-proton scattering length $α_{J/ψp}$. Consistency across datasets and support from perturbative QCD reinforce the reliability of this extraction. Future J-PARC data on $π^-~p\to n~J/ψ$ will test the observed hierarchy of vector meson-nucleon scattering lengths, aligning with the "young vector meson" hypothesis.
\n\n
007 和 CLAS12 对 $γ~p\to p~J/ψ$ 与 $γ^\ast~p\to p~J/ψ$ 反应的新阈值测量，结合先前的 GlueX 数据，改进了对 $J/ψ$-质子散射长度 $α_{J/ψp}$ 的提取。各数据集之间的一致性以及微扰 QCD 的支持增强了该结果的可靠性。未来 J-PARC 对 $π^-~p\to n~J/ψ$ 的测量将检验矢量介子-核子散射长度的层级关系 $|α_{Υp}| \ll |α_{J/ψp}| \ll |α_{φp}| \ll |α_{ωp}|$，这与“young vector meson”假设一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to improve the phenomenological determination of the $J/ψ$-proton scattering length $α_{J/ψp}$ by incorporating new near-threshold photoproduction data from 007 and CLAS12, complementing earlier GlueX results. It also seeks to address a puzzling trend in the magnitudes of vector meson-nucleon scattering lengths across different quark flavors, which may shed light on nonperturbative QCD dynamics and the nature of hadronic interactions involving heavy quarkonia.
\n\n
本文旨在通过引入 007 和 CLAS12 的新近阈值光致产生数据，结合早期 GlueX 结果，改进对 $J/ψ$-质子散射长度 $α_{J/ψp}$ 的唯象提取。同时，试图解释不同夸克味矢量介子-核子散射长度大小呈现的异常趋势（$|α_{Υp}| \ll |α_{J/ψp}| \ll |α_{φp}| \ll |α_{ωp}|$），以揭示非微扰 QCD 动力学及重夸克偶素参与的强子相互作用本质。

Method: The authors perform a combined analysis of threshold cross-section data from three experiments: GlueX ($γ~p\to p~J/ψ\to p~(e^+e^-)$), 007 ($γ~p\to p~J/ψ\to p~(μ^+μ^-)$), and CLAS12 ($γ^\ast~p\to p~J/ψ\to p~(e^+e^-)$). They use effective-range expansion near threshold to extract the scattering length $α_{J/ψp}$, assuming dominance of S-wave production. Consistency checks between datasets assess systematic uncertainties. Perturbative QCD calculations are invoked to support the extracted value. The upcoming J-PARC measurement of $π^-~p\to n~J/ψ$ is anticipated to provide an independent constraint.
\n\n
作者联合分析了三个实验的阈值截面数据：GlueX（$γ~p\to p~J/ψ\to p~(e^+e^-)$）、007（$γ~p\to p~J/ψ\to p~(μ^+μ^-)$）和 CLAS12（$γ^\ast~p\to p~J/ψ\to p~(e^+e^-)$）。他们利用阈值附近的有效程展开（effective-range expansion）提取散射长度 $α_{J/ψp}$，并假设 S 波产生占主导。通过数据集间的一致性检验系统误差。同时引用微扰 QCD 计算来支持提取结果。预期 J-PARC 对 $π^-~p\to n~J/ψ$ 的测量将提供独立约束。

Result: The combined analysis yields a robust determination of $α_{J/ψp}$ with reduced uncertainties, showing excellent agreement among GlueX, 007, and CLAS12 datasets—indicating no significant methodological systematics. The extracted value is consistent with perturbative QCD expectations. The observed hierarchy $|α_{Υp}| \ll |α_{J/ψp}| \ll |α_{φp}| \ll |α_{ωp}|$ remains unexplained within conventional models but aligns with the “young vector meson” hypothesis, which posits that heavier vector mesons interact more weakly due to shorter formation times.
\n\n
联合分析得到了更精确的 $α_{J/ψp}$ 值，且 GlueX、007 和 CLAS12 数据集之间高度一致，表明无显著方法学系统误差。提取结果与微扰 QCD 预期相符。观测到的层级关系 $|α_{Υp}| \ll |α_{J/ψp}| \ll |α_{φp}| \ll |α_{ωp}|$ 在传统模型中难以解释，但与“young vector meson”假设一致——该假设认为更重的矢量介子因形成时间更短而与核子相互作用更弱。

Conclusion: The convergence of experimental results from different facilities and reaction channels strengthens confidence in the phenomenological extraction of $α_{J/ψp}$. Perturbative QCD provides theoretical backing, while the anomalous trend in vector meson-nucleon scattering lengths suggests novel dynamics tied to quark mass and formation time. Future J-PARC data will be crucial to confirm this trend and test the “young vector meson” hypothesis rigorously.
\n\n
来自不同实验装置和反应道的结果一致性增强了对 $α_{J/ψp}$ 唯象提取的信心。微扰 QCD 提供了理论支持，而矢量介子-核子散射长度的反常趋势暗示了与夸克质量和形成时间相关的新物理机制。未来的 J-PARC 数据对确认该趋势并严格检验“young vector meson”假设至关重要。

Abstract: New threshold measurements for $γ~p\to p~J/ψ\to p~(μ^+μ^-)$ by 007 and $γ^\ast~p\to p~J/ψ\to p~(e^+e^-)$ by CLAS12 allow us to extend the previous phenomenological determination of the J/\ensuremathψ-proton scattering length, $α_{J/ψp}$, using GlueX threshold data for $γ~p\to p~J/ψ\to p~(e^+e^-)$. The agreement between all three J/\ensuremathψ data sets shows no indication of systematic differences between methodologies. Furthermore, perturbative QCD predictions support the phenomenological determination of heavy vector meson-nucleon scattering lengths. Upcoming J-PARC threshold measurements of the reaction $π^-~p\to n~J/ψ\to n~(l^+l^-)$ will help resolve a puzzle regarding the trend of the vector meson-nucleon scattering lengths, $|α_{Υp}| \ll |α_{J/ψp}| \ll |α_{φp}| \ll |α_{ωp}|$, which is consistent with the ``young vector meson'' hypothesis.

### [85] [The eikonal spin-dependent Odderon and gluon Sivers function of a proton, and its small-$x$ evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09630)
*Sanjin Benić,Adrian Dumitru,Florian Hechenberger,Tomasz Stebel*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper connects the eikonal Odderon operator matrix element with a helicity flip in the proton to the dipole gluon Sivers function, computes this function using a three-quark light-front model at moderate $x_0 \sim 0.1$ and $k_\perp \lesssim 1$ GeV, and predicts its behavior including a power-law tail $x f_{1T}^{\perp g}(x,k_\perp) \sim k_\perp^{-3.3}$ at larger $k_\perp$ via BFKL evolution.
\n\n
本文将质子中具有螺旋度翻转的eikonal Odderon算符矩阵元与偶极胶子Sivers函数联系起来，利用三夸克光前模型在中等$x_0 \sim 0.1$和$k_\perp \lesssim 1$ GeV下计算该函数，并通过BFKL演化预测其在较大$k_\perp$处的幂律尾部行为：$x f_{1T}^{\perp g}(x,k_\perp) \sim k_\perp^{-3.3}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to establish a concrete link between the eikonal Odderon operator (with helicity flip) and transverse-momentum-dependent parton distributions—specifically the dipole gluon Sivers function—and to provide a first-principles-based estimate of its magnitude and shape using a solvable light-front wave function model, bridging nonperturbative and perturbative QCD regimes.
\n\n
动机在于建立eikonal Odderon算符（含螺旋度翻转）与横向动量依赖部分子分布（特别是偶极胶子Sivers函数）之间的具体联系，并利用可解的光前波函数模型提供其大小和形状的第一性原理估计，从而连接非微扰与微扰QCD区域。

Method: The authors use a three-quark light-front (LC) wave function model of the proton to compute the matrix element corresponding to the dipole gluon Sivers function $f_{1T}^{\perp g}(x,k_\perp)$ at moderately small $x_0 \sim 0.1$. They extract properties such as magnitude, peak position in $k_\perp$, and small-$k_\perp$ behavior directly from the model. For the high-$k_\perp$ tail at small $x$, they apply BFKL evolution to compute the anomalous dimension, assuming $\\alpha_s \\log(x_0/x) = 1$, yielding a power-law decay.
\n\n
作者采用质子的三夸克光前（LC）波函数模型，在中等小的$x_0 \sim 0.1$下计算对应于偶极胶子Sivers函数$f_{1T}^{\perp g}(x,k_\perp)$的矩阵元，直接从模型中提取其整体大小、$k_\perp$空间中的峰值位置以及小$k_\perp$行为。对于小$x$下的高$k_\perp$尾部，他们应用BFKL演化计算反常维度，假设$\\alpha_s \\log(x_0/x) = 1$，从而得到幂律衰减形式。

Result: The model predicts that $x f_{1T}^{\perp g}(x,k_\perp)$ peaks at $k_\perp \\sim 0.5$–$1$ GeV and exhibits a power-law tail $x f_{1T}^{\perp g}(x,k_\perp) \\sim k_\perp^{-3.3}$ for $k_\perp \\gtrsim 1.5$ GeV, governed by the BFKL anomalous dimension at $\\alpha_s \\log(x_0/x) = 1$. This provides quantitative estimates for both nonperturbative and perturbative regimes of the gluon Sivers function.
\n\n
该模型预测$x f_{1T}^{\perp g}(x,k_\perp)$在$k_\perp \\sim 0.5$–$1$ GeV处出现峰值，并在$k_\perp \\gtrsim 1.5$ GeV时呈现由BFKL反常维度主导的幂律尾部$x f_{1T}^{\perp g}(x,k_\perp) \\sim k_\perp^{-3.3}$（在$\\alpha_s \\log(x_0/x) = 1$条件下）。这为胶子Sivers函数的非微扰与微扰区域提供了定量估计。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that the dipole gluon Sivers function can be consistently described across momentum scales: modeled nonperturbatively at moderate $k_\perp$ via a light-front wave function and extended perturbatively to high $k_\perp$ using BFKL dynamics. This bridges the eikonal Odderon formalism with TMD physics and offers testable predictions for future experiments.
\n\n
研究表明，偶极胶子Sivers函数可在全动量标度范围内一致描述：在中等$k_\perp$下通过光前波函数进行非微扰建模，并利用BFKL动力学微扰地延拓至高$k_\perp$区域。这连接了eikonal Odderon形式体系与TMD物理，并为未来实验提供了可检验的预言。

Abstract: The matrix element in the proton of the eikonal Odderon operator, with a helicity flip, has been shown to correspond to the dipole gluon Sivers function. We employ a three quark light-front model of the proton to determine the Sivers function at moderately small $x_0 \sim 0.1$ and transverse momentum $k_\perp \lesssim 1$~GeV. The model light-cone (LC) wave function predicts the properties of $x f_{1T}^{\perp g}(x,k_\perp)$ such as its overall magnitude, the position of its peak in $k_\perp$, and its behavior at small $k_\perp$. We then compute numerically the BFKL anomalous dimension characterizing the power-law tail at $k_\perp \gtrsim 1.5$~GeV of the gluon Sivers function at small LC momentum fractions, $α_s \log x_0/x = 1$: $x f_{1T}^{\perp g}(x,k_\perp) \sim k_\perp^{-3.3}$.

### [86] [Directed Flow of D and B Mesons in an Electrically and Chirally Conductive QGP at LHC Energies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09636)
*Ankit Kumar Panda,Pooja,Maria Lucia Sambataro,Salvatore Plumari,Santosh K. Das*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper studies the directed flow ($v_1$) of D and B mesons under strong electromagnetic fields in heavy-ion collisions at LHC energies, incorporating both finite electrical and chiral conductivities. Using Langevin dynamics within the extended quasiparticle model (QPMp) for heavy-quark propagation in the quark-gluon plasma (QGP), and analytical solutions of Maxwell’s equations for the electromagnetic fields, the authors find that charm- and bottom-containing mesons exhibit opposite signs of $v_1$, with chiral conductivity playing a negligible role compared to electrical conductivity.
\n\n
本文研究了在LHC能量下强电磁场中D介子和B介子的定向流（$v_1$），并考虑了有限的电导率和手征导率。作者采用扩展准粒子模型（QPMp）框架下的Langevin动力学描述重夸克在夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）中的传播，并利用Maxwell方程的解析解计算电磁场。结果表明，含粲夸克和底夸克的重介子表现出符号相反的$v_1$，且手征导率的影响远小于电导率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to understand the origin of the directed flow ($v_1$) of heavy-flavor mesons observed in relativistic heavy-ion collisions. Since heavy quarks are produced early and interact with the evolving quark-gluon plasma (QGP) and strong electromagnetic fields, their $v_1$ can serve as a probe of the initial electromagnetic field structure and transport properties like electrical and chiral conductivities. Clarifying the relative roles of these conductivities is essential for interpreting experimental data on charge-dependent flow asymmetries.
\n\n
动机源于理解相对论性重离子碰撞中观测到的重味介子定向流（$v_1$）的起源。由于重夸克在早期产生，并与演化的夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）及强电磁场相互作用，其$v_1$可作为初始电磁场结构及输运性质（如电导率和手征导率）的探针。厘清这些导率的相对作用对解释电荷依赖的流不对称性实验数据至关重要。

Method: The authors employ Langevin dynamics to simulate the momentum evolution of charm and bottom quarks in the QGP, using the extended quasiparticle model (QPMp) to describe their interactions with the medium. Electromagnetic fields are derived from analytical solutions of Maxwell’s equations that include both finite electrical conductivity ($\\sigma$) and chiral magnetic conductivity ($\\sigma_\\chi$). The resulting Lorentz force acts differently on particles and antiparticles, leading to a splitting in their directed flow $v_1$. The calculations are performed for Pb-Pb collisions at LHC energies.
\n\n
作者采用Langevin动力学模拟粲夸克和底夸克在QGP中的动量演化，利用扩展准粒子模型（QPMp）描述其与介质的相互作用。电磁场由包含有限电导率（$\\sigma$）和手征磁导率（$\\sigma_\\chi$）的Maxwell方程解析解给出。由此产生的Lorentz力对粒子与反粒子作用不同，导致其定向流$v_1$发生分裂。计算针对LHC能量下的Pb-Pb碰撞进行。

Result: The study finds that D mesons (containing charm quarks) and B mesons (containing bottom quarks) develop directed flows of opposite signs, with the magnitude of $v_1$ for B mesons being smaller than that for D mesons. Electrical conductivity significantly modifies the space-time profile of the electromagnetic fields and enhances the $v_1$ splitting between mesons and anti-mesons. In contrast, chiral conductivity has only a marginal effect on $v_1$, confirming its subdominant role in this context.
\n\n
研究发现，含粲夸克的D介子与含底夸克的B介子产生符号相反的定向流，且B介子的$v_1$幅度小于D介子。电导率显著改变了电磁场的时空分布，并增强了介子与反介子之间的$v_1$分裂。相比之下，手征导率对$v_1$的影响微乎其微，证实其在此情境下处于次要地位。

Conclusion: The opposite signs of $v_1$ for charm- and bottom-containing mesons, driven primarily by electromagnetic fields with finite electrical conductivity, suggest that simultaneous experimental measurements of $v_1$ for D and B mesons could disentangle the electromagnetic origin of heavy-quark directed flow. The negligible role of chiral conductivity implies that interpretations of $v_1$ splitting should focus on conventional electromagnetic effects rather than anomalous chiral transport.
\n\n
粲夸克与底夸克介子$v_1$符号相反的现象主要由具有有限电导率的电磁场驱动，表明同时测量D和B介子的$v_1$可有效区分重夸克定向流的电磁起源。手征导率的可忽略作用意味着对$v_1$分裂的解释应聚焦于常规电磁效应，而非反常手征输运。

Abstract: We investigate the directed flow of D and B mesons in the presence of electromagnetic fields incorporating finite electrical and chiral conductivities at LHC energies. The momentum evolution of heavy quarks in the quark-gluon plasma (QGP) is studied using Langevin dynamics, with their interactions with the medium described within the extended quasiparticle model (QPMp) framework. The electromagnetic fields are obtained from analytical solutions of Maxwell equations that account for both electrical and chiral conductivities. These conductivities modify the space-time evolution of the electromagnetic fields and influence the splitting of the directed flow between mesons and anti-mesons. However, the influence of chiral conductivity remains secondary to that of electrical conductivity and its impact on the directed flow is marginal. The results show that heavy mesons containing a charm quark develop a directed flow with a sign opposite to that of heavy mesons containing a bottom quark, with a smaller magnitude for the latter. The present study indicates that a simultaneous experimental measurement of v1 for heavy mesons containing both charm and bottom quarks would provide valuable insight into the electromagnetic field origin of v1 for heavy quarks.

</details>


### [87] [Dimuon production in neutrino-nucleus collisions at next-to-next-to-leading order in perturbative QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09646)
*Ilkka Helenius,Hannu Paukkunen,Sami Yrjänheikki*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We present a self-contained NNLO QCD calculation of dimuon production in charged-current neutrino-nucleus DIS using the semi-inclusive DIS (SIDIS) framework, improving upon previous inclusive approaches. The NNLO corrections reduce scale uncertainties at large $x$ and yield negative corrections at small $x$, alleviating tension between dimuon data and LHC constraints on the strange-quark PDF.
\n\n
本文基于半单举深度非弹性散射（semi-inclusive DIS, SIDIS）框架，提出了一个自洽的次次领头阶（NNLO）QCD计算，用于带电流中微子-原子核DIS中的双缪子产生过程，改进了以往的单举方法。NNLO修正显著降低了大$x$处的能标不确定性，并在小$x$处给出负修正，从而缓解了双缪子数据与LHC对奇异夸克PDF约束之间的张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Charm production in neutrino-nucleus DIS via dimuon final states provides a key constraint on the strange-quark parton distribution function (PDF), especially at small $x$. However, this constraint has historically conflicted with LHC measurements of heavy-gauge boson production, which suggest a larger strange-quark PDF. Previous NNLO calculations used fully inclusive charm production, which suffers from theoretical shortcomings when applied to dimuon observables. This motivates a more appropriate treatment within the semi-inclusive DIS formalism.
\n\n
中微子-原子核DIS中通过双缪子末态测量的粲夸克产生过程为奇异夸克部分子分布函数（PDF）提供了关键约束，尤其在小$x$区域。然而，这一约束与LHC重规范玻色子产生数据所暗示的更大奇异夸克PDF存在长期冲突。以往的NNLO计算采用全单举粲夸克产生方法，但该方法在应用于双缪子可观测量时存在理论缺陷，因此有必要在半单举DIS（SIDIS）框架下进行更恰当的处理。

Method: The authors perform a self-contained NNLO perturbative QCD calculation of dimuon production in charged-current neutrino-nucleus DIS using the semi-inclusive DIS (SIDIS) factorization framework. This approach explicitly accounts for the observed final-state muons, unlike inclusive calculations that integrate over unobserved charm hadrons. The method includes all relevant heavy-quark production channels opening up at NNLO, and evaluates perturbative convergence and scale dependence across the full $x$ range.
\n\n
作者采用半单举深度非弹性散射（SIDIS）因子化框架，对带电流中微子-原子核DIS中的双缪子产生过程进行了自洽的次次领头阶（NNLO）微扰QCD计算。该方法显式考虑了观测到的末态缪子，而不同于对未观测粲强子进行积分的单举计算。该方法包含了所有在NNLO开启的相关重夸克产生道，并评估了全$x$范围内的微扰收敛性和能标依赖性。

Result: The NNLO corrections significantly reduce scale uncertainties at large $x$, where they enhance the cross section. At small $x$, the NNLO corrections are negative, thereby reducing the inferred strange-quark PDF and bringing dimuon-based determinations into better agreement with LHC heavy-gauge boson data. The study also identifies new heavy-quark production channels that contribute at NNLO and demonstrates improved perturbative stability in the SIDIS formulation compared to inclusive approaches.
\n\n
NNLO修正显著降低了大$x$处的能标不确定性，并在此区域增强截面；而在小$x$处，NNLO修正为负，从而降低所推断的奇异夸克PDF，使基于双缪子的测定结果与LHC重规范玻色子数据更好地一致。研究还识别出在NNLO开启的新重夸克产生道，并表明SIDIS表述相比单举方法具有更好的微扰稳定性。

Conclusion: The SIDIS-based NNLO calculation provides a theoretically robust framework for interpreting dimuon data in neutrino DIS, resolving key limitations of inclusive approaches. The resulting negative NNLO corrections at small $x$ alleviate the long-standing tension between neutrino dimuon measurements and LHC constraints on strangeness, suggesting a more consistent global picture of the strange-quark PDF.
\n\n
基于SIDIS的NNLO计算为解释中微子DIS中的双缪子数据提供了一个理论上稳健的框架，解决了单举方法的关键局限性。小$x$处的负NNLO修正缓解了中微子双缪子测量与LHC对奇异夸克约束之间长期存在的张力，表明奇异夸克PDF的全局图像更具一致性。

Abstract: Charm production in charged-current neutrino-nucleus deep-inelastic scattering (DIS), measured through dimuon final states, remains an important constraint of strangeness in global analyses of parton distribution functions (PDFs). This process has traditionally favored a smaller strange-quark PDF at small momentum fractions $x$ than what the LHC heavy-gauge boson data have indicated. Here, we present a self-contained next-to-next-to-leading-order (NNLO) perturbative QCD calculation of dimuon production in neutrino-nucleus DIS based on semi-inclusive DIS (SIDIS). This process has been previously computed at NNLO through fully inclusive charm production. We discuss the shortcomings of this approach and how they are addressed in the SIDIS picture. We study the perturbative convergence and explore new heavy-quark production channels that become available at NNLO. We find that the NNLO corrections significantly reduce the scale uncertainties at large values of $x$ where the cross sections are enhanced by the NNLO corrections. At small $x$, the NNLO corrections tend to be negative instead, which alleviate the tension between the dimuon and LHC data.

</details>


### [88] [Extracting the speed of sound of QCD from transverse momentum fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09647)
*Mubarak Alqahtani,Tribhuban Parida,Jean-Yves Ollitrault*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper extracts the speed of sound $c_s$ in the quark-gluon plasma (QGP) from ATLAS data on transverse momentum per particle ($[p_T]$) distributions in ultra-central Pb+Pb collisions. By correcting for detector bias using variance and $v_0(p_T)$ data, and deblurring hadronization noise under the assumption of fixed QGP size at zero impact parameter, the authors find $c_s/c = 0.496 \pm 0.008$ at $T = 221 \pm 13$ MeV, matching lattice QCD predictions.
\n\n
该论文从ATLAS在超中心Pb+Pb碰撞中关于每粒子横向动量（$[p_T]$）分布的数据中提取了夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）中的声速 $c_s$。通过利用方差和 $v_0(p_T)$ 数据校正探测器偏差，并在零碰撞参数下假设QGP尺寸与强子多重数无关的前提下对强子化过程的噪声进行去模糊处理，作者得到在温度 $T = 221 \pm 13$ MeV 时 $c_s/c = 0.496 \pm 0.008$，与格点QCD的第一性原理计算高度一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to determine the equation of state of the quark-gluon plasma by measuring its speed of sound $c_s$, a fundamental thermodynamic quantity. While idealized analyses suggest $c_s$ can be inferred from the mean transverse momentum per particle as a function of multiplicity, real-world detector limitations—particularly the inability to detect low-$p_T$ particles—introduce significant biases that must be corrected to obtain reliable results consistent with first-principles theory.
\n\n
该研究旨在通过测量夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）的声速 $c_s$（一个基本热力学量）来确定其状态方程。尽管理想化分析表明 $c_s$ 可通过每粒子平均横向动量随多重数的变化推断，但现实探测器的局限性——尤其是无法探测低 $p_T$ 粒子——引入了显著偏差，必须加以校正才能获得与第一性原理理论一致的可靠结果。

Method: The authors develop a correction framework that uses two experimental inputs beyond the mean $[p_T]$: (1) the variance of $[p_T]$, which helps constrain the underlying distribution affected by detector inefficiencies, and (2) the recently measured $v_0(p_T)$ (the monopole flow coefficient), which provides information about radial flow and thus the hydrodynamic response linked to $c_s$. They also introduce a systematic deblurring technique to account for fluctuations introduced during hadronization. Crucially, they assume that in zero-impact-parameter collisions, the initial QGP fireball size is independent of final-state hadron multiplicity—a hypothesis supported by both high-energy QCD and heavy-ion collision data.
\n\n
作者构建了一个校正框架，除平均 $[p_T]$ 外还使用两个实验输入：(1) $[p_T]$ 的方差，用于约束受探测器效率影响的底层分布；(2) 最近测量的 $v_0(p_T)$（单极流系数），提供径向流信息，从而关联到与 $c_s$ 相关的流体动力学响应。他们还引入了一种系统性的去模糊技术，以处理强子化过程中引入的涨落。关键假设是：在零碰撞参数下，初始QGP火球的尺寸与末态强子多重数无关——这一假设得到高能QCD和重离子碰撞数据的支持。

Result: Applying their method to ATLAS data, the authors extract $c_s/c = 0.496 \pm 0.008$ at a temperature of $T = 221 \pm 13$ MeV. This value is in excellent agreement with first-principles lattice QCD calculations of the QGP equation of state near the crossover transition region, validating both the experimental approach and the underlying theoretical assumptions about QGP geometry and dynamics.
\n\n
将该方法应用于ATLAS数据，作者提取出在温度 $T = 221 \pm 13$ MeV 时 $c_s/c = 0.496 \pm 0.008$。该数值与格点QCD在交叉相变区域附近对QGP状态方程的第一性原理计算高度吻合，验证了该实验方法及关于QGP几何结构和动力学的基本理论假设。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that precision extraction of fundamental QGP properties like the speed of sound is possible from fluctuation observables in heavy-ion collisions, provided that detector effects and hadronization noise are properly accounted for. The agreement with lattice QCD confirms the reliability of hydrodynamic modeling and supports the picture of a thermalized, strongly-coupled QGP formed in ultra-central collisions.
\n\n
该研究表明，只要恰当地处理探测器效应和强子化噪声，就可从重离子碰撞中的涨落观测量中精确提取QGP的基本性质（如声速）。与格点QCD的一致性证实了流体动力学模型的可靠性，并支持在超中心碰撞中形成了热化且强耦合的QGP这一物理图像。

Abstract: We extract the speed of sound ($c_s$) in the quark-gluon plasma from ATLAS data on the probability distribution of the transverse momentum per particle, $[p_T]$, in ultra-central Pb+Pb collisions. With an ideal detector, $c_s$ can be inferred from the rise of the mean $[p_T]$ with the collision multiplicity. In practice, however, low-$p_T$ particles escape detection, which biases the analysis. We show how to correct for this bias by using data on the variance of $[p_T]$, as well as information from the recently-measured $v_0(p_T)$. We also introduce a systematic method for deblurring the noise from the hadronization process. Assuming that the size of the quark-gluon plasma is independent of the hadron multiplicity in collisions at zero impact parameter, which is the scenario preferred both by high-energy QCD and heavy-ion data, we obtain $c_s/c=0.496\pm 0.008$ at temperature $T=221\pm 13$ MeV, in perfect agreement with first-principles calculations from lattice QCD.

### [89] [Probing GPDs in exclusive electroproduction of dijets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09686)
*Trambak Jyoti Chall,Marta Łuszczak,Wolfgang Schäfer,Antoni Szczurek*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper presents a calculation of exclusive dijet production in $e p \\to e^{\\prime} jj p$ using collinear QCD factorization with Generalized Parton Distributions (GPDs) modeled via the Double Distribution (DD) approach. It includes leading-order contributions from light sea/valence quarks and gluons for both light $q\\bar{q}$ and heavy $c\\bar{c}$ final states, and compares theoretical predictions with ZEUS data in specific kinematic regions, highlighting distinct valence quark behavior at large $x_{\\mathbb{P}}$ relevant for future EIC studies.
\n\n
本文利用基于Double Distribution（DD）方法建模的Generalized Parton Distributions（GPDs），在collinear QCD factorization框架下计算了$e p \\to e^{\\prime} jj p$过程中的exclusive dijet产生。计算包含了light sea quark、valence quark和gluon在leading-order对light $q\\bar{q}$和heavy $c\\bar{c}$末态的贡献，并在特定运动学区域与ZEUS实验数据进行了比较，特别指出valence quark贡献在大$x_{\\mathbb{P}}$区域的独特行为，这对未来Electron Ion Collider（EIC）研究具有重要意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide a comprehensive theoretical framework for exclusive dijet production in diffractive deep inelastic scattering (DIS), which serves as a probe of Generalized Parton Distributions (GPDs)—particularly the gluon GPD—and to explore kinematic regions beyond those accessible at HERA, such as high $x_{\\mathbb{P}}$, which will be reachable at the Electron Ion Collider (EIC). Understanding the relative roles of valence, sea, and gluon contributions is essential for interpreting current and future data.
\n\n
该研究旨在为diffraction deep inelastic scattering（DIS）中的exclusive dijet产生提供一个完整的理论框架，以探测Generalized Parton Distributions（GPDs），特别是gluon GPD；并探索HERA未覆盖的运动学区域（如高$x_{\\mathbb{P}}$），这些区域将在未来的Electron Ion Collider（EIC）中可及。理解valence、sea和gluon贡献的相对作用对解释当前和未来实验数据至关重要。

Method: The authors employ collinear QCD factorization for exclusive processes, where the hard scattering amplitude is convoluted with GPDs. The GPDs are modeled using the Double Distribution (DD) formalism, ensuring polynomiality and support properties. Leading-order amplitudes for $\\gamma^* p \\to jj p$ are computed for all relevant partonic channels: light quark-antiquark ($q\\bar{q}$) and charm ($c\\bar{c}$) pairs, including contributions from valence quarks, sea quarks, and gluons. Differential cross sections and azimuthal angle modulations between the lepton and dijet planes are evaluated over a broad kinematic range, including comparisons with ZEUS data in the region $\\beta \\gtrsim 0.4$.
\n\n
作者采用用于exclusive过程的collinear QCD factorization方法，其中硬散射振幅与GPDs进行卷积。GPDs通过Double Distribution（DD）形式构建，以保证多项式性和支撑性质。计算了$\\gamma^* p \\to jj p$过程在leading-order下所有相关部分子道的振幅，包括light $q\\bar{q}$和charm $c\\bar{c}$对，并涵盖valence quark、sea quark和gluon的贡献。在广泛的运动学范围内计算了微分截面以及lepton平面与dijet平面之间的azimuthal angle调制，并在$\\beta \\gtrsim 0.4$区域与ZEUS数据进行了比较。

Result: The differential cross sections show that gluon and sea quark contributions have similar kinematic shapes, while the valence quark contribution—though small in magnitude—exhibits distinctly different behavior, especially at large $x_{\\mathbb{P}}$. The azimuthal angle modulation is computed for general kinematics and for the ZEUS setup, with reasonable agreement observed for $\\beta \\gtrsim 0.4$. This suggests that valence GPD effects may become measurable at the EIC, motivating further feasibility studies.
\n\n
微分截面结果显示，gluon和sea quark贡献具有相似的运动学形状，而valence quark贡献虽然幅度较小，但在大$x_{\\mathbb{P}}$区域表现出明显不同的行为。azimuthal angle调制在一般运动学和ZEUS实验条件下均被计算，在$\\beta \\gtrsim 0.4$区域与数据有合理的一致性。这表明valence GPD效应可能在EIC上被测量，从而推动进一步的可行性研究。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that exclusive dijet production in diffractive DIS is a viable channel to access GPDs, particularly to disentangle valence, sea, and gluon contributions. The distinct signature of valence quarks at large $x_{\\mathbb{P}}$ offers a new opportunity for probing nucleon structure at the EIC. Future work should focus on detailed feasibility analyses and higher-order QCD corrections to improve precision.
\n\n
研究表明，diffraction DIS中的exclusive dijet产生是获取GPDs的有效通道，尤其有助于区分valence、sea和gluon的贡献。valence quark在大$x_{\\mathbb{P}}$区域的独特信号为在EIC上探测核子结构提供了新机遇。未来工作应聚焦于详细的可行性分析和更高阶QCD修正，以提高理论精度。

Abstract: We summarize the formalism for calculating the exclusive dijet production in $e p \to e^{\prime} jj p$ in collinear QCD factorization, using generalized parton distributions (GPDs) as the soft hadronic input modeled in the double distribution (DD) approach. We include all leading-order contributions coming from light sea and valence quark exchanges, and gluon exchanges for both light quark-antiquark ($q\bar{q}$) production and also the heavy $c\bar{c}$ final state. We present results for several differential distributions for the cross section evaluated over a broad region of phase space, covering a wide range of inelasticity and photon virtuality. The gluon and sea contributions exhibit similar shapes, whereas the valence contribution, though relatively small, shows a markedly different behavior. The latter becomes particularly noticeable at large $x_{\mathbb{P}}$, a kinematic region not explored at HERA, but potentially accessible in future measurements at the Electron Ion Collider (EIC). This requires further feasibility studies. We also present the azimuthal angle modulation between the leptonic and the outgoing dijet planes for the general case, as well as for the ZEUS kinematic region where we see reasonable agreement with the data for diffractive deep inelastic scattering (DIS) parameter $β\gtrsim 0.4$.

</details>


### [90] [Event-by-Event Multiplicity Fluctuations in Heavy-Ion Collisions Using Modified HIJING Monte Carlo Generator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09732)
*Y. A. Rusak,L. F. Babichev*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper proposes event-by-event multiplicity fluctuations as a diagnostic probe to distinguish between hot (quark-gluon plasma) and cold nuclear matter in relativistic heavy-ion collisions, using a modified HIJING Monte Carlo generator that incorporates various partonic energy loss models. The analysis reveals that fluctuation patterns can reveal the medium type, validate energy loss mechanisms, and uncover signatures of a first-order QCD phase transition.
\n\n
本文提出利用逐事件（event-by-event）多重数涨落作为诊断工具，以区分相对论重离子碰撞中产生的热介质（夸克-胶子等离子体，quark-gluon plasma）与冷核物质。作者采用改进的HIJING蒙特卡洛生成器，该生成器整合了多种部分子在热介质和冷介质中的能量损失模型。分析表明，涨落的模式能够揭示介质类型、验证能量损失机制，并发现QCD一级相变的信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to identify unambiguous experimental signatures of the quark-gluon plasma (QGP) formation and to locate the critical point in the QCD phase diagram. Traditional observables often lack sensitivity to the microscopic properties of the created medium. Multiplicity fluctuations, being sensitive to the underlying dynamics and thermodynamic state, offer a promising avenue to probe the nature of the medium and possible phase transitions.
\n\n
该研究的动机源于寻找夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）形成的明确实验信号以及定位QCD相图中临界点的需求。传统观测量往往对所产生介质的微观性质缺乏敏感性。而多重数涨落对底层动力学和热力学状态敏感，为探测介质性质及可能的相变提供了有前景的途径。

Method: The authors employ a modified HIJING Monte Carlo event generator that includes different implementations of partonic energy loss—both in hot media (modeling QGP) and cold nuclear matter. They perform event-by-event simulations of relativistic heavy-ion collisions and compute multiplicity fluctuations across various kinematic regions. Statistical measures of these fluctuations are then correlated with the assumed medium properties and energy loss prescriptions to assess their diagnostic power.
\n\n
作者采用改进的HIJING蒙特卡洛事例生成器，其中包含多种部分子能量损失模型——分别用于热介质（模拟QGP）和冷核物质。他们对相对论重离子碰撞进行逐事件模拟，并在不同运动学区域计算多重数涨落。随后将这些涨落的统计量与假设的介质性质和能量损失方案相关联，以评估其诊断能力。

Result: The study finds that the magnitude and structure of multiplicity fluctuations differ significantly depending on whether the energy loss occurs in a hot or cold medium. These differences enable discrimination between QGP and hadronic scenarios. Furthermore, specific fluctuation patterns—such as non-monotonic behavior in certain kinematic windows—are identified as potential signals of a first-order phase transition, offering a new strategy for critical point searches in heavy-ion collision experiments.
\n\n
研究发现，多重数涨落的幅度和结构在热介质与冷介质中的能量损失情形下存在显著差异，从而可区分QGP与强子介质情景。此外，在特定运动学窗口中识别出非单调行为等特殊涨落模式，可作为一级相变的潜在信号，为重离子碰撞实验中寻找临界点提供了新策略。

Conclusion: Event-by-event multiplicity fluctuations serve as a powerful and sensitive probe of the medium created in relativistic heavy-ion collisions. By leveraging modified Monte Carlo simulations with realistic energy loss models, this work demonstrates that fluctuation analyses can constrain the nature of the QCD medium, test theoretical models of parton energy loss, and provide observable signatures of phase transitions, thereby aiding the experimental mapping of the QCD phase diagram.
\n\n
逐事件多重数涨落是探测相对论重离子碰撞中所产生介质的有力且敏感的工具。通过结合具有现实能量损失模型的改进蒙特卡洛模拟，本工作表明，涨落分析可约束QCD介质的性质、检验部分子能量损失的理论模型，并提供相变的可观测信号，从而助力实验对QCD相图的测绘。

Abstract: This work presents an analysis of event-by-event multiplicity fluctuations as a sensitive tool for diagnosing the state of matter produced in relativistic heavy-ion collisions. Using a modified version of the HIJING Monte Carlo generator, which integrates various models of partonic energy loss in hot (quark-gluon plasma) and cold media, the connection between fluctuation dynamics and system properties is investigated. It is shown that the nature and magnitude of fluctuations allow for the identification of the created medium type (hot or cold), the testing of the adequacy of energy loss models, and the detection of signatures of a first-order phase transition in different kinematic regions. The results obtained are important for interpreting the data from experiments aimed at mapping the QCD phase diagram and searching for the critical point.

### [91] [First Estimation of Model Parameters for Neutrino-Induced Nucleon Knockout Using Simulation-Based Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09778)
*Karla Tame-Narvaez,Steven Gardiner,Aleksandra Ćiprijanović,Giuseppe Cerati*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates the use of simulation-based inference (SBI), a machine learning technique, to tune neutrino interaction models in the GENIE event generator, showing that SBI can recover parameters consistent with—but slightly different from—those obtained via traditional empirical tuning by the MicroBooNE collaboration, and can also generalize to approximate simulations from a different generator (NuWro).  
\n\n
本文研究了使用基于仿真的推理（Simulation-Based Inference, SBI）这一机器学习技术来调节GENIE中微子事例生成器中的中微子相互作用模型，表明SBI能够恢复与MicroBooNE合作组通过传统经验调参获得的参数一致但略有不同的参数值，并且还能泛化以近似另一个生成器（NuWro）的模拟结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Current neutrino oscillation experiments rely on detailed Monte Carlo simulations of nuclear interactions in the GeV energy range, but existing models like GENIE suffer from theoretical and empirical limitations, necessitating ad hoc parameter tuning to match data. As experimental precision improves, the complexity of such tuning grows, motivating the exploration of more systematic and scalable approaches like machine learning–based simulation-based inference.  
\n\n
当前中微子振荡实验依赖于GeV能区核相互作用的详细蒙特卡洛模拟，但现有模型（如GENIE）存在理论和经验上的局限性，必须通过临时性的参数调优来匹配数据。随着实验精度不断提高，此类调参的复杂性日益增长，因此有必要探索更系统、可扩展的方法，例如基于机器学习的Simulation-Based Inference（SBI）。

Method: The authors apply simulation-based inference (SBI) using neural density estimators to infer four key physics parameters of the GENIE neutrino event generator. They train the SBI model on simulated data matching the MicroBooNE experimental configuration and compare inferred parameters against both the original tuned cross-section predictions and the actual MicroBooNE data. Additionally, they test the generalization capability of the trained SBI model by applying it to simulations from NuWro, a different event generator sharing only a subset of physics parameters with GENIE.  
\n\n
作者采用基于神经密度估计器的Simulation-Based Inference（SBI）方法，推断GENIE中微子事例生成器中的四个关键物理参数。他们在与MicroBooNE实验配置匹配的模拟数据上训练SBI模型，并将推断出的参数与原始调优的截面预测值及实际MicroBooNE数据进行比较。此外，他们还通过将训练好的SBI模型应用于NuWro（一个与GENIE仅共享部分物理参数的事件生成器）的模拟数据，测试其泛化能力。

Result: When applied to MicroBooNE’s experimental data, the SBI-inferred parameters differ modestly from the originally tuned values but remain within MicroBooNE’s reported uncertainties and yield a slightly improved goodness-of-fit. Furthermore, the same SBI model successfully approximates NuWro simulations despite differences in underlying physics modeling, demonstrating cross-generator generalizability.  
\n\n
当应用于MicroBooNE实验数据时，SBI推断出的参数与原始调优值略有不同，但仍处于MicroBooNE报告的不确定性范围内，并获得了略优的拟合优度（goodness-of-fit）。此外，尽管底层物理建模存在差异，同一SBI模型仍能成功近似NuWro的模拟结果，展现出跨生成器的泛化能力。

Conclusion: Simulation-based inference is a promising, flexible framework for tuning neutrino interaction models, capable of matching or improving upon conventional empirical tuning while offering potential for generalization across different simulation frameworks. This suggests SBI could play a key role in future high-precision neutrino experiments.  
\n\n
Simulation-Based Inference（SBI）是一种有前景且灵活的框架，可用于调节中微子相互作用模型，其性能可媲美甚至优于传统的经验调参方法，并具备跨不同模拟框架的泛化潜力。这表明SBI可能在未来高精度中微子实验中发挥关键作用。

Abstract: To enable an accurate determination of oscillation parameters, accelerator-based neutrino experiments require detailed simulations of nuclear interaction physics in the GeV regime. While substantial effort from both theory and experiment is currently being invested to improve the fidelity of these simulations, their present deficiencies typically oblige experimental collaborations to resort to empirical tuning of simulation model parameters. As the precision requirements of the field continue to become more stringent, machine learning techniques may provide a powerful means of handling corresponding growth in the complexity of future neutrino interaction model tuning exercises. To study the suitability of simulation-based inference (SBI) for this physics application, in this paper we revisit a tuned configuration of the GENIE neutrino event generator that was originally developed by the MicroBooNE collaboration. Despite closely reproducing the adopted values of four physics parameters when confronted with the tuned cross-section predictions as input, we find that our trained SBI algorithm prefers modestly different values (within MicroBooNE's assigned uncertainties) and achieves slightly better goodness-of-fit when inference is run on the experimental data set originally used by MicroBooNE. We also find that our trained algorithm can create a fair approximation of an alternative neutrino scattering simulation, NuWro, that shares only a subset of its physics model parameters with GENIE.

</details>


### [92] [Heavy dibaryons $Ξ^{(*)}_{cc}Ξ^{(*)}_{cc}$ and $Ξ^{(*)}_{bb}Ξ^{(*)}_{bb}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09830)
*An-Su Lu,Mao-Jun Yan,Chun-Sheng An,Cheng-Rong Deng*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates possible deuteronlike dibaryon bound states in the $\\Xi_{cc}\\Xi_{cc}$ and $\\Xi_{bb}\\Xi_{bb}$ systems using a nonrelativistic quark model, identifying specific isospin-spin channels that support binding via meson exchange, with notable enhancement from coupled-channel effects—especially yielding a compact hexaquark state in the di-$\\Xi_{bb}$ system.
\n\n
本文在非相对论夸克模型框架下系统研究了$\\Xi_{cc}\\Xi_{cc}$和$\\Xi_{bb}\\Xi_{bb}$系统中可能存在的类氘核双重重子束缚态，识别出特定同位旋-自旋通道可通过介子交换产生束缚，并发现耦合道效应显著增强吸引力——尤其在di-$\\Xi_{bb}$系统中形成一个紧致的六夸克态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the theoretical interest in exotic hadronic states beyond conventional mesons and baryons, particularly heavy-flavor dibaryons composed of doubly charmed or doubly bottomed baryons. Understanding whether such systems can form bound states analogous to the deuteron provides insight into QCD dynamics in the heavy-quark regime and the role of meson-exchange forces in multiquark systems.
\n\n
动机源于对超出传统介子和重子范畴的奇异强子态（特别是由双重粲或双重底重子构成的重味双重重子）的理论兴趣。探究此类系统能否形成类氘核的束缚态，有助于理解重夸克区域中的QCD动力学以及介子交换力在多夸克系统中的作用。

Method: The authors employ a nonrelativistic quark model incorporating meson-exchange interactions (e.g., $\\sigma$, $\\pi$) between constituent baryons. They analyze single-channel and coupled-channel dynamics for various isospin $I$ and total angular momentum-parity $J^P$ configurations of the $\\Xi^{(*)}_{cc}\\Xi^{(*)}_{cc}$ and $\\Xi^{(*)}_{bb}\\Xi^{(*)}_{bb}$ systems. Binding energies and spatial sizes are computed by solving the Schrödinger equation with effective potentials derived from quark-level interactions and meson exchanges.
\n\n
作者采用包含介子交换相互作用（如$\\sigma$、$\\pi$）的非相对论夸克模型，分析$\\Xi^{(*)}_{cc}\\Xi^{(*)}_{cc}$和$\\Xi^{(*)}_{bb}\\Xi^{(*)}_{bb}$系统在不同同位旋$I$和总角动量宇称$J^P$构型下的单道与耦合道动力学。通过求解由夸克层次相互作用和介子交换导出的有效势的薛定谔方程，计算束缚能和空间尺度。

Result: For di-$\\Xi_{cc}$, only $0(1^+)$ channels in $\\Xi_{cc}\\Xi^*_{cc}$ and $\\Xi^*_{cc}\\Xi^*_{cc}$ form weakly bound states ($\\sim -1.5$ to $-3.3$ MeV). Coupled-channel effects in $0(1^+)$ yield a deeper bound state at $-7.5$ MeV with size 1.40 fm. For di-$\\Xi_{bb}$, multiple $0(J^+)$ ($J=1,2,3$) and $1(J^+)$ ($J=0,2$) channels produce bound states with binding energies from $-0.5$ to $-14.3$ MeV. The coupled $0(1^+)$ channel forms a compact hexaquark with binding energy $-21.2$ MeV and radius 0.53 fm, driven dominantly by $\\pi$-exchange. Meson exchange is generally essential except for $\\Xi_{bb}^*\\Xi_{bb}^*$ with $1(0^+)$.
\n\n
对于di-$\\Xi_{cc}$，仅$0(1^+)$通道的$\\Xi_{cc}\\Xi^*_{cc}$和$\\Xi^*_{cc}\\Xi^*_{cc}$形成弱束缚态（约$-1.5$至$-3.3$ MeV）；考虑耦合道效应后，$0(1^+)$通道产生更深的束缚态（$-7.5$ MeV，尺度1.40 fm）。对于di-$\\Xi_{bb}$，多个$0(J^+)$（$J=1,2,3$）和$1(J^+)$（$J=0,2$）通道均产生束缚态，束缚能从$-0.5$到$-14.3$ MeV不等；其中耦合的$0(1^+)$通道形成一个紧致六夸克态（束缚能$-21.2$ MeV，半径0.53 fm），主要由$\\pi$交换驱动。除$1(0^+)$的$\\Xi_{bb}^*\\Xi_{bb}^*$外，介子交换在di-$\\Xi_{bb}$束缚态中普遍不可或缺。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that heavy-flavor dibaryon systems, particularly those with double-bottom quarks, can form stable deuteronlike or even compact hexaquark bound states due to strong meson-exchange forces, especially $\\pi$ and $\\sigma$ exchanges. Coupled-channel effects significantly enhance binding, suggesting that such exotic states may be observable in future high-energy experiments, offering a new window into nonperturbative QCD.
\n\n
研究表明，重味双重重子系统（尤其是双重底系统）可通过强介子交换力（特别是$\\pi$和$\\sigma$交换）形成稳定的类氘核甚至紧致六夸克束缚态。耦合道效应显著增强束缚，表明此类奇异态可能在未来的高能实验中被观测到，为探索非微扰QCD提供新途径。

Abstract: We systematically investigate the dibaryons $Ξ^{(*)}_{cc}Ξ^{(*)}_{cc}$ (di-$Ξ_{cc}$) and $Ξ^{(*)}_{bb}Ξ^{(*)}_{bb}$ (di-$Ξ_{bb}$), with various isospin-spin configurations $I(J^P)$ in a nonrelativistic quark model. For the di-$Ξ_{cc}$ system, only the single channels $Ξ_{cc}Ξ^*_{cc}$ and $Ξ^*_{cc}Ξ^*_{cc}$ with $0(1^+)$ are capable of forming deuteronlike bound states, with the $σ$ meson exchange playing a decisive role. Those states have binding energies of approximately $-1.5$ MeV and $-3.3$ MeV and sizes of 2.37 fm and 1.87 fm, respectively. The coupled channel effect in the di-$Ξ_{cc}$ system with $0(1^+)$ enhances the attraction. As a result, this di-$Ξ_{cc}$ system can establish a deuteronlike configuration, with the binding energy of $-7.5$ MeV relative to the threshold $Ξ_{cc}Ξ_{cc}$ and the size of approximately 1.40 fm. For the di-$Ξ_{bb}$ system, the single channels with $0(1^+)$, $0(2^+)$, and $0(3^+)$ can give rise to deuteronlike bound states with binding energies ranging from $-6.1$ MeV to $-14.3$ MeV. Additionally, the di-$Ξ_{bb}$ system with $1(0^+)$ and $1(2^+)$ can also establish deuteronlike bound states with binding energies of around $-0.5$ MeV. When considering the coupled channel effect in the di-$Ξ_{bb}$ system with $0(1^+)$, a compact hexaquark state is formed, exhibiting a binding energy of $-21.2$ MeV relative to the threshold $Ξ_{bb}Ξ_{bb}$ and a size of 0.53 fm. In this state, the $π$ meson exchange provides a very powerful attractive force. The meson exchange interactions in the quark model is dispensable in the di-$Ξ_{bb}$ bound states, except for $Ξ_{bb}^*Ξ_{bb}^*$ with $1(0^+)$.

### [93] [Subtracted Dispersion Relations for Virtual Compton Scattering off the Proton](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09831)
*I. Danilkin,B. Pasquini,M. Ronchi,M. Vanderhaeghen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper develops a once-subtracted dispersion relation (DR) formalism for virtual Compton scattering (VCS) up to the $\\Delta(1232)$ resonance region, enabling a data-driven extraction of the nucleon's electric and magnetic generalized polarizabilities from $e^- p \\to e^- \\gamma p$ experiments at Jefferson Lab. The subtraction constants in the DR correspond to scalar generalized polarizabilities, and the $s$- and $t$-channel discontinuities are constructed using empirical pion production and $\\pi\\pi$ scattering data.
\n\n
本文提出了一种单次减除的色散关系（DR）形式体系，用于处理从阈值到$\\Delta(1232)$共振区的虚康普顿散射（VCS）过程，旨在从$e^- p \\to e^- \\gamma p$实验中以数据驱动方式提取核子的电与磁广义极化率。该方法中的减除常数对应于标量广义极化率，而$s$-和$t$-道不连续性则基于π介子光/电产生及$\\pi\\pi$散射的实验数据构建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to extract nucleon generalized polarizabilities—fundamental structure observables—with high precision from ongoing and upcoming VCS experiments at Jefferson Lab. Existing unsubtracted DR approaches suffer from convergence issues and model dependence in the $\\Delta(1232)$ region; a once-subtracted DR improves convergence and isolates the polarizabilities as subtraction constants, enabling a more robust and data-driven analysis.
\n\n
动机源于需要从Jefferson Lab当前及未来虚康普顿散射（VCS）实验中高精度提取核子广义极化率——这些是描述核子内部结构的基本观测量。现有的无减除色散关系（DR）方法在$\\Delta(1232)$能区存在收敛性问题和模型依赖性；引入单次减除DR可改善收敛性，并将广义极化率作为减除常数分离出来，从而实现更稳健且数据驱动的分析。

Method: The authors employ a once-subtracted dispersion relation for the VCS amplitude, where the subtraction constants are identified with the scalar generalized polarizabilities. The $s$-channel discontinuity is reconstructed from $\\gamma^\\ast p \\to \\pi N \\to \\gamma p$ using empirical pion photo- and electro-production data. The $t$-channel discontinuity is derived from $\\gamma^\\ast \\gamma \\to \\pi\\pi \\to N \\bar{N}$ by combining recent dispersive analyses of $\\gamma^\\ast \\gamma \\to \\pi\\pi$ and $\\pi\\pi \\to N \\bar{N}$. This yields a fully data-constrained DR framework below the $\\Delta(1232)$ resonance.
\n\n
作者采用单次减除的色散关系来描述VCS振幅，其中减除常数被识别为标量广义极化率。$s$-道不连续性通过$\\gamma^\\ast p \\to \\pi N \\to \\gamma p$过程，利用π介子光致和电致产生实验数据重建；$t$-道不连续性则通过$\\gamma^\\ast \\gamma \\to \\pi\\pi \\to N \\bar{N}$过程，结合近期对$\\gamma^\\ast \\gamma \\to \\pi\\pi$和$\\pi\\pi \\to N \\bar{N}$的色散分析结果获得。由此构建了一个在$\\Delta(1232)$共振以下完全由数据约束的色散关系框架。

Result: The formalism successfully reproduces existing VCS cross-section data and demonstrates clear sensitivity to the scalar generalized polarizabilities through their role as subtraction constants. The data-driven construction of both $s$- and $t$-channel contributions significantly reduces model dependence compared to previous unsubtracted DR approaches, particularly in the $\\Delta(1232)$ energy region.
\n\n
该形式体系成功复现了现有的VCS微分截面数据，并通过标量广义极化率作为减除常数的角色，清晰展示了可观测量对其的敏感性。与以往无减除DR方法相比，$s$-和$t$-道贡献的数据驱动构建显著降低了模型依赖性，尤其在$\\Delta(1232)$能区表现突出。

Conclusion: The once-subtracted DR formalism provides a theoretically sound and empirically constrained framework for extracting nucleon generalized polarizabilities from VCS data. By anchoring the dispersion integrals in experimental inputs and identifying polarizabilities with subtraction constants, the approach meets the precision requirements of modern experiments and sets a foundation for future high-accuracy extractions at Jefferson Lab.
\n\n
单次减除的色散关系形式体系为从VCS数据中提取核子广义极化率提供了一个理论自洽且经验约束的框架。通过将色散积分锚定于实验输入，并将极化率与减除常数直接关联，该方法满足了现代实验的精度要求，为Jefferson Lab未来高精度提取奠定了基础。

Abstract: We present a once-subtracted dispersion relation (DR) formalism for the virtual Compton scattering (VCS) process from threshold up to the $Δ(1232)$ energy region. The formalism aims at extracting the nucleon's electric and magnetic generalized polarizabilities from the $e^- p \to e^- γp$ process, in view of the precision goals of the present and near future experiments at Jefferson Lab. The present work improves upon the existing unsubtracted DR formalism in several ways. The required $s$- and $t$-channel discontinuities in the subtracted dispersion integrals are obtained in a largely data-driven manner in this energy region. The $s$-channel dispersive integrals are reconstructed from $γ^\ast p \to πN \to γp$ using pion photo- and electro-production data, while the $t$-channel dispersion integrals are evaluated from $γ^\ast γ\to ππ\to N \bar N$ using recent dispersive analyses of both the $γ^\ast γ\to ππ$ and $ππ\to N \bar N$ processes. We compare our results to VCS data and show the sensitivity of the observables to the nucleon's scalar generalized polarizabilities, which enter the present formalism as subtraction constants.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent theoretical progress in enforcing elastic unitarity within the fixed center approximation (FCA) for particle–two-body cluster scattering, combined with the imminent release of ALICE data on the $p~f_1(1285)$ correlation function, motivates a reevaluation of prior predictions. Understanding the nature of axial-vector mesons—particularly whether they are elementary or dynamically generated—requires precise theoretical input that respects fundamental constraints like unitarity.
\n\n
近期在粒子–双体团簇散射的固定中心近似（FCA）框架中实现弹性幺正性的理论进展，结合 ALICE 即将发布的 $p~f_1(1285)$ 关联函数实验数据，促使作者重新评估先前的理论预言。要理解轴矢介子（axial-vector meson）的本质——特别是其是基本态还是动力学生成态——需要满足幺正性等基本约束的精确理论输入。

Method: The authors improve upon the standard Fixed Center Approximation (FCA) by implementing elastic unitarity in the scattering of a nucleon off a two-body cluster representing the $f_1(1285)$ meson. This involves solving Lippmann–Schwinger-type equations with unitarized amplitudes derived from chiral or effective Lagrangians, ensuring consistency with S-matrix unitarity.
