\n\n
作者在标准固定中心近似（FCA）基础上进行改进，通过在核子与代表 $f_1(1285)$ 介子的双体团簇散射过程中引入弹性幺正性。具体方法包括求解基于手征或有效拉氏量导出的幺正化振幅所构成的 Lippmann–Schwinger 型方程，以确保 S 矩阵满足幺正性。所得 T 矩阵随后通过 Koonin–Pratt 形式用于计算 $p~f_1(1285)$ 关联函数，适用于重离子碰撞实验分析。

Result: The updated calculation yields appreciable quantitative differences in the $p~f_1(1285)$ correlation function and low-energy scattering parameters (e.g., scattering length and effective range) compared to non-unitarized FCA results. These modifications enhance the reliability of theoretical predictions and provide a more robust basis for interpreting upcoming ALICE measurements.
\n\n
更新后的计算在 $p~f_1(1285)$ 关联函数和低能散射参数（如散射长度和有效力程）上相较于未实施幺正化的 FCA 结果展现出显著的定量差异。这些修正提升了理论预言的可靠性，为解读即将公布的 ALICE 测量结果提供了更坚实的基础。

Conclusion: Implementing elastic unitarity in the fixed center approximation significantly improves the description of hadronic correlation functions involving unstable resonances like $f_1(1285)$. 在固定中心近似中引入弹性幺正性显著改善了对涉及 $f_1(1285)$ 等不稳定共振态的强子关联函数的描述。将这些改进后的理论预言与即将获得的 ALICE 数据进行对比，将为轴矢介子的内部结构提供关键洞见，有助于区分紧致夸克模型态与分子态或动力学生成态。

Abstract: In view of the recent theoretical developments in the fixed center approximation for the scattering of a particle with a a two-body cluster, implementing elastic unitarity on the standard fixed center formalism, and the imminent availability of ALICE data on the correlation function of the $p~f_1(1285)$ system, we update the results of a previous work for this correlation function and the low-energy scattering observables. The new results show appreciable changes in some observables and should provide valuable input for comparison with the forthcoming experimental data. ### [95] [Polarization transfer in $ψ'\toψππ$: a complete spin density matrix analysis framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09858)
*Jiabao Gong,Guanyu Wang,Dongyu Yuan,Libo Liao,Yilun Wang,Jiarong Li,Xiaoshen Kang,Lei Zhang,Jin Zhang,Gang Li*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A Spin Density Matrix (SDM) formalism is developed to describe polarization transfer in the decay chain $e^+e^- \rightarrow ψ^\prime \rightarrow ψππ$, showing perfect SDM preservation for $S$-wave $ππ$ emission ($ρ_ψ = ρ_{ψ^\prime}$), with quantified $D$-wave corrections and a proposed self-consistency test. The framework applies broadly to charmonium, bottomonium, and electroweak processes like $e^+e^- \to Z^\ast \to ZH$.
\n\n
本文发展了一种基于自旋密度矩阵（Spin Density Matrix, SDM）的形式体系，用于描述衰变链 $e^+e^- \rightarrow ψ^\prime \rightarrow ψππ$ 中的极化转移。对于主导的 $S$ 波 $ππ$ 发射，SDM 完全守恒（$ρ_ψ = ρ_{ψ^\prime}$），使得 $ψ$ 成为初始极化态的理想探针；同时量化了 $D$ 波贡献引起的偏差，并提出了一种自洽性实验检验方法。该形式体系可推广至粲偶素（如 $ψ' \to h_cπ^0$）、底偶素（如 $Υ(nS) \to Υ(mS)ππ$）以及电弱过程（如 $e^+e^- \to Z^\ast \to ZH$）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to establish a rigorous and general theoretical framework for analyzing polarization transfer in sequential particle decays, particularly in $e^+e^- \rightarrow ψ^\prime \rightarrow ψππ$. Previous treatments, such as Cahn's analysis, are incomplete; a full Spin Density Matrix (SDM) description is needed to accurately relate the polarization states of parent and daughter particles and to enable precise amplitude analyses in background-free environments.
\n\n
动机在于建立一个严格且普适的理论框架，以分析级联粒子衰变（特别是 $e^+e^- \rightarrow ψ^\prime \rightarrow ψππ$）中的极化转移。以往的处理（如 Cahn 的分析）并不完整，需要完整的自旋密度矩阵（Spin Density Matrix, SDM）描述，以精确关联母粒子与子粒子的极化态，并在无连续谱背景的环境中实现精确的振幅分析。

Method: The authors generalize Cahn’s approach using the full Spin Density Matrix (SDM) formalism. They derive explicit relations between the SDMs of $ψ^\prime$ and $ψ$ by decomposing the $ππ$ emission into partial waves ($S$- and $D$-waves). Angular momentum conservation and the tensor structure of the transition amplitudes are used to compute the polarization transfer kernel. A self-consistency test is constructed by exploiting interference between partial waves to simultaneously validate the framework and constrain amplitudes.
\n\n
作者通过完整的自旋密度矩阵（Spin Density Matrix, SDM）形式体系推广了 Cahn 的方法。他们将 $ππ$ 发射按分波展开（$S$ 波和 $D$ 波），利用角动量守恒和跃迁振幅的张量结构，推导出 $ψ^\prime$ 与 $ψ$ 的 SDM 之间的显式关系，并计算极化转移核。通过利用分波之间的干涉，构建了一个自洽性检验，可同时验证该框架并约束分波振幅。

Result: For pure $S$-wave $ππ$ emission, the SDM is exactly preserved: $ρ_ψ = ρ_{ψ^\prime}$. $D$-wave contributions introduce calculable deviations. The framework enables clean extraction of $ψ$ polarization without continuum background contamination. It is validated through a proposed experimental self-consistency condition. The formalism is shown to apply universally across hadronic transitions in charmonium and bottomonium, and even to electroweak processes like $e^+e^- \to Z^\ast \to ZH$ due to shared angular-momentum structure.
\n\n
对于纯 $S$ 波 $ππ$ 发射，SDM 严格守恒：$ρ_ψ = ρ_{ψ^\prime}$；$D$ 波贡献引入可计算的偏差。该框架可在无连续谱背景污染的情况下干净地提取 $ψ$ 的极化信息，并通过提出的实验自洽性条件加以验证。由于共享相同的角动量结构，该形式体系被证明可普适应用于粲偶素和底偶素中的强子跃迁，甚至适用于 $e^+e^- \to Z^\ast \to ZH$ 等电弱过程。

Conclusion: The Spin Density Matrix formalism provides a complete, model-independent description of polarization transfer in two-pion-mediated sequential decays. It establishes $ψ$ as an ideal polarization probe when $S$-wave dominates and offers a robust method for amplitude analysis. Its universality across quarkonium systems and electroweak processes makes it a powerful tool for probing fundamental dynamics from QCD bound states to Higgs physics.
\n\n
自旋密度矩阵（SDM）形式体系为双π介子媒介的级联衰变中的极化转移提供了完整且模型无关的描述。当 $S$ 波主导时，该框架确立了 $ψ$ 作为理想极化探针的地位，并为振幅分析提供了稳健方法。其在夸克偶素系统和电弱过程中的普适性，使其成为从 QCD 束缚态到 Higgs 物理中探测基本动力学的有力工具。

Abstract: A theoretical framework based on the Spin Density Matrix (SDM) formalism is developed to describe polarization transfer in the decay chain $e^+e^- \rightarrow ψ^\prime \rightarrow ψππ$. Explicit relations connecting the SDMs of $ψ^\prime$ and $ψ$ are derived, generalizing Cahn's analysis into a complete SDM treatment. For the dominant $S$-wave $ππ$ emission, the SDM is shown to be perfectly preserved, $ρ_ψ= ρ_{ψ^\prime}$, rendering the $ψ$ an ideal probe of the initial polarization state. Deviations arising from $D$-wave contributions are quantified, and a self-consistency experimental test is proposed that simultaneously validates the framework and constrains partial wave amplitudes. This formalism provides a consistent basis for extracting $ψ$ polarization and for amplitude analyses of subsequent $ψ$ decays in a continuum-background-free environment. The framework extends to other hadronic transitions, including $ψ' \to h_cπ^0$ in charmonium and $Υ(nS) \to Υ(mS)ππ$ in bottomonium, as well as to electroweak processes such as $e^+e^- \to Z^\ast \to ZH$, where the same angular-momentum structure governs polarization transfer -- offering a unified probe of dynamics from charmonium to the Higgs sector.

</details>


### [96] [Jet energy loss in anisotropic plasmas meets limiting attractors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09912)
*Kirill Boguslavski,Lucas Hörl,Florian Lindenbauer*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper studies the energy loss of high-energy partons in an early-stage anisotropic quark-gluon plasma (QGP) formed in heavy-ion collisions. Using the harmonic approximation, the authors compute modifications to the mean energy of emitted gluons due to anisotropic jet quenching parameters ($\hat q_x \neq \hat q_y$). They find that anisotropy induces only small corrections and derive a simple "pocket formula" to quantify this effect. By combining their results with $\hat q$ values from QCD kinetic theory simulations, they show that the medium-length dependence of energy loss aligns with limiting attractor behavior seen in both weak- and strong-coupling limits, thereby linking jet energy loss to universal dynamics of anisotropic plasmas.
\n\n
本文研究了重离子碰撞中早期各向异性夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）内高能部分子的能量损失。作者在谐波近似下计算了由各向异性喷注淬火参数（$\hat q_x \neq \hat q_y$）引起的辐射胶子平均能量的修正。他们发现各向异性仅带来微小修正，并推导出一个简洁的“口袋公式”来量化该效应。通过将结果与QCD kinetic theory模拟提取的$\hat q$值结合，他们表明能量损失对介质长度的依赖呈现出极限吸引子（limiting attractors）的行为——这种行为可在弱耦合和强耦合极限下外推获得，从而将喷注部分子能量损失与各向异性等离子体的普适动力学联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to understand how jet quenching—a key probe of the quark-gluon plasma—is modified in the early, highly anisotropic stages of heavy-ion collisions, where standard isotropic approximations for the medium may break down. By quantifying the effect of momentum-space anisotropy on parton energy loss, the authors aim to bridge phenomenological jet observables with fundamental properties of non-equilibrium QCD matter and its universal dynamical features.
\n\n
动机源于理解喷注淬火（夸克-胶子等离子体的关键探针）在重离子碰撞早期高度各向异性阶段如何被修正，因为在该阶段介质的标准各向同性近似可能失效。通过量化动量空间各向异性对部分子能量损失的影响，作者旨在将唯象的喷注观测量与非平衡QCD物质的基本性质及其普适动力学特征联系起来。

Method: The authors employ the harmonic approximation to model the propagation of high-energy partons and the induced gluon radiation in an anisotropic medium. They introduce direction-dependent jet quenching parameters $\hat q_x$ and $\hat q_y$, solve the corresponding integrals for the mean emitted gluon energy numerically, and compare the results to the isotropic case ($\hat q_x = \hat q_y$). A simplified analytical “pocket formula” is then derived to capture the leading-order anisotropy correction. Finally, they incorporate realistic $\hat q$ values from QCD kinetic theory simulations to study the dependence of energy loss on the medium length $L$, and analyze its behavior in the limits of zero and infinite coupling.
\n\n
作者采用谐波近似来建模高能部分子在各向异性介质中的传播及诱导胶子辐射。他们引入方向依赖的喷注淬火参数$\hat q_x$和$\hat q_y$，数值求解辐射胶子平均能量的相应积分，并与各向同性情形（$\hat q_x = \hat q_y$）进行比较。随后推导出一个简化的解析“口袋公式”以捕捉主导阶的各向异性修正。最后，他们结合来自QCD kinetic theory模拟的真实$\hat q$值，研究能量损失对介质长度$L$的依赖性，并分析其在零耦合与无穷耦合极限下的行为。

Result: The numerical evaluation shows that anisotropy in the jet quenching parameters leads to only small changes in the mean energy of emitted gluons compared to the isotropic case. The derived pocket formula accurately captures this effect. When combined with $\hat q(L)$ from QCD kinetic theory, the mean energy loss as a function of medium length $L$ exhibits scaling behavior consistent with limiting attractors—namely, the asymptotic forms predicted by both weak-coupling (BDMPS-Z) and strong-coupling (AdS/CFT) frameworks. This suggests a universal character in the energy loss dynamics across coupling regimes in anisotropic plasmas.
\n\n
数值评估表明，与各向同性情形相比，喷注淬火参数的各向异性仅对辐射胶子的平均能量产生微小改变。所推导的口袋公式能准确描述这一效应。当结合QCD kinetic theory给出的$\hat q(L)$后，平均能量损失作为介质长度$L$的函数展现出与极限吸引子一致的标度行为——即弱耦合（BDMPS-Z）和强耦合（AdS/CFT）框架所预测的渐近形式。这表明在各向异性等离子体中，能量损失动力学在不同耦合强度下具有普适性。

Conclusion: The paper demonstrates that while anisotropy in the early-stage QGP induces only modest corrections to parton energy loss, its inclusion reveals a deeper connection between jet quenching and universal non-equilibrium dynamics. The emergence of limiting attractor behavior in the medium-length dependence of energy loss—spanning weak to strong coupling—suggests that jet observables can serve as probes of universal properties of anisotropic QCD matter, beyond perturbative descriptions.
\n\n
本文表明，尽管早期QGP中的各向异性仅对部分子能量损失带来适度修正，但其引入揭示了喷注淬火与普适非平衡动力学之间的深层联系。能量损失对介质长度依赖所呈现的极限吸引子行为（横跨弱耦合到强耦合）表明，喷注观测量可作为探测各向异性QCD物质普适性质的工具，超越微扰描述的范畴。

Abstract: We consider the energy loss of a high-energy parton in the early anisotropic plasma in heavy-ion collisions. Working in the harmonic approximation, we compute the change in the mean energy of an emitted gluon in the presence of an anisotropic background, characterized by anisotropic jet quenching parameters $\hat q_{x}\neq \hat q_{y}$. Evaluating the resulting integrals numerically, we compare with isotropic media, and obtain a simple pocket formula to estimate the impact of anisotropy on the mean emitted gluon energy, which is generally small. We then combine our results with the values of the jet quenching parameter extracted from QCD kinetic theory simulations and show that the medium length dependence of this mean energy loss exhibits the characteristics of limiting attractors, which can be obtained by extrapolating to zero and infinite coupling. Our study thus relates energy loss of jet partons to universal dynamics of anisotropic plasmas.

</details>


### [97] [Back-to-back dijet production in DIS with finite-energy corrections and twist-3 gluon TMDs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09960)
*Tolga Altinoluk,Guillaume Beuf,Alina Czajka,Cyrille Marquet*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper computes the dijet production cross section in deep inelastic scattering (DIS) at small $x$ to next-to-eikonal accuracy in the back-to-back jet limit, expressing it in terms of transverse-momentum-dependent (TMD) gluon distributions and linking next-to-eikonal corrections to the $x$-dependent phase of twist-2 gluon TMDs and twist-3 unpolarized gluon TMDs.
\n\n
本文在背对背喷注极限下，计算了小 $x$ 深度非弹性散射（DIS）中双喷注产生截面的次领头幂次（next-to-eikonal）精度结果，并将其用横动量依赖（TMD）胶子分布表示，特别揭示了次领头幂次修正与 twist-2 胶子 TMD 的 $x$ 依赖相位及 twist-3 无极化胶子 TMD 之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding dijet production in DIS at small $x$ provides a crucial probe of high-energy QCD dynamics, particularly in the saturation regime. Previous leading-eikonal treatments capture dominant contributions but miss subleading yet potentially significant corrections. The motivation is to extend the theoretical description beyond the eikonal approximation by incorporating next-to-eikonal effects, which are essential for precision phenomenology and for uncovering the structure of TMD parton distributions beyond leading twist.
\n\n
在小 $x$ 区域研究深度非弹性散射中的双喷注产生过程，是探测高能 QCD 动力学（尤其是饱和区域）的关键手段。以往的领头幂次（eikonal）处理虽然捕捉了主导贡献，但忽略了次领头但可能显著的修正项。本文旨在将理论描述推广至领头幂次近似之外，纳入次领头幂次效应，这对精确唯象学以及揭示超越领头 twist 的 TMD 部分子分布结构至关重要。

Method: The authors employ an effective field theory approach based on the high-energy (small-$x$) limit of QCD, building upon their prior work. They calculate the dijet cross section in the back-to-back configuration where the total transverse momentum of the dijet system is small. Using factorization theorems valid at small $x$, they express the cross section in terms of TMD gluon distributions. The next-to-eikonal corrections are systematically derived by analyzing subleading power contributions in the expansion of the scattering amplitude, connecting them to specific TMD matrix elements: namely, the $x$-dependent phase of the twist-2 gluon TMD and the twist-3 unpolarized gluon TMDs.
\n\n
作者基于 QCD 在高能（小 $x$）极限下的有效场论方法，依托其先前工作，在双喷注总横动量较小的背对背构型下计算截面。他们利用适用于小 $x$ 的因子化定理，将截面表示为 TMD 胶子分布的形式。通过系统分析散射振幅展开中的次领头幂次贡献，推导出次领头幂次修正，并将其与特定的 TMD 矩阵元联系起来：即 twist-2 胶子 TMD 的 $x$ 依赖相位和 twist-3 无极化胶子 TMD。

Result: The main result is an explicit expression for the dijet production cross section at next-to-eikonal accuracy in terms of TMD gluon distributions. The calculation reveals that next-to-eikonal corrections introduce two new structures: (1) an $x$-dependent complex phase multiplying the standard twist-2 gluon TMD, and (2) contributions proportional to twist-3 unpolarized gluon TMDs. This provides a concrete link between power-suppressed corrections in the high-energy limit and higher-twist TMD operators.
\n\n
主要结果是给出了以 TMD 胶子分布表示的次领头幂次精度双喷注产生截面的显式表达式。计算表明，次领头幂次修正引入了两种新结构：(1) 一个乘在标准 twist-2 胶子 TMD 上的 $x$ 依赖复相位；(2) 与 twist-3 无极化胶子 TMD 成正比的贡献。这建立了高能极限下幂次压低修正与高 twist TMD 算符之间的具体联系。

Conclusion: The inclusion of next-to-eikonal corrections enriches the TMD factorization framework for small-$x$ DIS by incorporating both dynamical phases and higher-twist effects. This advances the theoretical understanding of subleading power corrections in high-energy QCD and provides a more complete description of dijet production sensitive to the detailed structure of gluon TMDs, which can be tested in future electron-ion collider experiments.
\n\n
纳入次领头幂次修正确实丰富了小 $x$ DIS 的 TMD 因子化框架，同时包含了动力学相位和高 twist 效应。这推进了对高能 QCD 中次领头幂次修正的理论理解，并为双喷注产生过程提供了更完整的描述，使其对胶子 TMD 的精细结构敏感，可在未来的电子-离子对撞机实验中进行检验。

Abstract: This work presents the summary of calculation of the cross section of the dijet production in deep inelastic scattering at small x at next-to-eikonal accuracy. The cross section is calculated in the back-to-back limit of the produced jets using results obtained in our previous works. The cross section is expressed via the transverse-momentum-dependent (TMD) parton distributions. Specifically, we show how the next-to-eikonal corrections are related to the $x$ dependent phase of twist-2 gluon TMD and to twist-3 unpolarized gluon TMDs.

</details>
